Mat  The book of the generations of Jesus Christ the son of David the son of Abraham
Mat  The son of Abraham was Isaac and the son of Isaac was Jacob and the sons of Jacob were Judah and his brothers
Mat  And the sons of Judah were Perez and Zerah by Tamar and the son of Perez was Hezron and the son of Hezron was Ram
Mat  And the son of Ram was Amminadab and the son of Amminadab was Nahshon and the son of Nahshon was Salmon
Mat  And the son of Salmon by Rahab was Boaz and the son of Boaz by Ruth was Obed and the son of Obed was Jesse
Mat  And the son of Jesse was David the king and the son of David was Solomon by her who had been the wife of Uriah
Mat  And the son of Solomon was Rehoboam and the son of Rehoboam was Abijah and the son of Abijah was Asa
Mat  And the son of Asa was Jehoshaphat and the son of Jehoshaphat was Joram and the son of Joram was Uzziah
Mat  And the son of Uzziah was Jotham and the son of Jotham was Ahaz and the son of Ahaz was Hezekiah
Mat  And the son of Hezekiah was Manasseh and the son of Manasseh was Amon and the son of Amon was Josiah
Mat  And the sons of Josiah were Jechoniah and his brothers at the time of the taking away to Babylon
Mat  And after the taking away to Babylon Jechoniah had a son Shealtiel and Shealtiel had Zerubbabel
Mat  And Zerubbabel had Abiud and Abiud had Eliakim and Eliakim had Azor
Mat  And Azor had Zadok and Zadok had Achim and Achim had Eliud
Mat  And Eliud had Eleazar and Eleazar had Matthan and Matthan had Jacob
Mat  And the son of Jacob was Joseph the husband of Mary who gave birth to Jesus whose name is Christ
Mat  So all the generations from Abraham to David are fourteen generations and from David to the taking away to Babylon fourteen generations and from the taking away to Babylon to the coming of Christ fourteen generations
Mat  Now the birth of Jesus Christ was in this way when his mother Mary was going to be married to Joseph before they came together the discovery was made that she was with child by the Holy Spirit
Mat  And Joseph her husband being an upright man and not desiring to make her a public example had a mind to put her away privately
Mat  But when he was giving thought to these things an angel of the Lord came to him in a dream saying Joseph son of David have no fear of taking Mary as your wife because that which is in her body is of the Holy Spirit
Mat  And she will give birth to a son and you will give him the name Jesus for he will give his people salvation from their sins
Mat  Now all this took place so that the word of the Lord by the prophet might come true
Mat  See the virgin will be with child and will give birth to a son and they will give him the name Immanuel that is God with us
Mat  And Joseph did as the angel of the Lord had said to him and took her as his wife
Mat  And he had no connection with her till she had given birth to a son and he gave him the name Jesus
Mat  Now when the birth of Jesus took place in Bethlehem of Judaea in the days of Herod the king there came wise men from the east to Jerusalem
Mat  Saying Where is the King of the Jews whose birth has now taken place We have seen his star in the east and have come to give him worship
Mat  And when it came to the ears of Herod the king he was troubled and all Jerusalem with him
Mat  And he got together all the chief priests and scribes of the people questioning them as to where the birthplace of the Christ would be
Mat  And they said to him In Bethlehem of Judaea for so it is said in the writings of the prophet
Mat  You Bethlehem in the land of Judah are not the least among the chiefs of Judah out of you will come a ruler who will be the keeper of my people Israel
Mat  Then Herod sent for the wise men privately and put questions to them about what time the star had been seen
Mat  And he sent them to Bethlehem and said Go and make certain where the young child is and when you have seen him let me have news of it so that I may come and give him worship
Mat  And after hearing the king they went on their way and the star which they saw in the east went before them till it came to rest over the place where the young child was
Mat  And when they saw the star they were full of joy
Mat  And they came into the house and saw the young child with Mary his mother and falling down on their faces they gave him worship and from their store they gave him offerings of gold perfume and spices
Mat  And it was made clear to them by God in a dream that they were not to go back to Herod so they went into their country by another way
Mat  And when they had gone an angel of the Lord came to Joseph in a dream saying Get up and take the young child and his mother and go into Egypt and do not go from there till I give you word for Herod will be searching for the young child to put him to death
Mat  So he took the young child and his mother by night and went into Egypt
Mat  And was there till the death of Herod so that the word of the Lord through the prophet might come true Out of Egypt have I sent for my son
Mat  Then Herod when he saw that he had been tricked by the wise men was very angry and he sent out and put to death all the male children in Bethlehem and in all the parts round about it from two years old and under acting on the knowledge which he had got with care from the wise men
Mat  Then the word of Jeremiah the prophet came true
Mat  In Ramah there was a sound of weeping and great sorrow Rachel weeping for her children and she would not be comforted for their loss
Mat  But when Herod was dead an angel of the Lord came in a dream to Joseph in Egypt
Mat  Saying Get up and take the young child and his mother and go into the land of Israel because they who were attempting to take the young childs life are dead
Mat  And he got up and took the young child and his mother and came into the land of Israel
Mat  But when it came to his ears that Archelaus was ruling over Judaea in the place of his father Herod he was in fear of going there and God having given him news of the danger in a dream he went out of the way into the country parts of Galilee
Mat  And he came and was living in a town named Nazareth so that the word of the prophets might come true He will be named a Nazarene
Mat  And in those days John the Baptist came preaching in the waste land of Judaea
Mat  Saying Let your hearts be turned from sin for the kingdom of heaven is near
Mat  For this is he of whom Isaiah the prophet said The voice of one crying in the waste land Make ready the way of the Lord make his roads straight
Mat  Now John was clothed in camels hair with a leather band about him and his food was locusts and honey
Mat  Then Jerusalem and all Judaea went out to him and all the people from near Jordan
Mat  And they were given baptism by him in the river Jordan saying openly that they had done wrong
Mat  But when he saw a number of the Pharisees and Sadducees coming to his baptism he said to them Offspring of snakes at whose word are you going in flight from the wrath to come
Mat  Let your change of heart be seen in your works
Mat  And say not to yourselves We have Abraham for our father because I say to you that God is able from these stones to make children for Abraham
Mat  And even now the axe is put to the root of the trees every tree then which does not give good fruit is cut down and put into the fire
Mat  Truly I give baptism with water to those of you whose hearts are changed but he who comes after me is greater than I whose shoes I am not good enough to take up he will give you baptism with the Holy Spirit and with fire
Mat  In whose hand is the instrument with which he will make clean his grain he will put the good grain in his store but the waste will be burned up in the fire which will never be put out
Mat  Then Jesus came from Galilee to John at the Jordan to be given baptism by him
Mat  But John would have kept him back saying It is I who have need of baptism from you and do you come to me
Mat  But Jesus made answer saying to him Let it be so now because so it is right for us to make righteousness complete Then he gave him baptism
Mat  And Jesus having been given baptism straight away went up from the water and the heavens opening he saw the Spirit of God coming down on him as a dove
Mat  And a voice came out of heaven saying This is my dearly loved Son with whom I am well pleased
Mat  Then Jesus was sent by the Spirit into the waste land to be tested by the Evil One
Mat  And after going without food for forty days and forty nights he was in need of it
Mat  And the Evil One came and said to him If you are the Son of God give the word for these stones to become bread
Mat  But he made answer and said It is in the Writings Bread is not mans only need but every word which comes out of the mouth of God
Mat  Then the Evil One took him to the holy town and he put him on the highest point of the Temple and said to him
Mat  If you are the Son of God let yourself go down for it is in the Writings He will give his angels care over you and In their hands they will keep you up so that your foot may not be crushed against a stone
Mat  Jesus said to him Again it is in the Writings You may not put the Lord your God to the test
Mat  Again the Evil One took him up to a very high mountain and let him see all the kingdoms of the world and the glory of them
Mat  And he said to him All these things will I give you if you will go down on your face and give me worship
Mat  Then said Jesus to him Away Satan for it is in the Writings Give worship to the Lord your God and be his servant only
Mat  Then the Evil One went away from him and angels came and took care of him
Mat  Now when it came to his ears that John had been put in prison he went away to Galilee
Mat  And going away from Nazareth he came and made his livingplace in Capernaum which is by the sea in the country of Zebulun and Naphtali
Mat  So that the word of the prophet Isaiah might come true
Mat  The land of Zebulun and the land of Naphtali by the way of the sea the other side of Jordan Galilee of the Gentiles
Mat  The people who were in the dark saw a great light and to those in the land of the shade of death did the dawn come up
Mat  From that time Jesus went about preaching and saying Let your hearts be turned from sin for the kingdom of heaven is near
Mat  And when he was walking by the sea of Galilee he saw two brothers Simon whose other name was Peter and Andrew his brother who were putting a net into the sea for they were fishermen
Mat  And he said to them Come after me and I will make you fishers of men
Mat  And straight away they let go the nets and went after him
Mat  And going on from there he saw two other brothers James the son of Zebedee and John his brother in the boat with their father stitching up their nets and he said Come
Mat  And they went straight from the boat and their father and came after him
Mat  And Jesus went about in all Galilee teaching in their Synagogues and preaching the good news of the kingdom and making well those who were ill with any disease among the people
Mat  And news of him went out through all Syria and they took to him all who were ill with different diseases and pains those having evil spirits and those who were off their heads and those who had no power of moving And he made them well
Mat  And there went after him great numbers from Galilee and Decapolis and Jerusalem and Judaea and from the other side of Jordan
Mat  And seeing great masses of people he went up into the mountain and when he was seated his disciples came to him
Mat  And with these words he gave them teaching saying
Mat  Happy are the poor in spirit for the kingdom of heaven is theirs
Mat  Happy are those who are sad for they will be comforted
Mat  Happy are the gentle for the earth will be their heritage
Mat  Happy are those whose hearts desire is for righteousness for they will have their desire
Mat  Happy are those who have mercy for they will be given mercy
Mat  Happy are the clean in heart for they will see God
Mat  Happy are the peacemakers for they will be named sons of God
Mat  Happy are those who are attacked on account of righteousness for the kingdom of heaven will be theirs
Mat  Happy are you when men give you a bad name and are cruel to you and say all evil things against you falsely because of me
Mat  Be glad and full of joy for great is your reward in heaven for so were the prophets attacked who were before you
Mat  You are the salt of the earth but if its taste goes from the salt how will you make it salt again it is then good for nothing but to be put out and crushed under foot by men
Mat  You are the light of the world A town put on a hill may be seen by all
Mat  And a burning light is not put under a vessel but on its table so that its rays may be shining on all who are in the house
Mat  Even so let your light be shining before men so that they may see your good works and give glory to your Father in heaven
Mat  Let there be no thought that I have come to put an end to the law or the prophets I have not come for destruction but to make complete
Mat  Truly I say to you Till heaven and earth come to an end not the smallest letter or part of a letter will in any way be taken from the law till all things are done
Mat  Whoever then goes against the smallest of these laws teaching men to do the same will be named least in the kingdom of heaven but he who keeps the laws teaching others to keep them will be named great in the kingdom of heaven
Mat  For I say to you If your righteousness is not greater than the righteousness of the scribes and Pharisees you will never go into the kingdom of heaven
Mat  You have knowledge that it was said in old times You may not put to death and Whoever puts to death will be in danger of being judged
Mat  But I say to you that everyone who is angry with his brother will be in danger of being judged and he who says to his brother Raca will be in danger from the Sanhedrin and whoever says You foolish one will be in danger of the hell of fire
Mat  If then you are making an offering at the altar and there it comes to your mind that your brother has something against you
Mat  While your offering is still before the altar first go and make peace with your brother then come and make your offering
Mat  Come to an agreement quickly with him who has a cause against you at law while you are with him on the way for fear that he may give you up to the judge and the judge may give you to the police and you may be put into prison
Mat  Truly I say to you You will not come out from there till you have made payment of the very last farthing
Mat  You have knowledge that it was said You may not have connection with another mans wife
Mat  But I say to you that everyone whose eyes are turned on a woman with desire has had connection with her in his heart
Mat  And if your right eye is a cause of trouble to you take it out and put it away from you because it is better to undergo the loss of one part than for all your body to go into hell
Mat  And if your right hand is a cause of trouble to you let it be cut off and put it away from you because it is better to undergo the loss of one part than for all your body to go into hell
Mat  Again it was said Whoever puts away his wife has to give her a statement in writing for this purpose
Mat  But I say to you that everyone who puts away his wife for any other cause but the loss of her virtue makes her false to her husband and whoever takes her as his wife after she is put away is no true husband to her
Mat  Again you have knowledge that it was said in old times Do not take false oaths but give effect to your oaths to the Lord
Mat  But I say to you Take no oaths at all not by the heaven because it is the seat of God
Mat  Or by the earth because it is the restingplace for his foot or by Jerusalem because it is the town of the great King
Mat  You may not take an oath by your head because you are not able to make one hair white or black
Mat  But let your words be simply Yes or No and whatever is more than these is of the Evil One
Mat  You have knowledge that it was said An eye for an eye and a tooth for a tooth
Mat  But I say to you Do not make use of force against an evil man but to him who gives you a blow on the right side of your face let the left be turned
Mat  And if any man goes to law with you and takes away your coat do not keep back your robe from him
Mat  And whoever makes you go one mile go with him two
Mat  Give to him who comes with a request and keep not your property from him who would for a time make use of it
Mat  You have knowledge that it was said Have love for your neighbour and hate for him who is against you
Mat  But I say to you Have love for those who are against you and make prayer for those who are cruel to you
Mat  So that you may be the sons of your Father in heaven for his sun gives light to the evil and to the good and he sends rain on the upright man and on the sinner
Mat  For if you have love for those who have love for you what credit is it to you do not the taxfarmers the same
Mat  And if you say Good day to your brothers only what do you do more than others do not even the Gentiles the same
Mat  Be then complete in righteousness even as your Father in heaven is complete
Mat  Take care not to do your good works before men to be seen by them or you will have no reward from your Father in heaven
Mat  When then you give money to the poor do not make a noise about it as the falsehearted men do in the Synagogues and in the streets so that they may have glory from men Truly I say to you They have their reward
Mat  But when you give money let not your left hand see what your right hand does
Mat  So that your giving may be in secret and your Father who sees in secret will give you your reward
Mat  And when you make your prayers be not like the falsehearted men who take pleasure in getting up and saying their prayers in the Synagogues and at the street turnings so that they may be seen by men Truly I say to you They have their reward
Mat  But when you make your prayer go into your private room and shutting the door say a prayer to your Father in secret and your Father who sees in secret will give you your reward
Mat  And in your prayer do not make use of the same words again and again as the Gentiles do for they have the idea that God will give attention to them because of the number of their words
Mat  So be not like them because your Father has knowledge of your needs even before you make your requests to him
Mat  Let this then be your prayer Our Father in heaven may your name be kept holy
Mat  Let your kingdom come Let your pleasure be done as in heaven so on earth
Mat  Give us this day bread for our needs
Mat  And make us free of our debts as we have made those free who are in debt to us
Mat  And let us not be put to the test but keep us safe from the Evil One
Mat  For if you let men have forgiveness for their sins you will have forgiveness from your Father in heaven
Mat  But if you do not let men have forgiveness for their sins you will not have forgiveness from your Father for your sins
Mat  And when you go without food be not sadfaced as the falsehearted are For they go about with changed looks so that men may see that they are going without food Truly I say to you They have their reward
Mat  But when you go without food put oil on your head and make your face clean
Mat  So that no one may see that you are going without food but your Father in secret and your Father who sees in secret will give you your reward
Mat  Make no store of wealth for yourselves on earth where it may be turned to dust by worms and weather and where thieves may come in by force and take it away
Mat  But make a store for yourselves in heaven where it will not be turned to dust and where thieves do not come in to take it away
Mat  For where your wealth is there will your heart be
Mat  The light of the body is the eye if then your eye is true all your body will be full of light
Mat  But if your eye is evil all your body will be dark If then the light which is in you is dark how dark it will be
Mat  No man is able to be a servant to two masters for he will have hate for the one and love for the other or he will keep to one and have no respect for the other You may not be servants of God and of wealth
Mat  So I say to you Take no thought for your life about food or drink or about clothing for your body Is not life more than food and the body more than its clothing
Mat  See the birds of heaven they do not put seeds in the earth they do not get in grain or put it in storehouses and your Father in heaven gives them food Are you not of much more value than they
Mat  And which of you by taking thought is able to make himself a cubit taller
Mat  And why are you troubled about clothing See the flowers of the field how they come up they do no work they make no thread
Mat  But I say to you that even Solomon in all his glory was not clothed like one of these
Mat  But if God gives such clothing to the grass of the field which is here today and tomorrow is put into the oven will he not much more give you clothing O you of little faith
Mat  Then do not be full of care saying What are we to have for food or drink or With what may we be clothed
Mat  Because the Gentiles go in search of all these things for your Father in heaven has knowledge that you have need of all these things
Mat  But let your first care be for his kingdom and his righteousness and all these other things will be given to you in addition
Mat  Then have no care for tomorrow tomorrow will take care of itself Take the trouble of the day as it comes
Mat  Be not judges of others and you will not be judged
Mat  For as you have been judging so you will be judged and with your measure will it be measured to you
Mat  And why do you take note of the grain of dust in your brothers eye but take no note of the bit of wood which is in your eye
Mat  Or how will you say to your brother Let me take out the grain of dust from your eye when you yourself have a bit of wood in your eye
Mat  You false one first take out the bit of wood from your eye then will you see clearly to take out the grain of dust from your brothers eye
Mat  Do not give that which is holy to the dogs or put your jewels before pigs for fear that they will be crushed under foot by the pigs whose attack will then be made against you
Mat  Make a request and it will be answered what you are searching for you will get give the sign and the door will be open to you
Mat  Because to everyone who makes a request it will be given and he who is searching will get his desire and to him who gives the sign the door will be open
Mat  Or which of you if his son makes a request for bread will give him a stone
Mat  Or if he makes a request for a fish will give him a snake
Mat  If you then being evil are able to give good things to your children how much more will your Father in heaven give good things to those who make requests to him
Mat  All those things then which you would have men do to you even so do you to them because this is the law and the prophets
Mat  Go in by the narrow door for wide is the door and open is the way which goes to destruction and great numbers go in by it
Mat  For narrow is the door and hard the road to life and only a small number make discovery of it
Mat  Be on the watch for false prophets who come to you in sheeps clothing but inside they are cruel wolves
Mat  By their fruits you will get knowledge of them Do men get grapes from thorns or figs from thistles
Mat  Even so every good tree gives good fruit but the bad tree gives evil fruit
Mat  It is not possible for a good tree to give bad fruit and a bad tree will not give good fruit
Mat  Every tree which does not give good fruit is cut down and put in the fire
Mat  So by their fruits you will get knowledge of them
Mat  Not everyone who says to me Lord Lord will go into the kingdom of heaven but he who does the pleasure of my Father in heaven
Mat  A great number will say to me on that day Lord Lord were we not prophets in your name and did we not by your name send out evil spirits and by your name do works of power
Mat  And then will I say to them I never had knowledge of you go from me you workers of evil
Mat  Everyone then to whom my words come and who does them will be like a wise man who made his house on a rock
Mat  And the rain came down and there was a rush of waters and the winds were driving against that house but it was not moved because it was based on the rock
Mat  And everyone to whom my words come and who does them not will be like a foolish man who made his house on sand
Mat  And the rain came down and there was a rush of waters and the winds were driving against that house and it came down and great was its fall
Mat  And it came about when Jesus had come to the end of these words that the people were surprised at his teaching
Mat  for he was teaching as one having authority and not as their scribes
Mat  And when he had come down from the mountain great numbers of people came after him
Mat  And a leper came and gave him worship saying Lord if it is your pleasure you have power to make me clean
Mat  And he put his hand on him saying It is my pleasure be clean And straight away he was made clean
Mat  And Jesus said to him See that you say nothing about this to anyone but go and let the priest see you and make the offering which was ordered by Moses for a witness to them
Mat  And when Jesus was come into Capernaum a certain captain came to him with a request
Mat  Saying Lord my servant is ill in bed at the house with no power in his body and in great pain
Mat  And he said to him I will come and make him well
Mat  And the captain in answer said Lord I am not good enough for you to come under my roof but only say the word and my servant will be made well
Mat  Because I myself am a man under authority having under me fighting men and I say to this one Go and he goes and to another Come and he comes and to my servant Do this and he does it
Mat  And when these words came to the ears of Jesus he was surprised and said to those who came after him Truly I say to you I have not seen such great faith no not in Israel
Mat  And I say to you that numbers will come from the east and the west and will take their seats with Abraham and Isaac and Jacob in the kingdom of heaven
Mat  But the sons of the kingdom will be put out into the dark and there will be weeping and cries of pain
Mat  And Jesus said to the captain Go in peace as your faith is so let it be done to you And the servant was made well in that hour
Mat  And when Jesus had come into Peters house he saw his wifes mother in bed very ill
Mat  And he put his hand on hers and the disease went from her and she got up and took care of his needs
Mat  And in the evening they took to him a number of people who had evil spirits and he sent the spirits out of them with a word and made well all who were ill
Mat  So that the word of Isaiah the prophet might come true He himself took our pains and our diseases
Mat  Now when Jesus saw a great mass of people about him he gave an order to go to the other side
Mat  And there came a scribe and said to him Master I will come after you wherever you go
Mat  And Jesus said to him The foxes have holes and the birds of heaven have a restingplace but the Son of man has nowhere to put his head
Mat  And another of the disciples said to him Lord let me first go and give the last honours to my father
Mat  But Jesus said to him Come after me and let the dead take care of their dead
Mat  And when he had got into a boat his disciples went after him
Mat  And there came up a great storm in the sea so that the boat was covered with the waves but he was sleeping
Mat  And they came to him and awaking him said Help Lord destruction is near
Mat  And he said to them Why are you full of fear O you of little faith Then he got up and gave orders to the winds and the sea and there was a great calm
Mat  And the men were full of wonder saying What sort of man is this that even the winds and the sea do his orders
Mat  And when he had come to the other side to the country of the Gadarenes there came out to him from the place of the dead two who had evil spirits so violent that no man was able to go that way
Mat  And they gave a loud cry saying What have we to do with you you Son of God Have you come here to give us punishment before the time
Mat  Now there was some distance away a great herd of pigs taking their food
Mat  And the evil spirits made strong prayers to him saying If you send us out let us go into the herd of pigs
Mat  And he said to them Go And they came out and went into the pigs and the herd went rushing down a sharp slope into the sea and came to their end in the water
Mat  And their keepers went in flight to the town and gave an account of everything and of the men who had the evil spirits
Mat  And all the town came out to Jesus and seeing him they made request that he would go away from their part of the country
Mat  And he got into a boat and went across and came to his town
Mat  And they took to him a man stretched on a bed who had no power of moving and Jesus seeing their faith said to the man who was ill Son take heart you have forgiveness for your sins
Mat  And some of the scribes said among themselves This man has no respect for God
Mat  And Jesus having knowledge of what was in their minds said Why are your thoughts evil
Mat  For which is the simpler to say You have forgiveness for your sins or to say Get up and go
Mat  But so that you may see that on earth the Son of man has authority for the forgiveness of sins then said he to the man who was ill Get up and take up your bed and go to your house
Mat  And he got up and went away to his house
Mat  But when the people saw it they were full of fear and gave glory to God who had given such authority to men
Mat  And when Jesus was going from there he saw a man whose name was Matthew seated at the place where taxes were taken and he said to him Come after me And he got up and went after him
Mat  And it came about when he was in the house taking food that a number of taxfarmers and sinners came and took their places with Jesus and his disciples
Mat  And when the Pharisees saw it they said to his disciples Why does your Master take food with taxfarmers and sinners
Mat  But on hearing this he said Those who are well have no need of a medical man but those who are ill
Mat  But go and take to heart the sense of these words My desire is for mercy not offerings for I have come not to get the upright but sinners
Mat  Then the disciples of John came to him saying Why do we and the Pharisees frequently go without food but your disciples do not
Mat  And Jesus said to them Will the friends of the newlymarried man be sad as long as he is with them But the days will come when he will be taken away from them and then will they go without food
Mat  And no man puts a bit of new cloth on an old coat for by pulling away from the old it makes a worse hole
Mat  And men do not put new wine into old wineskins or the skins will be burst and the wine will come out and the skins are of no more use but they put new wine into new wineskins and so the two will be safe
Mat  While he was saying these things to them there came a ruler and gave him worship saying My daughter is even now dead but come and put your hand on her and she will come back to life
Mat  And Jesus got up and went after him and so did his disciples
Mat  And a woman who for twelve years had had a flow of blood came after him and put her hand on the edge of his robe
Mat  Because she said to herself if I may but put my hand on his robe I will be made well
Mat  But Jesus turning and seeing her said Daughter take heart your faith has made you well And the woman was made well from that hour
Mat  And when Jesus came into the rulers house and saw the players with their instruments and the people making a noise
Mat  He said Make room for the girl is not dead but sleeping And they were laughing at him
Mat  But when the people were sent out he went in and took her by the hand and the girl got up
Mat  And the news of it went out into all that land
Mat  And when Jesus went on from there two blind men came after him crying out Have mercy on us you Son of David
Mat  And when he had come into the house the blind men came to him and Jesus said to them Have you faith that I am able to do this They said to him Yes Lord
Mat  Then he put his hand on their eyes saying As your faith is let it be done to you
Mat  And their eyes were made open And Jesus said to them sharply Let no man have knowledge of it
Mat  But they went out and gave news of him in all that land
Mat  And while they were going away there came to him a man without the power of talking and with an evil spirit
Mat  And when the evil spirit had been sent out the man had the power of talking and they were all surprised saying Such a thing has never been seen in Israel
Mat  But the Pharisees said By the ruler of evil spirits he sends evil spirits out of men
Mat  And Jesus went about all the towns and small places teaching in their Synagogues and preaching the good news of the kingdom and making well all sorts of disease and pain
Mat  But when he saw all the people he was moved with pity for them because they were troubled and wandering like sheep without a keeper
Mat  Then he said to his disciples There is much grain but not enough men to get it in
Mat  Make prayer then to the Lord of the grainfields that he may send out workers to get in his grain
Mat  And he got together his twelve disciples and gave them the power of driving out unclean spirits and of making well all sorts of disease and pain
Mat  Now the names of the twelve are these The first Simon who is named Peter and Andrew his brother James the son of Zebedee and John his brother
Mat  Philip and Bartholomew Thomas and Matthew the taxfarmer James the son of Alphaeus and Thaddaeus
Mat  Simon the Zealot and Judas Iscariot who was false to him
Mat  These twelve Jesus sent out and gave them orders saying Do not go among the Gentiles or into any town of Samaria
Mat  But go to the wandering sheep of the house of Israel
Mat  And on your way say The kingdom of heaven is near
Mat  Make well those who are ill give life to the dead make lepers clean send evil spirits out of men freely it has been given to you freely give
Mat  Take no gold or silver or copper in your pockets
Mat  Take no bag for your journey and do not take two coats or shoes or a stick for the workman has a right to his food
Mat  And into whatever town or small place you go make search there for someone who is respected and make his house your restingplace till you go away
Mat  And when you go in say May peace be on this house
Mat  And if the house is good enough let your peace come on it but if not let your peace come back to you
Mat  And whoever will not take you in or give ear to your words when you go out from that house or that town put off its dust from your feet
Mat  Truly I say to you It will be better for the land of Sodom and Gomorrah in the day of Gods judging than for that town
Mat  See I send you out as sheep among wolves Be then as wise as snakes and as gentle as doves
Mat  But be on the watch against men for they will give you up to the Sanhedrins and in their Synagogues they will give you blows
Mat  And you will come before rulers and kings because of me for a witness to them and to the Gentiles
Mat  But when you are given up into their hands do not be troubled about what to say or how to say it for in that hour what you are to say will be given to you
Mat  Because it is not you who say the words but the Spirit of your Father in you
Mat  And brother will give up brother to death and the father his child and children will go against their fathers and mothers and put them to death
Mat  And you will be hated by all men because of my name but he who is strong to the end will have salvation
Mat  But when they are cruel to you in one town go in flight to another for truly I say to you You will not have gone through the towns of Israel before the Son of man comes
Mat  A disciple is not greater than his master or a servant than his lord
Mat  It is enough for the disciple that he may be as his master and the servant as his lord If they have given the name Beelzebub to the master of the house how much more to those of his house
Mat  Have then no fear of them because nothing is covered which will not come to light or secret which will not be made clear
Mat  What I say to you in the dark say in the light and what comes to your ear secretly say publicly from the housetops
Mat  And have no fear of those who put to death the body but are not able to put to death the soul But have fear of him who has power to give soul and body to destruction in hell
Mat  Are not sparrows two a farthing and not one of them comes to an end without your Father
Mat  But the hairs of your head are all numbered
Mat  Then have no fear you are of more value than a flock of sparrows
Mat  To everyone then who gives witness to me before men I will give witness before my Father in heaven
Mat  But if anyone says before men that he has no knowledge of me I will say that I have no knowledge of him before my Father in heaven
Mat  Do not have the thought that I have come to send peace on the earth I came not to send peace but a sword
Mat  For I have come to put a man against his father and the daughter against her mother and the daughterinlaw against her motherinlaw
Mat  And a man will be hated by those of his house
Mat  He who has more love for his father or mother than for me is not good enough for me he who has more love for son or daughter than for me is not good enough for me
Mat  And he who does not take his cross and come after me is not good enough for me
Mat  He who has the desire to keep his life will have it taken from him and he who gives up his life because of me will have it given back to him
Mat  He who gives honour to you gives honour to me and he who gives honour to me gives honour to him who sent me
Mat  He who gives honour to a prophet in the name of a prophet will be given a prophets reward and he who gives honour to an upright man in the name of an upright man will be given an upright mans reward
Mat  And whoever gives to one of these little ones a cup of cold water only in the name of a disciple truly I say to you he will not go without his reward
Mat  And it came about that when Jesus had come to the end of giving these orders to his twelve disciples he went away from there teaching and preaching in their towns
Mat  Now when John had news in prison of the works of the Christ he sent his disciples
Mat  To say to him Are you he who is to come or are we waiting for another
Mat  And Jesus answering said to them Go and give news to John of the things which you are seeing and hearing
Mat  The blind see those who were not able to are walking lepers are made clean those who were without hearing now have their ears open the dead come to life again and the poor have the good news given to them
Mat  And a blessing will be on him who has no doubts about me
Mat  And when they were going away Jesus talking of John said to all the people What went you out into the waste land to see a tall stem moving in the wind
Mat  But what went you out to see a man delicately clothed Those who have fair robes are in kings houses
Mat  But why did you go out to see a prophet Yes I say to you and more than a prophet
Mat  This is he of whom it has been said See I send my servant before your face who will make ready your way before you
Mat  Truly I say to you Among the sons of women there has not been a greater than John the Baptist but he who is least in the kingdom of heaven is greater than he
Mat  And from the days of John the Baptist till now the kingdom of heaven is forcing its way in and men of force take it
Mat  For all the prophets and the law were in force till John
Mat  And if you are able to see it this is Elijah who was to come
Mat  He who has ears let him give ear
Mat  But what comparison may I make of this generation It is like children seated in the marketplaces crying out to one another
Mat  We made music for you and you did not take part in the dance we gave cries of sorrow and you made no signs of grief
Mat  For John came taking no food or drink and they say He has an evil spirit
Mat  The Son of man has come feasting and they say See a lover of food and wine a friend of taxfarmers and sinners And wisdom is judged to be right by her works
Mat  Then he went on to say hard things to the towns where most of his works of power were done because they had not been turned from their sins
Mat  Unhappy are you Chorazin Unhappy are you Bethsaida For if the works of power which were done in you had been done in Tyre and Sidon they would have been turned from their sins in days gone by clothing themselves in haircloth and putting dust on their heads
Mat  But I say to you It will be better for Tyre and Sidon in the day of judging than for you
Mat  And you Capernaum were you not to be lifted up to heaven you will go down into hell for if the works of power which were done in you had been done in Sodom it would have been here to this day
Mat  But I say to you that it will be better for the land of Sodom in the day of judging than for you
Mat  At that time Jesus made answer and said I give praise to you O Father Lord of heaven and earth because you have kept these things secret from the wise and the men of learning and have made them clear to little children
Mat  Yes Father for so it was pleasing in your eyes
Mat  All things have been given to me by my Father and no one has knowledge of the Son but the Father and no one has knowledge of the Father but the Son and he to whom the Son will make it clear
Mat  Come to me all you who are troubled and weighted down with care and I will give you rest
Mat  Take my yoke on you and become like me for I am gentle and without pride and you will have rest for your souls
Mat  For my yoke is good and the weight I take up is not hard
Mat  At that time Jesus went through the fields on the Sabbath day and his disciples being in need of food were taking the heads of grain
Mat  But the Pharisees when they saw it said to him See your disciples do that which it is not right to do on the Sabbath
Mat  But he said to them Have you no knowledge of what David did when he had need of food and those who were with him
Mat  How he went into the house of God and took for food the holy bread which it was not right for him or for those who were with him to take but only for the priests
Mat  Or is it not said in the law how the Sabbath is broken by the priests in the Temple and they do no wrong
Mat  But I say to you that a greater thing than the Temple is here
Mat  But if these words had been in your minds My desire is for mercy and not for offerings you would not have been judging those who have done no wrong
Mat  For the Son of man is lord of the Sabbath
Mat  And he went from there into their Synagogue
Mat  And there was a man with a dead hand And they put a question to him saying Is it right to make a man well on the Sabbath day so that they might have something against him
Mat  And he said to them Which of you having a sheep if it gets into a hole on the Sabbath day will not put out a helping hand and get it back
Mat  Of how much more value is a man than a sheep For this reason it is right to do good on the Sabbath day
Mat  Then said he to the man Put out your hand And he put it out and it was made as well as the other
Mat  But the Pharisees went out and made designs against him how they might put him to death
Mat  And Jesus having knowledge of this went away from there and a great number went after him and he made them all well
Mat  Ordering them not to give people word of him
Mat  So that what was said by Isaiah the prophet might come true
Mat  See my servant the man of my selection my loved one in whom my soul is well pleased I will put my Spirit on him and he will make my decision clear to the Gentiles
Mat  His coming will not be with fighting or loud cries and his voice will not be lifted up in the streets
Mat  The crushed stem will not be broken by him and the feebly burning light will he not put out till he has made righteousness overcome all
Mat  And in his name will the Gentiles put their hope
Mat  Then they took to him one with an evil spirit who was blind and had no power of talking and he made him well so that he had the power of talking and seeing
Mat  And all the people were surprised and said Is not this the Son of David
Mat  But the Pharisees hearing of it said This man only sends evil spirits out of men by Beelzebub the ruler of evil spirits
Mat  And having knowledge of their thoughts he said to them Every kingdom having division in itself is made waste and every town or house having division in itself will come to destruction
Mat  And if Satan sends out Satan he makes war against himself how then will he keep his kingdom
Mat  And if I by Beelzebub send evil spirits out of men by whom do your sons send them out So let them be your judges
Mat  But if I by the Spirit of God send out evil spirits then is the kingdom of God come on you
Mat  Or how may one go into a strong mans house and take his goods if he does not first put cords round the strong man and then he may take his goods
Mat  Whoever is not with me is against me and he who does not take part with me in getting people together is driving them away
Mat  So I say to you Every sin and every evil word against God will have forgiveness but for evil words against the Spirit there will be no forgiveness
Mat  And whoever says a word against the Son of man will have forgiveness but whoever says a word against the Holy Spirit will not have forgiveness in this life or in that which is to come
Mat  Make the tree good and its fruit good or make the tree bad and its fruit bad for by its fruit you will get knowledge of the tree
Mat  You offspring of snakes how are you being evil able to say good things because out of the hearts store come the words of the mouth
Mat  The good man out of his good store gives good things and the evil man out of his evil store gives evil things
Mat  And I say to you that in the day when they are judged men will have to give an account of every foolish word they have said
Mat  For by your words will your righteousness be seen and by your words you will be judged
Mat  Then some of the scribes and Pharisees hearing this said to him Master we are looking for a sign from you
Mat  But he answering said to them An evil and false generation is looking for a sign and no sign will be given to it but the sign of the prophet Jonah
Mat  For as Jonah was three days and three nights in the stomach of the great fish so will the Son of man be three days and three nights in the heart of the earth
Mat  The men of Nineveh will come up in the day of judging and give their decision against this generation because they were turned from their sins at the preaching of Jonah and now a greater than Jonah is here
Mat  The queen of the South will come up in the day of judging and give her decision against this generation for she came from the ends of the earth to give ear to the wisdom of Solomon and now a greater than Solomon is here
Mat  But the unclean spirit when he is gone out of a man goes through dry places looking for rest and getting it not
Mat  Then he says I will go back into my house from which I came out and when he comes he sees that there is no one in it but that it has been made fair and clean
Mat  Then he goes and takes with him seven other spirits worse than himself and they go in and make it their livingplace and the last condition of that man is worse than the first Even so will it be with this evil generation
Mat  While he was still talking to the people his mother and his brothers came desiring to have talk with him
Mat  And one said to him See your mother and your brothers are outside desiring to have talk with you
Mat  But he in answer said to him who gave the news Who is my mother and who are my brothers
Mat  And he put out his hand to his disciples and said See my mother and my brothers
Mat  For whoever does the pleasure of my Father in heaven he is my brother and sister and mother
Mat  On that day Jesus went out of the house and was seated by the seaside
Mat  And great numbers of people came together to him so that he got into a boat and the people took up their position by the sea
Mat  And he gave them teaching in the form of a story saying A man went out to put seed in the earth
Mat  And while he did so some seeds were dropped by the wayside and the birds came and took them for food
Mat  And some of the seed went among the stones where it had not much earth and straight away it came up because the earth was not deep
Mat  And when the sun was high it was burned and because it had no root it became dry and dead
Mat  And some seeds went among thorns and the thorns came up and they had no room for growth
Mat  And some falling on good earth gave fruit some a hundred some sixty some thirty times as much
Mat  He who has ears let him give ear
Mat  And the disciples came and said to him Why do you say things to them in the form of stories
Mat  And he said to them in answer To you is given the knowledge of the secrets of the kingdom of heaven but to them it is not given
Mat  Because whoever has to him will be given and he will have more but from him who has not even what he has will be taken away
Mat  For this reason I put things into the form of stories because they see without seeing and give ear without hearing and the sense is not clear to them
Mat  And for them the words of Isaiah have come true Though you give ear you will not get knowledge and seeing you will see but the sense will not be clear to you
Mat  For the heart of this people has become fat and their ears are slow in hearing and their eyes are shut for fear that they might see with their eyes and give hearing with their ears and become wise in their hearts and be turned again to me so that I might make them well
Mat  But a blessing be on your eyes because they see and on your ears because they are open
Mat  For truly I say to you that prophets and upright men had a desire to see the things which you see and saw them not and to have knowledge of the words which have come to your ears and they had it not
Mat  Give ear then to the story of the man who put the seed in the earth
Mat  When the word of the kingdom comes to anyone and the sense of it is not clear to him then the Evil One comes and quickly takes away that which was put in his heart He is the seed dropped by the wayside
Mat  And that which went on the stones this is he who hearing the word straight away takes it with joy
Mat  But having no root in himself he goes on for a time and when trouble comes or pain because of the word he quickly becomes full of doubts
Mat  And that which was dropped among the thorns this is he who has the word and the cares of this life and the deceits of wealth put a stop to the growth of the word and it gives no fruit
Mat  And the seed which was put in good earth this is he who gives ear to the word and gets the sense of it who gives fruit some a hundred some sixty some thirty times as much
Mat  And he gave them another story saying The kingdom of heaven is like a man who put good seed in his field
Mat  But while men were sleeping one who had hate for him came and put evil seeds among the grain and went away
Mat  But when the green stem came up and gave fruit the evil plants were seen at the same time
Mat  And the servants of the master of the house came and said to him Sir did you not put good seed in your field how then has it evil plants
Mat  And he said Someone has done this in hate And the servants say to him Is it your pleasure that we go and take them up
Mat  But he says No for fear that by chance while you take up the evil plants you may be rooting up the grain with them
Mat  Let them come up together till the getting in of the grain and then I will say to the workers Take up first the evil plants and put them together for burning but put the grain into my storehouse
Mat  He put another story before them saying The kingdom of heaven is like a grain of mustard seed which a man took and put in his field
Mat  Which is smaller than all seeds but when it has come up it is greater than the plants and becomes a tree so that the birds of heaven come and make their restingplaces in its branches
Mat  Another story he gave to them The kingdom of heaven is like leaven which a woman took and put in three measures of meal till it was all leavened
Mat  All these things Jesus said to the people in the form of stories and without a story he said nothing to them
Mat  That it might come true which was said by the prophet Opening my mouth I will give out stories I will give knowledge of things kept secret from before all time
Mat  Then he went away from the people and went into the house and his disciples came to him saying Make clear to us the story of the evil plants in the field
Mat  And he made answer and said He who puts the good seed in the earth is the Son of man
Mat  And the field is the world and the good seed is the sons of the kingdom and the evil seeds are the sons of the Evil One
Mat  And he who put them in the earth is Satan and the getting in of the grain is the end of the world and those who get it in are the angels
Mat  As then the evil plants are got together and burned with fire so will it be in the end of the world
Mat  The Son of man will send out his angels and they will take out of his kingdom everything which is a cause of error and all those who do wrong
Mat  And will put them into the fire there will be weeping and cries of sorrow
Mat  Then will the upright be shining as the sun in the kingdom of their Father He who has ears let him give ear
Mat  The kingdom of heaven is like a secret store of wealth in a field which a man came across and put back again and in his joy he goes and gives all he has to get that field
Mat  Again the kingdom of heaven is like a trader searching for beautiful jewels
Mat  And having come across one jewel of great price he went and gave all he had in exchange for it
Mat  Again the kingdom of heaven is like a net which was put into the sea and took in every sort of fish
Mat  When it was full they took it up on the sands and seated there they put the good into vessels but the bad they put away
Mat  So will it be in the end of the world the angels will come and take out the bad from the good
Mat  And will put them into the fire there will be weeping and cries of sorrow
Mat  Are all these things now clear to you They say to him Yes
Mat  And he said to them For this reason every scribe who has become a disciple of the kingdom of heaven is like the owner of a house who gives out from his store things new and old
Mat  And when Jesus had come to the end of these stories he went away from there
Mat  And coming into his country he gave them teaching in their Synagogue so that they were greatly surprised and said Where did this man get this wisdom and these works of power
Mat  Is not this the woodworkers son is not his mother named Mary and his brothers James and Joseph and Simon and Judas
Mat  And his sisters are they not all with us from where then has he all these things
Mat  And they were bitter against him But Jesus said to them A prophet is nowhere without honour but in his country and among his family
Mat  And the works of power which he did there were small in number because they had no faith
Mat  At that time news of Jesus came to Herod the king
Mat  And he said to his servants This is John the Baptist he has come back from the dead and so these powers are working in him
Mat  For Herod had taken John and put him in prison because of Herodias his brother Philips wife
Mat  Because John had said to him It is not right for you to have her
Mat  And he would have put him to death but for his fear of the people because in their eyes John was a prophet
Mat  But when Herods birthday came the daughter of Herodias was dancing before them and Herod was pleased with her
Mat  So he gave her his word with an oath to let her have whatever she might make request for
Mat  And she at her mothers suggestion said Give me here on a plate the head of John the Baptist
Mat  And the king was sad but because of his oaths and because of his guests he gave the order for it to be given to her
Mat  And he sent and had Johns head cut off in the prison
Mat  And his head was put on a plate and given to the girl and she took it to her mother
Mat  And his disciples came and took up his body and put it in the earth and they went and gave Jesus news of what had taken place
Mat  Now when it came to the ears of Jesus he went away from there in a boat to a waste place by himself and the people hearing of it went after him on foot from the towns
Mat  And he came out and saw a great number of people and he had pity on them and made well those of them who were ill
Mat  And when evening had come the disciples came to him saying This place is waste land and the time is now past send the people away so that they may go into the towns and get themselves food
Mat  But Jesus said to them There is no need for them to go away give them food yourselves
Mat  And they say to him We have here but five cakes of bread and two fishes
Mat  And he said Give them to me
Mat  And he gave orders for the people to be seated on the grass and he took the five cakes of bread and the two fishes and looking up to heaven he said words of blessing and made division of the food and gave it to the disciples and the disciples gave it to the people
Mat  And they all took of the food and had enough and they took up twelve baskets full of broken bits which were not used
Mat  And those who had food were about five thousand men in addition to women and children
Mat  And straight away he made the disciples get into the boat and go before him to the other side till he had sent the people away
Mat  And after he had sent the people away he went up into the mountain by himself for prayer and when evening was come he was there by himself
Mat  But the boat was now in the middle of the sea and was troubled by the waves for the wind was against them
Mat  And in the fourth watch of the night he came to them walking on the sea
Mat  And when they saw him walking on the sea they were troubled saying It is a spirit and they gave cries of fear
Mat  But straight away Jesus said to them Take heart it is I have no fear
Mat  And Peter answering said to him Lord if it is you give me the order to come to you on the water
Mat  And he said Come And Peter got out of the boat and walking on the water went to Jesus
Mat  But when he saw the wind he was in fear and starting to go down he gave a cry saying Help Lord
Mat  And straight away Jesus put out his hand and took a grip of him and said to him O man of little faith why were you in doubt
Mat  And when they had got into the boat the wind went down
Mat  And those who were in the boat gave him worship saying Truly you are the Son of God
Mat  And when they had gone across they came to land at Gennesaret
Mat  And when the men of that place had news of him they sent into all the country round about and took to him all who were ill
Mat  With the request that they might only put their hands on the edge of his robe and all those who did so were made well
Mat  Then there came to Jesus from Jerusalem Pharisees and scribes saying
Mat  Why do your disciples go against the teaching of the fathers for they take food with unwashed hands
Mat  And in answer he said to them Why do you yourselves go against the word of God on account of the teaching which has been handed down to you
Mat  For God said Give honour to your father and mother and He who says evil of father or mother will be put to death
Mat  But you say If a man says to his father or his mother That by which you might have had profit from me is given to God
Mat  There is no need for him to give honour to his father And you have made the word of God without effect because of your teaching
Mat  You false ones well did Isaiah say of you
Mat  These people give me honour with their lips but their heart is far from me
Mat  But their worship is to no purpose while they give as their teaching the rules of men
Mat  And he got the people together and said to them Give ear and let my words be clear to you
Mat  Not that which goes into the mouth makes a man unclean but that which comes out of the mouth
Mat  Then the disciples came and said to him Did you see that the Pharisees were troubled when these words came to their ears
Mat  But he said in answer Every plant which my Father in heaven has not put in the earth will be taken up by the roots
Mat  Let them be they are blind guides And if a blind man is guiding a blind man the two will go falling into a hole together
Mat  Then Peter said to him Make the story clear to us
Mat  And he said Are you like them still without wisdom
Mat  Do you not see that whatever goes into the mouth goes on into the stomach and is sent out as waste
Mat  But the things which come out of the mouth come from the heart and they make a man unclean
Mat  For out of the heart come evil thoughts the taking of life broken faith between the married unclean desires of the flesh taking of property false witness bitter words
Mat  These are the things which make a man unclean but to take food with unwashed hands does not make a man unclean
Mat  And Jesus went away from there into the country of Tyre and Sidon
Mat  And a woman of Canaan came out from those parts crying and saying Have pity on me O Lord Son of David my daughter is greatly troubled with an unclean spirit
Mat  But he gave her no answer And his disciples came and said to him Send her away for she is crying after us
Mat  But he made answer and said I was sent only to the wandering sheep of the house of Israel
Mat  But she came and gave him worship saying Help Lord
Mat  And he made answer and said It is not right to take the childrens bread and give it to the dogs
Mat  But she said Yes Lord but even the dogs take the bits from under their masters table
Mat  Then Jesus answering said to her O woman great is your faith let your desire be done And her daughter was made well from that hour
Mat  And Jesus went from there and came to the sea of Galilee and he went up into the mountain and took his seat there
Mat  And there came to him great numbers of people having with them those who were broken in body or blind or without voice or wounded or ill in any way and a number of others they put them down at his feet and he made them well
Mat  So that the people were full of wonder when they saw that those who had no voice were talking the feeble were made strong those whose bodies were broken had the power of walking and the blind were able to see and they gave glory to the God of Israel
Mat  And Jesus got his disciples together and said I have pity for the people because they have now been with me three days and have no food and I will not send them away without food or they will have no strength for the journey
Mat  And the disciples say to him How may we get enough bread in a waste place to give food to such a number of people
Mat  And Jesus says to them How much bread have you And they said Seven cakes and some small fishes
Mat  Then he gave an order to the people to be seated on the earth
Mat  And he took the seven cakes of bread and the fishes and having given praise he gave the broken bread to the disciples and the disciples gave it to the people
Mat  And they all took food and had enough and they took up of the broken bits seven baskets full
Mat  And there were four thousand men who took food together with women and children
Mat  And when he had sent the people away he got into the boat and came into the country of Magadan
Mat  And the Pharisees and Sadducees came and testing him made a request to him to give them a sign from heaven
Mat  But in answer he said to them At nightfall you say The weather will be good for the sky is red
Mat  And in the morning The weather will be bad today for the sky is red and angry You are able to see the face of heaven but not the signs of the times
Mat  An evil and false generation is searching after a sign and no sign will be given to it but the sign of Jonah And he went away from them
Mat  And when the disciples came to the other side they had not taken thought to get bread
Mat  And Jesus said to them Take care to have nothing to do with the leaven of the Pharisees and Sadducees
Mat  And they were reasoning among themselves saying We took no bread
Mat  And Jesus seeing it said O you of little faith why are you reasoning among yourselves because you have no bread
Mat  Do you still not see or keep in mind the five cakes of bread of the five thousand and the number of baskets you took up
Mat  Or the seven cakes of bread of the four thousand and the number of baskets you took up
Mat  How is it that you do not see that I was not talking to you about bread but about keeping away from the leaven of the Pharisees and Sadducees
Mat  Then they saw that it was not the leaven of bread which he had in mind but the teaching of the Pharisees and Sadducees
Mat  Now when Jesus had come into the parts of Caesarea Philippi he said questioning his disciples Who do men say that the Son of man is
Mat  And they said Some say John the Baptist some Elijah and others Jeremiah or one of the prophets
Mat  He says to them But who do you say that I am
Mat  And Simon Peter made answer and said You are the Christ the Son of the living God
Mat  And Jesus made answer and said to him A blessing on you Simon Barjonah because this knowledge has not come to you from flesh and blood but from my Father in heaven
Mat  And I say to you that you are Peter and on this rock will my church be based and the doors of hell will not overcome it
Mat  I will give to you the keys of the kingdom of heaven and whatever is fixed by you on earth will be fixed in heaven and whatever you make free on earth will be made free in heaven
Mat  Then he gave orders to the disciples to give no man word that he was the Christ
Mat  From that time Jesus went on to make clear to his disciples how he would have to go up to Jerusalem and undergo much at the hands of those in authority and the chief priests and scribes and be put to death and the third day come again from the dead
Mat  And Peter protesting said to him Be it far from you Lord it is impossible that this will come about
Mat  But he turning to Peter said Get out of my way Satan you are a danger to me because your mind is not on the things of God but on the things of men
Mat  Then Jesus said to his disciples If any man would come after me let him give up all and take up his cross and come after me
Mat  Because whoever has a desire to keep his life safe will have it taken from him but whoever gives up his life because of me will have it given back to him
Mat  For what profit has a man if he gets all the world with the loss of his life or what will a man give in exchange for his life
Mat  For the Son of man will come in the glory of his Father with his angels and then he will give to every man the reward of his works
Mat  Truly I say to you There are some of those here who will not have a taste of death till they see the Son of man coming in his kingdom
Mat  And after six days Jesus takes with him Peter and James and John his brother and makes them go up with him into a high mountain by themselves
Mat  And he was changed in form before them and his face was shining like the sun and his clothing became white as light
Mat  And Moses and Elijah came before their eyes talking with him
Mat  And Peter made answer and said to Jesus Lord it is good for us to be here if you will let me I will make here three tents one for you and one for Moses and one for Elijah
Mat  While he was still talking a bright cloud came over them and a voice out of the cloud saying This is my dearly loved Son with whom I am well pleased give ear to him
Mat  And at these words the disciples went down on their faces in great fear
Mat  And Jesus came and put his hand on them and said Get up and have no fear
Mat  And lifting up their eyes they saw no one but Jesus only
Mat  And when they were coming down from the mountain Jesus gave them orders saying Let no man have word of what you have seen till the Son of man has come again from the dead
Mat  And his disciples questioning him said Why then do the scribes say that Elijah has to come first
Mat  And in answer he said Elijah truly has to come and put all things right
Mat  But I say to you that Elijah has come and they had no knowledge of him but did to him whatever they were pleased to do the same will the Son of man undergo at their hands
Mat  Then the disciples saw that he was talking to them of John the Baptist
Mat  And when they came to the people a man went down on his knees to him saying
Mat  Lord have mercy on my son for he is off his head and is in great pain and frequently he goes falling into the fire and frequently into the water
Mat  And I took him to your disciples and they were not able to make him well
Mat  And Jesus answering said O false and foolish generation how long will I be with you how long will I put up with you let him come here to me
Mat  And Jesus gave orders to the unclean spirit and it went out of him and the boy was made well from that hour
Mat  Then the disciples came to Jesus privately and said Why were we not able to send it out
Mat  And he says to them Because of your little faith for truly I say to you If you have faith as a grain of mustard seed you will say to this mountain Be moved from this place to that and it will be moved and nothing will be impossible to you
Mat  
Mat  And while they were going about in Galilee Jesus said to them The Son of man will be given up into the hands of men
Mat  And they will put him to death and the third day he will come again from the dead And they were very sad
Mat  And when they had come to Capernaum those who took the Temple tax came to Peter and said Does not your master make payment of the Temple tax
Mat  He says Yes And when he came into the house Jesus said to him What is your opinion Simon from whom do the kings of the earth get payment or tax from their sons or from other people
Mat  And when he said From other people Jesus said to him Then are the sons free
Mat  But so that we may not be a cause of trouble to them go to the sea and let down a hook and take the first fish which comes up and in his mouth you will see a bit of money take that and give it to them for me and you
Mat  In that hour the disciples came to Jesus saying Who is greatest in the kingdom of heaven
Mat  And he took a little child and put him in the middle of them
Mat  And said Truly I say to you If you do not have a change of heart and become like little children you will not go into the kingdom of heaven
Mat  Whoever then will make himself as low as this little child the same is the greatest in the kingdom of heaven
Mat  And whoever gives honour to one such little child in my name gives honour to me
Mat  But whoever is a cause of trouble to one of these little ones who have faith in me it would be better for him to have a great stone fixed to his neck and to come to his end in the deep sea
Mat  A curse is on the earth because of trouble for it is necessary for trouble to come but unhappy is that man through whom the trouble comes
Mat  And if your hand or your foot is a cause of trouble let it be cut off and put it away from you it is better for you to go into life with the loss of a hand or a foot than having two hands or two feet to go into the eternal fire
Mat  And if your eye is a cause of trouble to you take it out and put it away from you it is better for you to go into life with one eye than having two eyes to go into the hell of fire
Mat  Let it not seem to you that one of these little ones is of no value for I say to you that in heaven their angels see at all times the face of my Father in heaven
Mat  
Mat  What would you say now if a man has a hundred sheep and one of them has gone wandering away will he not let the ninetynine be and go to the mountains in search of the wandering one
Mat  And if he comes across it truly I say to you he has more joy over it than over the ninetynine which have not gone out of the way
Mat  Even so it is not the pleasure of your Father in heaven for one of these little ones to come to destruction
Mat  And if your brother does wrong to you go make clear to him his error between you and him in private if he gives ear to you you have got your brother back again
Mat  But if he will not give ear to you take with you one or two more that by the lips of two or three witnesses every word may be made certain
Mat  And if he will not give ear to them let it come to the hearing of the church and if he will not give ear to the church let him be to you as a Gentile and a taxfarmer
Mat  Truly I say to you Whatever things are fixed by you on earth will be fixed in heaven and whatever you make free on earth will be made free in heaven
Mat  Again I say to you that if two of you are in agreement on earth about anything for which they will make a request it will be done for them by my Father in heaven
Mat  For where two or three are come together in my name there am I among them
Mat  Then Peter came and said to him Lord what number of times may my brother do wrong against me and I give him forgiveness till seven times
Mat  Jesus says to him I say not to you Till seven times but Till seventy times seven
Mat  For this reason the kingdom of heaven is like a king who went over his accounts with his servants
Mat  And at the start one came to him who was in his debt for ten thousand talents
Mat  And because he was not able to make payment his lord gave orders for him and his wife and his sons and daughters and all he had to be given for money and payment to be made
Mat  So the servant went down on his face and gave him worship saying Lord give me time to make payment and I will give you all
Mat  And the lord of that servant being moved with pity let him go and made him free of the debt
Mat  But that servant went out and meeting one of the other servants who was in debt to him for one hundred pence he took him by the throat saying Make payment of your debt
Mat  So that servant went down on his face requesting him and saying Give me time and I will make payment to you
Mat  And he would not but went and put him into prison till he had made payment of the debt
Mat  So when the other servants saw what was done they were very sad and came and gave word to their lord of what had been done
Mat  Then his lord sent for him and said You evil servant I made you free of all that debt because of your request to me
Mat  Was it not right for you to have mercy on the other servant even as I had mercy on you
Mat  And his lord was very angry and put him in the hands of those who would give him punishment till he made payment of all the debt
Mat  So will my Father in heaven do to you if you do not everyone from your hearts give forgiveness to his brother
Mat  And it came about that after saying these words Jesus went away from Galilee and came into the parts of Judaea on the other side of Jordan
Mat  And a great number went after him and he made them well there
Mat  And certain Pharisees came to him testing him and saying Is it right for a man to put away his wife for every cause
Mat  And he said in answer Have you not seen in the Writings that he who made them at the first made them male and female and said
Mat  For this cause will a man go away from his father and mother and be joined to his wife and the two will become one flesh
Mat  So that they are no longer two but one flesh Then let not that which has been joined by God be parted by man
Mat  They say to him Why then did Moses give orders that a husband might give her a statement in writing and be free from her
Mat  He says to them Moses because of your hard hearts let you put away your wives but it has not been so from the first
Mat  And I say to you Whoever puts away his wife for any other cause than the loss of her virtue and takes another is a false husband and he who takes her as his wife when she is put away is no true husband to her
Mat  The disciples say to him If this is the position of a man in relation to his wife it is better not to be married
Mat  But he said to them Not all men are able to take in this saying but only those to whom it is given
Mat  For there are men who from birth were without sex and there are some who were made so by men and there are others who have made themselves so for the kingdom of heaven He who is able to take it let him take it
Mat  Then some people took little children to him so that he might put his hands on them in blessing and the disciples said sharp words to them
Mat  But Jesus said Let the little ones come to me and do not keep them away for of such is the kingdom of heaven
Mat  And he put his hands on them and went away
Mat  And one came to him and said Master what good thing have I to do so that I may have eternal life
Mat  And he said to him Why are you questioning me about what is good One there is who is good but if you have a desire to go into life keep the rules of the law
Mat  He says to him Which And Jesus said Do not put anyone to death Do not be untrue in married life Do not take what is not yours Do not give false witness
Mat  Give honour to your father and your mother and Have love for your neighbour as for yourself
Mat  The young man says to him All these things have I done what more is there
Mat  Jesus said to him If you have a desire to be complete go get money for your property and give it to the poor and you will have wealth in heaven and come after me
Mat  But hearing these words the young man went away sorrowing for he had much property
Mat  And Jesus said to his disciples Truly I say to you It is hard for a man with much money to go into the kingdom of heaven
Mat  And again I say to you It is simpler for a camel to go through a needles eye than for a man with much money to go into the kingdom of God
Mat  And the disciples hearing this were greatly surprised saying Who then may have salvation
Mat  And Jesus looking at them said With men this is not possible but with God all things are possible
Mat  Then Peter said to him See we have given up everything and have come after you what then will we have
Mat  And Jesus said to them Truly I say to you that in the time when all things are made new and the Son of man is seated in his glory you who have come after me will be seated on twelve seats judging the twelve tribes of Israel
Mat  And everyone who has given up houses or brothers or sisters or father or mother or child or land for my name will be given a hundred times as much and have eternal life
Mat  But a great number who are first will be last and some who are last will be first
Mat  For the kingdom of heaven is like the master of a house who went out early in the morning to get workers into his vinegarden
Mat  And when he had made an agreement with the workmen for a penny a day he sent them into his vinegarden
Mat  And he went out about the third hour and saw others in the marketplace doing nothing
Mat  And he said to them Go into the vinegarden with the others and whatever is right I will give you And they went to work
Mat  Again he went out about the sixth and the ninth hour and did the same
Mat  And about the eleventh hour he went out and saw others doing nothing and he says to them Why are you here all the day doing nothing
Mat  They say to him Because no man has given us work He says to them Go in with the rest into the vinegarden
