Mat  And when evening came the lord of the vinegarden said to his manager Let the workers come and give them their payment from the last to the first
Mat  And when those men came who had gone to work at the eleventh hour they were given every man a penny
Mat  Then those who came first had the idea that they would get more and they like the rest were given a penny
Mat  And when they got it they made a protest against the master of the house
Mat  Saying These last have done only one hours work and you have made them equal to us who have undergone the hard work of the day and the burning heat
Mat  But he in answer said to one of them Friend I do you no wrong did you not make an agreement with me for a penny
Mat  Take what is yours and go away it is my pleasure to give to this last even as to you
Mat  Have I not the right to do as seems good to me in my house or is your eye evil because I am good
Mat  So the last will be first and the first last
Mat  And when Jesus was going up to Jerusalem he took the twelve disciples on one side and said to them
Mat  See we go up to Jerusalem and the Son of man will be given into the hands of the chief priests and scribes and they will give orders for him to be put to death
Mat  And will give him up to the Gentiles to be made sport of and to be whipped and to be put to death on the cross and the third day he will come back again from the dead
Mat  Then the mother of the sons of Zebedee came to him with her sons giving him worship and making a request of him
Mat  And he said to her What is your desire She says to him Let my two sons be seated the one at your right hand and the other at your left in your kingdom
Mat  But Jesus made answer and said You have no idea what you are requesting Are you able to take of the cup which I am about to take
Mat  They say to him We are able He says to them Truly you will take of my cup but to be seated at my right hand and at my left is not for me to give but it is for those for whom my Father has made it ready
Mat  And when it came to the ears of the ten they were angry with the two brothers
Mat  But Jesus said to them You see that the rulers of the Gentiles are lords over them and their great ones have authority over them
Mat  Let it not be so among you but if anyone has a desire to become great among you let him be your servant
Mat  And whoever has a desire to be first among you let him take the lowest place
Mat  Even as the Son of man did not come to have servants but to be a servant and to give his life for the salvation of men
Mat  And when they were going out from Jericho a great number went after him
Mat  And two blind men seated by the wayside when they had the news that Jesus was going by gave a loud cry saying Lord Son of David have mercy on us
Mat  And the people gave them orders to be quiet but they went on crying even louder Lord Son of David have mercy on us
Mat  And Jesus stopping sent for them and said What would you have me do to you
Mat  They say to him Lord that our eyes may be open
Mat  And Jesus being moved with pity put his fingers on their eyes and straight away they were able to see and went after him
Mat  And when they were near Jerusalem and had come to Bethphage to the Mountain of Olives Jesus sent two disciples
Mat  Saying to them Go into the little town in front of you and straight away you will see an ass with a cord round her neck and a young one with her let them loose and come with them to me
Mat  And if anyone says anything to you you will say The Lord has need of them and straight away he will send them
Mat  Now this took place so that these words of the prophet might come true
Mat  Say to the daughter of Zion See your King comes to you gentle and seated on an ass and on a young ass
Mat  And the disciples went and did as Jesus had given them orders
Mat  And got the ass and the young one and put their clothing on them and he took his seat on it
Mat  And all the people put their clothing down in the way and others got branches from the trees and put them down in the way
Mat  And those who went before him and those who came after gave loud cries saying Glory to the Son of David A blessing on him who comes in the name of the Lord Glory in the highest
Mat  And when he came into Jerusalem all the town was moved saying Who is this
Mat  And the people said This is the prophet Jesus from Nazareth of Galilee
Mat  And Jesus went into the Temple and sent out all who were trading there overturning the tables of the moneychangers and the seats of those trading in doves
Mat  And he said to them It is in the Writings My house is to be named a house of prayer but you are making it a hole of thieves
Mat  And the blind and the broken in body came to him in the Temple and he made them well
Mat  But when the chief priests and the scribes saw the works of power which he did and the children crying out in the Temple Glory to the son of David they were angry and said to him
Mat  Have you any idea what these are saying And Jesus said to them Yes have you not seen in the Writings From the lips of children and babies at the breast you have made your praise complete
Mat  And he went away from them and went out of the town to Bethany and was there for the night
Mat  Now in the morning when he was coming back to the town he had a desire for food
Mat  And seeing a figtree by the wayside he came to it and saw nothing on it but leaves only and he said to it Let there be no fruit from you from this time forward for ever And straight away the figtree became dry and dead
Mat  And when the disciples saw it they were surprised saying How did the figtree become dry in so short a time
Mat  And Jesus in answer said to them Truly I say to you If you have faith without doubting not only may you do what has been done to the figtree but even if you say to this mountain Be taken up and put into the sea it will be done
Mat  And all things whatever you make request for in prayer having faith you will get
Mat  And when he had come into the Temple the chief priests and those in authority over the people came to him while he was teaching and said By what authority do you do these things and who gave you this authority
Mat  And Jesus said to them in answer I will put one question to you and if you give me the answer I will say by what authority I do these things
Mat  The baptism of John where did it come from from heaven or from men And they were reasoning among themselves saying If we say From heaven he will say to us Why then did you not have faith in him
Mat  But if we say From men we are in fear of the people because all take John to be a prophet
Mat  And they made answer and said We have no idea Then he said to them And I will not say to you by what authority I do these things
Mat  But how does it seem to you A man had two sons and he came to the first and said Son go and do work today in the vinegarden
Mat  And he said in answer I will not but later changing his decision he went
Mat  And he came to the second and said the same And he made answer and said I go sir and went not
Mat  Which of the two did his fathers pleasure They say The first Jesus said to them Truly I say to you that taxfarmers and loose women are going into the kingdom of God before you
Mat  For John came to you in the way of righteousness and you had no faith in him but the taxfarmers and the loose women had faith in him and you when you saw it did not even have regret for your sins so as to have faith in him
Mat  Give ear to another story A master of a house made a vine garden and put a wall round it and made a place for crushing out the wine and made a tower and let it out to fieldworkers and went into another country
Mat  And when the time for the fruit came near he sent his servants to the workmen to get the fruit
Mat  And the workmen made an attack on his servants giving blows to one putting another to death and stoning another
Mat  Again he sent other servants more in number than the first and they did the same to them
Mat  But after that he sent his son to them saying They will have respect for my son
Mat  But when the workmen saw the son they said among themselves This is he who will one day be the owner of the property come let us put him to death and take his heritage
Mat  And they took him and driving him out of the vinegarden put him to death
Mat  When then the lord of the vinegarden comes what will he do to those workmen
Mat  They say to him He will put those cruel men to a cruel death and will let out the vinegarden to other workmen who will give him the fruit when it is ready
Mat  Jesus says to them Did you never see in the Writings The stone which the builders put on one side the same has been made the chief stone of the building this was the Lords doing and it is a wonder in our eyes
Mat  For this reason I say to you The kingdom of God will be taken away from you and will be given to a nation producing the fruits of it
Mat  Any man falling on this stone will be broken but he on whom it comes down will be crushed to dust
Mat  And when his stories came to the ears of the chief priests and the Pharisees they saw that he was talking of them
Mat  And though they had a desire to take him they were in fear of the people because in their eyes he was a prophet
Mat  And Jesus talking to them again in stories said
Mat  The kingdom of heaven is like a certain king who made a feast when his son was married
Mat  And sent out his servants to get in the guests to the feast and they would not come
Mat  Again he sent out other servants with orders to say to the guests See I have made ready my feast my oxen and my fat beasts have been put to death and all things are ready come to the feast
Mat  But they gave no attention and went about their business one to his farm another to his trade
Mat  And the rest put violent hands on his servants and did evil to them and put them to death
Mat  But the king was angry and he sent his armies and those who had put his servants to death he gave to destruction burning down their town with fire
Mat  Then he said to his servants The feast is ready but the guests were not good enough
Mat  Go then to the crossroads and get all those whom you see to come to the bridefeast
Mat  And those servants went out into the streets and got together all those whom they came across bad and good and the feast was full of guests
Mat  But when the king came in to see the guests he saw there a man who had not on a guests robe
Mat  And he says to him Friend how came you in here not having a guests robe And he had nothing to say
Mat  Then the king said to the servants Put cords round his hands and feet and put him out into the dark there will be weeping and cries of sorrow
Mat  For out of all to whom the good news has come only a small number will get salvation
Mat  Then the Pharisees went and had a meeting to see how they might make use of his words to take him
Mat  And they sent to him their disciples with the Herodians saying Master we see that you are true and that you are teaching the true way of God and have no fear of anyone because you have no respect for a mans position
Mat  Give us then your opinion of this Is it right to give tax to Caesar or not
Mat  But Jesus saw their trick and said Oh false ones why are you attempting to put me in the wrong
Mat  Let me see the tax money And they gave him a penny
Mat  And he said to them Whose is this image and name on it
Mat  They say to him Caesars Then he said to them Give to Caesar the things which are Caesars and to God the things which are Gods
Mat  And hearing it they were full of wonder and went away from him
Mat  On the same day there came to him the Sadducees who say that there is no coming back from the dead and they put a question to him saying
Mat  Master Moses said If a man at the time of his death has no children let his brother take his wife and get a family for his brother
Mat  Now there were among us seven brothers and the first was married and at his death having no seed gave his wife to his brother
Mat  In the same way the second and the third up to the seventh
Mat  And last of all the woman came to her end
Mat  When they come back from the dead then whose wife will she be of the seven because they all had her
Mat  But Jesus said to them in answer You are in error not having knowledge of the Writings or of the power of God
Mat  For when they come back from the dead there are no husbands and wives but they are as the angels in heaven
Mat  But about the dead coming back to life have you no knowledge of what was said to you by God in the Writings
Mat  I am the God of Abraham and the God of Isaac and the God of Jacob God is not the God of the dead but of the living
Mat  And the people hearing it were surprised at his teaching
Mat  But the Pharisees hearing how the mouths of the Sadducees had been stopped came together
Mat  And one of them a teacher of the law put a question to him testing him and saying
Mat  Master which is the chief rule in the law
Mat  And he said to him Have love for the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind
Mat  This is the first and greatest rule
Mat  And a second like it is this Have love for your neighbour as for yourself
Mat  On these two rules all the law and the prophets are based
Mat  Now while the Pharisees were together Jesus put a question to them saying
Mat  What is your opinion of the Christ whose son is he They say to him The Son of David
Mat  He says to them How then does David in the Spirit give him the name of Lord saying
Mat  The Lord said to my Lord Be seated at my right hand till I put under your feet all those who are against you
Mat  If David then gives him the name of Lord how is he his son
Mat  And no one was able to give him an answer and so great was their fear of him that from that day no one put any more questions to him
Mat  Then Jesus said to the people and to his disciples
Mat  The scribes and the Pharisees have the authority of Moses
Mat  All things then which they give you orders to do these do and keep but do not take their works as your example for they say and do not
Mat  They make hard laws and put great weights on mens backs but they themselves will not put a finger to them
Mat  But all their works they do so as to be seen by men for they make wide their phylacteries and the edges of their robes
Mat  And the things desired by them are the first places at feasts and the chief seats in the Synagogues
Mat  And words of respect in the marketplaces and to be named by men Teacher
Mat  But you may not be named Teacher for one is your teacher and you are all brothers
Mat  And give no man the name of father on earth because one is your Father who is in heaven
Mat  And you may not be named guides because one is your Guide even Christ
Mat  But let the greatest among you be your servant
Mat  And whoever makes himself high will be made low and whoever makes himself low will be made high
Mat  But a curse is on you scribes and Pharisees false ones because you are shutting the kingdom of heaven against men for you do not go in yourselves and those who are going in you keep back
Mat  
Mat  A curse is on you scribes and Pharisees false ones for you go about land and sea to get one disciple and having him you make him twice as much a son of hell as yourselves
Mat  A curse is on you blind guides who say Whoever takes an oath by the Temple it is nothing but whoever takes an oath by the gold of the Temple he is responsible
Mat  You foolish ones and blind which is greater the gold or the Temple which makes the gold holy
Mat  And Whoever takes an oath by the altar it is nothing but whoever takes an oath by the offering which is on it he is responsible
Mat  You blind ones which is greater the offering or the altar which makes the offering holy
Mat  He then who takes an oath by the altar takes it by the altar and by all things on it
Mat  And he who takes an oath by the Temple takes it by the Temple and by him whose house it is
Mat  And he who takes an oath by heaven takes it by the seat of God and by him who is seated on it
Mat  A curse is on you scribes and Pharisees false ones for you make men give a tenth of all sorts of sweetsmelling plants but you give no thought to the more important things of the law righteousness and mercy and faith but it is right for you to do these and not to let the others be undone
Mat  You blind guides who take out a fly from your drink but make no trouble over a camel
Mat  A curse is on you scribes and Pharisees false ones for you make clean the outside of the cup and of the plate but inside they are full of violent behaviour and uncontrolled desire
Mat  You blind Pharisee first make clean the inside of the cup and of the plate so that the outside may become equally clean
Mat  A curse is on you scribes and Pharisees false ones for you are like the restingplaces of the dead which are made white and seem beautiful on the outside but inside are full of dead mens bones and of all unclean things
Mat  Even so you seem to men to be full of righteousness but inside you are all false and full of wrongdoing
Mat  A curse is on you scribes and Pharisees false ones because you put up buildings for housing the dead bodies of the prophets and make fair the last restingplaces of good men and say
Mat  If we had been living in the days of our fathers we would not have taken part with them in the blood of the prophets
Mat  So that you are witnesses against yourselves that you are the sons of those who put the prophets to death
Mat  Make full then the measure of your fathers
Mat  You snakes offspring of snakes how will you be kept from the punishment of hell
Mat  For this reason I send you prophets and wise men and scribes some of them you will put to death and put on the cross and to some of them you will give blows in your Synagogues driving them from town to town
Mat  So that on you may come all the blood of the upright on the earth from the blood of upright Abel to the blood of Zachariah son of Barachiah whom you put to death between the Temple and the altar
Mat  Truly I say to you All these things will come on this generation
Mat  O Jerusalem Jerusalem putting to death the prophets and stoning those who are sent to her Again and again would I have taken your children to myself as a bird takes her young ones under her wings and you would not
Mat  See your house is made waste
Mat  For I say to you You will not see me from this time till you say A blessing on him who comes in the name of the Lord
Mat  And Jesus went out of the Temple and on the way his disciples came to him pointing out the buildings of the Temple
Mat  But he answering said to them See you not all these things truly I say to you that here there will not be one stone resting on another which will not be pulled down
Mat  And while he was seated on the Mountain of Olives the disciples came to him privately saying Make clear to us when will these things be and what will be the sign of your coming and of the end of the world
Mat  And Jesus said to them in answer Take care that you are not tricked
Mat  For people will come in my name saying I am the Christ and a number will be turned from the true way through them
Mat  And news will come to you of wars and talk of wars do not be troubled for these things have to be but it is still not the end
Mat  For nation will be moved against nation and kingdom against kingdom and men will be without food and the earth will be shaking in different places
Mat  But all these things are the first of the troubles
Mat  Then they will be cruel to you and will put you to death and you will be hated by all nations because of my name
Mat  And numbers of people will be turned from the right way and will give one another up and have hate for one another
Mat  And a number of false prophets will come causing error
Mat  And because wrongdoing will be increased the love of most people will become cold
Mat  But he who goes through to the end will get salvation
Mat  And this good news of the kingdom will be given through all the world for a witness to all nations and then the end will come
Mat  When then you see in the holy place the unclean thing which makes destruction of which word was given by Daniel the prophet let this be clear to the reader
Mat  Then let those who are in Judaea go in flight to the mountains
Mat  Let not him who is on the housetop go down to take anything out of his house
Mat  And let not him who is in the field go back to get his coat
Mat  But it will be hard for women who are with child and for those with babies at the breast in those days
Mat  And say a prayer that your flight may not be in the winter or on a Sabbath
Mat  Because in those days there will be great sorrow such as there has not been from the start of the world till now or ever will be
Mat  And if those days had not been made short there would have been no salvation for any but because of the saints those days will be made short
Mat  Then if any man says to you See here is the Christ or Here do not put faith in him
Mat  For there will come up false Christs and false prophets who will do great signs and wonders so that if possible even the saints might be tricked
Mat  See I have made it clear to you before it comes about
Mat  If then they say to you See he is in the waste land go not out See he is in the inner rooms put no faith in it
Mat  Because as in a thunderstorm the bright light coming from the east is seen even in the west so will be the coming of the Son of man
Mat  Wherever the dead body is there will the eagles come together
Mat  But straight away after the trouble of those days the sun will be made dark and the moon will not give her light and the stars will come down from heaven and the powers of heaven will be moved
Mat  And then the sign of the Son of man will be seen in heaven and then all the nations of the earth will have sorrow and they will see the Son of man coming on the clouds of heaven with power and great glory
Mat  And he will send out his angels with a great sound of a horn and they will get his saints together from the four winds from one end of heaven to the other
Mat  Now take an example from the figtree when her branch has become soft and puts out its leaves you are certain that the summer is near
Mat  Even so when you see all these things you may be certain that he is near even at the doors
Mat  Truly I say to you This generation will not come to an end till all these things are complete
Mat  Heaven and earth will come to an end but my words will not come to an end
Mat  But of that day and hour no one has knowledge not even the angels in heaven or the Son but the Father only
Mat  And as were the days of Noah so will be the coming of the Son of man
Mat  Because as in those days before the overflowing of the waters they were feasting and taking wives and getting married till the day when Noah went into the ark
Mat  And they had no care till the waters came and took them all away so will be the coming of the Son of man
Mat  Then two men will be in the field one is taken and one let go
Mat  Two women will be crushing grain one is taken and one let go
Mat  Be watching then for you have no knowledge on what day your Lord will come
Mat  But be certain of this that if the master of the house had had knowledge of the time when the thief was coming he would have been watching and would not have let his house be broken into
Mat  Be ready then for at a time which you have no thought of the Son of man will come
Mat  Who is the true and wise servant whom his lord has put over those in his house to give them their food at the right time
Mat  A blessing on that servant who will be doing so when his lord comes
Mat  Truly I say to you he will put him over all he has
Mat  But if that evil servant says in his heart My lord is a long time in coming
Mat  And is cruel to the other servants taking his pleasure with those who are overcome with wine
Mat  The lord of that servant will come in a day when he is not looking for him and in an hour of which he has no knowledge
Mat  And will have him cut in two and will give him a part in the fate of the false ones there will be weeping and cries of sorrow
Mat  Then the kingdom of heaven will be like ten virgins the friends of the bride who took their lights and went out with the purpose of meeting the husband
Mat  And five of them were foolish and five were wise
Mat  For the foolish when they took their lights took no oil with them
Mat  But the wise took oil in their vessels with their lights
Mat  Now the husband was a long time in coming and they all went to sleep
Mat  But in the middle of the night there is a cry The husband comes Go out to him
Mat  Then all those virgins got up and made ready their lights
Mat  And the foolish said to the wise Give us of your oil for our lights are going out
Mat  But the wise made answer saying There may not be enough for us and you it would be better for you to go to the traders and get oil for yourselves
Mat  And while they went to get oil the master came and those who were ready went in with him to the feast and the door was shut
Mat  After that the other virgins came saying Lord Lord let us in
Mat  But he made answer and said Truly I say to you I have no knowledge of you
Mat  Keep watch then because you are not certain of the day or of the hour
Mat  For it is as when a man about to take a journey got his servants together and gave them his property
Mat  And to one he gave five talents to another two to another one to everyone as he was able and he went on his journey
Mat  Straight away he who had been given the five talents went and did trade with them and made five more
Mat  In the same way he who had been given the two got two more
Mat  But he who was given the one went away and put it in a hole in the earth and kept his lords money in a secret place
Mat  Now after a long time the lord of those servants comes and makes up his account with them
Mat  And he who had the five talents came with his other five talents saying Lord you gave into my care five talents see I have got five more
Mat  His lord said to him Well done good and true servant you have been true in a small thing I will give you control over great things take your part in the joy of your lord
Mat  And he who had the two talents came and said Lord you gave into my care two talents see I have got two more
Mat  His lord said to him Well done good and true servant you have been true in a small thing I will give you control over great things take your part in the joy of your lord
Mat  And he who had had the one talent came and said Lord I had knowledge that you are a hard man getting in grain where you have not put seed and making profits for which you have done no work
Mat  And I was in fear and went away and put your talent in the earth here is what is yours
Mat  But his lord in answer said to him You are a bad and unready servant if you had knowledge that I get in grain where I did not put seed and make profits for which I have done no work
Mat  Why then did you not put my money in the bank and at my coming I would have got back what is mine with interest
Mat  Take away then his talent and give it to him who has the ten talents
Mat  For to everyone who has will be given and he will have more but from him who has not even what he has will be taken away
Mat  And put out the servant who is of no profit into the outer dark there will be weeping and cries of sorrow
Mat  But when the Son of man comes in his glory and all the angels with him then will he be seated in his glory
Mat  And before him all the nations will come together and they will be parted one from another as the sheep are parted from the goats by the keeper
Mat  And he will put the sheep on his right but the goats on the left
Mat  Then will the King say to those on his right Come you who have the blessing of my Father into the kingdom made ready for you before the world was
Mat  For I was in need of food and you gave it to me I was in need of drink and you gave it to me I was wandering and you took me in
Mat  I had no clothing and you gave it to me when I was ill or in prison you came to me
Mat  Then will the upright make answer to him saying Lord when did we see you in need of food and give it to you or in need of drink and give it to you
Mat  And when did we see you wandering and take you in or without clothing and give it to you
Mat  And when did we see you ill or in prison and come to you
Mat  And the King will make answer and say to them Truly I say to you Because you did it to the least of these my brothers you did it to me
Mat  Then will he say to those on the left Go from me you cursed ones into the eternal fire which is ready for the Evil One and his angels
Mat  For I was in need of food and you gave it not to me I was in need of drink and you gave it not to me
Mat  I was wandering and you took me not in without clothing and you gave me no clothing ill and in prison and you came not to me
Mat  Then will they make answer saying Lord when did we see you in need of food or drink or wandering or without clothing or ill or in prison and did not take care of you
Mat  Then will he make answer to them saying Truly I say to you Because you did it not to the least of these you did it not to me
Mat  And these will go away into eternal punishment but the upright into eternal life
Mat  And when Jesus had come to the end of all these words he said to his disciples
Mat  After two days is the Passover and the Son of man will be given up to the death of the cross
Mat  Then the chief priests and the rulers of the people came together in the house of the high priest who was named Caiaphas
Mat  And they made designs together to take Jesus by some trick and put him to death
Mat  But they said Not while the feast is going on for fear of trouble among the people
Mat  Now when Jesus was in Bethany in the house of Simon the leper
Mat  There came to him a woman having a bottle of perfume of great price and she put the perfume on his head when he was seated at table
Mat  But when the disciples saw it they were angry saying To what purpose is this waste
Mat  For we might have got much money for this and given it to the poor
Mat  But Jesus seeing it said to them Why are you troubling the woman she has done a kind act to me
Mat  For the poor you have ever with you but me you have not for ever
Mat  For in putting this perfume on my body she did it to make me ready for my last restingplace
Mat  Truly I say to you Wherever this good news goes out in all the world what this woman has done will be talked of in memory of her
Mat  Then one of the twelve who was named Judas Iscariot went to the chief priests and said
Mat  What will you give me if I give him up to you And the price was fixed at thirty bits of silver
Mat  And from that time he was watching for a chance to give him into their hands
Mat  Now on the first day of unleavened bread the disciples came to Jesus saying Where are we to make ready for you to take the Passover meal
Mat  And he said to them Go into the town to such a man and say to him The Master says My time is near I will keep the Passover at your house with my disciples
Mat  And the disciples did as Jesus had said to them and they made ready the Passover
Mat  Now when evening was come he was seated at table with the twelve disciples
Mat  And while they were taking food he said Truly I say to you that one of you will be false to me
Mat  And they were very said and said to him one by one Is it I Lord
Mat  And he made answer and said He who puts his hand into the plate with me the same will be false to me
Mat  The Son of man goes even as the Writings say of him but a curse is on that man through whom the Son of man is given up it would have been well for that man if he had never come into the world
Mat  And Judas who was false to him made answer and said Is it I Master He says to him Yes
Mat  And when they were taking food Jesus took bread and after blessing it he gave the broken bread to the disciples and said Take it this is my body
Mat  And he took a cup and having given praise he gave it to them saying
Mat  Take of it all of you for this is my blood of the testament which is given for men for the forgiveness of sins
Mat  But I say to you that from now I will not take of this fruit of the vine till that day when I take it new with you in my Fathers kingdom
Mat  And after a song of praise to God they went out to the Mountain of Olives
Mat  Then said Jesus to them All of you will be turned away from me this night for it is said in the Writings I will put to death the keeper of the sheep and the sheep of the flock will be put to flight
Mat  But after I am come back from the dead I will go before you into Galilee
Mat  But Peter made answer and said to him Though all may be turned away from you I will never be turned away
Mat  Jesus said to him Truly I say to you that this night before the hour of the cocks cry you will say three times that you have no knowledge of me
Mat  Peter says to him Even if I am put to death with you I will not be false to you So said all the disciples
Mat  Then comes Jesus with them to a place named Gethsemane and says to his disciples Be seated here while I go over there for prayer
Mat  And he took with him Peter and the two sons of Zebedee and became sad and very troubled
Mat  Then says he to them My soul is very sad even to death keep watch with me here
Mat  And he went forward a little and falling down on his face in prayer he said O my Father if it is possible let this cup go from me but let not my pleasure but yours be done
Mat  And he comes to the disciples and sees that they are sleeping and says to Peter What were you not able to keep watch with me one hour
Mat  Keep watch with prayer so that you may not be put to the test the spirit truly is ready but the flesh is feeble
Mat  Again a second time he went away and said in prayer O my Father if this may not go from me without my taking it let your pleasure be done
Mat  And he came again and saw them sleeping for their eyes were tired
Mat  And he went away from them again and a third time said the same prayer
Mat  Then he comes to the disciples and says to them Go on sleeping now and take your rest for the hour is come and the Son of man is given into the hands of evil men
Mat  Up let us be going see he who gives me up is near
Mat  And while he was still talking Judas one of the twelve came and with him a band armed with swords and sticks from the chief priests and those in authority over the people
Mat  Now the false one had given them a sign saying The one to whom I give a kiss that is he take him
Mat  And straight away he came to Jesus and said Master and gave him a kiss
Mat  And Jesus said to him Friend do that for which you have come Then they came and put hands on Jesus and took him
Mat  And one of those who were with Jesus put out his hand and took out his sword and gave the servant of the high priest a blow cutting off his ear
Mat  Then says Jesus to him Put up your sword again into its place for all those who take the sword will come to death by the sword
Mat  Does it not seem possible to you that if I make request to my Father he will even now send me an army of angels
Mat  But how then would the Writings come true which say that so it has to be
Mat  In that hour Jesus said to the people Have you come out as against a thief with swords and sticks to take me I was teaching every day in the Temple and you took me not
Mat  But all this has taken place so that the writings of the prophets might come true Then all his disciples went from him in flight
Mat  And those who had made Jesus prisoner took him away to the house of Caiaphas the high priest where the scribes and those in authority over the people had come together
Mat  But Peter went after him at a distance to the house of the high priest and went in and took his seat with the servants to see the end
Mat  Now the chief priests and all the Sanhedrin were looking for false witness against Jesus so that they might put him to death
Mat  And they were not able to get it though a number of false witnesses came
Mat  But later there came two who said This man said I am able to give the Temple of God to destruction and to put it up again in three days
Mat  And the high priest got up and said to him Have you no answer what is it which these say against you
Mat  But Jesus said not a word And the high priest said to him I put you on oath by the living God that you will say to us if you are the Christ the Son of God
Mat  Jesus says to him You say so but I say to you From now you will see the Son of man seated at the right hand of power and coming on the clouds of heaven
Mat  Then the high priest violently parting his robes said He has said evil against God what more need have we of witnesses for now his words against God have come to your ears
Mat  What is your opinion They made answer and said It is right for him to be put to death
Mat  Then they put shame on him and were cruel to him and some gave him blows saying
Mat  Be a prophet O Christ and say who gave you a blow
Mat  Now Peter was seated in the open square outside the house and a servantgirl came to him saying You were with Jesus the Galilaean
Mat  But he said before them all that it was false saying I have no knowledge of what you say
Mat  And when he had gone out into the doorway another saw him and says to those who were there This man was with Jesus the Nazarene
Mat  And again he said with an oath I have no knowledge of the man
Mat  And after a little time those who were near came and said to Peter Truly you are one of them because your talk is witness against you
Mat  Then with curses and oaths he said I have no knowledge of the man And straight away there came the cry of a cock
Mat  And the word of Jesus came back to Peter when he said Before the hour of the cocks cry you will say three times that you have no knowledge of me And he went out weeping bitterly
Mat  Now when it was morning all the chief priests and those in authority took thought together with the purpose of putting Jesus to death
Mat  And they put cords on him and took him away and gave him up to Pilate the ruler
Mat  Then Judas who was false to him seeing that he was to be put to death in his regret took back the thirty bits of silver to the chief priests and those in authority
Mat  Saying I have done wrong in giving into your hands an upright man But they said What is that to us it is your business
Mat  And he put down the silver in the Temple and went out and put himself to death by hanging
Mat  And the chief priests took the silver and said It is not right to put it in the Temple store for it is the price of blood
Mat  And they made a decision to get with the silver the potters field as a place for the dead of other countries
Mat  For this cause that field was named The field of blood to this day
Mat  Then came true that which was said by Jeremiah the prophet And they took the thirty bits of silver the price of him who was valued by the children of Israel
Mat  And they gave them for the potters field as I had word from the Lord
Mat  And Jesus was before the ruler who put a question to him Are you the King of the Jews And Jesus said to him You say so
Mat  But when the chief priests and those in authority made statements against him he gave no answer
Mat  Then says Pilate to him Do you give no attention to what their witnesses say against you
Mat  And he gave him no answer not even a word so that the ruler was greatly surprised
Mat  Now at the feast it was the way for the ruler to let free to the people one prisoner at their selection
Mat  And they had then an important prisoner whose name was Barabbas
Mat  So when they came together Pilate said to them Whom will you have Barabbas or Jesus who is named Christ
Mat  For he saw that for envy they had given him up
Mat  And while he was on the judges seat his wife sent to him saying Have nothing to do with that upright man for I have had much trouble this day in a dream because of him
Mat  Now the chief priests and those in authority got the people to make request for Barabbas and for Jesus to be put to death
Mat  But the ruler made answer and said to them Which of the two is it your pleasure that I let go free And they said Barabbas
Mat  Pilate says to them What then am I to do with Jesus who is named Christ They all say Let him be put to death on the cross
Mat  And he said Why what evil has he done But they gave loud cries saying To the cross with him
Mat  So when Pilate saw that he was able to do nothing but that trouble was working up he took water and washing his hands before the people said The blood of this upright man is not on my hands you are responsible
Mat  And all the people made answer and said Let his blood be on us and on our children
Mat  Then he let Barabbas go free but after having Jesus whipped he gave him up to be put to death on the cross
Mat  Then the rulers armed men took Jesus into the open square and got all their band together
Mat  And they took off his clothing and put on him a red robe
Mat  And they made a crown of thorns and put it on his head and put a rod in his right hand and they went down on their knees before him and made sport of him saying Long life to the King of the Jews
Mat  And they put shame on him and gave him blows on the head with the rod
Mat  And when they had made sport of him they took the robe off him and put his clothing on him and took him away to put him on the cross
Mat  And while they were coming out they saw a man of Cyrene Simon by name and they made him go with them so that he might take up his cross
Mat  And when they came to the place named Golgotha that is to say Dead Mans Head
Mat  They gave him wine mixed with bitter drink and after tasting it he took no more
Mat  And when they had put him on the cross they made division of his clothing among them by the decision of chance
Mat  And they were seated there watching him
Mat  And they put up over his head the statement of his crime in writing THIS IS JESUS THE KING OF THE JEWS
Mat  Then two thieves were put on crosses with him one on the right and one on the left
Mat  And those who went by said bitter words to him shaking their heads and saying
Mat  You who would give the Temple to destruction and put it up again in three days get yourself free if you are the Son of God come down from the cross
Mat  In the same way the chief priests making sport of him with the scribes and those in authority said
Mat  A saviour of others he has no salvation for himself If he is the King of Israel let him now come down from the cross and we will have faith in him
Mat  He put his faith in God let God be his saviour now if he will have him for he said I am the Son of God
Mat  And the thieves who were on the crosses said evil words to him
Mat  Now from the sixth hour it was dark over all the land till the ninth hour
Mat  And about the ninth hour Jesus gave a loud cry saying Eli Eli lama sabachthani that is My God my God why are you turned away from me
Mat  And some of those who were near by hearing it said This man is crying to Elijah
Mat  And straight away one of them went quickly and took a sponge and made it full of bitter wine and put it on a rod and gave him drink
Mat  And the rest said Let him be let us see if Elijah will come to his help
Mat  And Jesus gave another loud cry and gave up his spirit
Mat  And the curtain of the Temple was parted in two from end to end and there was an earthshock and the rocks were broken
Mat  And the restingplaces of the dead came open and the bodies of a number of sleeping saints came to life
Mat  And coming out of their restingplaces after he had come again from the dead they went into the holy town and were seen by a number of people
Mat  Now the captain and those who were with him watching Jesus when they saw the earthshock and the things which were done were in great fear and said Truly this was a son of God
Mat  And a number of women were there watching from a distance who had come with Jesus from Galilee waiting on his needs
Mat  Among whom was Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of James and Joses and the mother of the sons of Zebedee
Mat  And in the evening there came a man of wealth from Arimathaea Joseph by name who was a disciple of Jesus
Mat  This man went in to Pilate and made a request for the body of Jesus Then Pilate gave orders for it to be given to him
Mat  And Joseph took the body folding it in clean linen
Mat  And put it in the restingplace which had been cut out of the rock for himself and after rolling a great stone to the door of it he went away
Mat  And Mary Magdalene was there and the other Mary seated by the place of the dead
Mat  Now on the day after the getting ready of the Passover the chief priests and Pharisees came together to Pilate
Mat  Saying Sir we have in mind how that false man said while he was still living After three days I will come again from the dead
Mat  Give orders then that the place where his body is may be made safe till the third day for fear that his disciples come and take him away secretly and say to the people He has come back from the dead and the last error will be worse than the first
Mat  Pilate said to them You have watchmen go and make it as safe as you are able
Mat  So they went and made safe the place where his body was putting a stamp on the stone and the watchmen were with them
Mat  Now late on the Sabbath when the dawn of the first day of the week was near Mary Magdalene and the other Mary came to see the place where his body was
Mat  And there was a great earthshock for an angel of the Lord came down from heaven and rolling back the stone took his seat on it
Mat  His form was shining like the light and his clothing was white as snow
Mat  And for fear of him the watchmen were shaking and became as dead men
Mat  And the angel said to the women Have no fear for I see that you are searching for Jesus who was put to death on the cross
Mat  He is not here for he has come to life again even as he said Come see the Lords restingplace
Mat  And go quickly and give his disciples the news that he has come back from the dead and is going before you into Galilee there you will see him as I have said to you
Mat  And they went away quickly with fear and great joy to give his disciples the news
Mat  And on the way Jesus came to them saying Be glad And they came and put their hands on his feet and gave him worship
Mat  Then said Jesus to them Have no fear go and give word to my brothers to go into Galilee and there they will see me
Mat  Now while they were going some of the watchmen came into the town and gave news to the chief priests of all the things which had taken place
Mat  And when they had come together with those in authority and had made their decision they gave much money to the watchmen saying
Mat  Say His disciples came by night and took him away secretly while we were sleeping
Mat  And if this comes to the rulers ears we will see that he does not make you responsible
Mat  So they took the money and did as they had been ordered and this account has been current among the Jews till the present time
Mat  But the eleven disciples went into Galilee to the mountain where Jesus had given them orders to go
Mat  And when they saw him they gave him worship but some were in doubt
Mat  And Jesus came to them and said All authority has been given to me in heaven and on earth
Mat  Go then and make disciples of all the nations giving them baptism in the name of the Father and of the Son and of the Holy Spirit
Mat  Teaching them to keep all the rules which I have given you and see I am ever with you even to the end of the world
Mak  The first words of the good news of Jesus Christ the Son of God
Mak  Even as it is said in the book of Isaiah the prophet See I send my servant before your face who will make ready your way
Mak  The voice of one crying in the waste land Make ready the way of the Lord make his roads straight
Mak  John came and gave baptism in the waste land preaching baptism as a sign of forgiveness of sin for those whose hearts were changed
Mak  And there went out to him all the people of Judaea and all those of Jerusalem and they were given baptism by him in the river Jordan saying that they were sinners
Mak  And John was clothed in camels hair with a leather band about him and his food was locusts and honey
Mak  And he said to them all There is one coming after me who is greater than I whose shoes I am not good enough to undo
Mak  I have given you baptism with water but he will give you baptism with the Holy Spirit
Mak  And it came about in those days that Jesus came from Nazareth of Galilee and was given baptism by John in the Jordan
Mak  And straight away coming up out of the water he saw the heavens broken open and the Spirit coming down on him as a dove
Mak  And a voice came out of heaven You are my dearly loved Son with whom I am well pleased
Mak  And straight away the Spirit sent him out into the waste land
Mak  And he was in the waste land for forty days being tested by Satan and he was with the beasts and the angels took care of him
Mak  Now after John had been put in prison Jesus came into Galilee preaching the good news of God
Mak  And saying The time has come and the kingdom of God is near let your hearts be turned from sin and have faith in the good news
Mak  And going by the sea of Galilee he saw Simon and Andrew the brother of Simon putting a net into the sea for they were fishermen
Mak  And Jesus said to them Come after me and I will make you fishers of men
Mak  And they went straight from their nets and came after him
Mak  And going on a little farther he saw James the son of Zebedee and John his brother who were in their boat stitching up their nets
Mak  And he said Come after me and they went away from their father Zebedee who was in the boat with the servants and came after him
Mak  And they came to Capernaum and on the Sabbath he went into the Synagogue and gave teaching
Mak  And they were full of wonder at his teaching because he gave it as one having authority and not like the scribes
Mak  And there was in their Synagogue a man with an unclean spirit and he gave a cry
Mak  Saying What have we to do with you Jesus of Nazareth have you come to put an end to us I see well who you are the Holy One of God
Mak  And Jesus said to him sharply Be quiet and come out of him
Mak  And the unclean spirit shaking him violently and crying with a loud voice came out of him
Mak  And they were all greatly surprised so that they put questions to one another saying What is this a new teaching with authority he gives orders even to the unclean spirits and they do what he says
Mak  And news of him went out quickly everywhere into all parts of Galilee round about
Mak  And when they came out of the Synagogue they went into the house of Simon and Andrew with James and John
Mak  Now Simons wifes mother was ill with a burning heat and they gave him word of her
Mak  And he came and took her by the hand lifting her up and she became well and took care of their needs
Mak  And in the evening at sundown they took to him all who were diseased and those who had evil spirits
Mak  And all the town had come together at the door
Mak  And a number who were ill with different diseases he made well and sent out evil spirits but he did not let the evil spirits say anything because they had knowledge of him
Mak  And in the morning a long time before daylight he got up and went out to a quiet place and there he gave himself up to prayer
Mak  And Simon and those who were with him came after him
Mak  And when they came up with him they said to him Everyone is looking for you
Mak  And he said to them Let us go to other parts into the nearest towns so that I may give teaching there because for this purpose I came
Mak  And he went into their Synagogues in every part of Galilee preaching and driving out evil spirits
Mak  And a leper came to him and going down on his knees before him made a request saying If it is your pleasure you have the power to make me clean
Mak  And being moved with pity he put out his hand and touching him said to him It is my pleasure be made clean
Mak  And straight away the disease went from him and he was made clean
Mak  And he sent him away saying to him very sharply
Mak  See that you say nothing to any man but go and let the priest see you and make yourself clean by an offering of the things ordered by Moses for a witness to them
Mak  But he went out and made it public giving an account of it everywhere so that Jesus was no longer able to go openly into a town but was outside in the waste land and they came to him from every part
Mak  And when he came into Capernaum again after some days the news went about that he was in the house
Mak  And a great number had come together so that there was no longer room for them no not even about the door and he gave them teaching
Mak  And four men came to him with one on a bed who had no power of moving
Mak  And when they were unable to get near him because of all the people they got the roof uncovered where he was and when it was broken up they let down the bed on which the man was
Mak  And Jesus seeing their faith said to him Son you have forgiveness for your sins
Mak  But there were certain of the scribes seated there and reasoning in their hearts
Mak  Why does this man say such things he has no respect for God from whom does forgiveness come but from God only
Mak  And Jesus having knowledge in his spirit of their thoughts said to them Why are you reasoning about these things in your hearts
Mak  Which is the simpler to say to a man who is ill You have forgiveness for your sins or Get up take up your bed and go
Mak  But so that you may see that the Son of man has authority for the forgiveness of sins on earth he said to the man
Mak  I say to you Get up take up your bed and go to your house
Mak  And he got up and straight away took up the bed and went out before them all so that they were all full of wonder and gave glory to God saying We have never seen anything like this
Mak  And he went out again by the seaside and all the people came to him and he gave them teaching
Mak  And when he went by he saw Levi the son of Alphaeus seated at the place where taxes were taken and he said to him Come with me And he got up and went with him
Mak  And it came about that he was seated at meat in his house and a number of taxfarmers and sinners were at table with Jesus and his disciples for there were a great number of them and they came after him
Mak  And the scribes of the Pharisees when they saw that he was taking food with the taxfarmers and sinners said to his disciples Why does he take food and drink with such men
Mak  And Jesus hearing it said to them Those who are well have no need of a medical man but those who are ill I have come not to get the upright but sinners
Mak  And Johns disciples and the Pharisees were taking no food and they came and said to him Why do Johns disciples and the disciples of the Pharisees go without food but your disciples do not
Mak  And Jesus said to them Will the friends of a newlymarried man go without food while he is with them as long as they have him with them they will not go without food
Mak  But the days will come when the husband will be taken away from them and then they will go without food
Mak  No man puts a bit of new cloth on an old coat or the new by pulling away from the old makes a worse hole
Mak  And no man puts new wine into old wineskins or the skins will be burst by the wine and the wine and the skins will be wasted but new wine has to be put into new wineskins
Mak  And it came about that on the Sabbath day he was going through the grainfields and while they were walking his disciples took the heads of grain
Mak  And the Pharisees said to him Why are they doing what it is not right to do on the Sabbath
Mak  And he said to them Have you no knowledge of what David did when he had need and was without food he and those who were with him
Mak  How he went into the house of God when Abiathar was high priest and took for food the holy bread which only the priests may take and gave it to those who were with him
Mak  And he said to them The Sabbath was made for man and not man for the Sabbath
Mak  So that the Son of man is lord even of the Sabbath
Mak  And he went again into the Synagogue and there was a man there whose hand was dead
Mak  And they were watching him to see if he would make him well on the Sabbath day so that they might have something against him
Mak  And he said to the man Get up and come forward
Mak  And he said to them Is it right to do good on the Sabbath or to do evil to give life or to put to death But they said nothing
Mak  And looking round on them he was angry being sad because of their hard hearts and he said to the man Put out your hand And he put it out and his hand was made well
Mak  And the Pharisees went out and straight away made designs with the Herodians about how they might put him to death
Mak  And Jesus went away with his disciples to the sea and a great number from Galilee came after him and from Judaea
Mak  And from Jerusalem and from Idumaea and the other side of Jordan and the country about Tyre and Sidon a great number hearing what great things he did came to him
Mak  And he made a request to his disciples to have a little boat ready for him so that he might not be crushed by the people
Mak  For he had made such a great number well that all those who were diseased were falling down before him for the purpose of touching him
Mak  And the unclean spirits whenever they saw him went down before him crying out and saying You are the Son of God
Mak  And he gave them special orders not to say who he was
Mak  And he went up into the mountain and sent for those whom it was his pleasure to have with him and they went to him
Mak  And he took twelve to be with him so that he might send them out as preachers
Mak  And give them the power of driving out evil spirits
Mak  To Simon he gave the second name of Peter
Mak  And to James the son of Zebedee and John the brother of James he gave the second name of Boanerges which is Sons of thunder
Mak  And Andrew and Philip and Bartholomew and Matthew and Thomas and James the son of Alphaeus and Thaddaeus and Simon the Zealot
Mak  And Judas Iscariot who was false to him
Mak  And he went into a house And the people came together again so that they were not even able to take bread
Mak  And when his friends had news of it they went out to get him saying He is off his head
Mak  And the scribes who came down from Jerusalem said He has Beelzebub and By the ruler of evil spirits he sends evil spirits out of men
Mak  And turning to them he said to them in the form of a story How is it possible for Satan to put out Satan
Mak  If there is division in a kingdom that kingdom will come to destruction
Mak  And if there is division in a house that house will come to destruction
Mak  And if Satan is at war with himself and there is division in him he will not keep his place but will come to an end
Mak  But no one is able to go into the house of the strong man and take his goods without first putting cords round the strong man and then he will take his goods
Mak  Truly I say to you The sons of men will have forgiveness for all their sins and for all the evil words they say
Mak  But whoever says evil things against the Holy Spirit will never have forgiveness but the evil he has done will be with him for ever
Mak  Because they said He has an unclean spirit
Mak  And his mother and brothers came and were outside and sent for him requesting to see him
Mak  And a great number were seated round him and they said to him See your mother and your brothers are outside looking for you
Mak  And he said in answer Who are my mother and my brothers
Mak  And looking round at those who were seated about him he said See my mother and my brothers
Mak  Whoever does Gods pleasure the same is my brother and sister and mother
Mak  And again he was teaching by the seaside And a very great number of people had come to him so that he got into a boat on the sea and took his seat and all the people were on the land by the seaside
Mak  And he gave them teaching about a number of things in the form of stories and said to them in his teaching Give ear
Mak  A man went out to put seed in the earth
Mak  And while he was doing it some was dropped by the wayside and the birds came and took it for food
Mak  And some went on the stones where it had not much earth and it came up straight away because the earth was not deep
Mak  And when the sun was high it was burned and because it had no root it became dry and dead
Mak  And some went among the thorns and the thorns came up and it had no room for growth and gave no fruit
Mak  And some falling on good earth gave fruit coming up and increasing and giving thirty sixty and a hundred times as much
Mak  And he said to them Whoever has ears let him give ear
Mak  And when he was by himself those who were round him with the twelve put questions to him about the purpose of the stories
Mak  And he said to them To you is given the secret of the kingdom of God but to those who are outside all things are given in the form of stories
Mak  So that seeing they may see and it will not be clear to them and hearing it they will not get the sense for fear that they may be turned again to me and have forgiveness
Mak  And he said to them If you are not clear about this story how will you be clear about the others
Mak  The seed is the word
Mak  And these are they by the wayside where the word is planted and when they have given ear the Evil One comes straight away and takes away the word which has been planted in them
Mak  And in the same way these are they who are planted on the stones who when the word has come to their ears straight away take it with joy
Mak  And they have no root in themselves but go on for a time then when trouble comes or pain because of the word they quickly become full of doubts
Mak  And others are those planted among the thorns these are they who have given ear to the word
Mak  And the cares of this life and the deceits of wealth and the desire for other things coming in put a stop to the growth of the word and it gives no fruit
Mak  And these are they who were planted on the good earth such as give ear to the word and take it into their hearts and give fruit thirty and sixty and a hundred times as much
Mak  And he said to them When the light comes in do people put it under a vessel or under the bed and not on its table
Mak  There is nothing covered which will not be seen openly and nothing has been made secret which will not come to light
Mak  If any man has ears let him give ear
Mak  And he said to them Take care what you give ear to in the same measure as you give you will get and more will be given to you
Mak  He who has to him will be given and he who has not from him will be taken even that which he has
Mak  And he said Such is the kingdom of God as if a man put seed in the earth
Mak  And went to sleep and got up night and day and the seed came to growth though he had no idea how
Mak  The earth gives fruit by herself first the leaf then the head then the full grain
Mak  But when the grain is ready he quickly sends men to get it cut because the time for cutting has come
Mak  And he said What picture may we give of the kingdom of God or with what story may we make it clear
Mak  It is like a grain of mustard seed which when it is put in the earth is smaller than all the seeds on the earth
Mak  But when it is planted it comes up and becomes taller than all the plants and puts out great branches so that the birds of heaven are able to take rest in its shade
Mak  And with a number of such stories he gave them his teaching as they were able to take it
Mak  And without a story he said nothing to them but privately to his disciples he made all things clear
Mak  And on that day when the evening had come he said to them Let us go over to the other side
Mak  And going away from the people they took him with them as he was in the boat And other boats were with him
Mak  And a great storm of wind came up and the waves came into the boat so that the boat was now becoming full
Mak  And he himself was in the back of the boat sleeping on the cushion and they awaking him said Master is it nothing to you that we are in danger of destruction
Mak  And he came out of his sleep and gave strong orders to the wind and said to the sea Peace be at rest And the wind went down and there was a great calm
Mak  And he said to them Why are you full of fear have you still no faith
Mak  And their fear was great and they said one to another Who then is this that even the wind and the sea do his orders
Mak  And they came to the other side of the sea into the country of the Gerasenes
Mak  And when he had got out of the boat straight away there came to him from the place of the dead a man with an unclean spirit
Mak  He was living in the place of the dead and no man was able to keep him down no not with a chain
Mak  Because he had frequently been prisoned in chains and iron bands and the chains had been parted and the bands broken by him and no man was strong enough to make him quiet
Mak  And all the time by day and by night in the place of the dead and in the mountains he was crying out and cutting himself with stones
Mak  And when he saw Jesus from far off he went quickly to him and gave him worship
Mak  And crying out with a loud voice he said What have I to do with you Jesus Son of the Most High God In Gods name do not be cruel to me
Mak  For Jesus had said to him Come out of the man you unclean spirit
Mak  And Jesus said What is your name And he made answer My name is Legion because there are a great number of us
Mak  And he made strong prayers to him not to send them away out of the country
Mak  Now on the mountain side there was a great herd of pigs getting their food
Mak  And they said to him Send us into the pigs so that we may go into them
Mak  And he let them do it And the unclean spirits came out and went into the pigs and the herd went rushing down a sharp slope into the sea about two thousand of them and they came to their death in the sea
Mak  And their keepers went running and gave an account of it in the town and in the country And people came to see what had taken place
Mak  And they came to Jesus and saw the man in whom had been the evil spirits seated clothed and with full use of his senses and they were full of fear
Mak  And those who had seen it gave them an account of what had been done to him who had the evil spirits and of the fate of the pigs
Mak  And they made a request to him to go out of their country
Mak  And when he was getting into the boat the man in whom had been the evil spirits had a great desire to come with him
Mak  And he would not let him but said to him Go to your house to your friends and give them news of the great things the Lord has done for you and how he had mercy on you
Mak  And he went on his way and made public in the country of Decapolis what great things Jesus had done for him and all men were full of wonder
Mak  And when Jesus had gone over again in the boat to the other side a great number of people came to him and he was by the sea
Mak  And one of the rulers of the Synagogue Jairus by name came and seeing him went down at his feet
Mak  And made strong prayers to him saying My little daughter is near to death it is my prayer that you will come and put your hands on her so that she may be made well and have life
Mak  And he went with him and a great number of people went after him and came round him
Mak  And a woman who had had a flow of blood for twelve years
Mak  And had undergone much at the hands of a number of medical men and had given all she had and was no better but even worse
Mak  When she had news of the things which Jesus did went among the people coming after him and put her hand on his robe
Mak  For she said If I may only put my hand on his robe I will be made well
Mak  And straight away the fountain of her blood was stopped and she had a feeling in her body that her disease had gone and she was well
Mak  And straight away Jesus was conscious that power had gone out of him and turning to the people he said Who was touching my robe
Mak  And his disciples said to him You see the people round you on every side and you say Who was touching me
Mak  And on his looking round to see her who had done this thing
Mak  The woman shaking with fear conscious of what had been done to her came and falling on her face before him gave him a true account of everything
Mak  And he said to her Daughter your faith has made you well go in peace and be free from your disease
Mak  And while he was still talking they came from the ruler of the Synagogues house saying Your daughter is dead why are you still troubling the Master
Mak  But Jesus giving no attention to their words said to the ruler of the Synagogue Have no fear only have faith
Mak  And he did not let anyone come with him but Peter and James and John the brother of James
Mak  And they came to the house of the ruler of the Synagogue and he saw people running this way and that and weeping and crying loudly
Mak  And when he had gone in he said to them Why are you making such a noise and weeping The child is not dead but sleeping
Mak  And they were laughing at him But he having sent them all out took the father of the child and her mother and those who were with him and went in where the child was
Mak  And taking her by the hand he said to her Talitha cumi which is My child I say to you Get up
Mak  And the young girl got up straight away and was walking about she being twelve years old And they were overcome with wonder
Mak  And he gave them special orders that they were not to say anything of this and he said that some food was to be given to her
Mak  And he went away from there and came into his country and his disciples went with him
Mak  And when the Sabbath day had come he was teaching in the Synagogue and a number of people hearing him were surprised saying From where did this man get these things and What is the wisdom given to this man and what are these works of power done by his hands
Mak  Is not this the woodworker the son of Mary and brother of James and Joses and Judas and Simon and are not his sisters here with us And they were bitter against him
Mak  And Jesus said to them A prophet is nowhere without honour but in his country and among his relations and in his family
Mak  And he was unable to do any work of power there but only to put his hands on one or two persons who were ill and make them well
Mak  And he was greatly surprised because they had no faith And he went about the country places teaching
Mak  And he gave orders to the twelve and sent them out two by two and he gave them authority over the unclean spirits
Mak  And he said that they were to take nothing for their journey but a stick only no bread no bag no money in their pockets
Mak  They were to go with common shoes on their feet and not to take two coats
Mak  And he said to them Wherever you go into a house make that your restingplace till you go away
Mak  And whatever place will not take you in and will not give ear to you when you go away put off the dust from your feet as a witness against them
Mak  And they went out preaching the need for a change of heart in men
Mak  And they sent out a number of evil spirits and put oil on a great number who were ill and made them well
Mak  And king Herod had news of him because his name was on the lips of all and he said John the Baptist has come back from the dead and for this reason these powers are working in him
Mak  But others said It is Elijah And others said It is a prophet even like one of the prophets
Mak  But Herod when he had news of it said John whom I put to death has come back from the dead
Mak  For Herod himself had sent men out to take John and put him in prison because of Herodias his brother Philips wife whom he had taken for himself
Mak  For John said to Herod It is wrong for you to have your brothers wife
Mak  And Herodias was bitter against him desiring to put him to death but she was not able
Mak  For Herod was in fear of John being conscious that he was an upright and holy man and kept him safe And hearing him he was much troubled and he gave ear to him gladly
Mak  And the chance came when Herod on his birthday gave a feast to his lords and the high captains and the chief men of Galilee
Mak  And when the daughter of Herodias herself came in and did a dance Herod and those who were at table with him were pleased with her and the king said to the girl Make a request for anything and I will give it you
Mak  And he took an oath saying to her Whatever is your desire I will give it to you even half of my kingdom
Mak  And she went out and said to her mother What is my request to be And she said The head of John the Baptist
Mak  And she came in quickly to the king and said My desire is that you give me straight away on a plate the head of John the Baptist
Mak  And the king was very sad but because of his oaths and those who were with him at table he would not say No to her
Mak  And straight away the king sent out one of his armed men and gave him an order to come back with the head and he went and took off Johns head in prison
Mak  And came back with the head on a plate and gave it to the girl and the girl gave it to her mother
Mak  And when his disciples had news of it they came and took up his body and put it in its last restingplace
Mak  And the twelve came together to Jesus and they gave him an account of all the things they had done and all they had been teaching
Mak  And he said to them Come away by yourselves to a quiet place and take a rest for a time Because there were a great number coming and going and they had no time even for food
Mak  And they went away in the boat to a waste place by themselves
Mak  And the people saw them going and a number of them having knowledge who they were went running there together on foot from all the towns and got there before them
Mak  And he got out and saw a great mass of people and he had pity on them because they were like sheep without a keeper and he gave them teaching about a number of things
Mak  And at the end of the day his disciples came to him and said This place is waste land and it is late
Mak  Send them away so that they may go into the country and small towns round about and get some food for themselves
Mak  But he said to them in answer Give them food yourselves And they said to him Are we to go and get bread for two hundred pence and give it to them
Mak  And he said to them How much bread have you go and see And when they had seen they said Five cakes of bread and two fishes
Mak  And he made them all be seated in groups on the green grass
Mak  And they were placed in groups by hundreds and by fifties
Mak  And he took the five cakes of bread and the two fishes and looking up to heaven he said words of blessing over them and when the cakes were broken he gave them to the disciples to put before the people and he made division of the two fishes among them all
Mak  And they all took of the food and had enough
Mak  And they took up twelve baskets full of the broken bits and of the fishes
Mak  And those who took of the bread were five thousand men
Mak  And straight away he made his disciples get into the boat and go before him to the other side to Bethsaida while he himself sent the people away
Mak  And after he had sent them away he went up into a mountain for prayer
Mak  And by evening the boat was in the middle of the sea and he by himself on the land
Mak  And seeing that they had trouble in getting their boat through the water because the wind was against them about the fourth watch of the night he came to them walking on the sea and he would have gone past them
Mak  But they when they saw him walking on the sea took him for a spirit and gave a loud cry
Mak  For they all saw him and were troubled But straight away he said to them Take heart it is I have no fear
Mak  And he went to them into the boat and the wind went down and they were full of wonder in themselves
Mak  For it was not clear to them about the bread but their hearts were hard
Mak  And when they had gone across they came to Gennesaret and got their boat to land
Mak  And when they had got out of the boat the people quickly had news of him
Mak  And went running through all the country round about and took on their beds those who were ill to where it was said that he was
Mak  And wherever he went into small towns or great towns or into the country they took those who were ill into the marketplaces requesting him that they might put their hands even on the edge of his robe and all those who did so were made well
Mak  And there came together to him the Pharisees and certain of the scribes who had come from Jerusalem
Mak  And had seen that some of his disciples took their bread with unclean that is unwashed hands
Mak  Now the Pharisees and all the Jews do not take food without washing their hands with care keeping the old rule which has been handed down to them
Mak  And when they come from the marketplace they take no food till their hands are washed and a number of other orders there are which have been handed down to them to keepwashings of cups and pots and brass vessels
Mak  And the Pharisees and the scribes put the question to him Why do your disciples not keep the rules of the fathers but take their bread with unwashed hands
Mak  And he said Well did Isaiah say of you you false ones These people give me honour with their lips but their heart is far from me
Mak  But their worship is to no purpose while they give as their teaching the rules of men
Mak  For turning away from the law of God you keep the rules of men
Mak  And he said to them Truly you put on one side the law of God so that you may keep the rules which have been handed down to you
Mak  For Moses said Give honour to your father and mother and He who says evil of father or mother let him have the punishment of death
Mak  But you say If a man says to his father or his mother That by which you might have had profit from me is Corban that is to say Given to God
Mak  You no longer let him do anything for his father or his mother
Mak  Making the word of God of no effect by your rule which you have given and a number of other such things you do
Mak  And turning to the people again he said to them Give ear to me all of you and let my words be clear to you
Mak  There is nothing outside the man which going into him is able to make him unclean but the things which come out of the man are those which make the man unclean
Mak  
Mak  And when he had gone into the house away from all the people his disciples put questions to him about the saying
Mak  And he said to them Have even you so little wisdom Do you not see that whatever goes into a man from outside is not able to make him unclean
Mak  Because it goes not into the heart but into the stomach and goes out with the waste He said this making all food clean
Mak  And he said That which comes out of the man that makes the man unclean
Mak  Because from inside from the heart of men come evil thoughts and unclean pleasures
Mak  The taking of goods and of life broken faith between husband and wife the desire of wealth wrongdoing deceit sins of the flesh an evil eye angry words pride foolish acts
Mak  All these evil things come from inside and make the man unclean
Mak  And he went away from there to the country of Tyre and Sidon And he went into a house desiring that no man might have knowledge of it and he was not able to keep it secret
