Mak  But a woman whose little daughter had an unclean spirit having had news of him came straight away and went down at his feet
Mak  Now the woman was a Greek a Syrophoenician by birth and she made a request to him that he would send the evil spirit out of her daughter
Mak  And he said to her Let the children first have their food for it is not right to take the childrens bread and give it to the dogs
Mak  But she said to him in answer Yes Lord even the dogs under the table take the bits dropped by the children
Mak  And he said to her For this saying go your way the evil spirit has gone out of your daughter
Mak  And she went away to her house and saw the child on the bed and the evil spirit gone out
Mak  And again he went out from Tyre and came through Sidon to the sea of Galilee through the country of Decapolis
Mak  And they came to him with one who had no power of hearing and had trouble in talking and they made a request to him to put his hands on him
Mak  And he took him on one side from the people privately and put his fingers into his ears and he put water from his mouth on the mans tongue with his finger
Mak  And looking up to heaven he took a deep breath and said to him Ephphatha that is Be open
Mak  And his ears became open and the band of his tongue was made loose and his words became clear
Mak  And he gave them orders not to give news of it to anyone but the more he made this request so much the more they made it public
Mak  And they were overcome with wonder saying He has done all things well he even gives back the power of hearing and the power of talking to those who have been without them
Mak  In those days again when there was a great mass of people and they had no food he made his disciples come to him and said to them
Mak  I have pity for these people because they have been with me now three days and have no food
Mak  If I send them away to their houses with no food they will be overcome by weariness on the way and some of them have come from far
Mak  And his disciples said in answer How will it be possible to get enough bread for these men here in a waste place
Mak  And he put the question How much bread have you And they said Seven cakes
Mak  And he made the people be seated on the earth and he took the seven cakes and having given praise he gave the broken bread to his disciples to put before them and they put it before the people
Mak  And they had some small fishes and blessing them he had them put before the people in the same way
Mak  And they took the food and had enough and they took up seven baskets full of the broken bits
Mak  And there were about four thousand people and he sent them away
Mak  And he got into the boat with his disciples straight away and came into the country of Dalmanutha
Mak  And the Pharisees came out and put questions to him requesting from him a sign from heaven testing him
Mak  And he was very sad in spirit and said Why is this generation looking for a sign truly I say to you No sign will be given to this generation
Mak  And he went away from them and again got into the boat and went across to the other side
Mak  And they had taken no thought to get bread and they had only one cake of bread with them in the boat
Mak  And he said to them Take care to be on the watch against the leaven of the Pharisees and the leaven of Herod
Mak  And they said to one another We have no bread
Mak  And Jesus hearing it said to them Why are you reasoning among yourselves because you have no bread do you still not see and is it still not clear to you are your hearts so hard
Mak  Having eyes do you not see and having ears have you no hearing and have you no memory
Mak  When I made a division of the five cakes of bread among the five thousand what number of baskets full of broken bits did you take up They said to him Twelve
Mak  And when the seven among the four thousand what number of baskets full of broken bits did you take up And they said to him Seven
Mak  And he said to them Is it still not clear to you
Mak  And they came to Bethsaida And they took a blind man to him requesting him to put his hands on him
Mak  And he took the blind man by the hand and went with him out of the town and when he had put water from his mouth on his eyes and put his hands on him he said Do you see anything
Mak  And looking up he said I see men I see them like trees walking
Mak  Then again he put his hands on his eyes and looking hard he was able to see and saw all things clearly
Mak  And he sent him away to his house saying Do not even go into the town
Mak  And Jesus went out with his disciples into the little towns round Caesarea Philippi and on the way he put a question to his disciples saying Who do men say that I am
Mak  And they made answer John the Baptist and others Elijah but others One of the prophets
Mak  And he said to them But who do you say I am Peter said in answer You are the Christ
Mak  And he put them under orders not to say this of him to anyone
Mak  And teaching them he said that the Son of man would have to undergo much and be hated by those in authority and the chief priests and the scribes and be put to death and after three days come back from the dead
Mak  And he said this openly And Peter took him and was protesting
Mak  But he turning about and seeing his disciples said sharply to Peter Get out of my way Satan for your mind is not on the things of God but on the things of men
Mak  And turning to the mass of people with his disciples he said to them If any man has the desire to come after me let him give up all other desires and take up his cross and come after me
Mak  Whoever has a desire to keep his life will have it taken from him and whoever gives up his life because of me and the good news will keep it
Mak  What profit has a man if he gets all the world with the loss of his life
Mak  And what would a man give in exchange for his life
Mak  Whoever has a feeling of shame because of me and my words in this false and evil generation the Son of man will have a feeling of shame because of him when he comes in the glory of his Father with the holy angels
Mak  And he said to them Truly I say to you There are some here who will have no taste of death till they see the kingdom of God come with power
Mak  And after six days Jesus took with him Peter and James and John and made them go up with him into a high mountain by themselves and he was changed in form before them
Mak  And his clothing became shining very white as no cleaner on earth would make it
Mak  And there came before them Elijah with Moses and they were talking with Jesus
Mak  And Peter said to Jesus Master it is good for us to be here and let us make three tents one for you one for Moses and one for Elijah
Mak  Because he was not certain what to say for they were in great fear
Mak  And a cloud came over them and a voice came out of the cloud saying This is my dearly loved Son give ear to him
Mak  And suddenly looking round about they saw no one any longer but Jesus only with themselves
Mak  And while they were coming down from the mountain he gave them orders not to give word to any man of the things they had seen till the Son of man had come back from the dead
Mak  And they kept the saying questioning among themselves what the coming back from the dead might be
Mak  And they put a question to him saying Why do the scribes say that Elijah has to come first
Mak  And he said to them Truly Elijah does come first and puts all things in order and how is it said in the Writings that the Son of man will go through much sorrow and be made as nothing
Mak  But I say to you that Elijah has come and they have done to him whatever they were pleased to do even as the Writings say about him
Mak  And when they came to the disciples they saw a great mass of people about them and scribes questioning them
Mak  And straight away all the people when they saw him were full of wonder and running to him gave him worship
Mak  And he said What are you questioning them about
Mak  And one of the number said to him in answer Master I came to you with my son who has in him a spirit which takes away his power of talking
Mak  And wherever it takes him it puts him down violently streaming at the lips and twisted with pain and his strength goes from him and I made a request to your disciples to send it out and they were not able
Mak  And he said to them in answer O generation without faith how long will I have to be with you how long will I put up with you let him come to me
Mak  And they took him to him and when he saw him the spirit in him straight away became violent and he went down on the earth rolling about and streaming at the lips
Mak  And Jesus questioning the father said How long has he been like this And he said From a child
Mak  And frequently it has sent him into the fire and into the water for his destruction but if you are able to do anything have pity on us and give us help
Mak  And Jesus said to him If you are able All things are possible to him who has faith
Mak  Straight away the father of the child gave a cry saying I have faith make my feeble faith stronger
Mak  And when Jesus saw that the people came running together he gave orders to the unclean spirit saying to him You spirit who are the cause of his loss of voice and hearing I say to you come out of him and never again go into him
Mak  And after crying out and shaking him violently it came out and the child became like one dead so that most of them said He is dead
Mak  But Jesus took him by the hand lifting him up and he got up
Mak  And when he had gone into the house his disciples said to him privately Why were we unable to send it out
Mak  And he said to them Nothing will make this sort come out but prayer
Mak  And they went out from there through Galilee and it was his desire that no man might have knowledge of it
Mak  For he was giving his disciples teaching and saying to them The Son of man is given up into the hands of men and they will put him to death and when he is dead after three days he will come back from the dead
Mak  But the saying was not clear to them and they were in fear of questioning him about it
Mak  And they came to Capernaum and when he was in the house he put the question to them What were you talking about on the way
Mak  But they said nothing because they had had an argument between themselves on the way about who was the greatest
Mak  And seating himself he made the twelve come to him and he said to them If any man has the desire to be first he will be last of all and servant of all
Mak  And he took a little child and put him in the middle of them and taking him in his arms he said to them
Mak  Whoever will give honour to one such little child in my name gives honour to me and whoever gives honour to me gives honour not to me but to him who sent me
Mak  John said to him Master we saw one driving out evil spirits in your name and we said that he might not because he is not one of us
Mak  But Jesus said Say not so for there is no man who will do a great work in my name and be able at the same time to say evil of me
Mak  He who is not against us is for us
Mak  Whoever gives you a cup of water because you are Christs truly I say to you he will in no way be without his reward
Mak  And whoever is a cause of trouble to one of these little ones who have faith in me it would be better for him if a great stone was put round his neck and he was dropped into the sea
Mak  And if your hand is a cause of trouble to you let it be cut off it is better for you to go into life with one hand than to have two hands and go into hell into the eternal fire
Mak  
Mak  And if your foot is a cause of trouble to you let it be cut off it is better for you to go into life with one foot than to have two feet and go into hell
Mak  
Mak  And if your eye is a cause of trouble to you take it out it is better for you to go into the kingdom of God with one eye than having two eyes to go into hell
Mak  Where their worm is ever living and the fire is not put out
Mak  Everyone will be salted with fire
Mak  Salt is good but if the taste goes from it how will you make it salt again Have salt in yourselves and be at peace one with another
Mak  And he got up and went into the country of Judaea on the other side of Jordan and great numbers of people came together to him again and as was his way he gave them teaching
Mak  And Pharisees came to him testing him with the question Is it right for a man to put away his wife
Mak  And he said to them in answer What did Moses say you were to do
Mak  And they said to him Moses let us give her a statement in writing and be free from her
Mak  But Jesus said to them Because of your hard hearts he gave you this law
Mak  But from the first male and female made he them
Mak  For this cause will a man go away from his father and mother and be joined to his wife
Mak  And the two will become one flesh so that they are no longer two but one flesh
Mak  Let not that which has been joined together by God be parted by man
Mak  And in the house the disciples put questions to him again about this thing
Mak  And he said to them Whoever puts away his wife and takes another is false to his wife
Mak  And if she herself puts away her husband and takes another she is false to her husband
Mak  And they took to him little children so that he might put his hands on them and the disciples said sharp words to them
Mak  And when Jesus saw it he was angry and said to them Let the little children come to me and do not keep them away for of such is the kingdom of God
Mak  Truly I say to you Whoever does not put himself under the kingdom of God like a little child will not come into it at all
Mak  And he took them in his arms and gave them a blessing putting his hands on them
Mak  And while he was going out into the way a man came running to him and went down on his knees saying Good Master what have I to do so that I may have eternal life
Mak  And Jesus said to him Why do you say I am good no one is good but one and that is God
Mak  You have knowledge of what is said in the law Do not put any one to death Do not be untrue in married life Do not take what is not yours Do not give false witness Do not get money by deceit Give honour to your father and mother
Mak  And he said to him Master all these laws I have kept from the time when I was young
Mak  And Jesus looking on him and loving him said There is one thing needed go get money for your goods and give it to the poor and you will have wealth in heaven and come with me
Mak  But his face became sad at the saying and he went away sorrowing for he was one who had much property
Mak  And Jesus looking round about said to his disciples How hard it is for those who have wealth to come into the kingdom of God
Mak  And the disciples were full of wonder at his words But Jesus said to them again Children how hard it is for those who put faith in wealth to come into the kingdom of God
Mak  It is simpler for a camel to go through a needles eye than for a man of wealth to come into the kingdom of God
Mak  And they were greatly surprised saying to him Who then may have salvation
Mak  Jesus looking on them said With men it is impossible but not with God for all things are possible with God
Mak  Peter said to him See we have given up everything and come after you
Mak  Jesus said Truly I say to you There is no man who has given up house or brothers or sisters or mother or father or children or land because of me and the good news
Mak  Who will not get a hundred times as much now in this time houses and brothers and sisters and mothers and children and landthough with great troubles and in the world to come eternal life
Mak  But a great number who are first will be last and those who are last will be first
Mak  And they were on the way going up to Jerusalem and Jesus was going before them and they were full of wonder but those who came after him were in fear And again he took the twelve and gave them word of the things which were to come on him
Mak  Saying See we go up to Jerusalem and the Son of man will be given up to the chief priests and the scribes and they will give an order for his death and will give him up to the Gentiles
Mak  And they will make sport of him and put shame on him and give him cruel blows and will put him to death and after three days he will come back from the dead
Mak  And there came to him James and John the sons of Zebedee saying to him Master will you give us whatever may be our request
Mak  And he said to them What would you have me do for you
Mak  And they said to him Let us be seated one at your right hand and one at your left in your glory
Mak  But Jesus said to them You have no knowledge of what you are saying Are you able to take of my cup or to undergo the baptism which I am to undergo
Mak  And they said to him We are able And Jesus said to them You will take of the cup from which I take and the baptism which I am about to undergo you will undergo
Mak  But to be seated at my right hand or at my left is not for me to give but it is for those for whom it has been made ready
Mak  And hearing this the ten became very angry with James and John
Mak  And Jesus made them come to him and said to them You see that those who are made rulers over the Gentiles are lords over them and their great ones have authority over them
Mak  But it is not so among you but whoever has a desire to become great among you let him be your servant
Mak  And whoever has a desire to be first among you let him be servant of all
Mak  For truly the Son of man did not come to have servants but to be a servant and to give his life for the salvation of men
Mak  And they came to Jericho and when he was going out of Jericho with his disciples and a great number of people the son of Timaeus Bartimaeus a blind man was seated by the wayside with his hand out for money
Mak  And when it came to his ears that it was Jesus of Nazareth he gave a cry and said Jesus Son of David have mercy on me
Mak  And some of them turning in protest gave him an order to be quiet but he went on crying out all the more Son of David have mercy on me
Mak  And Jesus came to a stop and said Let him come And crying out to the blind man they said to him Be comforted come he has sent for you
Mak  And he putting off his coat got up quickly and came to Jesus
Mak  And Jesus said to him What would you have me do to you And the blind man said Master make me able to see
Mak  And Jesus said to him Go on your way your faith has made you well And straight away he was able to see and went after him in the way
Mak  And when they came near to Jerusalem to Bethphage and Bethany at the Mountain of Olives he sent two of his disciples
Mak  And said to them Go into the little town opposite and when you come to it you will see a young ass with a cord round his neck on which no man has ever been seated let him loose and come back with him
Mak  And if anyone says to you Why are you doing this say The Lord has need of him and will send him back straight away
Mak  And they went away and saw a young ass by the door outside in the open street and they were getting him loose
Mak  And some of those who were there said to them What are you doing taking the ass
Mak  And they said to them the words which Jesus had said and they let them go
Mak  And they took the young ass to Jesus and put their clothing on him and he got on his back
Mak  And a great number put down their clothing in the way and others put down branches which they had taken from the fields
Mak  And those who went in front and those who came after were crying Glory A blessing on him who comes in the name of the Lord
Mak  A blessing on the coming kingdom of our father David Glory in the highest
Mak  And he went into Jerusalem into the Temple and after looking round about on all things it being now evening he went out to Bethany with the twelve
Mak  And on the day after when they had come out from Bethany he was in need of food
Mak  And seeing a figtree in the distance with leaves he went to see if by chance it had anything on it and when he came to it he saw nothing but leaves for it was not the time for the fruit
Mak  And he said to it Let no man take fruit from you for ever And his disciples took note of his words
Mak  And they came to Jerusalem and he went into the Temple and sent out those who were trading there overturning the tables of the moneychangers and the seats of those who were offering doves for money
Mak  And he would not let any man take a vessel through the Temple
Mak  And he gave them teaching and said to them Is it not in the Writings My house is to be named a house of prayer for all the nations but you have made it a hole of thieves
Mak  And it came to the ears of the chief priests and scribes and they took thought how they might put him to death being in fear of him because all the people were full of wonder at his teaching
Mak  And every evening he went out of the town
Mak  And when they were going by in the morning they saw the figtree dead from the roots
Mak  And Peter having a memory of it said to him Master see the tree which was cursed by you is dead
Mak  And Jesus answering said to them Have Gods faith
Mak  Truly I say to you Whoever says to this mountain Be taken up and be put into the sea and has no doubt in his heart but has faith that what he says will come about he will have his desire
Mak  For this reason I say to you Whatever you make a request for in prayer have faith that it has been given to you and you will have it
Mak  And whenever you make a prayer let there be forgiveness in your hearts if you have anything against anyone so that you may have forgiveness for your sins from your Father who is in heaven
Mak  
Mak  And they came again to Jerusalem and while he was walking in the Temple there came to him the chief priests and the scribes and those in authority
Mak  And they said to him By what authority do you do these things or who gave you authority to do these things
Mak  And Jesus said to them I will put to you one question give me an answer and I will say by what authority I do these things
Mak  The baptism of John was it from heaven or from men give me an answer
Mak  And they gave thought to it among themselves saying If we say From heaven he will say Why then did you not have faith in him
Mak  But if we say From menthey were in fear of the people because all took John to be truly a prophet
Mak  And they said in answer to Jesus We have no idea And Jesus said to them And I will not say to you by what authority I do these things
Mak  And he gave them teaching in the form of stories A man had a vinegarden planted and put a wall about it and made a place for crushing out the wine and put up a tower and let it out to fieldworkers and went into another country
Mak  And when the time came he sent a servant to get from the workmen some of the fruit of the garden
Mak  And they took him and gave him blows and sent him away with nothing
Mak  And again he sent to them another servant and they gave him wounds on the head and were very cruel to him
Mak  And he sent another and they put him to death and a number of others whipping some and putting some to death
Mak  He still had one a dearly loved son he sent him last to them saying They will have respect for my son
Mak  But those workmen said among themselves This is he who will one day be the owner of the property come let us put him to death and the heritage will be ours
Mak  And they took him and put him to death pushing his body out of the garden
Mak  What then will the master of the garden do He will come and put the workmen to death and will give the garden into the hands of others
Mak  Have you not seen this which is in the Writings The stone which the builders put on one side the same was made the chief stone of the building
Mak  This was the Lords doing and it is a wonder in our eyes
Mak  And they made attempts to take him but they were in fear of the people because they saw that the story was against them and they went away from him
Mak  Then they sent to him certain of the Pharisees and the Herodians so that they might make use of his words to take him by a trick
Mak  And when they had come they said to him Master we are certain that you are true and have no fear of anyone you have no respect for a mans position but you are teaching the true way of God Is it right to give taxes to Caesar or not
Mak  Are we to give or not to give But he conscious of their false hearts said to them Why do you put me to the test give me a penny so that I may see it
Mak  And they gave him one And he said to them Whose is this image and name on it And they said to him Caesars
Mak  And Jesus said to them Give to Caesar the things which are Caesars and to God the things which are Gods And they were full of wonder at him
Mak  And there came to him Sadducees who say there is no coming back from the dead and they put a question to him saying
Mak  Master in the law Moses says If a mans brother comes to his end and has a wife still living and no child it is right for his brother to take his wife and get a family for his brother
Mak  There were seven brothers and the first took a wife and at his death there were no offspring
Mak  And the second took her and at his death there were no offspring and the third the same
Mak  And all the seven had no seed Last of all the woman herself came to her death
Mak  In the future life when they come back from the dead whose wife will she be for the seven had her for a wife
Mak  Jesus said to them Is not this the reason for your error that you have no knowledge of the holy Writings or of the power of God
Mak  When they come back from the dead they do not get married but are like the angels in heaven
Mak  But as to the dead coming back to life have you not seen in the book of Moses about the burning thorntree how God said to him I am the God of Abraham and the God of Isaac and the God of Jacob
Mak  He is not the God of the dead but of the living you are greatly in error
Mak  And one of the scribes came and hearing their argument together and seeing that he had given them a good answer put the question to him Which law is the first of all
Mak  Jesus said in answer The first is Give ear O Israel The Lord our God is one Lord
Mak  And you are to have love for the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind and with all your strength
Mak  The second is this Have love for your neighbour as for yourself There is no other law greater than these
Mak  And the scribe said to him Truly Master you have well said that he is one and there is no other but he
Mak  And to have love for him with all the heart and with all the mind and with all the strength and to have the same love for his neighbour as for himself is much more than all forms of offerings
Mak  And when Jesus saw that he gave a wise answer he said to him You are not far from the kingdom of God And every man after that was in fear of questioning him any more
Mak  And Jesus when he was teaching in the Temple said How do the scribes say that the Christ is the Son of David
Mak  David himself said in the Holy Spirit The Lord said to my Lord Be seated at my right hand till I put those who are against you under your feet
Mak  David himself gives him the name of Lord and how then is he his son And the common people gave ear to him gladly
Mak  And in his teaching he said Be on your watch against the scribes whose pleasure it is to go about in long robes and be respected in the marketplaces
Mak  And to have the chief seats in the Synagogues and the first places at feasts
Mak  Who take away the property of widows and before the eyes of men make long prayers these will be judged more hardly
Mak  And he took a seat by the place where the money was kept and saw how the people put money into the boxes and a number who had wealth put in much
Mak  And there came a poor widow and she put in two little bits of money which make a farthing
Mak  And he made his disciples come to him and said to them Truly I say to you This poor widow has put in more than all those who are putting money into the box
Mak  Because they all put in something out of what they had no need for but she out of her need put in all she had even all her living
Mak  And when he was going out of the Temple one of his disciples said to him Master see what stones and what buildings
Mak  And Jesus said to him Do you see these great buildings there is not one stone here resting on another which will not be overturned
Mak  And while he was seated on the Mountain of Olives opposite the Temple Peter and James and John and Andrew said to him privately
Mak  Say when these things will be and what will be the sign when these things are all about to be done
Mak  And Jesus said to them Take care that you are not tricked by anyone
Mak  People will come in my name saying I am he and a number will be turned from the true way
Mak  And when you have news of wars and talk of wars do not be troubled these things have to be but it is still not the end
Mak  Nation will go to war with nation and kingdom with kingdom there will be earthshocks in different places there will be times when there is no food these things are the first of the troubles
Mak  But take care for they will give you up to the Sanhedrins and in Synagogues you will be whipped and you will be taken before rulers and kings because of me for a sign to them
Mak  And the good news has first to be given to all the nations
Mak  And when you are taken and given up to be judged do not be troubled about what to say but whatever is given to you in that hour say because it is not you who say it but the Holy Spirit
Mak  And brother will give up brother to death and the father his child and children will go against their fathers and mothers and put them to death
Mak  And you will be hated by all men because of my name but he who goes through to the end will have salvation
Mak  But when you see the unclean thing which makes destruction in the place where it has no right to be let this be clear to the reader then let those who are in Judaea go quickly to the mountains
Mak  And let him who is on the housetop not go down or go in to take anything out of his house
Mak  And let not him who is in the field go back to take his coat
Mak  And it will be hard for women who are with child and for her who has a baby at the breast in those days
Mak  And say a prayer that it may not be in the winter
Mak  For in those days there will be sorrow such as there has not been from the time when God made the world till now and will not ever be again
Mak  And if the Lord had not made the time short no flesh would have been kept from destruction but because of the saints he has made the time short
Mak  And then if any man says to you See here is Christ or See there have no faith in it
Mak  Because there will be false Christs and false prophets and they will give signs and wonders in the hope of turning even the saints from the true way
Mak  But take care see I have made all things clear to you before the time
Mak  But in those days after that time of trouble the sun will be made dark and the moon will not give her light
Mak  And the stars will be falling from heaven and the powers which are in the heavens will be moved
Mak  And then they will see the Son of man coming in clouds with great power and glory
Mak  And then he will send out the angels and will get together his saints from the four winds from the farthest part of the earth to the farthest part of heaven
Mak  Take an example from the figtree when its branches become soft and put out their leaves you see that the summer is near
Mak  Even so when you see these things taking place you may be certain that he is near even at the doors
Mak  Truly I say to you This generation will not come to an end till all these things are complete
Mak  Heaven and earth will come to an end but my words will not come to an end
Mak  But of that day or that hour no one has knowledge not even the angels in heaven or the Son but the Father
Mak  Take care keep watch with prayer for you are not certain when the time will be
Mak  It is as when a man who is in another country for a time having gone away from his house and given authority to his servants and to everyone his work gives the porter an order to keep watch
Mak  So you are to keep watch because you are not certain when the master of the house is coming in the evening or in the middle of the night or at the cocks cry or in the morning
Mak  For fear that coming suddenly he sees you sleeping
Mak  And what I say to you I say to all Keep watch
Mak  It was now two days before the feast of the Passover and the unleavened bread and the chief priests and the scribes made designs how they might take him by deceit and put him to death
Mak  But they said Not while the feast is going on for fear there may be trouble among the people
Mak  And while he was in Bethany in the house of Simon the leper seated at table there came a woman with a bottle of perfumed oil of great price and when the bottle was broken she put the perfume on his head
Mak  But some of them were angry among themselves saying For what purpose has this oil been wasted
Mak  We might have got more than three hundred pence for it and given the money to the poor And they said things against her among themselves
Mak  But Jesus said Let her be why are you troubling her she has done a kind act to me
Mak  The poor you have ever with you and whenever you have the desire you may do them good but me you have not for ever
Mak  She has done what she was able she has put oil on my body to make it ready for its last restingplace
Mak  And truly I say to you Wherever the good news goes out through all the earth what this woman has done will be talked of in memory of her
Mak  And Judas Iscariot who was one of the twelve went away to the chief priests so that he might give him up to them
Mak  And hearing what he said they were glad and gave him their word to make him a payment of money And he took thought how he might best give him up to them
Mak  And on the first day of unleavened bread when the Passover lamb is put to death his disciples said to him Where are we to go and make ready for you to take the Passover meal
Mak  And he sent two of his disciples and said to them Go into the town and there will come to you a man with a vessel of water go after him
Mak  And wherever he goes in say to the owner of the house The Master says Where is my guestroom where I may take the Passover with my disciples
Mak  And he will take you up himself to a great room with a table and seats there make ready for us
Mak  And the disciples went out and came into the town and saw that it was as he had said and they made ready the Passover
Mak  And when it was evening he came with the twelve
Mak  And while they were seated taking food Jesus said Truly I say to you One of you will be false to me one who is taking food with me
Mak  They were sad and said to him one by one Is it I
Mak  And he said to them It is one of the twelve one who is putting his bread with me into the same plate
Mak  The Son of man goes even as the Writings say of him but cursed is that man through whom the Son of man is given up It would have been well for that man if he had never been given birth
Mak  And while they were taking food he took bread and after blessing it he gave the broken bread to them and said Take it this is my body
Mak  And he took a cup and when he had given praise he gave it to them and they all had a drink from it
Mak  And he said to them This is my blood of the testament which is given for men
Mak  Truly I say to you I will take no more of the fruit of the vine till the day when I take it new in the kingdom of God
Mak  And after a song of praise to God they went out to the Mountain of Olives
Mak  And Jesus said to them You will all be turned away from me for it is in the Writings I will put the keeper of the sheep to death and the sheep will be put to flight
Mak  But after I have come back from the dead I will go before you into Galilee
Mak  But Peter said to him Though the others may be turned away from you I will not
Mak  And Jesus said to him Truly I say to you that you today even this night before the cocks second cry will say three times that you have no knowledge of me
Mak  But he said with passion If I have to be put to death with you I will not be false to you And they all said the same
Mak  And they came to a place which was named Gethsemane and he said to his disciples Be seated here while I say a prayer
Mak  And he took with him Peter and James and John and grief and great trouble came on him
Mak  And he said to them My soul is very sad even to death be here a little time and keep watch
Mak  And he went forward a little and falling down on the earth made request that if possible the hour might go from him
Mak  And he said Abba Father all things are possible to you take away this cup from me but even so let not my pleasure but yours be done
Mak  And he came and saw them sleeping and said to Peter Simon are you sleeping were you not able to keep watch one hour
Mak  Keep watch with prayer so that you may not be put to the test the spirit truly is ready but the flesh is feeble
Mak  And again he went away and said a prayer using the same words
Mak  And again he came and saw them sleeping because their eyes were very tired and they had nothing to say in answer
Mak  And he came the third time and said to them Go on sleeping now and take your rest it is enough the hour has come see the Son of man is given up into the hands of evil men
Mak  Get up let us be going see he who gives me up is near
Mak  And straight away while he was still talking Judas one of the twelve came and with him a great band with swords and sticks from the chief priests and the scribes and those in authority
Mak  Now he who had been false to him had given them a sign saying The one to whom I give a kiss that is he take him and get him away safely
Mak  And when he had come he went straight to him and said Master and gave him a kiss
Mak  And they put their hands on him and took him
Mak  But a certain one of those who were near took out his sword and gave the servant of the high priest a blow cutting off his ear
Mak  And Jesus said to them Have you come out as against a thief with swords and sticks to take me
Mak  I was with you every day in the Temple teaching and you did not take me but this is done so that the Writings may come true
Mak  And they all went away from him in fear
Mak  And a certain young man went after him with only a linen cloth about his body and they put their hands on him
Mak  But he got away unclothed without the linen cloth
Mak  And they took Jesus away to the high priest and there came together with him all the chief priests and those in authority and the scribes
Mak  And Peter had come after him at a distance even into the house of the high priest and he was seated with the captains warming himself in the light of the fire
Mak  Now the chief priests and all the Sanhedrin were looking for witness against Jesus so that they might put him to death and they were unable to get any
Mak  For a number gave false witness against him and their witness was not in agreement
Mak  Then some got up and gave false witness against him saying
Mak  He said in our hearing I will put an end to this Temple which is made with hands and in three days I will make another without hands
Mak  And even so their witness was not in agreement
Mak  And the high priest got up in the middle of them and said to Jesus Do you say nothing in answer what is it which these say against you
Mak  But he kept quiet and said nothing Again the high priest questioning him said Are you the Christ the son of the Holy One
Mak  And Jesus said I am and you will see the Son of man seated at the right hand of power and coming with the clouds of heaven
Mak  And the high priest violently parting his robes said What more need have we of witnesses
Mak  His words against God have come to your ears what is your opinion And they all said it was right for him to be put to death
Mak  And some put shame on him and covering his face gave him blows and said to him Now say what is to come and the captains took him and gave him blows with their hands
Mak  And while Peter was down in the open square of the building one of the servantgirls of the high priest came
Mak  And seeing Peter warming himself by the fire she gave him a look and said You were with this Nazarene even Jesus
Mak  But he said I have no knowledge of him or of what you are saying and he went out into the doorway and there came the cry of a cock
Mak  And the girl saw him and said again to those who were near This is one of them
Mak  But again he said it was not so And after a little time again those who were near said to Peter Truly you are one of them for you are a Galilaean
Mak  But with curses and oaths he said I have no knowledge of the man about whom you are talking
Mak  And in the same minute the cock gave a second cry And it came to Peters mind how Jesus had said to him Before the cocks second cry you will say three times that you have no knowledge of me And at this thought he was overcome with weeping
Mak  And the first thing in the morning the chief priests with those in authority and the scribes and all the Sanhedrin had a meeting and put cords round Jesus and took him away and gave him up to Pilate
Mak  And Pilate put a question to him Are you the King of the Jews And he answering said to him You say so
Mak  And the chief priests said a number of things against him
Mak  And Pilate again put a question Do you say nothing in answer see how much evil they say you have done
Mak  But Jesus gave no more answers so that Pilate was full of wonder
Mak  Now at the feast every year he let one prisoner go free at their request
Mak  And there was one named Barabbas in prison with those who had gone against the government and in the fight had taken life
Mak  And the people went up requesting him to do as he had done for them in other years
Mak  And Pilate said in answer to them Is it your desire that I let the King of the Jews go free
Mak  For he saw that the chief priests had given him up through envy
Mak  But the people were moved by the chief priests to make him let Barabbas go free
Mak  And Pilate again said in answer to them What then am I to do to him to whom you give the name of the King of the Jews
Mak  And they said again loudly To the cross with him
Mak  And Pilate said to them Why what evil has he done But their cry was the louder To the cross
Mak  And Pilate desiring to do what was pleasing to the people let Barabbas go free and gave up Jesus when he had been whipped to be put to death on the cross
Mak  And the men of the army took him away into the square in front of the building which is the Praetorium and they got together all the band
Mak  And they put a purple robe on him and twisting a crown of thorns they put it on him
Mak  And as if honouring him they said Long life to the King of the Jews
Mak  And they gave him blows on the head with a stick and put shame on him and going down on their knees gave him worship
Mak  And when they had made sport of him they took the purple robe off him and put his clothing on him And they took him out to put him to death on the cross
Mak  And they made one Simon of Cyrene the father of Alexander and Rufus who was going by coming from the country go with them so that he might take his cross
Mak  And they took him to the place named Golgotha which is Dead Mans Head
Mak  And they gave him wine mixed with myrrh but he did not take it
Mak  And he was nailed to the cross and they made a division of his clothing among them putting to the decision of chance what everyone was to take
Mak  And it was the third hour when they put him on the cross
Mak  And the statement of his crime was put in writing on the cross THE KING OF THE JEWS
Mak  And they put two thieves on crosses with him one on his right side and one on his left
Mak  
Mak  And those who went by made sport of him shaking their heads and saying Ha you who give the Temple to destruction and put it up again in three days
Mak  Keep yourself from death and come down from the cross
Mak  In the same way the chief priests laughing at him among themselves with the scribes said A saviour of others he has no salvation for himself
Mak  Let the Christ the King of Israel come down now from the cross so that we may see and have belief And those who were put on crosses with him said evil things against him
Mak  And when the sixth hour had come it was dark over all the land till the ninth hour
Mak  And at the ninth hour Jesus said in a loud voice Eloi Eloi lama sabachthani which is My God my God why are you turned away from me
Mak  And some of those who were near hearing it said See he is crying to Elijah
Mak  And one of them went quickly and getting a sponge full of bitter wine put it on a rod and gave it to him for drink saying Let be let us see if Elijah will come to take him down
Mak  And Jesus gave a loud cry and gave up his spirit
Mak  And the curtain of the Temple was parted in two from end to end
Mak  And when the captain who was near saw how he gave up his spirit he said Truly this man was a son of God
Mak  And there were women watching from a distance among them were Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of James the less and of Joses and Salome
Mak  Who went with him when he was in Galilee and took care of him and a number of other women who came up with him to Jerusalem
Mak  And when it was evening because it was the time of getting ready that is the day before the Sabbath
Mak  There came Joseph of Arimathaea a responsible man in high honour who was himself waiting for the kingdom of God and he went in to Pilate without fear and made a request for the body of Jesus
Mak  And Pilate was surprised that he was dead and sending for the captain he put a question to see if he had been dead for long
Mak  And when he had news of it from the captain he let Joseph have the body
Mak  And he got a linen cloth and taking him down put the linen cloth round him and put him in a place for the dead which had been cut out of a rock and a stone was rolled against the door
Mak  And Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of Joses saw where he was put
Mak  And when the Sabbath was past Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of James and Salome got spices so that they might come and put them on him
Mak  And very early after dawn on the first day of the week they came at the time of the coming up of the sun to the place where the body had been put
Mak  And they were saying among themselves Who will get the stone rolled away from the door for us
Mak  And looking up they saw that the stone was rolled back and it was of great size
Mak  And when they went in they saw a young man seated on the right side dressed in a white robe and they were full of wonder
Mak  And he said to them Do not be troubled you are looking for Jesus the Nazarene who has been put to death on the cross he has come back from the dead he is not here see the place where they put him
Mak  But go say to his disciples and to Peter He goes before you into Galilee there you will see him as he said to you
Mak  And they went out quickly from the place because fear and great wonder had come on them and they said nothing to anyone because they were full of fear that 
Mak  Now when he came back from the dead early on the first day of the week he went first to Mary Magdalene from whom he had sent out seven evil spirits
Mak  She went and gave news of it to those who had been with him while they were sorrowing and weeping
Mak  And they when it came to their ears that he was living and had been seen by her had no belief in it
Mak  And after these things he was seen in another form by two of them while they were walking on their way into the country
Mak  And they went away and gave news of it to the rest and they had no belief in what was said
Mak  And later he was seen by the eleven themselves while they were taking food and he said sharp words to them because they had no faith and their hearts were hard and because they had no belief in those who had seen him after he had come back from the dead
Mak  And he said to them Go into all the world and give the good news to everyone
Mak  He who has faith and is given baptism will get salvation but he who has not faith will be judged
Mak  And these signs will be with those who have faith in my name they will send out evil spirits and they will make use of new languages
Mak  They will take up snakes and if there is poison in their drink it will do them no evil they will put their hands on those who are ill and they will get well
Mak  So then the Lord Jesus after he had said these words to them was taken up into heaven and took his seat at the right hand of God
Mak  And they went out preaching everywhere the Lord working with them and giving witness to the word by the signs which came after So be it
Luk  As a number of attempts have been made to put together in order an account of those events which took place among us
Luk  As they were handed down to us by those who saw them from the first and were preachers of the word
Luk  It seemed good to me having made observation with great care of the direction of events in their order to put the facts in writing for you most noble Theophilus
Luk  So that you might have certain knowledge of those things about which you were given teaching
Luk  In the days of Herod king of Judaea there was a certain priest by name Zacharias of the order of Abijah and he had a wife of the family of Aaron and her name was Elisabeth
Luk  They were upright in the eyes of God keeping all the rules and orders of God and doing no wrong
Luk  And they were without children because Elisabeth had never given birth and they were at that time very old
Luk  Now it came about that in his turn he was acting as priest before God
Luk  And as was the way of the priests he had to go into the Temple to see to the burning of perfumes
Luk  And all the people were offering prayers outside at the time of the burning of perfumes
Luk  And he saw an angel of the Lord in his place on the right side of the altar
Luk  And Zacharias was troubled when he saw him and fear came on him
Luk  But the angel said Have no fear Zacharias for your prayer has come to the ears of God and your wife Elisabeth will have a son and his name will be John
Luk  And you will be glad and have great delight and numbers of people will have joy at his birth
Luk  For he will be great in the eyes of the Lord he will not take wine or strong drink and he will be full of the Spirit of God from his birth
Luk  And through him great numbers of the children of Israel will be turned to the Lord their God
Luk  And he will go before his face in the spirit and power of Elijah turning the hearts of fathers to their children and wrongdoers to the way of righteousness to make ready a people whose hearts have been turned to the Lord
Luk  And Zacharias said to the angel How may I be certain of this For I am an old man and my wife is far on in years
Luk  And the angel answering said I am Gabriel whose place is before God I have been sent to say these words to you and to give you this good news
Luk  Now see you will be without voice or language till the day when these things come about because you had not faith in my words which will have effect at the right time
Luk  And the people were waiting for Zacharias and were surprised because he was in the Temple for such a long time
Luk  And when he came out he was not able to say anything and they saw that he had seen a vision in the Temple and he was making signs to them without words
Luk  And when the days of his work in the Temple were ended he went back to his house
Luk  After that time Elisabeth being certain that she was to become a mother kept herself from mens eyes for five months saying
Luk  The Lord has done this to me for his eyes were on me to take away my shame in the eyes of men
Luk  Now in the sixth month the angel Gabriel was sent from God to a town in Galilee named Nazareth
Luk  To a virgin who was to be married to a man named Joseph of the family of David and the name of the virgin was Mary
Luk  And the angel came in to her and said Peace be with you to whom special grace has been given the Lord is with you
Luk  But she was greatly troubled at his words and said to herself What may be the purpose of these words
Luk  And the angel said to her Have no fear Mary for you have Gods approval
Luk  And see you will give birth to a son and his name will be Jesus
Luk  He will be great and will be named the Son of the Most High and the Lord God will give him the kingdom of David his father
Luk  He will have rule over the house of Jacob for ever and of his kingdom there will be no end
Luk  And Mary said to the angel How may this be because I have had no knowledge of a man
Luk  And the angel in answer said to her The Holy Spirit will come on you and the power of the Most High will come to rest on you and so that which will come to birth will be named holy Son of God
Luk  Even now Elisabeth who is of your family is to be a mother though she is old and this is the sixth month with her who was without children
Luk  For there is nothing which God is not able to do
Luk  And Mary said I am the servant of the Lord may it be to me as you say And the angel went away
Luk  Then Mary got up and went quickly into the high lands to a town of Judah
Luk  And went into the house of Zacharias and took Elisabeth in her arms
Luk  And when the voice of Mary came to the ears of Elisabeth the baby made a sudden move inside her then Elisabeth was full of the Holy Spirit
Luk  And she said with a loud voice May blessing be on you among women and a blessing on the child of your body
Luk  How is it that the mother of my Lord comes to me
Luk  For truly when the sound of your voice came to my ears the baby in my body made a sudden move for joy
Luk  Happy will she be who had faith that the things which the Lord has said to her will be done
Luk  And Mary said My soul gives glory to God
Luk  My spirit is glad in God my Saviour
Luk  For he has had pity on his servant though she is poor and lowly placed and from this hour will all generations give witness to the blessing which has come to me
Luk  For he who is strong has done great things for me and holy is his name
Luk  His mercy is for all generations in whom is the fear of him
Luk  With his arm he has done acts of power he has put to flight those who have pride in their hearts
Luk  He has put down kings from their seats lifting up on high the men of low degree
Luk  Those who had no food he made full of good things the men of wealth he sent away with nothing in their hands
Luk  His help he has given to Israel his servant so that he might keep in mind his mercy to Abraham and his seed for ever
Luk  As he gave his word to our fathers
Luk  And Mary was with her for about three months and then went back to her house
Luk  Now it was time for Elisabeth to give birth and she had a son
Luk  And it came to the ears of her neighbours and relations that the Lord had been very good to her and they took part in her joy
Luk  And on the eighth day they came to see to the circumcision of the child and they would have given him the name of Zacharias his fathers name
Luk  But his mother made answer and said No his name is John
Luk  And they said Not one of your relations has that name
Luk  And they made signs to his father to say what name was to be given to him
Luk  And he sent for writing materials and put down His name is John and they were all surprised
Luk  And straight away his mouth was open and his tongue was free and he gave praise to God
Luk  And fear came on all those who were living round about them and there was much talk about all these things in all the hillcountry of Judaea
Luk  And all who had word of them kept them in their minds and said What will this child be For the hand of the Lord was with him
Luk  And his father Zacharias was full of the Holy Spirit and with the voice of a prophet said these words
Luk  Praise be to the Lord the God of Israel for he has come to his people and made them free
Luk  Lifting up a horn of salvation for us in the house of his servant David
Luk  As he said by the mouth of his holy prophets from the earliest times
Luk  Salvation from those who are against us and from the hands of those who have hate for us
Luk  To do acts of mercy to our fathers and to keep in mind his holy word
Luk  The oath which he made to Abraham our father
Luk  That we being made free from the fear of those who are against us might give him worship
Luk  In righteousness and holy living before him all our days
Luk  And you child will be named the prophet of the Most High you will go before the face of the Lord to make ready his ways
Luk  To give knowledge of salvation to his people through the forgiveness of sins
Luk  Because of the loving mercies of our God by which the dawn from heaven has come to us
Luk  To give light to those in dark places and in the shade of death so that our feet may be guided into the way of peace
Luk  And the child became tall and strong in spirit and he was living in the waste land till the day when he came before the eyes of Israel
Luk  Now it came about in those days that an order went out from Caesar Augustus that there was to be a numbering of all the world
Luk  This was the first numbering which was made when Quirinius was ruler of Syria
Luk  And all men went to be numbered everyone to his town
Luk  And Joseph went up from Galilee out of the town of Nazareth into Judaea to Bethlehem the town of David because he was of the house and family of David
Luk  To be put on the list with Mary his future wife who was about to become a mother
Luk  And while they were there the time came for her to give birth
Luk  And she had her first son and folding him in linen she put him to rest in the place where the cattle had their food because there was no room for them in the house
Luk  And in the same country there were keepers of sheep in the fields watching over their flock by night
Luk  And an angel of the Lord came to them and the glory of the Lord was shining round about them and fear came on them
Luk  And the angel said Have no fear for truly I give you good news of great joy which will be for all the people
Luk  For on this day in the town of David a Saviour has come to birth who is Christ the Lord
Luk  And this is the sign to you you will see a young child folded in linen in the place where the cattle have their food
Luk  And suddenly there was with the angel a great band of spirits from heaven giving praise to God and saying
Luk  Glory to God in the highest and on the earth peace among men with whom he is well pleased
Luk  And when the angels had gone away from them into heaven the keepers of the sheep said to one another Let us go now to Bethlehem and see this thing which has come about which the Lord has made clear to us
Luk  And they came quickly and saw Mary and Joseph and the child in the place where the cattle had their food
Luk  And when they saw it they gave them an account of the things which had been said to them about the child
Luk  And all those to whose ears it came were full of wonder at the things said by the keepers of the sheep
Luk  But Mary kept all these words in her heart and gave much thought to them
Luk  Then the keepers of the sheep went back giving glory and praise to God for all the things which had come to their ears and which they had seen as it had been said to them
Luk  And when after eight days the time came for his circumcision he was named Jesus the name which the angel had given to him before his birth
Luk  And when the necessary days for making them clean by the law of Moses had come to an end they took him to Jerusalem to give him to the Lord
Luk  As it says in the law of the Lord Every mothers first male child is to be holy to the Lord
Luk  And to make an offering as it is ordered in the law of the Lord of two doves or other young birds
Luk  And there was then in Jerusalem a man whose name was Simeon and he was an upright man fearing God and waiting for the comfort of Israel and the Holy Spirit was on him
Luk  And he had knowledge through the Holy Spirit that he would not see death till he had seen the Lords Christ
Luk  And full of the Spirit he came into the Temple and when the father and mother came in with the child Jesus to do with him what was ordered by the law
Luk  Then he took him in his arms and gave praise to God and said
Luk  Now you are letting your servant go in peace O Lord as you have said
Luk  For my eyes have seen your salvation
Luk  Which you have made ready before the face of all nations
Luk  A light of revelation to the Gentiles and the glory of your people Israel
Luk  And his father and mother were full of wonder at the things which were said about him
Luk  And Simeon gave them his blessing and said to Mary his mother See this child will be the cause of the downfall and the lifting up of great numbers of people in Israel and he will be a sign against which hard words will be said
Luk  And a sword will go through your heart so that the secret thoughts of men may come to light
Luk  And there was one Anna a woman prophet the daughter of Phanuel of the family of Asher she was very old and after seven years of married life
Luk  She had been a widow for eightyfour years she was in the Temple at all times worshipping with prayers and going without food night and day
Luk  And coming up at that time she gave praise to God talking of him to all those who were waiting for the freeing of Jerusalem
Luk  And when they had done all the things which were ordered by the law of the Lord they went back to Galilee to Nazareth the town where they were living
Luk  And the child became tall and strong and full of wisdom and the grace of God was on him
Luk  And every year his father and mother went to Jerusalem at the feast of the Passover
Luk  And when he was twelve years old they went up as their way was to the feast
Luk  And when the days of the feast came to an end and they were going back the boy Jesus was still in Jerusalem but they had no knowledge of it
Luk  And in the belief that he was with some of their number they went a days journey and after looking for him among their relations and friends
Luk  And seeing that he was not there they went back to Jerusalem to make search for him
Luk  And after three days they came across him in the Temple seated among the wise men giving ear to their words and putting questions to them
Luk  And all to whose ears it came were full of wonder at his knowledge and the answers which he gave
Luk  And when they saw him they were surprised and his mother said to him Son why have you done this to us see your father and I have been looking for you with sorrow
Luk  And he said to them Why were you looking for me was it not clear to you that my right place was in my Fathers house
Luk  And his words seemed strange to them
Luk  And he went down with them and came to Nazareth and did as he was ordered and his mother kept all these words in her heart
Luk  And Jesus was increasing in wisdom and in years and in grace before God and men
Luk  Now in the fifteenth year of the rule of Tiberius Caesar Pontius Pilate being ruler of Judaea and Herod being king of Galilee his brother Philip king of the country of Ituraea and Trachonitis and Lysanias king of Abilene
Luk  When Annas and Caiaphas were high priests the word of the Lord came to John the son of Zacharias in the waste land
Luk  And he came into all the country round about Jordan preaching baptism as a sign of forgiveness of sin for those whose hearts were changed
Luk  As it says in the book of the words of Isaiah the prophet The voice of one crying in the waste land Make ready the way of the Lord make his roads straight
Luk  Every valley will be lifted up and all the mountains and hills made low and the twisted will be made straight and the rough ways smooth
Luk  And all flesh will see the salvation of God
Luk  So he said to the people who went out to him for baptism You offspring of snakes at whose word are you going in flight from the wrath to come
Luk  Make clear by your acts that your hearts have been changed and do not say to yourselves We have Abraham for our father for I say to you that God is able from these stones to make children of Abraham
Luk  And even now the axe is put to the root of the trees and every tree which does not have good fruit will be cut down and put into the fire
Luk  And the people put questions to him saying What have we to do
Luk  And he made answer and said to them He who has two coats let him give to him who has not even one and he who has food let him do the same
Luk  Then taxfarmers came to him for baptism and said to him Master what have we to do
Luk  And he said to them Do not make an attempt to get more money than the right amount
Luk  And men of the army put questions to him saying And what have we to do And he said to them Do no violent acts to any man and do not take anything without right and let your payment be enough for you
Luk  And while the people were waiting and all men were questioning in their hearts about John if he was the Christ or not
Luk  John made answer saying to them all Truly I give you baptism with water but one is coming who is greater than I whose shoes I am not good enough to undo he will give you baptism with the Holy Spirit and with fire
Luk  In whose hand is the instrument with which he will make clean his grain he will put the good grain in his store but the waste will be burned in the fire which will never be put out
Luk  And so comforting them with these and other words he gave the good news to the people
Luk  But Herod the king because John had made a protest on account of Herodias his brothers wife and other evil things which Herod had done

Luk  For forty days being tested by the Evil One And he had no food in those days and when they came to an end he was in need of food

Luk  And Jesus came back to Galilee in the power of the Spirit and the news of him went through all the country round about

Luk  The Spirit of the Lord is on me because I am marked out by him to give good news to the poor he has sent me to make well those who are brokenhearted to say that the prisoners will be let go and the blind will see and to make the wounded free from their chains
Luk  To give knowledge that the year of the Lords good pleasure is come
Luk  And shutting the book he gave it back to the servant and took his seat and the eyes of all in the Synagogue were fixed on him

Luk  And they were all giving witness with wonder to the words of grace which came from his mouth and they said Is not this the son of Joseph
