Luk  And he said to them Truly I say to you No prophet is honoured in his country
Luk  Truly I say to you There were a number of widows in Israel in the days of Elijah when the heaven was shut up for three years and six months and there was no food in the land
Luk  But Elijah was not sent to one of them but only to Zarephath in the land of Sidon to a woman who was a widow
Luk  And there were a number of lepers in Israel in the time of Elisha the prophet and not one of them was made clean but only Naaman the Syrian
Luk  And all who were in the Synagogue were very angry when these things were said to them
Luk  And they got up and took him out of the town to the edge of the mountain on which their town was so that they might send him down to his death
Luk  But he came through them and went on his way
Luk  And he came down to Capernaum a town of Galilee and he was giving them teaching on the Sabbath
Luk  And they were surprised at his teaching for his word was with authority
Luk  And there was a man in the Synagogue who had an unclean spirit and he gave a loud cry and said
Luk  Let us be what have we to do with you Jesus of Nazareth have you come to put an end to us I have knowledge who you are the Holy One of God
Luk  And Jesus said to him Be quiet and come out of him And when the evil spirit had put him down on the earth in the middle of them he came out of him having done him no damage
Luk  And wonder came on them all and they said to one another What are these words for with authority and power he gives orders to the evil spirits and they come out
Luk  And there was much talk about him in all the places round about
Luk  And he got up and went out of the Synagogue and went into the house of Simon And Simons wifes mother was very ill with a burning heat and in answer to their prayers for her
Luk  He went near her and with a sharp word he gave orders to the disease and it went away from her and straight away she got up and took care of their needs
Luk  And at sundown all those who had anyone ill with any sort of disease took them to him and he put his hands on every one of them and made them well
Luk  And evil spirits came out of a number of them crying out and saying You are the Son of God But he gave them sharp orders not to say a word because they had knowledge that he was the Christ
Luk  And when it was day he came out and went to a waste place and great numbers of people came looking for him and they came to him and would have kept him from going away
Luk  But he said to them I have to give the good news of the kingdom of God in other towns because that is why I was sent
Luk  And he was teaching in the Synagogues of Galilee
Luk  Now it came about that while the people came pushing to be near him and to have knowledge of the word of God he was by a wide stretch of water named Gennesaret
Luk  And he saw two boats by the edge of the water but the fishermen had gone out of them and were washing their nets
Luk  And he got into one of the boats the property of Simon and made a request to him to go a little way out from the land And being seated he gave the people teaching from the boat
Luk  And when his talk was ended he said to Simon Go out into deep water and let down your nets for fish
Luk  And Simon answering said Master we were working all night and we took nothing but at your word I will let down the nets
Luk  And when they had done this they got such a great number of fish that it seemed as if their nets would be broken
Luk  And they made signs to their friends in the other boat to come to their help And they came and the two boats were so full that they were going down
Luk  But Simon when he saw it went down at the knees of Jesus and said Go away from me O Lord for I am a sinner
Luk  For he was full of wonder and so were all those who were with him at the number of fish which they had taken
Luk  And so were James and John the sons of Zebedee who were working with Simon And Jesus said to Simon Have no fear from this time forward you will be a fisher of men
Luk  And when they had got their boats to the land they gave up everything and went after him
Luk  And it came about that while he was in one of the towns there was a leper there and when he saw Jesus he went down on his face in prayer to him saying Lord if it is your pleasure you have power to make me clean
Luk  And he put out his hand to him and said It is my pleasure be clean And straight away his disease went from him
Luk  And he gave him orders Say nothing to any man but let the priest see you and give an offering so that you may be made clean as the law of Moses says and for a witness to them
Luk  But news of him went out all the more in every direction and great numbers of people came together to give hearing to his words and to be made well from their diseases
Luk  But he went away by himself to a waste place for prayer
Luk  And it came about that on one of these days he was teaching and some Pharisees and teachers of the law were seated there who had come from every town of Galilee and Judaea and from Jerusalem and the power of the Lord was with him to make those who were ill free from their diseases
Luk  And some men had with them on a bed a man who was ill without power of moving and they made attempts to get him in and put him before Jesus
Luk  And because of the mass of people there was no way to get him in so they went up on the top of the house and let him down through the roof on his bed into the middle in front of Jesus
Luk  And seeing their faith he said Man you have forgiveness for your sins
Luk  And the scribes and Pharisees were having an argument saying Who is this who has no respect for God who is able to give forgiveness for sins but God only
Luk  But Jesus who had knowledge of their thoughts said to them Why are you reasoning in your hearts
Luk  Which is the simpler to say You have forgiveness for your sins or to say Get up and go
Luk  But so that you may see that on earth the Son of man has authority for the forgiveness of sins he said to the man who was ill I say to you Get up and take up your bed and go into your house
Luk  And straight away he got up before them and took up his bed and went away to his house giving praise to God
Luk  And wonder overcame them all and they gave glory to God and they were full of fear saying We have seen strange things today
Luk  And after these things he went out and saw Levi a taxfarmer seated at the place where taxes were taken and said to him Come after me
Luk  And giving up his business he got up and went after him
Luk  And Levi made a great feast for him in his house and a great number of taxfarmers and others were seated at table with them
Luk  And the Pharisees and their scribes made protests against his disciples saying Why do you take food and drink with taxfarmers and sinners
Luk  And Jesus answering said to them Those who are well have no need of a medical man but those who are ill
Luk  I have come not to get the upright but sinners so that they may be turned from their sins
Luk  And they said to him The disciples of John frequently go without food and make prayers and so do the disciples of the Pharisees but your disciples take food and drink
Luk  And Jesus said Are you able to make the friends of the newlymarried man go without food when he is with them
Luk  But the days will come when he will be taken away from them and then they will go without food
Luk  And he said to them in a story No man takes a bit of cloth from a new coat and puts it on to an old coat for so the new coat would be damaged and the bit from the new would not go well with the old
Luk  And no man puts new wine into old wineskins for fear that the skins will be burst by the new wine and the wine be let out and the skins come to destruction
Luk  But new wine has to be put into new wineskins
Luk  And no man having had old wine has any desire for new for he says The old is better
Luk  Now it came about that on the Sabbath he was going through the fields of grain and his disciples took the heads of the grain for food crushing them in their hands
Luk  But some of the Pharisees said Why do you do what it is not right to do on the Sabbath
Luk  And Jesus said Have you not seen in the Writings what David did when he was in need of food he and those who were with him
Luk  How he went into the house of God and took for food the holy bread which only the priests may take and gave it to those who were with him
Luk  And he said The Son of man is lord even of the Sabbath
Luk  And it came about on another Sabbath that he went into the Synagogue and was teaching there And a man was there whose right hand was dead
Luk  And the scribes and Pharisees were watching him to see if he would make him well on the Sabbath so that they might be able to say something against him
Luk  But he had knowledge of their thoughts and he said to the man whose hand was dead Get up and come into the middle And he got up and came forward
Luk  And Jesus said I put the question to you Is it right to do good on the Sabbath or to do evil to give life or to take it away
Luk  And looking round on all of them he said to him Put out your hand And he did so and his hand was made well
Luk  But they were full of wrath and were talking together about what they might do to Jesus
Luk  And it came about in those days that he went out to the mountain for prayer and he was all night in prayer to God
Luk  And the day came and turning to his disciples he made a selection from among them of twelve to whom he gave the name of Apostles
Luk  Simon to whom he gave the name of Peter and Andrew his brother and James and John and Philip and Bartholomew
Luk  And Matthew and Thomas and James the son of Alphaeus and Simon who was named the Zealot
Luk  And Judas the son of James and Judas Iscariot he who was false to him
Luk  And he came down with them to a level place and a great band of his disciples and a very great number of people from all Judaea and Jerusalem and from the parts of Tyre and Sidon by the sea came to give hearing to him and to be made well from their diseases
Luk  And those who were troubled with unclean spirits were made well
Luk  And all the people were desiring to be touched by him for power came from him and made them all well
Luk  And turning his eyes to his disciples he said Happy are you who are poor for the kingdom of God is yours
Luk  Happy are you who are in need of food now for you will be made full Happy are you who are weeping now for you will be glad
Luk  Happy are you when men have hate for you and put you away from among them and say angry words to you turning away in disgust at your name because of the Son of man
Luk  Be glad in that day and be lifted up for joy for your reward in heaven will be great for their fathers did these same things to the prophets
Luk  But unhappy are you who have wealth for you have been comforted now
Luk  Unhappy are you who are full of food now for you will be in need Unhappy are you who are laughing now for you will be crying in sorrow
Luk  Unhappy are you when all men give you their approval for so their fathers did to the false prophets
Luk  But I say to you who give ear to me Have love for those who are against you do good to those who have hate for you
Luk  Give blessing to those who give you curses say prayers for those who are cruel to you
Luk  If a man gives you a blow on one side of your face then let the other side be turned to him from him who takes away your coat do not keep back your robe
Luk  Give to everyone who comes with a request and if a man takes away your property make no attempt to get it back again
Luk  Do to others as you would have them do to you
Luk  If you have love for those who have love for you what credit is it to you for even sinners have love for those who have love for them
Luk  And if you do good to those who do good to you what credit is it to you for even sinners do the same
Luk  And if you let those have the use of your money from whom you are hoping to get it back what credit is it to you even sinners do so to sinners hoping to get back as much as they gave
Luk  But be loving to those who are against you and do them good and give them your money not giving up hope and your reward will be great and you will be the sons of the Most High for he is kind to evil men and to those who have hard hearts
Luk  Be full of pity even as your Father is full of pity
Luk  Be not judges of others and you will not be judged do not give punishment to others and you will not get punishment yourselves make others free and you will be made free
Luk  Give and it will be given to you good measure crushed down full and running over they will give to you For in the same measure as you give it will be given to you again
Luk  And he gave them teaching in the form of a story saying Is it possible for one blind man to be guide to another will they not go falling together into a hole
Luk  The disciple is not greater than his master but everyone whose learning is complete will be like his master
Luk  And why do you take note of the grain of dust in your brothers eye but take no note of the bit of wood which is in your eye
Luk  How will you say to your brother Brother let me take the grain of dust out of your eye when you yourself do not see the bit of wood in your eye O false one first take the wood out of your eye and then you will see clearly to take the dust out of your brothers eye
Luk  For no good tree gives bad fruit and no bad tree gives good fruit
Luk  For every tree is judged by its fruit Men do not get figs from thorns or grapes from blackberry plants
Luk  The good man out of the good store of his heart gives good things and the evil man out of his evil store gives evil for out of the full store of the heart come the words of the mouth
Luk  Why do you say to me Lord Lord and do not the things which I say
Luk  Everyone who comes to me and gives ear to my words and does them I will make clear to you what he is like
Luk  He is like a man building a house who went deep and put the base of it on a rock and when the water came up and the river was driving against that house it was not moved because the building was good
Luk  But he who gives hearing without doing is like a man building a house on the earth without a base for it and when the force of the river came against it straight away it came down and the destruction of that house was great
Luk  After he had come to the end of all his words in the hearing of the people he went into Capernaum
Luk  And a certain captain had a servant who was very dear to him this servant was ill and near to death
Luk  And when news of Jesus came to his ears he sent to him rulers of the Jews requesting that he would come and make his servant well
Luk  And they when they came to Jesus made their request warmly saying
Luk  It is right for you to do this for him because he is a friend to our nation and himself has put up a Synagogue for us
Luk  And Jesus went with them And when he was not far from the house the man sent friends to him saying Lord do not give yourself trouble for I am not important enough for you to come into my house
Luk  And I had the feeling that I was not even good enough to come to you but say the word only and my servant will be well
Luk  For I myself am a man under authority having men under me and I say to this one Go and he goes and to another Come and he comes and to my servant Do this and he does it
Luk  And when these things were said to Jesus he was surprised and turning to the mass of people coming after him said I have not seen such great faith no not in Israel
Luk  And when those who were sent came back to the house they saw that the servant was well
Luk  And it came about after a little time that he went to a town named Nain and his disciples went with him and a great number of people
Luk  Now when he came near the door of the town a dead man was being taken out the only son of his mother who was a widow and a great number of people from the town were with her
Luk  And when the Lord saw her he had pity on her and said to her Be not sad
Luk  And he came near and put his hand on the stretcher where the dead man was and those who were moving it came to a stop And he said Young man I say to you Get up
Luk  And the dead man got up and words came from his lips And he gave him to his mother
Luk  And fear came on all and they gave praise to God saying A great prophet is among us and God has given thought to his people
Luk  And this story about him went through all Judaea and the places round about
Luk  And the disciples of John gave him an account of all these things
Luk  Then John sent two of his disciples to the Lord saying Are you he who is to come or are we waiting for another
Luk  And when the men came to him they said John the Baptist has sent us to you saying Are you he who is to come or are we waiting for another
Luk  At that time he made a number of people free from their diseases and their pains and from evil spirits and to others who were blind he gave back the use of their eyes
Luk  And answering them he said Go back and give news to John of what you have seen and the things which have come to your ears the blind now see those who had no power in their legs are walking lepers are made clean those who had no hearing now have their ears open dead men come to life again and the poor have the good news given to them
Luk  And a blessing will be on him who has no doubts about me
Luk  And when the men who were sent by John had gone away he said to the people about John What did you go out into the waste land to see a tall stem moving in the wind
Luk  But what did you go out to see a man in soft clothing See now those who have beautiful clothing and delicate food are in kings houses
Luk  But what did you go out to see a prophet Yes I say to you and more than a prophet
Luk  This is he of whom it has been said See I send my servant before your face who will make ready your way before you
Luk  I say to you Among all the sons of women not one is greater than John but he who is least in the kingdom of God is greater than he
Luk  And all the people and the taxfarmers to whom John had given baptism when they had knowledge of these things gave glory to God
Luk  But the Pharisees and the teachers of the law were against the purpose of God for themselves not having had his baptism
Luk  What comparison am I to make of the men of this generation what are they like
Luk  They are like children who are seated in the marketplace crying out to one another and saying We made music for you but you did not take part in the dance we gave cries of sorrow but you were not sad
Luk  For John the Baptist came taking no food or drink and you say He has an evil spirit
Luk  The Son of man came feasting and you say Here is a lover of food and wine a friend of taxfarmers and sinners
Luk  But wisdom is judged to be right by all her children
Luk  And one of the Pharisees made a request that he would take a meal with him And he went into the Pharisees house and took his seat at the table
Luk  And there was a woman in the town who was a sinner and when she had news that he was a guest in the Pharisees house she took a bottle of perfume
Luk  And went in and took her place at the back of him near his feet weeping so that his feet were washed with the drops from her eyes and with her hair she made them dry and kissing his feet she put the perfume on them
Luk  Now when the Pharisee in whose house he was saw it he said to himself This man if he was a prophet would be conscious what sort of woman this is who has put her hands on him that she is a sinner
Luk  And Jesus answering said Simon I have something to say to you And he said Master say on
Luk  And he said Two men were in debt to a certain man of business one had a debt of five hundred pence and the other of fifty
Luk  When they were unable to make payment he made the two of them free of their debts Which of them now will have the greater love for him
Luk  Simon in answer said It seems he whose debt was greater And he said Your decision is right
Luk  And turning to the woman he said to Simon You see this woman I came into your house you did not give me water for my feet but she has been washing my feet with the drops from her eyes and drying them with her hair
Luk  You did not give me a kiss but she from the time when I came in has gone on kissing my feet
Luk  You put no oil on my head but she has put perfume on my feet
Luk  And so I say to you She will have forgiveness for her sins which are great in number because of her great love but he who has small need of forgiveness gives little love
Luk  And he said to her You have forgiveness for your sins
Luk  And those who were seated at table with him said to themselves Who is this who even gives forgiveness of sins
Luk  And he said to the woman By your faith you have salvation go in peace
Luk  And it came about after a short time that he went through town and country giving the good news of the kingdom of God and with him were the twelve
Luk  And certain women who had been made free from evil spirits and diseases Mary named Magdalene from whom seven evil spirits had gone out
Luk  And Joanna the wife of Chuza Herods chief houseservant and Susanna and a number of others who gave him of their wealth for his needs
Luk  And when a great number of people came together and men from every town went out to him he gave them teaching in the form of a story
Luk  A man went out to put in seed and while he was doing it some was dropped by the wayside and it was crushed under foot and was taken by the birds of heaven
Luk  And some went on the rock and when it came up it became dry and dead because it had no water
Luk  And some went among thorns and the thorns came up with it and it had no room for growth
Luk  And some falling on good earth came up and gave fruit a hundred times as much And with these words he said in a loud voice He who has ears let him give ear
Luk  And his disciples put questions to him about the point of the story
Luk  And he said To you is given knowledge of the secrets of the kingdom of God but to the others they are given in stories so that seeing they may not see and though they give hearing the sense will not be clear to them
Luk  Now this is the point of the story The seed is the word of God
Luk  Those by the side of the road are those who have given hearing then the Evil One comes and takes away the word from their hearts so that they may not have faith and get salvation
Luk  And those on the rock are those who with joy give hearing to the word but having no root they have faith for a time and when the test comes they give up
Luk  And those which went among thorns are those who have given hearing and go on their way but they are overcome by cares and wealth and the pleasures of life and they give no fruit
Luk  And those in the good earth are those who having given ear to the word keep it with a good and true heart and in quiet strength give fruit
Luk  No man when the light is lighted puts a cover over it or puts it under a bed but he puts it on its table so that those who come in may see the light
Luk  For nothing is put out of view which will not be made clear and nothing is secret of which the knowledge will not come to light
Luk  So take care how you give hearing for to him who has will be given and from him who has not will be taken even what he seems to have
Luk  And his mother and his brothers came to him and they were not able to get near him because of the great number of people
Luk  And someone said to him Your mother and your brothers are outside desiring to see you
Luk  But he said to them in answer My mother and my brothers are those who have knowledge of the word of God and do it
Luk  Now it came about on one of those days that he got into a boat with his disciples and he said to them Let us go over to the other side of the water and they put out the boat
Luk  But while they were sailing he went to sleep and a storm of wind came down on the sea and the boat became full of water and they were in danger
Luk  Then they came to him and awaking him out of his sleep said Master Master destruction is near And he when he was awake gave orders to the wind and the rolling waves and the storm came to an end and all was calm
Luk  And he said to them Where is your faith And fear and wonder overcame them and they said to one another Who then is this who gives orders even to the winds and the water and they do what he says
Luk  And they came to the country of the Gerasenes which is opposite Galilee
Luk  And when he had come to the land there came to him a certain man from the town who had evil spirits and for a long time he had had no clothing on and was not living in a house but in the place of the dead
Luk  And when he saw Jesus he gave a loud cry and went down on the earth before him and in a loud voice said What have I to do with you Jesus Son of the Most High God Do not be cruel to me
Luk  For he gave an order to the evil spirit to come out of the man For frequently it would take a grip of him and he was kept under control and prisoned with chains but parting the chains in two he would be sent by the driving of the evil spirit into waste places
Luk  And Jesus said to him What is your name And he said Legion for a number of spirits had gone into him
Luk  And they made a request to him that he would not give them an order to go away into the deep
Luk  Now there was a great herd of pigs in that place getting food on the mountain and the evil spirits made a request to him that he would let them go into the pigs and he let them
Luk  And the evil spirits came out of the man and went into the pigs and the herd went rushing down a sharp slope into the water and came to destruction
Luk  And when the men who took care of them saw what had come about they went quickly and gave news of it in the town and the country
Luk  And they went out to see what had taken place and they came to Jesus and saw the man out of whom the evil spirits had gone seated clothed and with full use of his senses at the feet of Jesus and fear came on them
Luk  And those who had seen it gave them an account of how the man who had the evil spirits was made well
Luk  And all the people of the country of the Gerasenes made a request to him to go away from them for they were in great fear and he got into a boat and went back
Luk  But the man from whom the evil spirits had gone out had a great desire to be with him but he sent him away saying
Luk  Go back to your house and let them have news of all the great things which God has done for you And he went away giving word through all the town of the great things which Jesus had done for him
Luk  And when Jesus went back the people were glad to see him for they were all waiting for him
Luk  Then there came a man named Jairus who was a ruler in the Synagogue and he went down at the feet of Jesus desiring him to come to his house
Luk  For he had an only daughter about twelve years old and she was near to death But while he was on his way the people were pushing to be near him
Luk  And a woman who had had a flow of blood for twelve years and had given all her money to medical men and not one of them was able to make her well
Luk  Came after him and put her hand on the edge of his robe and straight away the flowing of her blood was stopped
Luk  And Jesus said Who was touching me And when they all said It is not I Peter and those who were with him said Master the people are pushing round you on every side
Luk  But Jesus said Someone was touching me for I had the feeling that power had gone out from me
Luk  And when the woman saw that she was not able to keep it secret she came shaking with fear and falling down before him she made clear before all the people the reason for her touching him and how she was made well straight away
Luk  And he said to her Daughter your faith has made you well go in peace
Luk  While he was still talking someone came from the house of the ruler of the Synagogue saying Your daughter is dead do not go on troubling the Master
Luk  But Jesus at these words said to him Have no fear only have faith and she will be made well
Luk  And when he came to the house he did not let any man go in with him but only Peter and John and James and the father of the girl and her mother
Luk  And all the people were weeping and crying for her but he said Do not be sad for she is not dead but sleeping
Luk  And they were laughing at him being certain that she was dead
Luk  But he taking her hand said to her My child get up
Luk  And her spirit came back to her and she got up straight away and he gave orders that food was to be given to her
Luk  And her father and mother were full of wonder but he gave orders to them to say nothing about it to anyone
Luk  And getting the twelve together he gave them power and authority over all evil spirits and over diseases to make them well
Luk  And he sent them out to be preachers of the kingdom of God and to make well those who were ill
Luk  And he said to them Take nothing for your journey no stick or bag or bread or money and do not take two coats
Luk  And if you go into a house let that house be your restingplace till you go away
Luk  And if any people will not take you in when you go away from that town put off its dust from your feet for a witness against them
Luk  And they went away journeying through all the towns preaching the good news and making people free from diseases in all places
Luk  Now Herod the king had news of all these things and he was in doubt because it was said by some people that John had come back from the dead
Luk  And by some that Elijah had come and by others that one of the old prophets had come back to life
Luk  And Herod said I put John to death but who is this of whom such stories are given to me And he had a desire to see him
Luk  And the twelve when they came back gave him an account of what they had done And he took them with him and went away from the people to a town named Bethsaida
Luk  But the people getting news of it went after him and he was pleased to see them and gave them teaching about the kingdom of God and made those well who were in need of it
Luk  And the day went on and the twelve came to him and said Send these people away so that they may go into the towns and the country round about and get restingplaces and food for themselves for we are in a waste place
Luk  But he said Give them food yourselves And they said We have only five cakes of bread and two fishes if we do not go and get food for all these people
Luk  For there were about five thousand men And he said to his disciples Make them be seated in groups about fifty to a group
Luk  And they did so and made them all be seated
Luk  And he took the five cakes of bread and the two fishes and looking up to heaven he said words of blessing over them and when they had been broken he gave them to the disciples to give to the people
Luk  And they all took the food and had enough and they took up of the broken bits which were over twelve baskets full
Luk  And it came about that when he was in prayer by himself and the disciples were with him he put a question to them saying Who do the people say I am
Luk  And they answering said John the Baptist but others say Elijah and others that one of the old prophets has come back
Luk  And he said But who do you say that I am And Peter answering said The Christ of God
Luk  But he gave them special orders not to say this to any man
Luk  Saying The Son of man will undergo much and be put on one side by the rulers and the chief priests and the teachers of the law and be put to death and on the third day he will come back to life
Luk  And he said to them all If any man has a desire to come after me let him give up all and take up his cross every day and come after me
Luk  For whoever has a desire to keep his life will have it taken from him but whoever gives up his life because of me will keep it
Luk  For what profit will a man have if he gets all the world but undergoes loss or destruction himself
Luk  For if any man has a feeling of shame because of me or of my words the Son of man will have shame because of him when he comes in his glory and the glory of the Father and of the holy angels
Luk  But truly I say to you Some of those who are here now will have no taste of death till they see the kingdom of God
Luk  And about eight days after he had said these things he took Peter and John and James with him and went up into the mountain for prayer
Luk  And while he was in prayer his face was changed and his clothing became white and shining
Luk  And two men Moses and Elijah were talking with him
Luk  Who were seen in glory and were talking of his death which was about to take place in Jerusalem
Luk  Now Peter and those who were with him were overcome with sleep but when they were fully awake they saw his glory and the two men who were with him
Luk  And when they were about to go away from him Peter said to Jesus Master it is good for us to be here let us make three tents one for you and one for Moses and one for Elijah having no knowledge of what he was saying
Luk  And while he said these things the shade of a cloud came over them and they were full of fear when they went into the cloud
Luk  And there was a voice from the cloud saying This is my Son the man of my selection give ear to him
Luk  And after the voice was gone they saw that Jesus was by himself And they kept quiet and said nothing at that time to anyone of the things which they had seen
Luk  And on the day after when they came down from the mountain a great band of people came to him
Luk  And a man from among them crying out said Master I make a request to you give a thought to my son for he is my only child
Luk  And see a spirit takes him and suddenly he gives a cry twisted in pain and streaming at the lips and when it goes away from him at last he is marked as from blows
Luk  And I made a request to your disciples to send it out of him but they were not able to do it
Luk  And Jesus said O generation without faith and false in heart how long will I have to be with you and put up with you let your son come here
Luk  And while he was coming he was pushed violently down and twisted by the evil spirit But Jesus gave sharp orders to the unclean spirit and made the boy well and gave him back to his father
Luk  And they were full of wonder at the great power of God But while they were all wondering at all the things which he did he said to his disciples
Luk  Let these words go deep into your ears for the Son of man will be given up into the hands of men
Luk  But this saying was not clear to them and its sense was kept secret from them so that they were not able to see it and they had fear of questioning him about it
Luk  Now there was a discussion among them about which of them would be the greatest
Luk  But when Jesus saw the reasoning of their hearts he took a small child and put him by his side
Luk  And said to them Whoever gives honour to this child in my name gives honour to me and whoever gives honour to me gives honour to him who sent me for whoever is least among you all that man is great
Luk  And John answering said Master we saw a man driving out evil spirits in your name and we did not let him do it because he was not one of us
Luk  But Jesus said to him Let him do it for he who is not against you is for you
Luk  And it came about that when the days were near for him to be taken up his face was turned to go to Jerusalem
Luk  And he sent men before and they came to a small town of Samaria to make ready for him
Luk  But they would not have him there because he was clearly going to Jerusalem
Luk  And when his disciples James and John saw this they said Lord may we send fire from heaven and put an end to them
Luk  But turning round he said sharp words to them
Luk  And they went to another small town
Luk  And when they were on the way a certain man said to him I will come after you wherever you go
Luk  And Jesus said to him Foxes have holes and the birds of the air have restingplaces but the Son of man has nowhere to put his head
Luk  And he said to another Come after me But he said Lord let me first go and give the last honours to my father
Luk  But he said to him Let the dead take care of their dead it is for you to go and give news of the kingdom of God
Luk  And another man said I will come with you Lord but first let me say a last goodday to those who are at my house
Luk  But Jesus said No man having put his hand to the plough and looking back is good enough for the kingdom of God
Luk  Now after these things the Lord made selection of seventy others and sent them before him two together into every town and place where he himself was about to come
Luk  And he said to them There is much grain ready to be cut but not enough workers so make prayer to the Lord of the grainfields that he will send workers to get in the grain
Luk  Go on your way see I send you out like lambs among wolves
Luk  Take no bag for money or for food and no shoes say no word to any man on the way
Luk  And whenever you go into a house first say Peace be to this house
Luk  And if a son of peace is there your peace will be with him but if not it will come back to you again
Luk  And keep in that same house taking what food and drink they give you for the worker has a right to his reward Do not go from house to house
Luk  And into whatever town you go if they take you in take whatever food is given to you
Luk  And make well those in it who are ill and say to them The kingdom of God is near to you
Luk  But if you go into a town where they will not have you go out into the streets of it and say
Luk  Even the dust of your town which is on our feet we put off as a witness against you but be certain of this that the kingdom of God is near
Luk  I say to you It will be better in that day for Sodom than for that town
Luk  A curse is on you Chorazin A curse is on you Bethsaida For if such works of power had been done in Tyre and Sidon as have been done in you they would have been turned from their sins in days gone by seated in the dust
Luk  But it will be better for Tyre and Sidon in the day of judging than for you
Luk  And you Capernaum were you not lifted up to heaven you will go down to hell
Luk  Whoever gives ear to you gives ear to me and whoever is against you is against me and whoever is against me is against him who sent me
Luk  And the seventy came back with joy saying Lord even the evil spirits are under our power in your name
Luk  And he said I was watching for Satan falling from heaven like a star
Luk  See I have given you power to put your feet on snakes and evil beasts and over all the strength of him who is against you and nothing will do you damage
Luk  Do not be glad however because you have power over spirits but because your names are recorded in heaven
Luk  In that same hour he was full of joy in the Holy Spirit and said I give praise to you O Father Lord of heaven and earth because you have kept these things secret from the wise and the men of learning and have made them clear to little children for so O Father it was pleasing in your eyes
Luk  All things have been given to me by my Father and no one has knowledge of the Son but only the Father and of the Father but only the Son and he to whom the Son will make it clear
Luk  And turning to the disciples he said privately Happy are the eyes which see the things you see
Luk  For I say to you that numbers of prophets and kings have had a desire to see the things which you see and have not seen them and to have knowledge of the things which have come to your ears and they had it not
Luk  And a certain teacher of the law got up and put him to the test saying Master what have I to do so that I may have eternal life
Luk  And he said to him What does the law say in your reading of it
Luk  And he answering said Have love for the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your strength and with all your mind and for your neighbour as for yourself
Luk  And he said You have given the right answer do this and you will have life
Luk  But he desiring to put himself in the right said to Jesus And who is my neighbour
Luk  And Jesus answering him said A certain man was going down from Jerusalem to Jericho and he got into the hands of thieves who took his clothing and gave him cruel blows and when they went away he was half dead
Luk  And by chance a certain priest was going down that way and when he saw him he went by on the other side
Luk  And in the same way a Levite when he came to the place and saw him went by on the other side
Luk  But a certain man of Samaria journeying that way came where he was and when he saw him he was moved with pity for him
Luk  And came to him and put clean linen round his wounds with oil and wine and he put him on his beast and took him to a house and took care of him
Luk  And the day after he took two pennies and gave them to the owner of the house and said Take care of him and if this money is not enough when I come again I will give you whatever more is needed
Luk  Which of these three men in your opinion was neighbour to the man who came into the hands of thieves
Luk  And he said The one who had mercy on him And Jesus said Go and do the same
Luk  Now while they were on their way he came to a certain town and a woman named Martha took him into her house
Luk  And she had a sister by name Mary who took her seat at the Lords feet and gave attention to his words
Luk  But Martha had her hands full of the work of the house and she came to him and said Lord is it nothing to you that my sister has let me do all the work Say to her that she is to give me some help
Luk  But the Lord answering said to her Martha Martha you are full of care and troubled about such a number of things
Luk  Little is needed or even one thing only for Mary has taken that good part which will not be taken away from her
Luk  And it came about that he was in prayer in a certain place and when he came to an end one of his disciples said to him Lord will you give us teaching about prayer as John did to his disciples
Luk  And he said to them When you say your prayers say Father may your name be kept holy and your kingdom come
Luk  Give us every day bread for our needs
Luk  May we have forgiveness for our sins as we make free all those who are in debt to us And let us not be put to the test
Luk  And he said to them Which of you having a friend would go to him in the middle of the night and say to him Friend let me have three cakes of bread
Luk  Because a friend of mine has come to me on a journey and I have nothing to put before him
Luk  And he from inside the house would say in answer Do not be a trouble to me the door is now shut and my children are with me in bed it is not possible for me to get up and give to you
Luk  I say to you Though he will not get up and give to him because he is his friend still if he keeps on making his request he will get up and give him as much as he has need of
Luk  And I say to you Make requests and they will be answered what you are searching for you will get when you give the sign the door will be open to you
Luk  For to everyone who makes a request it will be given and he who is searching will get his desire and to him who gives the sign the door will be open
Luk  And which of you being a father will give a stone to his son who makes request for bread or for a fish will give him a snake
Luk  Or for an egg will give him a scorpion
Luk  If then you who are evil are able to give good things to your children how much more will your Father in heaven give the Holy Spirit to those who make request to him
Luk  And he was sending an evil spirit out of a man who was without the power of talking And it came about that when the spirit had gone the man had the power of talking and the people were full of wonder
Luk  But some of them said He sends out evil spirits by Beelzebul the ruler of evil spirits
Luk  And others testing him were looking for a sign from heaven from him
Luk  But he having knowledge of their thoughts said to them Every kingdom in which there is division is made waste and a house in which there is division comes to destruction
Luk  If then Satan is at war with himself how will he keep his kingdom because you say that I send evil spirits out of men by the help of Beelzebul
Luk  And if I by Beelzebul send out evil spirits by whose help do your sons send them out so let them be your judges
Luk  But if I by the finger of God send out evil spirits then the kingdom of God has overtaken you
Luk  When the strong man armed keeps watch over his house then his goods are safe
Luk  But when one who is stronger makes an attack on him and overcomes him he takes away his instruments of war in which he had put his faith and makes division of his goods
Luk  He who is not with me is against me and he who will not give me help in getting people together is driving them away
Luk  The unclean spirit when he has gone out of a man goes through dry places looking for rest and when he does not get it he says I will go back to my house from which I came
Luk  And when he comes he sees that it has been made fair and clean
Luk  Then he goes and gets seven other spirits more evil than himself and they go in and take their places there and the last condition of that man is worse than the first

Luk  But he said More happy are they who give hearing to the word of God and keep it
Luk  And when a great number of people came together to him he said This generation is an evil generation it is looking for a sign and no sign will be given to it but the sign of Jonah
Luk  For even as Jonah became a sign to the Ninevites so will the Son of man be to this generation
Luk  The queen of the South will come up on the day of judging and give her decision against the men of this generation for she came from the ends of the earth to give ear to the wisdom of Solomon and now something greater than Solomon is here
Luk  The men of Nineveh will come up in the day of judging and give their decision against this generation for they were turned away from their sins at the preaching of Jonah but now something greater than Jonah is here
Luk  No man when the light has been lighted puts it in a secret place or under a vessel but on its table so that those who come in may see the light
Luk  The light of the body is the eye when your eye is true all your body is full of light but when it is evil your body is dark
Luk  So take care that the light which is in you is not dark
Luk  If then all your body is light with no part of it dark it will be completely full of light as when a flame with its bright shining gives you light
Luk  Now while he was talking a Pharisee made a request that he would come to a meal with him and he went in and took his seat at the meal

Luk  O you foolish ones did not he who made the outside in the same way make the inside
Luk  But if you give to the poor such things as you are able then all things are clean to you
Luk  But a curse is on you Pharisees for you make men give a tenth of every sort of plant and give no thought to right and the love of God but it is right for you to do these things and not let the others be undone
Luk  A curse is on you Pharisees for your desires are for the most important seats in the Synagogues and for words of respect said to you in the marketplace
Luk  A curse is on you for you are like the restingplaces of dead men which are not seen and men go walking over them without knowledge of it
Luk  And one of the teachers of the law answering said to him Master in saying this you give a bad name to us as to them

Luk  A curse is on you for you make restingplaces for the bodies of the prophets but your fathers put them to death
Luk  So you are witnesses and give approval to the work of your fathers for they put them to death and you make their last restingplaces
Luk  For this reason the wisdom of God has said I will send them prophets and teachers and to some of them they will give death and cruel pains
Luk  So that punishment may come on this generation for the blood of all the prophets which was given from the earliest days
Luk  From the blood of Abel to the blood of Zachariah who was put to death between the altar and the Temple Yes I say to you It will come on this generation
Luk  A curse is on you teachers of the law for you have taken away the key of knowledge you did not go in yourselves and you got in the way of those who were going in
Luk  And when he had come out of that place the scribes and the Pharisees came round him angrily questioning him about more things
Luk  And watching him for a chance to get something from his words which might be used against him

Luk  So whatever you have said in the dark will come to mens hearing in the light and what you have said secretly inside the house will be made public from the housetops
Luk  And I say to you my friends Have no fear of those who may put the body to death and are able to do no more than that
Luk  But I will make clear to you of whom you are to be in fear of him who after death has power to send you to hell yes truly I say Have fear of him
Luk  Are not five sparrows given in exchange for two farthings and God has every one of them in mind

Luk  And I say to you that to everyone who gives witness to me before men the Son of man will give witness before the angels of God

Luk  And if anyone says a word against the Son of man he will have forgiveness but for him who says evil words against the Holy Spirit there will be no forgiveness

Luk  For the Holy Spirit will make clear to you in that very hour what to say

Luk  But he said Man who made me a judge or a maker of decisions for you

Luk  And he said to them in a story The land of a certain man of great wealth was very fertile
Luk  And he said to himself What is to be done for I have no place in which to put all my fruit
Luk  And he said This I will do I will take down my storehouses and make greater ones and there I will put all my grain and my goods
Luk  And I will say to my soul Soul you have a great amount of goods in store enough for a number of years be at rest take food and wine and be happy
Luk  But God said to him You foolish one tonight I will take your soul from you and who then will be the owner of all the things which you have got together
Luk  So that is what comes to the man who gets wealth for himself and has not wealth in the eyes of God
Luk  And he said to his disciples For this reason I say to you Take no thought for your life about what food you will take or for your body how it may be clothed
Luk  Is not life more than food and the body than its clothing
Luk  Give thought to the ravens they do not put seeds into the earth or get together grain they have no storehouses or buildings and God gives them their food of how much greater value are you than the birds
Luk  And which of you by taking thought is able to make himself any taller
Luk  If then you are not able to do even that which is least why are you troubled about the rest
Luk  Give thought to the flowers they do no work they make no thread and still I say to you Even Solomon in all his glory was not clothed like one of these
Luk  But if God gives such clothing to the grass in the field which today is living and tomorrow will be burned in the oven how much more will he give clothing to you O men of little faith
Luk  And do not give overmuch thought to your food and drink and let not your mind be full of doubts
Luk  For the nations of the world go in search of all these things but your Father has knowledge that you have need of them

Luk  Have no fear little flock for it is your Fathers good pleasure to give you the kingdom

Luk  For where your wealth is there will your heart be
Luk  Be ready dressed as for a journey with your lights burning
Luk  And be like men who are looking for their lord when he comes back from the bridefeast so that when he comes to the door it will be open to him quickly
Luk  Happy are those servants who are watching when the lord comes truly I say to you he will make himself their servant and placing them at the table he will come out and give them food
Luk  And if he comes in the second division of the night or in the third and they are watching for him happy are those servants
Luk  But be certain of this that if the master of the house had had knowledge of the time when the thief was coming he would have been watching and would not have let his house be broken into
Luk  So be ready for the Son of man is coming at a time when you are not looking for him
Luk  And Peter said to him Lord are these words said to us only or to all men

Luk  And the servant who had knowledge of his lords desires and was not ready for him and did not do as he was ordered will be given a great number of blows
Luk  But he who without knowledge did things for which punishment is given will get only a small number of blows The man to whom much is given will have to give much if much is given into his care of him more will be requested

Luk  Then he said to the people When you see a cloud coming up in the west straight away you say There will be rain and so it is
Luk  And when you see a south wind blowing you say There will be heat and so it is
Luk  O false ones the face of the earth and the heaven is clear to you how is it that the signs of these times are not as clear to you
Luk  And why are you in your hearts unable to be judges of what is right
Luk  For if anyone has a cause at law against you and you are going with him before the ruler make an attempt on the way to come to an agreement with him for if you do not he may take you before the judge and the judge will give you up to the police and they will put you in prison
Luk  I say to you You will not come out of it till you have made payment to the very last farthing
Luk  Now some people who were there at that time gave him an account of how the blood of some Galilaeans had been mixed by Pilate with their offerings

Luk  I say to you It is not so but if your hearts are not changed you will all come to an end in the same way
Luk  And he made up this story for them A certain man had a figtree in his garden and he came to get fruit from it and there was no fruit
Luk  And he said to the gardener See for three years I have been looking for fruit from this tree and I have not had any let it be cut down why is it taking up space
Luk  And he said Lord let it be for this year and I will have the earth turned up round it and put animal waste on it to make it fertile
Luk  And if after that it has fruit it is well if not let it be cut down
Luk  And he was teaching in one of the Synagogues on the Sabbath

Luk  And he put his hands on her and she was made straight and gave praise to God

Luk  But I have to go on my way today and tomorrow and the third day for it is not right for a prophet to come to his death outside Jerusalem
Luk  O Jerusalem Jerusalem putting to death the prophets and stoning those who were sent to her again and again would I have taken your children to myself as a bird takes her young ones under her wings but you would not
Luk  Now see your house is waste and I say to you You will not see me again till you say A blessing on him who comes in the name of the Lord
Luk  And it came about that when he went into the house of one of the chief Pharisees on the Sabbath to have a meal they were watching him
Luk  And a certain man was there who had a disease
Luk  And Jesus answering said to the scribes and Pharisees Is it right to make people well on the Sabbath or not
Luk  But they said nothing And he made him well and sent him away
Luk  And he said to them Which of you whose ox or ass has got into a waterhole will not straight away get him out on the Sabbath
Luk  And they had no answer to that question
Luk  And he gave teaching in the form of a story to the guests who came to the feast when he saw how they took the best seats saying to them
Luk  When you get a request to come to a feast do not take the best seat for a more important man than you may be coming
Luk  And then the giver of the feast will come to you and say Give your place to this man and you with shame will have to take the lowest seat
Luk  But when you come go and take the lowest seat so that when the giver of the feast comes he may say to you Friend come up higher and then you will have honour in the eyes of all the others who are there
Luk  For every man who gives himself a high place will be put down but he who takes a low place will be lifted up
Luk  And he said to the master of the house When you give a feast do not send for your friends and your brothers and your family or your neighbours who have wealth for they may give a feast for you and so you will get a reward
Luk  But when you give a feast send for the poor and the blind and those who are broken in body
Luk  And you will have a blessing because they will not be able to give you any payment and you will get your reward when the upright come back from the dead
Luk  And hearing these words one of those who were at table with him said to him Happy is the man who will be a guest in the kingdom of God
Luk  And he said to them A certain man gave a great feast and sent word of it to a number of people
Luk  And when the time had come he sent his servants to say to them Come for all things are now ready
Luk  And they all gave reasons why they were not able to come The first said to him I have got a new field and it is necessary for me to go and see it I am full of regret that I am unable to come
Luk  And another said I have got some cattle and I am going to make a test of them I am full of regret that I am unable to come
Luk  And another said I have been married and so I am not able to come
Luk  And the servant came back and gave his master an account of these things Then the master of the house was angry and said to the servant Go out quickly into the streets of the town and get the poor the blind and those who are broken in body
Luk  And the servant said Lord your orders have been done and still there is room
Luk  And the lord said to the servant Go out into the roads and the fields and make them come in so that my house may be full
Luk  For I say to you that not one of those who were requested to come will have a taste of my feast
Luk  Now a great number of people went with him
Luk  And turning round he said to them If any man comes to me and has not hate for his father and mother and wife and children and brothers and sisters and even for his life he may not be my disciple
Luk  Whoever does not take up his cross and come after me may not be my disciple
Luk  For which of you desiring to put up a tower does not first give much thought to the price if he will have enough to make it complete
Luk  For fear that if he makes a start and is not able to go on with it to the end all who see it will be laughing at him
Luk  And saying This man made a start at building and is not able to make it complete
Luk  Or what king going to war with another king will not first take thought if he will be strong enough with ten thousand men to keep off him who comes against him with twenty thousand
Luk  Or while the other is still a great distance away he sends representatives requesting conditions of peace
Luk  And so whoever is not ready to give up all he has may not be my disciple
Luk  For salt is good but if the taste goes from it of what use is it
Luk  It is no good for the land or for the place of waste no one has a use for it He who has ears let him give ear
Luk  Now all the taxfarmers and sinners came near to give ear to him
Luk  And the Pharisees and scribes were angry saying This man gives approval to sinners and takes food with them
Luk  And he made a story for them saying
Luk  What man of you having a hundred sheep if one of them gets loose and goes away will not let the ninetynine be in the waste land by themselves and go after the wandering one till he sees where it is
Luk  And when he has got it again he takes it in his arms with joy
Luk  And when he gets back to his house he sends for his neighbours and friends saying to them Be glad with me for I have got back my sheep which had gone away
Luk  I say to you that even so there will be more joy in heaven when one sinner is turned away from his wrongdoing than for ninetynine good men who have no need of a change of heart
Luk  Or what woman having ten bits of silver if one bit has gone from her hands will not get a light and go through her house searching with care till she sees it
Luk  And when she has it again she gets her friends and neighbours together saying Be glad with me for I have got back the bit of silver which had gone from me
Luk  Even so I say to you There is joy among the angels of God when one sinner is turned away from his wrongdoing
Luk  And he said A certain man had two sons
Luk  And the younger of them said to his father Father give me that part of your property which will be mine And he made division of his goods between them
Luk  And not long after the younger son got together everything which was his and took a journey into a faraway country and there all his money went in foolish living
Luk  And when everything was gone there was no food to be had in that country and he was in need
Luk  And he went and put himself into the hands of one of the people of that country and he sent him into his fields to give the pigs their food
Luk  And so great was his need that he would have been glad to take the pigs food and no one gave him anything
Luk  But when he came to his senses he said What numbers of my fathers servants have bread enough and more while I am near to death here through need of food
Luk  I will get up and go to my father and will say to him Father I have done wrong against heaven and in your eyes
Luk  I am no longer good enough to be named your son make me like one of your servants
Luk  And he got up and went to his father But while he was still far away his father saw him and was moved with pity for him and went quickly and took him in his arms and gave him a kiss
Luk  And his son said to him Father I have done wrong against heaven and in your eyes I am no longer good enough to be named your son
Luk  But the father said to his servants Get out the first robe quickly and put it on him and put a ring on his hand and shoes on his feet
Luk  And get the fat young ox and put it to death and let us have a feast and be glad
Luk  For this my son who was dead is living again he had gone away from me and has come back And they were full of joy
Luk  Now the older son was in the field and when he came near the house the sounds of music and dancing came to his ears
Luk  And he sent for one of the servants questioning him about what it might be
Luk  And he said to him Your brother has come and your father has had the young ox put to death because he has come back safely
Luk  But he was angry and would not go in and his father came out and made a request to him to come in
Luk  But he made answer and said to his father See all these years I have been your servant doing your orders in everything and you never gave me even a young goat so that I might have a feast with my friends
Luk  But when this your son came who has been wasting your property with bad women you put to death the fat young ox for him
Luk  And he said to him Son you are with me at all times and all I have is yours
Luk  But it was right to be glad and to have a feast for this your brother who was dead is living again he had gone away and has come back
Luk  And another time he said to the disciples There was a certain man of great wealth who had a servant and it was said to him that this servant was wasting his goods
Luk  And he sent for him and said What is this which is said about you give me an account of all you have done for you will no longer be the manager of my property
Luk  And the servant said to himself What am I to do now that my lord takes away my position I have not enough strength for working in the fields and I would be shamed if I made requests for money from people in the streets
Luk  I have come to a decision what to do so that when I am put out of my position they will take me into their houses
Luk  And sending for every one who was in debt to his lord he said to the first What is the amount of your debt to my lord
Luk  And he said A hundred measures of oil And he said Take your account straight away and put down fifty
Luk  Then he said to another What is the amount of your debt And he said A hundred measures of grain And he said to him Take your account and put down eighty
Luk  And his lord was pleased with the false servant because he had been wise for the sons of this world are wiser in relation to their generation than the sons of light
Luk  And I say to you Make friends for yourselves through the wealth of this life so that when it comes to an end you may be taken into the eternal restingplaces
Luk  He who is true in a little is true in much he who is false in small things is false in great
Luk  If then you have not been true in your use of the wealth of this life who will give into your care the true wealth
Luk  And if you have not been true in your care of the property of other people who will give you that which is yours
Luk  No man may be a servant to two masters for he will have hate for the one and love for the other or he will keep to the one and have no respect for the other You may not be servants of God and of wealth
Luk  And the Pharisees who had a great love of money hearing these things were making sport of him
Luk  And he said You take care to seem right in the eyes of men but God sees your hearts and those things which are important in the opinion of men are evil in the eyes of God
Luk  The law and the prophets were till John but then came the preaching of the kingdom of God and everyone makes his way into it by force
Luk  But heaven and earth will come to an end before the smallest letter of the law may be dropped out
Luk  Everyone who puts away his wife and takes another is a false husband and he who is married to a woman whose husband has put her away is no true husband to her
Luk  Now there was a certain man of great wealth who was dressed in fair clothing of purple and delicate linen and was shining and glad every day
Luk  And a certain poor man named Lazarus was stretched out at his door full of wounds
Luk  Desiring the broken bits of food which came from the table of the man of wealth and even the dogs came and put their tongues on his wounds
Luk  And in time the poor man came to his end and angels took him to Abrahams breast And the man of wealth came to his end and was put in the earth
Luk  And in hell being in great pain lifting up his eyes he saw Abraham far away and Lazarus on his breast
Luk  And he gave a cry and said Father Abraham have mercy on me and send Lazarus so that he may put the end of his finger in water and put it on my tongue for I am cruelly burning in this flame
Luk  But Abraham said Keep in mind my son that when you were living you had your good things while Lazarus had evil things but now he is comforted and you are in pain
Luk  And in addition there is a deep division fixed between us and you so that those who might go from here to you are not able to do so and no one may come from you to us
Luk  And he said Father it is my request that you will send him to my fathers house
Luk  For I have five brothers and let him give them an account of these things so that they may not come to this place of pain
Luk  But Abraham said They have Moses and the prophets let them give ear to what they say
Luk  And he said No father Abraham but if someone went to them from the dead their hearts would be changed
Luk  And he said to him If they will not give attention to Moses and the prophets they will not be moved even if someone comes back from the dead
Luk  And he said to his disciples It is necessary for causes of trouble to come about but unhappy is he by whom they come
Luk  It would be well for him if a great stone was put round his neck and he was dropped into the sea before he made trouble for any of these little ones
Luk  Give attention to yourselves if your brother does wrong say a sharp word to him and if he has sorrow for his sin let him have forgiveness
Luk  And if he does you wrong seven times in a day and seven times comes to you and says I have regret for what I have done let him have forgiveness
Luk  And the twelve said to the Lord Make our faith greater
Luk  And the Lord said If your faith was only as great as a grain of mustard seed you might say to this tree Be rooted up and planted in the sea and it would be done
Luk  But which of you having a servant who is ploughing or keeping sheep will say to him when he comes in from the field Come now and be seated and have a meal
Luk  Will he not say Get a meal for me and make yourself ready and see to my needs till I have had my food and drink and after that you may have yours
Luk  Does he give praise to the servant because he did what was ordered
Luk  In the same way when you have done all the things which are given you to do say There is no profit in us for we have only done what we were ordered to do
Luk  And it came about that when they were on the way to Jerusalem he went through Samaria and Galilee
Luk  And when he went into a certain small town he came across ten men who were lepers and they keeping themselves at a distance
Luk  Said in loud voices Jesus Master have mercy on us
Luk  And when he saw them he said Go and let the priests see you And while they were going they were made clean
Luk  And one of them when he saw that he was clean turning back gave praise to God in a loud voice
Luk  And falling down on his face at the feet of Jesus he gave the credit to him and he was a man of Samaria
Luk  And Jesus said Were there not ten men who were made clean where are the nine
Luk  Have not any of them come back to give glory to God but only this one from a strange land
Luk  And he said to him Get up and go on your way your faith has made you well
Luk  And when the Pharisees put questions to him about when the kingdom of God would come he gave them an answer and said The kingdom of God will not come through observation
Luk  And men will not say See it is here or There for the kingdom of God is among you
Luk  And he said to his disciples The time will come when you will have a great desire to see one of the days of the Son of man but you will not see it
Luk  And if they say to you See it is there or It is here do not go away or go after them
Luk  For as in a thunderstorm the bright light is seen from one end of the sky to the other so will the Son of man be when his time comes
Luk  But first he will have to undergo much and be put on one side by this generation
Luk  And as it was in the days of Noah so will it be in the day of the Son of man
Luk  They were feasting and taking wives and getting married till the day of the overflowing of the waters when Noah went into the ark and they all came to destruction
Luk  In the same way in the days of Lot they were feasting and trading they were planting and building
Luk  But on the day when Lot went out of Sodom fire came down from heaven and destruction came on them all
Luk  So will it be in the day of the revelation of the Son of man
Luk  On that day if anyone is on the roof of the house and his goods are in the house let him not go down to take them away and let him who is in the field not go back to his house
Luk  Keep in mind Lots wife
Luk  If anyone makes an attempt to keep his life it will be taken from him but if anyone gives up his life he will keep it
Luk  I say to you In that night there will be two men sleeping in one bed and one will be taken away and the other let go
Luk  Two women will be crushing grain together one will be taken away and the other let go

Luk  And they answering him said Where Lord And he said to them Where the body is there will the eagles come together
Luk  And he made a story for them the point of which was that men were to go on making prayer and not get tired
Luk  Saying There was a judge in a certain town who had no fear of God or respect for man
Luk  And there was a widow in that town and she kept on coming to him and saying Give me my right against the man who has done me wrong
Luk  And for a time he would not but later he said to himself Though I have no fear of God or respect for man
Luk  Because this widow is a trouble to me I will give her her right for if not I will be completely tired out by her frequent coming
Luk  And the Lord said Give ear to the words of the evil judge
Luk  And will not God do right in the cause of his saints whose cries come day and night to his ears though he is long in doing it
Luk  I say to you that he will quickly do right in their cause But when the Son of man comes will there be any faith on earth

Luk  The Pharisee taking up his position said to himself these words God I give you praise because I am not like other men who take more than their right who are evildoers who are untrue to their wives or even like this taxfarmer
Luk  Twice in the week I go without food I give a tenth of all I have
Luk  The taxfarmer on the other hand keeping far away and not lifting up even his eyes to heaven made signs of grief and said God have mercy on me a sinner

Luk  And they took their children to him so that he might put his hands on them but when the disciples saw it they said sharp words to them

Luk  You have knowledge of what the law says Do not be untrue to your wife Do not put anyone to death Do not take what is not yours Do not give false witness Give honour to your father and mother
Luk  And he said All these things I have done from the time when I was a boy
Luk  And Jesus hearing it said to him One thing you still have need of get money for your goods and give it away to the poor and you will have wealth in heaven and come after me
Luk  But at these words he became very sad for he had great wealth
Luk  And Jesus looking at him said How hard it is for those who have wealth to get into the kingdom of God
Luk  It is simpler for a camel to go through the eye of a needle than for a man who has much money to come into the kingdom of God
Luk  And those who were present said Then who may have salvation
Luk  But he said Things which are not possible with man are possible with God

Luk  And he will be given cruel blows and put to death and on the third day he will come back to life
Luk  But they did not take in the sense of any of these words and what he said was not clear to them and their minds were not able to see it
Luk  And it came about that when he got near Jericho a certain blind man was seated by the side of the road making requests for money from those who went by

Luk  And straight away he was able to see and he went after him giving glory to God and all the people when they saw it gave praise to God
Luk  And he went into Jericho and when he was going through it

Luk  For the Son of man came to make search for those who are wandering from the way and to be their Saviour
Luk  And while they were giving ear to these words he made another story for them because he was near Jerusalem and because they were of the opinion that the kingdom of God was coming straight away
Luk  So he said A certain man of high birth went into a faraway country to get a kingdom for himself and to come back
Luk  And he sent for ten of his servants and gave them ten pounds and said to them Do business with this till I come
Luk  But his people had no love for him and sent representatives after him saying We will not have this man for our ruler
Luk  And when he came back again having got his kingdom he gave orders for those servants to whom he had given the money to come to him so that he might have an account of what business they had done
Luk  And the first came before him saying Lord your pound has made ten pounds
Luk  And he said to him You have done well O good servant because you have done well in a small thing you will have authority over ten towns
Luk  And another came saying Your pound has made five pounds
Luk  And he said You will be ruler over five towns
Luk  And another came saying Lord here is your pound which I put away in a cloth
Luk  Because I was in fear of you for you are a hard man you take up what you have not put down and get in grain where you have not put seed
Luk  He said to him By the words of your mouth you will be judged you bad servant You had knowledge that I am a hard man taking up what I have not put down and getting in grain where I have not put seed
Luk  Why then did you not put my money in a bank so that when I came I would get it back with interest
Luk  And he said to the others who were near Take the pound away from him and give it to the man who has ten
Luk  And they say to him Lord he has ten pounds
Luk  And I say to you that to everyone who has more will be given but from him who has not even what he has will be taken away

Luk  And when he had said this he went on in front of them going up to Jerusalem
Luk  And it came about that when he got near Bethphage and Bethany by the mountain which is named the Mountain of Olives he sent two of the disciples

Luk  And if anyone says to you Why are you taking him say The Lord has need of him
Luk  And those whom he sent went away and it was as he said
Luk  And when they were getting the young ass the owners of it said to them Why are you taking the young ass
Luk  And they said The Lord has need of him
Luk  And they took him to Jesus and they put their clothing on the ass and Jesus got on to him
Luk  And while he went on his way they put their clothing down on the road in front of him
Luk  And when he came near the foot of the Mountain of Olives all the disciples with loud voices gave praise to God with joy because of all the great works which they had seen

Luk  And some of the Pharisees among the people said to him Master make your disciples be quiet

Luk  And he went into the Temple and put out those who were trading there

Luk  But they were not able to do anything because the people all kept near him being greatly interested in his words
Luk  And it came about on one of those days when he was teaching the people in the Temple and preaching the good news
Luk  That the chief priests and the scribes and the rulers of the people came to him and said Make clear to us by what authority you do these things and who gave you this authority
Luk  And in answer he said to them I will put a question to you and do you give me an answer
Luk  The baptism of John was it from heaven or of men

Luk  And he gave the people this story A man made a vinegarden and gave the use of it to some fieldworkers and went into another country for a long time
Luk  And at the right time he sent a servant to the workers to get part of the fruit from the vines but the workmen gave him blows and sent him away with nothing

Luk  And he sent a third and they gave him wounds and put him out

Luk  And they put a question to him saying Master we are certain that your teaching and your words are right and that you have no respect for a mans position but you are teaching the true way of God

Luk  And some of the Sadducees came to him who say that there is no coming back from the dead and they said to him

Luk  And the third took her and in the same way all the seven without having any children came to their end

Luk  And in the hearing of all the people he said to his disciples

Luk  And looking up he saw the men of wealth putting their offerings in the moneybox

Luk  And some were talking about the Temple how it was made fair with beautiful stones and with offerings but he said
