Luk  Then he said to them Nation will be moved against nation and kingdom against kingdom
Luk  There will be great earthshocks and outbursts of disease in a number of places and men will be without food and there will be wonders and great signs from heaven
Luk  But before all this they will take you and be very cruel to you giving you up to the Synagogues and to prisons taking you before kings and rulers because of my name
Luk  And it will be turned to a witness for you
Luk  So take care not to be troubled before the time comes about what answers you will give
Luk  For I will give you words and wisdom so that not one of those who are against you will be able to get the better of you or to put you in the wrong
Luk  But you will be given up even by your fathers and mothers your brothers and relations and friends and some of you will be put to death
Luk  And you will be hated by all men because of me
Luk  But not a hair of your head will come to destruction
Luk  By going through all these things you will keep your lives
Luk  But when you see armies all round about Jerusalem then be certain that her destruction is near
Luk  Then let those who are in Judaea go in flight to the mountains and those who are in the middle of the town go out and let not those who are in the country come in
Luk  For these are the days of punishment in which all the things in the Writings will be put into effect
Luk  It will be hard for women who are with child and for her with a baby at the breast in those days For great trouble will come on the land and wrath on this people
Luk  And they will be put to death with the sword and will be taken as prisoners into all the nations and Jerusalem will be crushed under the feet of the Gentiles till the times of the Gentiles are complete
Luk  And there will be signs in the sun and moon and stars and on the earth fear among the nations and doubt because of the loud noise of the sea and the waves
Luk  Mens strength will go from them in fear and in waiting for the things which are coming on the earth for the powers of the heavens will be moved
Luk  And then they will see the Son of man coming in a cloud with power and great glory
Luk  But when these things come about let your heads be lifted up because your salvation is near
Luk  And he made a story for them See the figtree and all the trees
Luk  When they put out their young leaves you take note of it and it is clear to you that summer is coming
Luk  In the same way when you see these things taking place you may be certain that the kingdom of God is near
Luk  Truly I say to you This generation will not come to an end till all things are complete
Luk  Heaven and earth will come to an end but my words will not come to an end
Luk  But give attention to yourselves for fear that your hearts become overfull of the pleasures of food and wine and the cares of this life and that day may come on you suddenly and take you as in a net
Luk  For so it will come on all those who are living on the face of all the earth
Luk  But keep watch at all times with prayer that you may be strong enough to come through all these things and take your place before the Son of man
Luk  And every day he was teaching in the Temple and every night he went out to the mountain which is named the Mountain of Olives to take his rest
Luk  And all the people came early in the morning to give ear to his words in the Temple
Luk  Now the feast of unleavened bread was near which is called the Passover

Jhn  From the first he was the Word and the Word was in relation with God and was God
Jhn  This Word was from the first in relation with God
Jhn  All things came into existence through him and without him nothing was
Jhn  What came into existence in him was life and the life was the light of men
Jhn  And the light goes on shining in the dark it is not overcome by the dark
Jhn  There was a man sent from God whose name was John
Jhn  He came for witness to give witness about the light so that all men might have faith through him
Jhn  He himself was not the light he was sent to give witness about the light
Jhn  The true light which gives light to every man was then coming into the world
Jhn  He was in the world the world which came into being through him but the world had no knowledge of him
Jhn  He came to the things which were his and his people did not take him to their hearts
Jhn  To all those who did so take him however he gave the right of becoming children of Godthat is to those who had faith in his name
Jhn  Whose birth was from God and not from blood or from an impulse of the flesh and mans desire
Jhn  And so the Word became flesh and took a place among us for a time and we saw his glorysuch glory as is given to an only son by his fathersaw it to be true and full of grace
Jhn  John gave witness about him crying This is he of whom I said He who is coming after me is put over me because he was in existence before me
Jhn  From his full measure we have all been given grace on grace
Jhn  For the law was given through Moses grace and the true way of life are ours through Jesus Christ
Jhn  No man has seen God at any time the only Son who is on the breast of the Father he has made clear what God is
Jhn  And this is the witness of John when the Jews sent priests and Levites from Jerusalem to him with the question Who are you
Jhn  He said quite openly and straightforwardly I am not the Christ
Jhn  And they said to him What then Are you Elijah And he said I am not Are you the prophet And his answer was I am not
Jhn  So they said to him Who are you then We have to give some answer to those who sent us What have you to say about yourself
Jhn  He said I am the voice of one crying in the waste land Make straight the way of the Lord as said Isaiah the prophet
Jhn  Those who had been sent came from the Pharisees
Jhn  And they put this question to him saying Why then are you giving baptism if you are not the Christ or Elijah or the prophet
Jhn  Johns answer was I give baptism with water but there is one among you of whom you have no knowledge
Jhn  It is he who is coming after me I am not good enough to undo his shoes
Jhn  These things took place at Bethany on the other side of the Jordan where John was giving baptism
Jhn  The day after John sees Jesus coming to him and says See here is the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world
Jhn  This is he of whom I said One is coming after me who is put over me because he was in existence before me
Jhn  I myself had no knowledge of him but I came giving baptism with water so that he might be seen openly by Israel
Jhn  And John gave this witness saying I saw the Spirit coming down from heaven like a dove and resting on him
Jhn  I had no knowledge who he was but he who sent me to give baptism with water said to me The one on whom you see the Spirit coming down and resting it is he who gives baptism with the Holy Spirit
Jhn  This I saw myself and my witness is that he is the Son of God
Jhn  The day after John was there again with two of his disciples
Jhn  And looking at Jesus while he was walking he said See there is the Lamb of God
Jhn  Hearing what he said the two disciples went after Jesus
Jhn  And Jesus turning round saw them coming after him and said to them What are you looking for They said to him Rabbi which is to say Master where are you living
Jhn  He said to them Come and see They went with him then and saw where he was living and they were with him all that day it was then about the tenth hour of the day
Jhn  Andrew Simon Peters brother was one of the two men who hearing what John said went after Jesus
Jhn  Early in the morning he came across his brother and said to him We have made discovery It is the Messiah which is to say the Christ
Jhn  And he took him to Jesus Looking at him fixedly Jesus said You are Simon the son of John your name will be Cephas which is to say Peter
Jhn  The day after this Jesus had a desire to go into Galilee He came across Philip and said to him Come and be my disciple
Jhn  Now Philips town was Bethsaida where Andrew and Peter came from
Jhn  Philip came across Nathanael and said to him We have made a discovery It is he of whom Moses in the law and the prophets were writing Jesus of Nazareth the son of Joseph
Jhn  Nazareth said Nathanael Is it possible for any good to come out of Nazareth Philip said to him Come and see
Jhn  Jesus saw Nathanael coming to him and said of him See here is a true son of Israel in whom there is nothing false
Jhn  Nathanael said to him Where did you get knowledge of me In answer Jesus said Before Philip was talking with you while you were still under the figtree I saw you
Jhn  Nathanael said to him Rabbi you are the Son of God you are King of Israel
Jhn  In answer Jesus said to him You have faith because I said to you I saw you under the figtree You will see greater things than these
Jhn  And he said to him Truly I say to you all You will see heaven opening and Gods angels going up and coming down on the Son of man
Jhn  On the third day two people were going to be married at Cana in Galilee The mother of Jesus was there
Jhn  And Jesus with his disciples came as guests
Jhn  When they had not enough wine the mother of Jesus said to him They have no wine
Jhn  Jesus said to her Woman this is not your business my time is still to come
Jhn  His mother said to the servants Whatever he says to you do it
Jhn  Now six pots of stone every one taking two or three firkins of water were placed there for the purpose of washing as is the way of the Jews
Jhn  Jesus said to the servants Make the pots full of water And they made them full to the top
Jhn  Then he said to them Now take some and give it to the master of the feast So they took it to him
Jhn  After tasting the water which had now become wine the master of the feast having no idea where it came from though it was clear to the servants who took the water out sent for the newlymarried man
Jhn  And said to him Every man first puts out his best wine and when all have had enough he puts out what is not so good but you have kept the good wine till now
Jhn  This the first of his signs Jesus did at Cana in Galilee and let his glory be seen openly and his disciples put their faith in him
Jhn  After this he went down to Capernaum with his mother his brothers and his disciples and they were there not more than two or three days
Jhn  The time of the Passover of the Jews was near and Jesus went up to Jerusalem
Jhn  And there in the Temple he saw men trading in oxen and sheep and doves and he saw the changers of money in their seats
Jhn  And he made a whip of small cords and put them all out of the Temple with the sheep and the oxen sending in all directions the small money of the changers and overturning their tables
Jhn  And to those who were trading in doves he said Take these things away do not make my Fathers house a market
Jhn  And it came to the minds of the disciples that the Writings say I am on fire with passion for your house
Jhn  Then the Jews put this question to him What sign of authority have you to give us seeing that you do these things
Jhn  And Jesus said to them Send destruction on this Temple and I will put it up again in three days
Jhn  The Jews said The building of this Temple took fortysix years and you will put it up in three days
Jhn  But his words were about that holy building which was his body
Jhn  So when he had come back again from the dead the memory of these words came back to the disciples and they had faith in the holy Writings and in the word which Jesus had said
Jhn  Now while he was in Jerusalem at the feast of the Passover a great number of people came to have faith in his name after seeing the signs which he did
Jhn  But Jesus did not have faith in them because he had knowledge of them all
Jhn  He had no need for any witness about man for he himself had knowledge of what was in man
Jhn  Now there was among the Pharisees a man named Nicodemus who was one of the rulers of the Jews
Jhn  He came to Jesus by night and said to him Rabbi we are certain that you have come from God as a teacher because no man would be able to do these signs which you do if God was not with him
Jhn  Jesus said to him Truly I say to you Without a new birth no man is able to see the kingdom of God
Jhn  Nicodemus said to him How is it possible for a man to be given birth when he is old Is he able to go into his mothers body a second time and come to birth again
Jhn  Jesus said in answer Truly I say to you If a mans birth is not from water and from the Spirit it is not possible for him to go into the kingdom of God
Jhn  That which has birth from the flesh is flesh and that which has birth from the Spirit is spirit
Jhn  Do not be surprised that I say to you It is necessary for you to have a second birth
Jhn  The wind goes where its pleasure takes it and the sound of it comes to your ears but you are unable to say where it comes from and where it goes so it is with everyone whose birth is from the Spirit
Jhn  And Nicodemus said to him How is it possible for these things to be
Jhn  And Jesus answering said Are you the teacher of Israel and have no knowledge of these things
Jhn  Truly I say to you We say that of which we have knowledge we give witness of what we have seen and you do not take our witness to be true
Jhn  If you have no belief when my words are about the things of earth how will you have belief if my words are about the things of heaven
Jhn  And no one has ever gone up to heaven but he who came down from heaven the Son of man
Jhn  As the snake was lifted up by Moses in the waste land even so it is necessary for the Son of man to be lifted up
Jhn  So that whoever has faith may have in him eternal life
Jhn  For God had such love for the world that he gave his only Son so that whoever has faith in him may not come to destruction but have eternal life
Jhn  God did not send his Son into the world to be judge of the world he sent him so that the world might have salvation through him
Jhn  The man who has faith in him does not come up to be judged but he who has no faith in him has been judged even now because he has no faith in the name of the only Son of God
Jhn  And this is the test by which men are judged the light has come into the world and men have more love for the dark than for the light because their acts are evil
Jhn  The light is hated by everyone whose acts are evil and he does not come to the light for fear that his acts will be seen
Jhn  But he whose life is true comes to the light so that it may be clearly seen that his acts have been done by the help of God
Jhn  After these things Jesus and his disciples went into the land of Judaea and there he was with them for some time giving baptism
Jhn  Now John was then giving baptism at Aenon near Salim because there was much water there and people came and were given baptism
Jhn  For at this time John had not been put into prison
Jhn  Then a question came up between Johns disciples and a Jew about washing
Jhn  And they went to John and said to him Rabbi the man who was with you on the other side of the Jordan the man to whom you gave witness is now giving baptism and everyone is going to him
Jhn  And this was Johns answer A man is unable to have anything if it is not given to him from heaven
Jhn  You yourselves give witness that I said I am not the Christ What I said was I am sent before the Christ
Jhn  He who has the bride is the husband but the husbands friend whose place is by his side and whose ears are open to him is full of joy because of the husbands voice such is my joy and it is complete
Jhn  He has to become greater while I become less
Jhn  He who comes from heaven is greater than all others he who comes from earth is of the earth and of the earth are his words he who comes from heaven is over all
Jhn  He gives witness of what he has seen and of what has come to his ears and no man takes his witness as true
Jhn  He who so takes his witness has made clear his faith that God is true
Jhn  For he whom God has sent says Gods words and God does not give him the Spirit by measure
Jhn  The Father has love for the Son and has put all things into his hands
Jhn  He who has faith in the Son has eternal life but he who has not faith in the Son will not see life Gods wrath is resting on him
Jhn  Now when it was clear to the Lord that word had come to the ears of the Pharisees that Jesus was making more disciples than John and was giving them baptism
Jhn  Though in fact it was his disciples who gave baptism not Jesus himself
Jhn  He went out of Judaea into Galilee again
Jhn  And it was necessary for him to go through Samaria
Jhn  So he came to a town of Samaria which was named Sychar near to the bit of land which Jacob gave to his son Joseph
Jhn  Now Jacobs fountain was there Jesus being tired after his journey was resting by the fountain It was about the sixth hour
Jhn  A woman of Samaria came to get water and Jesus said to her Give me some water
Jhn  For his disciples had gone to the town to get food
Jhn  The woman of Samaria said to him Why do you a Jew make a request for water to me a woman of Samaria She said this because Jews have nothing to do with the people of Samaria
Jhn  In answer Jesus said If you had knowledge of what God gives freely and who it is who says to you Give me water you would make your prayer to him and he would give you living water
Jhn  The woman said to him Sir you have no vessel and the fountain is deep from where will you get the living water
Jhn  Are you greater than our father Jacob who gave us the fountain and took the water of it himself with his children and his cattle
Jhn  Jesus said to her Everyone who takes this water will be in need of it again
Jhn  But whoever takes the water I give him will never be in need of drink again for the water I give him will become in him a fountain of eternal life
Jhn  The woman said to him Sir give me this water so that I may not be in need again of drink and will not have to come all this way for it
Jhn  Jesus said to her Go get your husband and come back here with him
Jhn  In answer the woman said I have no husband Jesus said to her You have said rightly I have no husband
Jhn  You have had five husbands and the man you have now is not your husband that was truly said
Jhn  The woman said to him Sir I see that you are a prophet
Jhn  Our fathers gave worship on this mountain but you Jews say that the right place for worship is in Jerusalem
Jhn  Jesus said to her Woman take my word for this the time is coming when you will not give worship to the Father on this mountain or in Jerusalem
Jhn  You give worship but without knowledge of what you are worshipping we give worship to what we have knowledge of for salvation comes from the Jews
Jhn  But the time is coming and is even now here when the true worshippers will give worship to the Father in the true way of the spirit for these are the worshippers desired by the Father
Jhn  God is Spirit then let his worshippers give him worship in the true way of the spirit
Jhn  The woman said to him I am certain that the Messiah who is named Christ is coming when he comes he will make all things clear to us
Jhn  Jesus said to her I who am talking to you am he
Jhn  At that point the disciples came back and they were surprised to see him talking to a woman but not one of them said to him What is your purpose or Why are you talking to her
Jhn  Then the woman put down her waterpot and went into the town and said to the people
Jhn  Come and see a man who has been talking to me of everything I ever did Is it possible that this is the Christ
Jhn  So they went out of the town and came to him
Jhn  While this was taking place the disciples were saying to Jesus Master take some food
Jhn  But he said to them I have food of which you have no knowledge
Jhn  So the disciples said one to another Did anyone give him food
Jhn  Jesus said My food is to do the pleasure of him who sent me and to make his work complete
Jhn  You would say Four months from now is the time of the graincutting Take a look I say to you at the fields they are even now white for cutting
Jhn  He who does the cutting now has his reward he is getting together fruit for eternal life so that he who did the planting and he who gets in the grain may have joy together
Jhn  In this the saying is a true one One does the planting and another gets in the grain
Jhn  I sent you to get in grain which you had no hand in planting other men did that work and you take the reward
Jhn  Now a number of the people of that town had faith in him because of the womans witness He has been talking to me of everything I ever did
Jhn  So when the people came to him they made request to him to be among them for a time and he was there two days
Jhn  And a great number more of them came to have faith in him because of what he himself said
Jhn  And they said to the woman Now we have faith but not because of your story we ourselves have given ear to his words and we are certain that he is truly the Saviour of the world
Jhn  And after the two days he went on from there into Galilee
Jhn  For Jesus himself said that a prophet has no honour in the country of his birth
Jhn  So when he came into Galilee the Galilaeans took him to their hearts because of the things which they had seen him do in Jerusalem at the feastthey themselves having been there at the feast
Jhn  So he came to Cana in Galilee where he had made the water wine And there was a certain man of high position whose son was ill at Capernaum
Jhn  When it came to his ears that Jesus had come from Judaea into Galilee he went to him and made a request that he would come down to his son who was near to death and make him well
Jhn  Then Jesus said to him You will not have faith if you do not see signs and wonders
Jhn  The man said Sir come down before my boy is dead
Jhn  And Jesus said Go in peace your son is living The man had faith in the word which Jesus said to him and went away
Jhn  And while he was going down his servants came to him and said Your boy is living
Jhn  So he put a question to them as to the hour when he became better and they said to him The disease went from him yesterday at the seventh hour
Jhn  It was clear then to the father that this was the very time at which Jesus said to him Your son is living And he had faith in Jesus he and all his family
Jhn  Now this is the second sign which Jesus did after he had come out of Judaea into Galilee
Jhn  After these things there was a feast of the Jews and Jesus went up to Jerusalem
Jhn  Now in Jerusalem near the sheepmarket there is a public bath which in Hebrew is named Bethzatha It has five doorways
Jhn  In these doorways there were a great number of people with different diseases some unable to see some without the power of walking some with wasted bodies
Jhn  
Jhn  One man was there who had been ill for thirtyeight years
Jhn  When Jesus saw him there on the floor it was clear to him that he had been now a long time in that condition and so he said to the man Is it your desire to get well
Jhn  The ill man said in answer Sir I have nobody to put me into the bath when the water is moving and while I am on the way down some other person gets in before me
Jhn  Jesus said to him Get up take your bed and go
Jhn  And the man became well straight away and took up his bed and went Now that day was the Sabbath
Jhn  So the Jews said to the man who had been made well It is the Sabbath and it is against the law for you to take up your bed
Jhn  He said to them But he who made me well said to me Take up your bed and go
Jhn  Then they put to him the question Who is the man who said to you Take it up and go
Jhn  Now he who had been made well had no knowledge who it was Jesus having gone away because of the number of people who were in that place
Jhn  After a time Jesus came across him in the Temple and said to him See you are well and strong do no more sin for fear a worse thing comes to you
Jhn  The man went away and said to the Jews that it was Jesus who had made him well
Jhn  And for this reason the Jews were turned against Jesus because he was doing these things on the Sabbath
Jhn  But his answer was My Father is still working even now and so I am working
Jhn  For this cause the Jews had an even greater desire to put Jesus to death because not only did he not keep the Sabbath but he said God was his Father so making himself equal with God
Jhn  So Jesus made answer and said Truly I say to you The Son is not able to do anything himself he is able to do only what he sees the Father doing whatever the Father does the Son does it in the same way
Jhn  For the Father has love for the Son and lets him see everything which he does and he will let him see greater works than these so that you may be full of wonder
Jhn  In the same way as the Father gives life to the dead even so the Son gives life to those to whom he is pleased to give it
Jhn  The Father is not the judge of men but he has given all decisions into the hands of the Son
Jhn  So that all men may give honour to the Son even as they give honour to the Father He who gives no honour to the Son gives no honour to the Father who sent him
Jhn  Truly I say to you The man whose ears are open to my word and who has faith in him who sent me has eternal life he will not be judged but has come from death into life
Jhn  Truly I say to you The time is coming it has even now come when the voice of the Son of God will come to the ears of the dead and those hearing it will have life
Jhn  For even as the Father has life in himself so he has given to the Son to have life in himself
Jhn  And he has given him authority to be judge because he is the Son of man
Jhn  Do not be surprised at this for the time is coming when his voice will come to all who are in the place of the dead
Jhn  And they will come out those who have done good into the new life and those who have done evil to be judged
Jhn  Of myself I am unable to do anything as the voice comes to me so I give a decision and my decision is right because I have no desire to do what is pleasing to myself but only what is pleasing to him who sent me
Jhn  If I gave witness about myself my witness would not be true
Jhn  There is another who gives witness about me and I am certain that the witness he gives about me is true
Jhn  You sent to John and he gave true witness
Jhn  But I have no need of a mans witness I only say these things so that you may have salvation
Jhn  He was a burning and shining light and for a time you were ready to be happy in his light
Jhn  But the witness which I have is greater than that of John the work which the Father has given me to do the very work which I am now doing is a witness that the Father has sent me
Jhn  And the Father himself who sent me has given witness about me Not one of you has ever given ear to his voice his form you have not seen
Jhn  And you have not kept his word in your hearts because you have not faith in him whom he has sent
Jhn  You make search in the holy Writings in the belief that through them you get eternal life and it is those Writings which give witness about me
Jhn  And still you have no desire to come to me so that you may have life
Jhn  I do not take honour from men
Jhn  But I have knowledge of you that you have no love for God in your hearts
Jhn  I have come in my Fathers name and your hearts are not open to me If another comes with no other authority but himself you will give him your approval
Jhn  How is it possible for you to have faith while you take honour one from another and have no desire for the honour which comes from the only God
Jhn  Put out of your minds the thought that I will say things against you to the Father the one who says things against you is Moses on whom you put your hopes
Jhn  If you had belief in Moses you would have belief in me for his writings are about me
Jhn  If you have no belief in his writings how will you have belief in my words
Jhn  After these things Jesus went away to the other side of the sea of Galileethat is the sea of Tiberias
Jhn  And a great number of people went after him because they saw the signs which he did on those who were ill
Jhn  Then Jesus went up the mountain and was seated there with his disciples
Jhn  Now the Passover a feast of the Jews was near
Jhn  Lifting up his eyes Jesus saw a great number of people coming to where he was and he said to Philip Where may we get bread for all these people
Jhn  This he said testing him for he had no doubt what he himself would do
Jhn  Philip made answer Bread to the value of two hundred pence would not be enough even to give everyone a little
Jhn  One of his disciples Andrew the brother of Simon Peter said to Jesus
Jhn  There is a boy here with five barley cakes and two fishes but what is that among such a number
Jhn  Jesus said Let the people be seated Now there was much grass in that place And those seated on the grass were about five thousand
Jhn  Then Jesus took the cakes and having given praise to God he gave them to the people who were seated and the fishes in the same way as much as they had need of
Jhn  And when they had had enough Jesus said to his disciples Take up the broken bits which are over so that nothing may be wasted
Jhn  So they took them up twelve baskets full of broken bits of the five cakes which were over after the people had had enough
Jhn  And when the people saw the sign which he had done they said Truly this is the prophet who is to come into the world
Jhn  Now when Jesus saw that the people were about to come and take him by force to make him a king he went away again up the mountain by himself
Jhn  When evening came the disciples went down to the sea
Jhn  And they took a boat and went across the sea in the direction of Capernaum By then it was dark and still Jesus had not come to them
Jhn  The sea was getting rough because of a strong wind which was blowing
Jhn  After they had gone three or four miles they saw Jesus walking on the sea and coming near to the boat and they had great fear
Jhn  But he said to them It is I have no fear
Jhn  Then they readily took him into the boat and straight away the boat was at the land to which they were going
Jhn  The day after the people who were on the other side of the sea saw that only one small boat had been there that Jesus had not gone in that boat with the disciples but that the disciples had gone away by themselves
Jhn  Some other boats however came from Tiberias near to the place where they had taken the bread after the Lord had given praise
Jhn  So when the people saw that Jesus was not there or his disciples they got into those boats and went over to Capernaum looking for Jesus
Jhn  And when they came across him on the other side of the sea they said Rabbi when did you come here
Jhn  Jesus answering them said Truly I say to you You come after me not because you saw signs but because you were given the bread and had enough
Jhn  Let your work not be for the food which comes to an end but for the food which goes on for eternal life which the Son of man will give to you for on him has God the Father put his mark
Jhn  Then they said to him How may we do the works of God
Jhn  Jesus answering said to them This is to do the work of God to have faith in him whom God has sent
Jhn  So they said What sign do you give us so that we may see and have faith in you What do you do
Jhn  Our fathers had the manna in the waste land as the Writings say He gave them bread from heaven
Jhn  Jesus then said to them Truly I say to you What Moses gave you was not the bread from heaven it is my Father who gives you the true bread from heaven
Jhn  The bread of God is the bread which comes down out of heaven and gives life to the world
Jhn  Ah Lord they said give us that bread for ever
Jhn  And this was the answer of Jesus I am the bread of life He who comes to me will never be in need of food and he who has faith in me will never be in need of drink
Jhn  But it is as I said to you you have seen me and still you have no faith
Jhn  Whatever the Father gives to me will come to me and I will not send away anyone who comes to me
Jhn  For I have come down from heaven not to do my pleasure but the pleasure of him who sent me
Jhn  And this is the pleasure of him who sent me that I am not to let out of my hands anything which he has given me but I am to give it new life on the last day
Jhn  This I say is my Fathers pleasure that everyone who sees the Son and has faith in him may have eternal life and I will take him up on the last day
Jhn  Now the Jews said bitter things about Jesus because of his words I am the bread which came down from heaven
Jhn  And they said Is not this Jesus the son of Joseph whose father and mother we have seen How is it then that he now says I have come down from heaven
Jhn  Jesus made answer and said Do not say things against me one to another
Jhn  No man is able to come to me if the Father who sent me does not give him the desire to come and I will take him up from the dead on the last day
Jhn  The writings of the prophets say And they will all have teaching from God Everyone whose ears have been open to the teaching of the Father comes to me
Jhn  Not that anyone has ever seen the Father only he who is from God he has seen the Father
Jhn  Truly I say to you He who has faith in me has eternal life
Jhn  I am the bread of life
Jhn  Your fathers took the manna in the waste landand they are dead
Jhn  The bread which comes from heaven is such bread that a man may take it for food and never see death
Jhn  I am the living bread which has come from heaven if any man takes this bread for food he will have life for ever and more than this the bread which I will give is my flesh which I will give for the life of the world
Jhn  Then the Jews had an angry discussion among themselves saying How is it possible for this man to give us his flesh for food
Jhn  Then Jesus said to them Truly I say to you If you do not take the flesh of the Son of man for food and if you do not take his blood for drink you have no life in you
Jhn  He who takes my flesh for food and my blood for drink has eternal life and I will take him up from the dead at the last day
Jhn  My flesh is true food and my blood is true drink
Jhn  He who takes my flesh for food and my blood for drink is in me and I in him
Jhn  As the living Father has sent me and I have life because of the Father even so he who takes me for his food will have life because of me
Jhn  This is the bread which has come down from heaven It is not like the food which your fathers had they took of the manna and are dead but he who takes this bread for food will have life for ever
Jhn  Jesus said these things in the Synagogue while he was teaching at Capernaum
Jhn  Then hearing this a number of his disciples said This is a hard saying who is able to take in such teaching
Jhn  When Jesus became conscious that his disciples were protesting about what he said he said to them Does this give you trouble
Jhn  What then will you say if you see the Son of man going up to where he was before
Jhn  The spirit is the life giver the flesh is of no value the words which I have said to you are spirit and they are life
Jhn  But still some of you have no faith For it was clear to Jesus from the first who they were who had no faith and who it was who would be false to him
Jhn  And he said This is why I said to you No man is able to come to me if he is not given the power to do so by the Father
Jhn  Because of what he said a number of the disciples went back and would no longer go with him
Jhn  So Jesus said to the twelve Have you a desire to go away
Jhn  Then Simon Peter gave this answer Lord to whom are we to go you have the words of eternal life
Jhn  And we have faith and are certain that you are the Holy One of God
Jhn  Then Jesus said Did I not make a selection of you the twelve and one of you is a son of the Evil One
Jhn  He was talking of Judas the son of Simon Iscariot It was he who was to be false to Jesusone of the twelve
Jhn  After this Jesus went from place to place in Galilee He did not go about in Judaea because the Jews were looking for a chance to put him to death
Jhn  But the feast of the Jews the feast of tents was near
Jhn  So his brothers said to him Go away from here into Judaea so that your disciples may see the works which you do
Jhn  Because no man does things secretly if he has a desire that men may have knowledge of him If you do these things let yourself be seen by all men
Jhn  For even his brothers had no belief in him
Jhn  Jesus said to them My time is still to come but any time is good for you
Jhn  It is not possible for you to be hated by the world but I am hated by it because I give witness that what it does is evil
Jhn  Go you up to the feast I am not going up now to the feast because my time has not fully come
Jhn  Having said these things to them he still kept in Galilee
Jhn  But after his brothers had gone up to the feast then he went up not publicly but in secret
Jhn  At the feast the Jews were looking for him and saying Where is he
Jhn  And there was much discussion about him among the mass of the people Some said He is a good man but others said No he is giving people false ideas
Jhn  But no man said anything about him openly for fear of the Jews
Jhn  Now in the middle of the feast Jesus went up to the Temple and was teaching
Jhn  Then the Jews were surprised and said How has this man got knowledge of books He has never been to school
Jhn  Jesus gave them this answer It is not my teaching but his who sent me
Jhn  If any man is ready to do Gods pleasure he will have knowledge of the teaching and of where it comes fromfrom God or from myself
Jhn  The man whose words come from himself is looking for glory for himself but he who is looking for the glory of him who sent himthat man is true and there is no evil in him
Jhn  Did not Moses give you the law Even so not one of you keeps the law Why have you a desire to put me to death
Jhn  The people said in answer You have an evil spirit who has any desire to put you to death
Jhn  This was the answer of Jesus I have done one work and you are all surprised at it
Jhn  Moses gave you circumcisionnot that it comes from Moses but from the fathersand even on the Sabbath you give a child circumcision
Jhn  If a child is given circumcision on the Sabbath so that the law of Moses may not be broken why are you angry with me because I made a man completely well on the Sabbath
Jhn  Let not your decisions be based on what you see but on righteousness
Jhn  Then some of the people of Jerusalem said Is not this the man whose death is desired
Jhn  And here he is talking openly and they say nothing to him Is it possible that the rulers have knowledge that this is truly the Christ
Jhn  However it is clear to us where this man comes from but when the Christ comes no one will have knowledge where he comes from
Jhn  Then when he was teaching in the Temple Jesus said with a loud voice You have knowledge of me and you have knowledge of where I come from and I have not come of myself but there is One who has sent me he is true but you have no knowledge of him
Jhn  I have knowledge of him because I came from him and he sent me
Jhn  Then they had a desire to take him but no man put hands on him because his hour was still to come
Jhn  And numbers of the people had belief in him and they said When the Christ comes will he do more signs than this man has done
Jhn  This discussion of the people came to the ears of the Pharisees and the chief priests and the Pharisees sent servants to take him
Jhn  Then Jesus said I will be with you a little longer and then I go to him who sent me
Jhn  You will be looking for me and you will not see me and where I am you may not come
Jhn  So the Jews said among themselves To what place is he going where we will not see him will he go to the Jews living among the Greeks and become the teacher of the Greeks
Jhn  What is this saying of his You will be looking for me and will not see me and where I am you may not come
Jhn  On the last day the great day of the feast Jesus got up and said in a loud voice If any man is in need of drink let him come to me and I will give it to him
Jhn  He who has faith in me out of his body as the Writings have said will come rivers of living water
Jhn  This he said of the Spirit which would be given to those who had faith in him the Spirit had not been given then because the glory of Jesus was still to come
Jhn  When these words came to their ears some of the people said This is certainly the prophet
Jhn  Others said This is the Christ But others said Not so will the Christ come from Galilee
Jhn  Do not the Writings say that the Christ comes of the seed of David and from Bethlehem the little town where David was
Jhn  So there was a division among the people because of him
Jhn  And some of them had a desire to take him but no man put hands on him
Jhn  Then the servants went back to the chief priests and Pharisees who said to them Why have you not got him with you
Jhn  The servants made answer No man ever said things like this man
Jhn  Then the Pharisees said to them Have you like the others been given false ideas
Jhn  Have any of the rulers belief in him or any one of the Pharisees
Jhn  But these people who have no knowledge of the law are cursed
Jhn  Nicodemushe who had come to Jesus before being himself one of themsaid to them
Jhn  Is a man judged by our law before it has given him a hearing and has knowledge of what he has done
Jhn  This was their answer And do you come from Galilee Make search and you will see that no prophet comes out of Galilee
Jhn  And every man went to his house
Jhn  But Jesus went to the Mountain of Olives
Jhn  And early in the morning he came again into the Temple and all the people came to him and he was seated teaching them
Jhn  Now the scribes and Pharisees came with a woman who had been taken in the act of sinning against the married relation
Jhn  And putting her forward they said to him Master this woman has been taken in the very act of sinning against the married relation
Jhn  Now in the law Moses gave directions that such women were to be stoned what do you say about it
Jhn  They said this testing him so that they might have something against him But Jesus with his head bent down made letters on the floor with his finger
Jhn  But when they went on with their questions he got up and said to them Let him among you who is without sin be the first to send a stone at her
Jhn  And again with bent head he made letters on the floor
Jhn  And when his words came to their ears they went out one by one starting with the oldest even to the last because they were conscious of what was in their hearts and Jesus was there by himself with the woman before him
Jhn  Then Jesus got up and seeing nobody but the woman he said to her Where are the men who said things against you did no one give a decision against you
Jhn  And she said No man Lord And Jesus said And I do not give a decision against you go and never do wrong again
Jhn  Then again Jesus said to them I am the light of the world he who comes with me will not be walking in the dark but will have the light of life
Jhn  So the Pharisees said to him The witness you give is about yourself your witness is not true
Jhn  Jesus said in answer Even if I give witness about myself my witness is true because I have knowledge of where I came from and where I am going but you have no knowledge of where I come from or of where I am going
Jhn  You are judging from what you see I am judging no man
Jhn  Even if I am judging my decision is right because I am not by myselfwith me is the Father who sent me
Jhn  Even in your law it is said that the witness of two men is true
Jhn  I give witness about myself and the Father who sent me gives witness about me
Jhn  Then they said to him Where is your Father Jesus said in answer You have no knowledge of me or of my Father if you had knowledge of me you would have knowledge of my Father
Jhn  Jesus said these words in the place where the offerings were stored while he was teaching in the Temple but no man took him because his time was still to come
Jhn  Then he said to them again I am going away and you will be looking for me but death will overtake you in your sins It is not possible for you to come where I am going
Jhn  So the Jews said Will he take his life Is that why he says Where I go it is not possible for you to come
Jhn  And he said to them You are of the earth I am from heaven you are of this world I am not of this world
Jhn  For this reason I said to you that death will overtake you in your sins for if you have not faith that I am he death will come to you while you are in your sins
Jhn  Then they said to him Who are you Jesus said What I said to you from the first
Jhn  I have much to say about you and against you but he who sent me is true and what he has said to me I say to the world
Jhn  They did not see that his words were about the Father
Jhn  So Jesus said When the Son of man has been lifted up by you then it will be clear to you who I am and that I do nothing of myself but say as the Father gave me teaching
Jhn  He who sent me is with me he has not gone from me because at all times I do the things which are pleasing to him
Jhn  When he said this a number came to have faith in him
Jhn  Then Jesus said to the Jews who had faith in him If you keep my word then you are truly my disciples
Jhn  And you will have knowledge of what is true and that will make you free
Jhn  They said to him in answer We are Abrahams seed and have never been any mans servant why do you say You will become free
Jhn  And this was the answer Jesus gave them Truly I say to you Everyone who does evil is the servant of sin
Jhn  Now the servant does not go on living in the house for ever but the son does
Jhn  If then the son makes you free you will be truly free
Jhn  I am conscious that you are Abrahams seed but you have a desire to put me to death because my word has no place in you
Jhn  I say the things which I have seen in my Fathers house and you do the things which come to you from your fathers house
Jhn  In answer they said to him Our father is Abraham Jesus said to them If you were Abrahams children you would do what Abraham did
Jhn  But now you have a desire to put me to death a man who has said to you what is true as I had it from God Abraham did not do that
Jhn  You are doing the works of your father They said to him We are true sons of Abraham we have one Father who is God
Jhn  Jesus said to them If God was your Father you would have love for me because it was from God I came and am here I did not come of myself but he sent me
Jhn  Why are my words not clear to you It is because your ears are shut to my teaching
Jhn  You are the children of your father the Evil One and it is your pleasure to do his desires From the first he was a taker of life and he did not go in the true way because there is no true thing in him When he says what is false it is natural to him for he is false and the father of what is false
Jhn  But because I say what is true you have no belief in me
Jhn  Which of you is able truly to say that I am a sinner If I say what is true why have you no belief in me
Jhn  He who is a child of God gives ear to the words of God your ears are not open to them because you are not from God
Jhn  The Jews said to him in answer Are we not right in saying that you are of Samaria and have an evil spirit
Jhn  And this was the answer of Jesus I have not an evil spirit but I give honour to my Father and you do not give honour to me
Jhn  I however am not in search of glory for myself there is One who is searching for it and he is judge
Jhn  Truly I say to you If a man keeps my word he will never see death
Jhn  The Jews said to him Now we are certain that you have an evil spirit Abraham is dead and the prophets are dead and you say If a man keeps my word he will never see death
Jhn  Are you greater than our father Abraham who is dead and the prophets are dead who do you say that you are
Jhn  Jesus said in answer If I take glory for myself my glory is nothing it is my Father who gives me glory of whom you say that he is your God
Jhn  You have no knowledge of him but I have knowledge of him and if I said I have no knowledge of him I would be talking falsely like you but I have full knowledge of him and I keep his word
Jhn  Your father Abraham was full of joy at the hope of seeing my day he saw it and was glad
Jhn  Then the Jews said to him You are not fifty years old have you seen Abraham
Jhn  Jesus said to them Truly I say to you Before Abraham came into being I am
Jhn  So they took up stones to send at him but Jesus got secretly out of their way and went out of the Temple
Jhn  And when he went on his way he saw a man blind from birth
Jhn  And his disciples put a question to him saying Master was it because of this mans sin or the sin of his father and mother that he has been blind from birth
Jhn  Jesus said in answer It was not because of his sin or because of his fathers or mothers it was so that the works of God might be seen openly in him
Jhn  While it is day we have to do the works of him who sent me the night comes when no work may be done
Jhn  As long as I am in the world I am the light of the world
Jhn  Having said these words he put earth mixed with water from his mouth on the mans eyes
Jhn  And said to him Go and make yourself clean in the bath of Siloam the sense of the name is Sent So he went away and after washing came back able to see
Jhn  Then the neighbours and others who had seen him before in the street with his hand out for money said Is not this the man who got money from people
Jhn  Some said It is he others said No but he is like him He said I am he
Jhn  So they said to him How then were your eyes made open
Jhn  His answer was The man who is named Jesus put earth mixed with water on my eyes and said to me Go and make yourself clean in Siloam so I went away and after washing am now able to see
Jhn  And they said to him Where is he His answer was I have no knowledge
Jhn  They took him before the Phariseesthis man who had been blind
Jhn  Now the day on which the earth was mixed by Jesus and the mans eyes were made open was the Sabbath
Jhn  So the Pharisees put more questions to him about how his eyes had been made open And he said to them He put earth on my eyes and I had a wash and am able to see
Jhn  Then some of the Pharisees said That man has not come from God for he does not keep the Sabbath Others said How is it possible for a sinner to do such signs So there was a division among them
Jhn  Again they said to the blind man What have you to say about him for opening your eyes And he said He is a prophet
Jhn  Now the Jews had no belief in the statement that he had been blind and was now able to see till they sent for the father and mother of the man whose eyes had been made open
Jhn  And put the question to them saying Is this your son of whom you say that he was blind at birth how is it then that he is now able to see
Jhn  In answer his father and mother said We are certain that this is our son and that he was blind at birth
Jhn  But how it is he is now able to see or who made his eyes open we are not able to say put the question to him he is old enough to give an answer for himself
Jhn  They said this because of their fear of the Jews for the Jews had come to an agreement that if any man said that Jesus was the Christ he would be put out of the Synagogue
Jhn  That was the reason why they said He is old enough put the question to him
Jhn  So they sent a second time for the man who had been blind and they said to him Give glory to God it is clear to us that this man is a sinner
Jhn  He said in answer I have no knowledge if he is a sinner or not but one thing I am certain about I was blind and now I see
Jhn  Then they said to him What did he do to you how did he give you the use of your eyes
Jhn  His answer was I have said it before but your ears were shut why would you have me say it again is it your desire to become his disciples
Jhn  And they were angry with him and said You are his disciple but we are disciples of Moses
Jhn  We are certain that God gave his word to Moses but as for this man we have no knowledge where he comes from
Jhn  The man said in answer Why here is a strange thing You have no knowledge where he comes from though he gave me the use of my eyes
Jhn  We have knowledge that God does not give ear to sinners but if any man is a worshipper of God and does his pleasure to him Gods ears are open
Jhn  In all the years nobody has ever before seen the eyes of a man blind from birth made open
Jhn  If this man did not come from God he would be unable to do anything
Jhn  Their answer was You came to birth through sin do you make yourself our teacher And they put him out of the Synagogue
Jhn  It came to the ears of Jesus that they had put him out and meeting him he said Have you faith in the Son of man
Jhn  He said in answer And who is he Lord Say so that I may have faith in him
Jhn  Jesus said to him You have seen him it is he who is talking to you
Jhn  And he said Lord I have faith And he gave him worship
Jhn  And Jesus said I came into this world to be a judge so that those who do not see may see and those who see may become blind
Jhn  These words came to the ears of the Pharisees who were with him and they said to him Are we then blind
Jhn  Jesus said to them If you were blind you would have no sin but now that you say We see your sin is there still
Jhn  Truly I say to you He who does not go through the door into the place where the sheep are kept but gets in by some other way is a thief and an outlaw
Jhn  He who goes in by the door is the keeper of the sheep
Jhn  The porter lets him in and the sheep give ear to his voice he says over the names of the sheep and takes them out
Jhn  When he has got them all out he goes before them and the sheep go after him for they have knowledge of his voice
Jhn  They will not go after another who is not their keeper but will go from him in flight because his voice is strange to them
Jhn  In this Jesus was teaching them in the form of a story but what he said was not clear to them
Jhn  So Jesus said again Truly I say to you I am the door of the sheep
Jhn  All who came before me are thieves and outlaws but the sheep did not give ear to them
Jhn  I am the door if any man goes in through me he will have salvation and will go in and go out and will get food
Jhn  The thief comes only to take the sheep and to put them to death he comes for their destruction I have come so that they may have life and have it in greater measure
Jhn  I am the good keeper of sheep the good keeper gives his life for the sheep
Jhn  He who is a servant and not the keeper or the owner of the sheep sees the wolf coming and goes in flight away from the sheep and the wolf comes down on them and sends them in all directions
Jhn  Because he is a servant he has no interest in the sheep
Jhn  I am the good keeper I have knowledge of my sheep and they have knowledge of me
Jhn  Even as the Father has knowledge of me and I of the Father and I am giving my life for the sheep
Jhn  And I have other sheep which are not of this field I will be their guide in the same way and they will give ear to my voice so there will be one flock and one keeper
Jhn  For this reason am I loved by the Father because I give up my life so that I may take it again
Jhn  No one takes it away from me I give it up of myself I have power to give it up and I have power to take it again These orders I have from my Father
Jhn  There was a division again among the Jews because of these words
Jhn  And a number of them said He has an evil spirit and is out of his mind why do you give ear to him
Jhn  Others said These are not the words of one who has an evil spirit Is it possible for an evil spirit to make blind people see
Jhn  Then came the feast of the opening of the Temple in Jerusalem it was winter
Jhn  And Jesus was walking in the Temple in Solomons covered way
Jhn  Then the Jews came round him saying how long are you going to keep us in doubt If you are the Christ say so clearly
Jhn  Jesus said in answer I have said it and you have no belief the works which I do in my Fathers name these give witness about me
Jhn  But you have no belief because you are not of my sheep
Jhn  My sheep give ear to my voice and I have knowledge of them and they come after me
Jhn  And I give them eternal life they will never come to destruction and no one will ever take them out of my hand
Jhn  That which my Father has given to me has more value than all and no one is able to take anything out of the Fathers hand
Jhn  I and my Father are one
Jhn  Then the Jews took up stones again to send at him
Jhn  Jesus said to them in answer I have let you see a number of good works from the Father for which of those works are you stoning me
Jhn  This was their answer We are not stoning you for a good work but for evil words because being a man you make yourself God
Jhn  In answer Jesus said Is there not a saying in your law I said You are gods
Jhn  If he said they were gods to whom the word of God came and the Writings may not be broken
Jhn  Do you say of him whom the Father made holy and sent into the world Your words are evil because I said I am Gods Son
Jhn  If I am not doing the works of my Father do not have belief in me
Jhn  But if I am doing them then have belief in the works even if you have no belief in me so that you may see clearly and be certain that the Father is in me and I am in the Father
Jhn  Then again they made an attempt to take him but he got away from them
Jhn  And he went again to the other side of the Jordan to the place where John first gave baptism and he was there for a time
Jhn  And a great number of people came to him saying John did no sign but everything John said of this man was true
Jhn  And a number came to have faith in him there
Jhn  Now a certain man named Lazarus was ill he was of Bethany the town of Mary and her sister Martha
Jhn  The Mary whose brother Lazarus was ill was the Mary who put perfumed oil on the Lord and made his feet dry with her hair
Jhn  So the sisters sent to him saying Lord your dear friend is ill
Jhn  When this came to his ears Jesus said The end of this disease is not death but the glory of God so that the Son of God may have glory because of it
Jhn  Now Jesus had love in his heart for Martha and her sister and Lazarus
Jhn  So when the news came to him that Lazarus was ill he did not go from the place where he was for two days
Jhn  Then after that time he said to his disciples Let us go into Judaea again
Jhn  The disciples said to him Master the Jews were attempting only the other day to have you stoned and are you going back there again
Jhn  Then Jesus said in answer Are there not twelve hours in the day A man may go about in the day without falling because he sees the light of this world
Jhn  But if a man goes about in the night he may have a fall because the light is not in him
Jhn  These things said he and after that he said to them Lazarus our friend is at rest but I go so that I may make him come out of his sleep
Jhn  Then his disciples said to him Lord if he is resting he will get well
Jhn  Jesus however was talking of his death but they had the idea that he was talking about taking rest in sleep
Jhn  Then Jesus said to them clearly Lazarus is dead
Jhn  And because of you I am glad I was not there so that you may have faith but let us go to him
Jhn  Then Thomas who was named Didymus said to the other disciples Let us go so that we may be with him in death
Jhn  Now when Jesus came he made the discovery that Lazarus had been put into the earth four days before
Jhn  Now Bethany was near to Jerusalem about two miles away
Jhn  And a number of Jews had come to Martha and Mary to give them comfort about their brother
Jhn  When Martha had the news that Jesus was on the way she went out to him but Mary did not go from the house
Jhn  Then Martha said to Jesus Lord if you had been here my brother would not be dead
Jhn  But I am certain that even now whatever request you make to God God will give it to you
Jhn  Jesus said to her Your brother will come to life again
Jhn  Martha said to him I am certain that he will come to life again when all come back from the dead at the last day
Jhn  Jesus said to her I am myself that day and that life he who has faith in me will have life even if he is dead
Jhn  And no one who is living and has faith in me will ever see death Is this your faith
Jhn  She said to him Yes Lord my faith is that you are the Christ the Son of God who was to come into the world
Jhn  And having said this she went away and said secretly to her sister Mary The Master is here and has sent for you
Jhn  And Mary hearing this got up quickly and went to him
Jhn  Now Jesus had not at this time come into the town but was still in the place where Martha had seen him
Jhn  Then the Jews who were with her in the house comforting her when they saw Mary get up quickly and go out went after her in the belief that she was going to the place of the dead and would be weeping there
Jhn  When Mary came to where Jesus was and saw him she went down at his feet saying Lord if you had been here my brother would not be dead
Jhn  And when Jesus saw her weeping and saw the Jews weeping who came with her his spirit was moved and he was troubled
Jhn  And said Where have you put him They said Come and see Lord
Jhn  And Jesus himself was weeping
Jhn  So the Jews said See how dear he was to him
Jhn  But some of them said This man who made open the eyes of the blind man was he not able to keep his friend from death
Jhn  So Jesus deeply troubled in heart came to the place of the dead It was a hole in the rock and a stone was over the opening
Jhn  Jesus said Take away the stone Martha the sister of him who was dead said Lord by this time the body will be smelling for he has been dead four days
Jhn  Jesus said to her Did I not say to you that if you had faith you would see the glory of God
Jhn  So they took away the stone And Jesus looking up to heaven said Father I give praise to you for hearing me
Jhn  I was certain that your ears are at all times open to me but I said it because of these who are here so that they may see that you sent me
Jhn  Then he said in a loud voice Lazarus come out
Jhn  And he who was dead came out with linen bands folded tightly about his hands and feet and a cloth about his face Jesus said to them Make him free and let him go
Jhn  Then a number of the Jews who had come to Mary and had seen the things which Jesus did had belief in him
Jhn  But some of them went to the Pharisees with the news of what Jesus had done
Jhn  Then the high priests and the Pharisees had a meeting and said What are we doing This man is doing a number of signs
Jhn  If we let him go on in this way everybody will have belief in him and the Romans will come and take away our place and our nation
Jhn  But one of them Caiaphas who was high priest that year said to them You have no knowledge of anything
Jhn  You do not see that it is in your interest for one man to be put to death for the people so that all the nation may not come to destruction
Jhn  He did not say this of himself but being the high priest that year he said as a prophet that Jesus would be put to death for the nation
Jhn  And not for that nation only but for the purpose of uniting in one body the children of God all over the world
Jhn  And from that day they took thought together how to put him to death
Jhn  So Jesus no longer went about publicly among the Jews but went from there into the country near to the waste land to a town named Ephraim where he was for some time with the disciples
Jhn  Now the Passover of the Jews was near and numbers of people went up from the country to Jerusalem to make themselves clean before the Passover
Jhn  They were looking for Jesus and saying to one another while they were in the Temple What is your opinion Will he not come to the feast
Jhn  Now the chief priests and the Pharisees had given orders that if anyone had knowledge where he was he was to give them word so that they might take him
Jhn  Then six days before the Passover Jesus came to Bethany where Lazarus was whom Jesus had made to come back from the dead
Jhn  So they made him a meal there and he was waited on by Martha and Lazarus was among those who were seated with him at table
Jhn  Then Mary taking a pound of perfumed oil of great value put it on the feet of Jesus and made them dry with her hair and the house became full of the smell of the perfume
Jhn  But one of his disciples Judas Iscariot who was to give him up said
Jhn  Why was not this perfume traded for three hundred pence and the money given to the poor
Jhn  He said this not because he had any love for the poor but because he was a thief and having the moneybag took for himself what was put into it
Jhn  Then Jesus said Let her be Let her keep what she has for the day of my death
Jhn  The poor you have ever with you but me you have not for ever
Jhn  Then a great number of the Jews had news that he was there and they came not only because of Jesus but so that they might see Lazarus who had been dead and to whom he had given life
Jhn  Now there was talk among the chief priests of putting Lazarus to death
Jhn  For because of him a great number of the Jews went away and had belief in Jesus
Jhn  The day after a great number of people who were there for the feast when they had the news that Jesus was coming to Jerusalem
Jhn  Took branches of palmtrees and went out to him crying A blessing on him who comes in the name of the Lord the King of Israel
Jhn  And Jesus saw a young ass and took his seat on it as the Writings say
Jhn  Have no fear daughter of Zion see your King is coming seated on a young ass
Jhn  These things were not clear to his disciples at first but when Jesus had been lifted up into his glory then it came to their minds that these things in the Writings were about him and that they had been done to him
Jhn  Now the people who were with him when his voice came to Lazarus in the place of the dead and gave him life again had been talking about it
Jhn  And that was the reason the people went out to him because it had come to their ears that he had done this sign
Jhn  Then the Pharisees said one to another You see you are unable to do anything the world has gone after him
Jhn  Now there were some Greeks among the people who had come up to give worship at the feast
Jhn  They came to Philip who was of Bethsaida in Galilee and made a request saying Sir we have a desire to see Jesus
Jhn  Philip went and gave word of it to Andrew and Andrew went with Philip to Jesus
Jhn  And Jesus said to them in answer The hour of the glory of the Son of man has come
Jhn  Truly I say to you If a seed of grain does not go into the earth and come to an end it is still a seed and no more but through its death it gives much fruit
Jhn  He who is in love with life will have it taken from him and he who has no care for his life in this world will keep it for ever and ever
Jhn  If any man is my servant let him come after me and where I am there will my servant be If any man becomes my servant my Father will give him honour
Jhn  Now is my soul troubled and what am I to say Father keep me from this hour No for this purpose have I come to this hour
Jhn  Father give glory to your name Then there came a voice out of heaven saying I have given it glory and I will give it glory again
Jhn  Hearing the sound a number of people who were there said that it was thunder others said An angel was talking to him
Jhn  Jesus said in answer This voice came not for me but for you
Jhn  Now is this world to be judged now will the ruler of this world be sent out
Jhn  And I if I am lifted up from the earth will make all men come to me
Jhn  This he said pointing to the sort of death he would have
Jhn  Then the people in answer said to him The law says that the Christ will have life without end how say you then that it is necessary for the Son of man to be lifted up Who is this Son of man
Jhn  Jesus said to them For a little time longer the light will be among you while you have the light go on walking in it so that the dark may not overtake you one walking in the dark has no knowledge of where he is going
Jhn  In so far as you have the light put your faith in the light so that you may become sons of light With these words Jesus went away and for a time was not seen again by them
Jhn  But though he had done such a number of signs before them they still had no belief in him
Jhn  So that the words of the prophet Isaiah might come true when he said Lord who has any belief in our preaching and the arm of the Lord to whom has it been unveiled
Jhn  For this reason they were unable to have belief because Isaiah said again
Jhn  He has made their eyes blind and their hearts hard for fear that they might see with their eyes and get knowledge with their hearts and be changed and I might make them well
Jhn  Isaiah said these words because he saw his glory His words were about him
Jhn  However a number even of the rulers had belief in him but because of the Pharisees they did not say so openly for fear that they might be shut out from the Synagogue
Jhn  For the praise of men was dearer to them than the approval of God
Jhn  Then Jesus said with a loud voice He who has faith in me has faith not in me but in him who sent me
Jhn  And he who sees me sees him who sent me
Jhn  I have come as a light into the world so that no one who has faith in me will go on living in the dark
Jhn  And if any man gives ear to my words and does not keep them I am not his judge I did not come to be judge of the world but to give salvation to the world
Jhn  He who puts me on one side and does not take my words to heart is not without a judge the word which I have said will be his judge on the last day
Jhn  For I have not said it on my authority but the Father who sent me gave me orders what to say and how to say it
Jhn  And I have knowledge that his order is eternal life so that the things which I say I say them even as the Father says them to me
Jhn  Now before the feast of the Passover it was clear to Jesus that the time had come for him to go away from this world to the Father Having once had love for those in the world who were his his love for them went on to the end
Jhn  So while a meal was going on the Evil One having now put it into the heart of Judas Iscariot Simons son to be false to him
Jhn  Jesus being conscious that the Father had put everything into his hands and that he came from God and was going to God
Jhn  Got up from table put off his robe and took a cloth and put it round him
Jhn  Then he put water into a basin and was washing the feet of the disciples and drying them with the cloth which was round him
Jhn  So he came to Simon Peter Peter said Lord are my feet to be washed by you
Jhn  And Jesus answering said to him What I do is not clear to you now but it will be clear to you in time to come
Jhn  Peter said I will never let my feet be washed by you never Jesus said in answer If I do not make you clean you have no part with me
Jhn  Simon Peter said to him Lord not my feet only but my hands and my head
Jhn  Jesus said to him He who is bathed has need only to have his feet washed and then he is clean all over and you my disciples are clean but not all of you
Jhn  He had knowledge who was false to him that is why he said You are not all clean
Jhn  Then after washing their feet and putting on his robe again he took his seat and said to them Do you see what I have done to you
Jhn  You give me the name of Master and Lord and you are right that is what I am
Jhn  If then I the Lord and the Master have made your feet clean it is right for you to make one anothers feet clean
Jhn  I have given you an example so that you may do what I have done to you
Jhn  Truly I say to you A servant is not greater than his lord and he who is sent is not greater than the one who sent him
Jhn  If these things are clear to you happy are you if you do them
Jhn  I am not talking of you all I have knowledge of my true disciples but things are as they are so that the Writings may come true The foot of him who takes bread with me is lifted up against me
Jhn  From this time forward I give you knowledge of things before they come about so that when they come about you may have belief that I am he
Jhn  Truly I say to you He who takes to his heart anyone whom I send takes me to his heart and he who so takes me takes him who sent me
Jhn  When Jesus had said this he was troubled in spirit and gave witness saying Truly I say to you that one of you will be false to me
Jhn  Then the eyes of the disciples were turned on one another in doubt as to whom he had in mind
Jhn  There was at table one of his disciples the one dear to Jesus resting his head on Jesus breast
Jhn  Making a sign to him Simon Peter said Who is it he is talking about
Jhn  He then resting his head on Jesus breast said to him Lord who is it
Jhn  This was the answer Jesus gave It is the one to whom I will give this bit of bread after I have put it in the vessel Then he took the bit of bread put it into the vessel and gave it to Judas the son of Simon Iscariot
Jhn  And when Judas took the bread Satan went into him Then Jesus said to him Do quickly what you have to do
Jhn  Now it was not clear to anyone at table why he said this to him
Jhn  Some were of the opinion that because Judas kept the moneybag Jesus said to him Get the things we have need of for the feast or that he was to give something to the poor
Jhn  So Judas having taken the bit of bread straight away went out and it was night
Jhn  Then when he had gone out Jesus said Now is glory given to the Son of man and God is given glory in him
Jhn  If God is given glory in him God will give him glory in himself and will give him glory even now
Jhn  My dear children I am only to be with you a little longer Then you will be looking for me and as I said to the Jews so now I say to you Where I am going you may not come
Jhn  I give you a new law Have love one for another even as I have had love for you so are you to have love one for another
Jhn  By this it will be clear to all men that you are my disciples if you have love one for another
Jhn  Simon Peter said to him Lord where are you going Jesus said in answer Where I am going you may not come with me now but you will come later
Jhn  Peter said to him Why may I not come with you even now I will give up my life for you
Jhn  Jesus said in answer Will you give up your life for me Truly I say to you Before the cry of the cock you will have said three times that you are not my disciple
Jhn  Let not your heart be troubled have faith in God and have faith in me
Jhn  In my Fathers house are rooms enough if it was not so would I have said that I am going to make ready a place for you
Jhn  And if I go and make ready a place for you I will come back again and will take you to be with me so that you may be where I am
Jhn  And you all have knowledge of where I am going and of the way to it
Jhn  Thomas said Lord we have no knowledge of where you are going how may we have knowledge of the way
Jhn  Jesus said to him I am the true and living way no one comes to the Father but by me
Jhn  If you had knowledge of me you would have knowledge of my Father you have knowledge of him now and have seen him
Jhn  Philip said to him Lord let us see the Father and we have need of nothing more
Jhn  Jesus said to him Philip have I been with you all this time and still you have no knowledge of me He who has seen me has seen the Father Why do you say Let us see the Father
Jhn  Have you not faith that I am in the Father and the Father is in me The words which I say to you I say not from myself but the Father who is in me all the time does his works
Jhn  Have faith that I am in the Father and that the Father is in me at least have faith in me because of what I do
Jhn  Truly I say to you He who puts his faith in me will do the very works which I do and he will do greater things than these because I am going to my Father
Jhn  And whatever request you make in my name that I will do so that the Father may have glory in the Son
Jhn  If you make any request to me in my name I will do it
Jhn  If you have love for me you will keep my laws
Jhn  And I will make prayer to the Father and he will give you another Helper to be with you for ever
Jhn  Even the Spirit of true knowledge That Spirit the world is not able to take to its heart because it sees him not and has no knowledge of him but you have knowledge of him because he is ever with you and will be in you
Jhn  I will not let you be without a friend I am coming to you
Jhn  A little time longer and the world will see me no more but you will see me and you will be living because I am living
Jhn  At that time it will be clear to you that I am in my Father and you are in me and I in you
Jhn  He who has my laws and keeps them he it is who has love for me and he who has love for me will be loved by my Father and I will have love for him and will let myself be seen clearly by him
Jhn  Judas not Iscariot said to him How is it that you will let yourself be seen clearly by us and not by the world
Jhn  Jesus said to him in answer If anyone has love for me he will keep my words and he will be dear to my Father and we will come to him and make our livingplace with him
Jhn  He who has no love for me does not keep my words and the word which you are hearing is not my word but the Fathers who sent me
Jhn  I have said all this to you while I am still with you
Jhn  But the Helper the Holy Spirit whom the Father will send in my name will be your teacher in all things and will put you in mind of everything I have said to you
Jhn  May peace be with you my peace I give to you I give it not as the world gives Let not your heart be troubled let it be without fear
Jhn  Keep in mind how I said to you I go away and come to you again If you had love for me you would be glad because I am going to the Father for the Father is greater than I
Jhn  And now I have given you word of it before it comes so that when it comes you may have faith
Jhn  After this I will not say much to you because the ruler of this world comes and he has no power over me
Jhn  But he comes so that the world may see that I have love for the Father and that I am doing as I am ordered by the Father Get up and let us go
Jhn  I am the true vine and my Father is the gardener
Jhn  He takes away every branch in me which has no fruit and every branch which has fruit he makes clean so that it may have more fruit
Jhn  You are clean even now through the teaching which I have given you
Jhn  Be in me at all times as I am in you As the branch is not able to give fruit of itself if it is not still on the vine so you are not able to do so if you are not in me
Jhn  I am the vine you are the branches he who is in me at all times as I am in him gives much fruit because without me you are able to do nothing
Jhn  If a man does not keep himself in me he becomes dead and is cut off like a dry branch such branches are taken up and put in the fire and burned
Jhn  If you are in me at all times and my words are in you then anything for which you make a request will be done for you
Jhn  Here is my Fathers glory in that you give much fruit and so are my true disciples
Jhn  Even as the Father has given me his love so I have given my love to you be ever in my love
Jhn  If you keep my laws you will be ever in my love even as I have kept my Fathers laws and am ever in his love
Jhn  I have said these things to you so that I may have joy in you and so that your joy may be complete
