Jhn  This is the law I give you Have love one for another even as I have love for you
Jhn  Greater love has no man than this that a man gives up his life for his friends
Jhn  You are my friends if you do what I give you orders to do
Jhn  No longer do I give you the name of servants because a servant is without knowledge of what his master is doing I give you the name of friends because I have given you knowledge of all the things which my Father has said to me
Jhn  You did not take me for yourselves but I took you for myself and I gave you the work of going about and producing fruit which will be for ever so that whatever request you make to the Father in my name he may give it to you
Jhn  So this is my law for you Have love one for another
Jhn  If you are hated by the world keep in mind that I was hated by the world before you
Jhn  If you were of the world you would be loved by the world but because you are not of the world but I have taken you out of the world you are hated by the world
Jhn  Keep in mind the words I said to you A servant is not greater than his lord If they were cruel to me they will be cruel to you if they kept my words they will keep yours
Jhn  They will do all this to you because of my namebecause they have no knowledge of him who sent me
Jhn  If I had not come and been their teacher they would have had no sin but now they have no reason to give for their sin
Jhn  He who has hate for me has hate for my Father
Jhn  If I had not done among them the works which no other man ever did they would have had no sin but now they have seen and they have had hate in their hearts for me and my Father
Jhn  This comes about so that the writing in their law may be made true Their hate for me was without cause
Jhn  When the Helper comes whom I will send to you from the Father even the Spirit of true knowledge who comes from the Fatherhe will give witness about me
Jhn  And you in addition will give witness because you have been with me from the first
Jhn  I have said these things to you so that you may not be in doubt
Jhn  They will put you out of the Synagogues yes the time is coming when whoever puts you to death will have the belief that he is doing Gods pleasure
Jhn  They will do these things to you because they have not had knowledge of the Father or of me
Jhn  I have said these things to you so that when the time comes what I have said may come to your mind I did not say them to you at the first because then I was still with you
Jhn  But now I am going to him who sent me and not one of you says to me Where are you going
Jhn  But your hearts are full of sorrow because I have said these things
Jhn  But what I am saying is true my going is for your good for if I do not go away the Helper will not come to you but if I go I will send him to you
Jhn  And he when he comes will make the world conscious of sin and of righteousness and of being judged
Jhn  Of sin because they have not faith in me
Jhn  Of righteousness because I go to the Father and you will see me no more
Jhn  Of being judged because the ruler of this world has been judged
Jhn  I have still much to say to you but you are not strong enough for it now
Jhn  However when he the Spirit of true knowledge has come he will be your guide into all true knowledge for his words will not come from himself but whatever has come to his hearing that he will say and he will make clear to you the things to come
Jhn  He will give me glory because he will take of what is mine and make it clear to you
Jhn  Everything which the Father has is mine that is why I say He will take of what is mine and will make it clear to you
Jhn  After a little time you will see me no longer and then again after a little time you will see me
Jhn  So some of the disciples said one to another What is this he is saying After a little time you will see me no longer and then again after a little time you will see me and I am going to the Father
Jhn  So they said again and again What is this he is saying A little time His words are not clear to us
Jhn  Jesus saw that they had a desire to put the question to him so he said to them Is this what you are questioning one with another why I said After a little time you will see me no longer and then again after a little time you will see me
Jhn  Truly I say to you You will be weeping and sorrowing but the world will be glad you will be sad but your sorrow will be turned into joy
Jhn  When a woman is about to give birth she has sorrow because her hour is come but when she has given birth to the child the pain is put out of her mind by the joy that a man has come into the world
Jhn  So you have sorrow now but I will see you again and your hearts will be glad and no one will take away your joy
Jhn  And on that day you will put no questions to me Truly I say to you Whatever request you make to the Father he will give it to you in my name
Jhn  Up to now you have made no request in my name do so and it will be answered so that your hearts may be full of joy
Jhn  All this I have said to you in veiled language but the time is coming when I will no longer say things in veiled language but will give you knowledge of the Father clearly
Jhn  In that day you will make requests in my name and I do not say that I will make prayer to the Father for you
Jhn  For the Father himself gives his love to you because you have given your love to me and have had faith that I came from God
Jhn  I came out from the Father and have come into the world again I go away from the world and go to the Father
Jhn  His disciples said Now you are talking clearly and not in veiled language
Jhn  Now we are certain that you have knowledge of all things and have no need for anyone to put questions to you through this we have faith that you came from God
Jhn  Jesus made answer Have you faith now
Jhn  See a time is coming yes it is now here when you will go away in all directions every man to his house and I will be by myself but I am not by myself because the Father is with me
Jhn  I have said all these things to you so that in me you may have peace In the world you have trouble but take heart I have overcome the world
Jhn  Jesus said these things then lifting his eyes to heaven he said Father the time has now come give glory to your Son so that the Son may give glory to you
Jhn  Even as you gave him authority over all flesh to give eternal life to all those whom you have given to him
Jhn  And this is eternal life to have knowledge of you the only true God and of him whom you have sent even Jesus Christ
Jhn  I have given you glory on the earth having done all the work which you gave me to do
Jhn  And now Father let me have glory with you even that glory which I had with you before the world was
Jhn  I have given knowledge of your name to the men whom you gave me out of the world yours they were and you gave them to me and they have kept your words
Jhn  Now it is clear to them that whatever you have given to me comes from you
Jhn  Because I have given them the words which you gave to me and they have taken them to heart and have certain knowledge that I came from you and they have faith that you sent me
Jhn  My prayer is for them my prayer is not for the world but for those whom you have given to me because they are yours
Jhn  All mine are yours and yours are mine and I have glory in them
Jhn  And now I will be no longer in the world but they are in the world and I come to you Holy Father keep them in your name which you have given to me so that they may be one even as we are one
Jhn  While I was with them I kept them safe in your name which you have given to me I took care of them and not one of them has come to destruction but only the son of destruction so that the Writings might come true
Jhn  And now I come to you and these things I say in the world so that they may have my joy complete in them
Jhn  I have given your word to them and they are hated by the world because they are not of the world even as I am not of the world
Jhn  My prayer is not that you will take them out of the world but that you will keep them from the Evil One
Jhn  They are not of the world any more than I am of the world
Jhn  Make them holy by the true word your word is the true word
Jhn  Even as you have sent me into the world so I have sent them into the world
Jhn  And for them I make myself holy so that they may be made truly holy
Jhn  My prayer is not for them only but for all who will have faith in me through their word
Jhn  May they all be one Even as you Father are in me and I am in you so let them be in us so that all men may come to have faith that you sent me
Jhn  And the glory which you have given to me I have given to them so that they may be one even as we are one
Jhn  I in them and you in me so that they may be made completely one and so that it may become clear to all men that you have sent me and that they are loved by you as I am loved by you
Jhn  Father it is my desire that these whom you have given to me may be by my side where I am so that they may see my glory which you have given to me because you had love for me before the world came into being
Jhn  Father of righteousness I have knowledge of you though the world has not and to these it is clear that you sent me
Jhn  And I have given to them knowledge of your name and will give it so that the love which you have for me may be in them and I in them
Jhn  When Jesus had said these words he went out with his disciples over the stream Kedron to a garden into which he went with his disciples
Jhn  And Judas who was false to him had knowledge of the place because Jesus went there frequently with his disciples
Jhn  So Judas getting a band of armed men and police from the chief priests and Pharisees went there with lights and with arms
Jhn  Then Jesus having knowledge of everything which was coming on him went forward and said to them Who are you looking for
Jhn  Their answer was Jesus the Nazarene Jesus said I am he And Judas who was false to him was there at their side
Jhn  And when he said to them I am he they went back falling to the earth
Jhn  So again he put the question to them Who are you looking for And they said Jesus the Nazarene
Jhn  Jesus made answer I have said that I am he if you are looking for me let these men go away
Jhn  He said this so that his words might come true I have kept safe all those whom you gave to me
Jhn  Then Simon Peter who had a sword took it out and gave the high priests servant a blow cutting off his right ear The servants name was Malchus
Jhn  Then Jesus said to Peter Put back your sword am I not to take the cup which my Father has given to me
Jhn  Then the band and the chief captain and the police took Jesus and put cords round him
Jhn  They took him first to Annas because Annas was the fatherinlaw of Caiaphas who was the high priest that year
Jhn  It was Caiaphas who had said to the Jews that it was in their interest for one man to be put to death for the people
Jhn  And Simon Peter went after Jesus with another disciple Now that disciple was a friend of the high priest and he went in with Jesus into the house of the high priest
Jhn  But Peter was kept outside at the door Then this other disciple who was a friend of the high priest came out and had a word with the girl who kept the door and took Peter in
Jhn  Then the girl who was the doorkeeper said to Peter Are you not one of this mans disciples In answer he said I am not
Jhn  Now the servants and the police had made a fire of coals because it was cold they were warming themselves in front of it and Peter was there with them warming himself
Jhn  Then the high priest put questions to Jesus about his disciples and his teaching
Jhn  Jesus made answer I said things openly to the world at all times I have given my teaching in the Synagogues and in the Temple to which all the Jews come and I have said nothing secretly
Jhn  Why are you questioning me put questions to my hearers about what I have said to them they have knowledge of what I said
Jhn  When he said this one of the police by his side gave him a blow with his open hand saying Do you give such an answer to the high priest
Jhn  Jesus said in answer If I have said anything evil give witness to the evil but if I said what is true why do you give me blows
Jhn  Then Annas sent him chained to Caiaphas the high priest
Jhn  But Simon Peter was still there warming himself by the fire They said to him Are you not one of his disciples He said No I am not
Jhn  One of the servants of the high priest a relation of him whose ear had been cut off by Peter said Did I not see you with him in the garden
Jhn  Then again Peter said No And straight away a cock gave its cry
Jhn  So they took Jesus from the house of Caiaphas to the Praetorium It was early They themselves did not go into the Praetorium so that they might not become unclean but might take the Passover
Jhn  So Pilate came out to them and put the question What have you to say against this man
Jhn  They said to him in answer If the man was not a wrongdoer we would not have given him up to you
Jhn  Then Pilate said to them Take him yourselves and let him be judged by your law But the Jews said to him We have no right to put any man to death
Jhn  That the word of Jesus might come true pointing to the sort of death he would have
Jhn  Then Pilate went back into the Praetorium and sent for Jesus and said to him Are you the King of the Jews
Jhn  Jesus made answer Do you say this of yourself or did others say it about me
Jhn  Pilate said Am I a Jew Your nation and the chief priests have given you into my hands what have you done
Jhn  Jesus said in answer My kingdom is not of this world if my kingdom was of this world my disciples would have made a good fight to keep me out of the hands of the Jews but my kingdom is not here
Jhn  Then Pilate said to him Are you then a king Jesus made answer You say that I am a king For this purpose was I given birth and for this purpose I came into the world that I might give witness to what is true Every lover of what is true gives ear to my voice
Jhn  Pilate said to him True what is true Having said this he went out again to the Jews and said to them I see no wrong in him
Jhn  But every year you make a request to me to let a prisoner go free at the Passover Is it your desire that I let the King of the Jews go free
Jhn  Then again they gave a loud cry Not this man but Barabbas Now Barabbas was an outlaw
Jhn  Then Pilate took Jesus and had him whipped with cords
Jhn  And the men of the army made a crown of thorns and put it on his head and they put a purple robe on him
Jhn  And they kept coming and saying Long life to the King of the Jews And they gave him blows with their hands
Jhn  And Pilate went out again and said to them See I let him come out to you to make it clear to you that I see no wrong in him
Jhn  Then Jesus came out with the crown of thorns and the purple robe And Pilate said to them Here is the man
Jhn  So when the chief priests and the police saw him they gave a loud cry To the cross to the cross Pilate said to them Take him yourselves and put him on the cross I see no crime in him
Jhn  And the Jews made answer We have a law and by that law it is right for him to be put to death because he said he was the Son of God
Jhn  When this saying came to Pilates ears his fear became greater
Jhn  And he went again into the Praetorium and said to Jesus Where do you come from But Jesus gave him no answer
Jhn  Then Pilate said to him You say nothing to me is it not clear to you that I have power to let you go free and power to put you to death on the cross
Jhn  Jesus gave this answer You would have no power at all over me if it was not given to you by God so that he who gave me up to you has the greater sin
Jhn  Hearing this Pilate had a desire to let him go free but the Jews said in a loud voice If you let this man go you are not Caesars friend everyone who makes himself a king goes against Caesar
Jhn  So when these words came to Pilates ear he took Jesus out seating himself in the judges seat in a place named in Hebrew Gabbatha or the Stone Floor
Jhn  It was the day when they made ready for the Passover and it was about the sixth hour And he said to the Jews There is your King
Jhn  Then they gave a loud cry Away with him away with him to the cross Pilate said to them Am I to put your King to death on the cross The chief priests said in answer We have no king but Caesar
Jhn  So then he gave him up to them to be put to death on the cross And they took Jesus away
Jhn  And he went out with his cross on him to the place which is named Dead Mans Head in Hebrew Golgotha
Jhn  Where they put him on the cross with two others one on this side and one on that and Jesus in the middle
Jhn  And Pilate put on the cross a statement in writing The writing was JESUS THE NAZARENE THE KING OF THE JEWS
Jhn  The writing was seen by a number of the Jews for the place where Jesus was put to death on the cross was near the town and the writing was in Hebrew and Latin and Greek
Jhn  Then the chief priests of the Jews said to Pilate Do not put The King of the Jews but He said I am the King of the Jews
Jhn  But Pilate made answer What I have put in writing will not be changed
Jhn  And when Jesus was nailed to the cross the men of the army took his clothing and made a division of it into four parts to every man a part and they took his coat now the coat was without a join made out of one bit of cloth
Jhn  So they said among themselves Let this not be cut up but let us put it to the decision of chance and see who gets it They did this so that the Writings might come true which say They made a distribution of my clothing among them and my coat they put to the decision of chance This was what the men of the army did
Jhn  Now by the side of the cross of Jesus were his mother and his mothers sister Mary the wife of Cleopas and Mary Magdalene
Jhn  So when Jesus saw his mother and the disciple who was dear to him he said to his mother Mother there is your son
Jhn  Then he said to the disciple There is your mother And from that hour the disciple took her to his house
Jhn  After this being conscious that all things had now been done so that the Writings might come true Jesus said Give me water
Jhn  Now there was a vessel ready full of bitter wine and they put a sponge full of it on a stick and put it to his mouth
Jhn  So when Jesus had taken the wine he said All is done And with his head bent he gave up his spirit
Jhn  Now it was the day of getting ready for the Passover and so that the bodies might not be on the cross on the Sabbath because the day of that Sabbath was a great day the Jews made a request to Pilate that their legs might be broken and that they might be taken away
Jhn  So the men of the army came and the legs of the first were broken and then of the other who was put to death on the cross with Jesus
Jhn  But when they came to Jesus they saw that he was dead by this time and so his legs were not broken
Jhn  But one of the men made a wound in his side with a spear and straight away there came out blood and water
Jhn  And he who saw it has given witness and his witness is true he is certain that what he says is true so that you may have belief
Jhn  These things came about so that the Writings might be true No bone of his body will be broken
Jhn  And again another verse says They will see him who was wounded by their spears
Jhn  After these things Joseph of Arimathaea who was a disciple of Jesus but secretly for fear of the Jews made a request to Pilate to let him take away the body of Jesus and Pilate said he might do so So he went and took away his body
Jhn  And Nicodemus came he who had first come to Jesus by night with a roll of myrrh and aloes mixed about a hundred pounds
Jhn  Then they took the body of Jesus folding linen about it with the spices as is the way of the Jews when they put the dead to rest
Jhn  Now there was a garden near the cross and in the garden a new place for the dead in which no man had ever been put
Jhn  So they put Jesus there because it was the Jews day of getting ready for the Passover and the place was near
Jhn  Now on the first day of the week very early while it was still dark Mary Magdalene came to the place and saw that the stone had been taken away from it
Jhn  Then she went running to Simon Peter and to the other disciple who was loved by Jesus and said to them They have taken away the Lord out of the place of the dead and we have no knowledge where they have put him
Jhn  So Peter and the other disciple went out to the place of the dead
Jhn  They went running together and the other disciple got in front of Peter and came first to the hole in the rock
Jhn  And looking in he saw the linen bands on the earth but he did not go in
Jhn  Then Simon Peter came after him and went into the hole in the rock and he saw the linen bands on the earth
Jhn  And the cloth which had been round his head not with the linen bands but rolled up in a place by itself
Jhn  Then the other disciple who came there first went in and he saw and belief came to him
Jhn  For at that time they had no knowledge that the Writings said that he would have to come again from the dead
Jhn  So then the disciples went away again to their houses
Jhn  But Mary was still there outside the hole in the rock weeping and while she was weeping and looking into the hole
Jhn  She saw two angels in white seated where the body of Jesus had been one at the head and the other at the feet
Jhn  They said to her Woman why are you weeping She said to them Because they have taken away my Lord and I have no knowledge where they have put him
Jhn  And then looking round she saw Jesus there but had no idea that it was Jesus
Jhn  Jesus said to her Woman why are you weeping who are you looking for She taking him for the gardener said to him Sir if you have taken him away from here say where you have put him and I will take him away
Jhn  Jesus said to her Mary Turning she said to him in Hebrew Rabboni which is to say Master
Jhn  Jesus said to her Do not put your hand on me for I have not gone up to the Father but go to my brothers and say to them I go up to my Father and your Father to my God and your God
Jhn  Mary Magdalene went with the news to the disciples and said she had seen the Lord and that he had said these things to her
Jhn  At evening on that day the first day of the week when for fear of the Jews the doors were shut where the disciples were Jesus came among them and said to them May peace be with you
Jhn  And when he had said this he let them see his hands and his side Then the disciples were glad when they saw the Lord
Jhn  And Jesus said to them again May peace be with you As the Father sent me even so I now send you
Jhn  And when he had said this breathing on them he said to them Let the Holy Spirit come on you
Jhn  Any to whom you give forgiveness will be made free from their sins and any from whom you keep back forgiveness will still be in their sins
Jhn  Now Thomas one of the twelve named Didymus was not with them when Jesus came
Jhn  So the other disciples said to him We have seen the Lord But he said to them If I do not see in his hands the print of the nails and put my finger into the print of the nails and if I do not put my hand into his side I will never have belief
Jhn  And after eight days his disciples were again in the house and Thomas was with them Though the doors were shut Jesus came and taking his place in the middle of them he said May peace be with you
Jhn  Then he said to Thomas Put out your finger and see my hands and put your hand here into my side and be no longer in doubt but have belief
Jhn  And Thomas said in answer My Lord and my God
Jhn  Jesus said to him Because you have seen me you have belief a blessing will be on those who have belief though they have not seen me
Jhn  A number of other signs Jesus did before his disciples which are not recorded in this book
Jhn  But these are recorded so that you may have faith that Jesus is the Christ the Son of God and so that having this faith you may have life in his name
Jhn  After these things Jesus let himself be seen again by the disciples at the sea of Tiberias and it came about in this way
Jhn  Simon Peter Thomas named Didymus Nathanael of Cana in Galilee the sons of Zebedee and two others of his disciples were all together
Jhn  Simon Peter said to them I am going fishing They said to him And we will come with you They went out and got into the boat but that night they took no fish
Jhn  Now very early in the morning Jesus was there by the edge of the sea though the disciples were not conscious that it was Jesus
Jhn  So Jesus said to them Children have you taken any fish They made answer No
Jhn  And he said to them Let down the net on the right side of the boat and you will get some So they put it in the water and now they were not able to get it up again because of the great number of fish
Jhn  So the disciple who was dear to Jesus said to Peter It is the Lord Hearing that it was the Lord Peter put his coat round him because he was not clothed and went into the sea
Jhn  And the other disciples came in the little boat they were not far from land only about two hundred cubits off pulling the net full of fish
Jhn  When they got to land they saw a fire of coals there with fish cooking on it and bread
Jhn  Jesus said to them Get some of the fish which you have now taken
Jhn  So Peter went to the boat and came back pulling the net to land full of great fish a hundred and fiftythree and though there was such a number the net was not broken
Jhn  Jesus said to them Come and take some food And all the disciples were in fear of putting the question Who are you being conscious that it was the Lord
Jhn  Then Jesus came and took the bread and gave it to them and the fish in the same way
Jhn  Now this was the third time that Jesus let himself be seen by the disciples after he had come back from the dead
Jhn  Then when they had taken food Jesus said to Simon Peter Simon son of John is your love for me greater than the love of these others He said to him Yes Lord you are certain of my love for you He said to him Then give my lambs food
Jhn  Again a second time he said to him Simon son of John have you any love for me Yes Lord he said you are certain of my love for you Then take care of my sheep said Jesus
Jhn  He said to him a third time Simon son of John am I dear to you Now Peter was troubled in his heart because he put the question a third time Am I dear to you And he said to him Lord you have knowledge of all things you see that you are dear to me Jesus said to him Then give my sheep food
Jhn  Truly I say to you When you were young you made yourself ready and went wherever you had a desire to go but when you are old you will put out your hands and another will make you ready and you will be taken where you have no desire to go
Jhn  Now this he said pointing out the sort of death by which he would give God glory And after saying this he said to him Come after me
Jhn  Then Peter turning round saw the disciple who was dear to Jesus coming after themthe disciple who was resting on his breast at the last meal and said Lord who is it who will be false to you
Jhn  Seeing him Peter said to Jesus What about this man
Jhn  Jesus said to him If it is my desire for him to be here till I come back what is that to you come yourself after me
Jhn  So this saying went about among the brothers that this disciple would not undergo death Jesus however did not say that he would not undergo death but If it is my desire for him to be here till I come back what is that to you
Jhn  This is the disciple who gives witness about these things and who put them in writing and we have knowledge that his witness is true
Jhn  And Jesus did such a number of other things that if every one was recorded it is my opinion that even the world itself is not great enough for the books there would be
Act  I have given an earlier account O Theophilus of all the things which Jesus did and of his teaching from the first
Act  Till the day when he was taken up to heaven after he had given his orders through the Holy Spirit to the Apostles of whom he had made selection
Act  And to whom he gave clear and certain signs that he was living after his death for he was seen by them for forty days and gave them teaching about the kingdom of God
Act  And when they were all together with him he gave them orders not to go away from Jerusalem but to keep there waiting till the word of the Father was put into effect of which he said I have given you knowledge
Act  For the baptism of John was with water but you will have baptism with the Holy Spirit after a little time
Act  So when they were together they said to him Lord will you at this time give back the kingdom to Israel
Act  And he said to them It is not for you to have knowledge of the time and the order of events which the Father has kept in his control
Act  But you will have power when the Holy Spirit has come on you and you will be my witnesses in Jerusalem and all Judaea and Samaria and to the ends of the earth
Act  And when he had said these things while they were looking he was taken up and went from their view into a cloud
Act  And while they were looking up to heaven with great attention two men came to them in white clothing
Act  And said O men of Galilee why are you looking up into heaven This Jesus who was taken from you into heaven will come again in the same way as you saw him go into heaven
Act  Then they went back to Jerusalem from the mountain named Olivet which is near Jerusalem a Sabbath days journey away
Act  And when they came in they went up into the room where they were living Peter and John and James and Andrew Philip and Thomas Bartholomew and Matthew James the son of Alphaeus and Simon the Zealot and Judas the son of James
Act  And they all with one mind gave themselves up to prayer with the women and Mary the mother of Jesus and his brothers
Act  And in those days Peter got up among the brothers there were about one hundred and twenty of them and said
Act  My brothers the word of God had to be put into effect which the Holy Spirit had said before by the mouth of David about Judas who was guide to those who took Jesus
Act  For he was numbered among us and had his part in our work
Act  Now this man with the reward of his evildoing got for himself a field and falling head first came to a sudden and violent end there
Act  And this came to the knowledge of all those who were living in Jerusalem so that the field was named in their language Akeldama or The field of blood
Act  For in the book of Psalms it says Let his house be waste and let no man be living in it and Let his position be taken by another
Act  For this reason of the men who have been with us all the time while the Lord Jesus went in and out among us
Act  Starting from the baptism of John till he went up from us one will have to be a witness with us of his coming back from death
Act  And they made selection of two Joseph named Barsabbas whose other name was Justus and Matthias
Act  And they made prayers and said Lord having knowledge of the hearts of all men make clear which of these two has been marked out by you
Act  To take that position as a servant and Apostle from which Judas by his sin was shut out so that he might go to his place
Act  And they put it to the decision of chance and the decision was given for Matthias and he was numbered with the eleven Apostles
Act  And when the day of Pentecost was come they were all together in one place
Act  And suddenly there came from heaven a sound like the rushing of a violent wind and all the house where they were was full of it
Act  And they saw tongues like flames of fire coming to rest on every one of them
Act  And they were all full of the Holy Spirit and were talking in different languages as the Spirit gave them power
Act  Now there were living at Jerusalem Jews Godfearing men from every nation under heaven
Act  And when this sound came to their ears they all came together and were greatly surprised because every man was hearing the words of the disciples in his special language
Act  And they were full of wonder and said Are not all these men Galilaeans
Act  And how is it that every one of us is hearing their words in the language which was ours from our birth
Act  Men of Parthia Media and Elam and those living in Mesopotamia in Judaea and Cappadocia in Pontus and Asia
Act  In Phrygia and Pamphylia in Egypt and the parts of Libya about Cyrene and those who have come from Rome Jews by birth and others who have become Jews
Act  Men of Crete and Arabia to all of us they are talking in our different languages of the great works of God
Act  And they were all surprised and in doubt saying to one another What is the reason of this
Act  But others making sport of them said They are full of new wine
Act  But Peter getting up with the eleven said in a loud voice O men of Judaea and all you who are living in Jerusalem take note of this and give ear to my words
Act  For these men are not overcome with wine as it seems to you for it is only the third hour of the day
Act  But this is the thing which was said by the prophet Joel
Act  And it will come about in the last days says God that I will send out my Spirit on all flesh and your sons and your daughters will be prophets and your young men will see visions and your old men will have dreams
Act  And on my menservants and my womenservants I will send my Spirit and they will be prophets
Act  And wonders will be seen in heaven and signs on the earth blood and fire and smoke
Act  The sun will become dark and the moon will be turned to blood before that great day of the Lord comes in glory
Act  And whoever makes his prayer to the Lord will have salvation
Act  Men of Israel give ear to these words Jesus of Nazareth a man who had the approval of God as was made clear to you by the great works and signs and wonders which God did by him among you as you yourselves have knowledge
Act  Him when he was given up by the decision and knowledge of God you put to death on the cross by the hands of evil men
Act  But God gave him back to life having made him free from the pains of death because it was not possible for him to be overcome by it
Act  For David said of him I saw the Lord before my face at all times for he is at my right hand so that I may not be moved
Act  And for this cause my heart was glad and my tongue full of joy and my flesh will be resting in hope
Act  For you will not let my soul be in hell and you will not give up your Holy One to destruction
Act  You have made me see the ways of life I will be full of joy when I see your face
Act  My brothers I may say to you openly that David came to his death and was put in the earth and his restingplace is with us today
Act  But being a prophet and having in mind the oath which God had given to him that of the fruit of his body one would take his place as a king
Act  He having knowledge of the future was talking of the coming again of Christ from the dead that he was not kept in hell and his body did not see destruction
Act  This Jesus God has given back to life of which we all are witnesses
Act  And so being lifted up to the right hand of God and having the Fathers word that the Holy Spirit would come he has sent this thing which now you see and have knowledge of
Act  For David has not gone up into heaven but says himself The Lord said to my Lord Be seated at my right hand
Act  Till I put all those who are against you under your feet
Act  For this reason let all Israel be certain that this Jesus whom you put to death on the cross God has made Lord and Christ
Act  Now when these words came to their ears their hearts were troubled and they said to Peter and the other Apostles Brothers what are we to do
Act  And Peter said Let your hearts be changed every one of you and have baptism in the name of Jesus Christ for the forgiveness of your sins and you will have the Holy Spirit given to you
Act  For the word of God is for you and for your children and for all those who are far off even all those who may be marked out by the Lord our God
Act  And with more such words he gave his witness offering them salvation and saying Come out from this evil generation
Act  Then those who gave hearing to his words had baptism and about three thousand souls were joined to them that day
Act  And they kept their attention fixed on the Apostles teaching and were united together in the taking of broken bread and in prayer
Act  But fear came on every soul and all sorts of wonders and signs were done by the Apostles
Act  And all those who were of the faith kept together and had all things in common
Act  And exchanging their goods and property for money they made division of it among them all as they had need
Act  And day by day going in agreement together regularly to the Temple and taking broken bread together in their houses they took their food with joy and with true hearts
Act  Giving praise to God and having the approval of all the people and every day the number of those who had salvation was increased by the Lord
Act  Now Peter and John were going up to the Temple at the ninth hour the hour of prayer
Act  And a certain man who from birth had had no power in his legs was taken there every day and put down at the door of the Temple which is named Beautiful requesting money from those who went into the Temple
Act  He then seeing Peter and John going into the Temple made a request to them
Act  And Peter looking at him with John said Keep your eyes on us
Act  And he gave attention to them hoping to get something from them
Act  But Peter said I have no silver or gold but what I have that I give to you In the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth get up on your feet
Act  And he took him by his right hand lifting him up and straight away his feet and the bones of his legs became strong
Act  And jumping up he got on to his feet and went into the Temple with them walking and jumping and giving praise to God
Act  And all the people saw him walking and praising God
Act  And they saw that it was the man who made requests for money at the door of the Temple and they were full of wonder and surprise at what had taken place
Act  And while he kept his hands on Peter and John all the people came running together to the covered way which is named Solomons full of wonder
Act  And when Peter saw it he said to the people You men of Israel why are you so greatly surprised at this man or why are you looking at us as if by our power or virtue we had given him the use of his legs
Act  The God of Abraham of Isaac and of Jacob the God of our fathers has given glory to his servant Jesus whom you gave up turning your backs on him when Pilate had made the decision to let him go free
Act  But you would have nothing to do with the Holy and Upright One and made request for a man of blood to be given to you
Act  And put to death the Lord of life whom God gave back from the dead of which fact we are witnesses
Act  And his name through faith in his name has made this man strong whom you see and have knowledge of yes the faith which is through him has made him well before you all
Act  And now my brothers I am conscious that you did this as did your rulers without knowledge
Act  But the things which God had made clear before by the mouth of all the prophets that the Christ would have to undergo he has put into effect in this way
Act  So then let your hearts be changed and be turned to God so that your sins may be completely taken away and times of blessing may come from the Lord
Act  And that he may send the Christ who was marked out for you from the first even Jesus
Act  Who is to be kept in heaven till the time when all things are put right of which God has given word by the mouth of his holy prophets who have been from the earliest times
Act  For Moses said The Lord will give you a prophet from among your people like me you will give ear to everything which he will say to you
Act  And every soul who does not give attention to that prophet will be cut off from among the people
Act  And all the prophets from Samuel and those who came after every one of them gave word of these days
Act  You are the sons of the prophets and of the agreement which God made with your fathers saying to Abraham Through your seed a blessing will come on all the families of the earth
Act  To you first God sent his servant blessing you by turning every one of you from his sins
Act  And while they were talking to the people the priests and the captain of the Temple and the Sadducees came up to them
Act  Being greatly troubled because they were teaching the people and preaching Jesus as an example of the coming back from the dead
Act  And they took them and put them in prison till the morning for it was now evening
Act  But a number of those who gave hearing to the word had faith and they were now about five thousand
Act  And on the day after the rulers and those in authority and the scribes came together in Jerusalem
Act  And Annas the high priest was there and Caiaphas and John and Alexander and all the relations of the high priest
Act  Then sending for Peter and John they said By what power and in whose name have you done this
Act  Then Peter being full of the Holy Spirit said to them O you rulers of the people and men of authority
Act  If we are questioned today about a good work done to a man who was ill as to how he has been made well
Act  Take note all of you and all the people of Israel that in the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth whom you put to death on the cross whom God gave back from the dead even through him is this man now before you completely well
Act  He is the stone which you builders had no use for but which has been made the chief stone of the building
Act  And in no other is there salvation for there is no other name under heaven given among men through which we may have salvation
Act  Now when they saw that Peter and John were without fear though they were men of no education or learning they were greatly surprised and they took note of them that they had been with Jesus
Act  And seeing that the man who had been made well was there with them they were not able to say anything against it
Act  But when they had given them orders to go out of the Sanhedrin they had a discussion among themselves
Act  Saying What are we to do with these men for certainly it is clear to all who are living in Jerusalem that a most important sign has been done by them and it is not possible to say that it is not so
Act  But so that it may not go farther among the people let us put them in fear of punishment if they say anything in future in this name
Act  And they sent for them and gave them orders not to make statements or give teaching in the name of Jesus
Act  But Peter and John in answer said to them It is for you to say if it is right in the eyes of God to give attention to you more than to God
Act  For it is not possible for us to keep from saying what we have seen and have knowledge of
Act  And when they had said more sharp words to them they let them go not seeing what punishment they might give them because of the people for all men were giving praise to God for what had taken place
Act  For the man on whom this act of power was done was more than forty years old
Act  And when they had been made free they came back to their friends and gave an account of all the things which the chief priests and the authorities had said to them
Act  And hearing it they all with one mind made prayer to God and said O Lord maker of heaven and earth and the sea and all things in them
Act  Who has said by the Holy Spirit through the mouth of our father David your servant Why are the nations so violently moved and why are the thoughts of the people so foolish
Act  The kings of the earth were lifted up the rulers came together against the Lord and against his Christ
Act  For truly in this town against your holy servant Jesus who was marked out by you as Christ Herod and Pontius Pilate with the Gentiles and the people of Israel came together
Act  To do that which had been fixed before by your hand and your purpose
Act  And now Lord take note of their cruel words and give your servants power to be preachers of your word without fear
Act  While your hand is stretched out to do works of mercy so that signs and wonders may be done through the name of your holy servant Jesus
Act  And when their prayer was ended the place where they were was violently moved and they all became full of the Holy Spirit preaching the word of God without fear
Act  And all those who were of the faith were one in heart and soul and not one of them said that any of the things which he had was his property only but they had all things in common
Act  And with great power the Apostles gave witness of the coming back of the Lord Jesus from the dead and grace was on them all
Act  And no one among them was in need for everyone who had land or houses exchanging them for money took the price of them
Act  And put it at the feet of the Apostles for distribution to everyone as he had need
Act  And Joseph who was given by the Apostles the name of Barnabas the sense of which is Son of comfort a Levite and a man of Cyprus by birth
Act  Having a field got money for it and put the money at the feet of the Apostles
Act  But a certain man named Ananias with Sapphira his wife got money for his property
Act  And kept back part of the price his wife having knowledge of it and took the rest and put it at the feet of the Apostles
Act  But Peter said Ananias why has the Evil One put it into your heart to be false to the Holy Spirit and to keep back part of the price of the land
Act  While you had it was it not your property and after you had given it in exchange was it not still in your power how has this purpose come into your mind you have been false not to men but to God
Act  And at these words Ananias went down on the earth and his life went from him and great fear came on all who were present
Act  And the young men went and made ready his body and took it out and put it in the earth
Act  And about three hours after his wife having no knowledge of what had taken place came in
Act  And Peter said to her Give me an answer was this amount of money the price of the land And she said Yes it was
Act  But Peter said to her Why have you made an agreement together to be false to the Spirit of the Lord See the feet of the young men who have put the body of your husband in the earth are at the door and they will take you out
Act  And straight away she went down at his feet and her life went from her and the young men came in and saw her dead and they took her out and put her in the earth with her husband
Act  Then great fear came on all the church and on all who had knowledge of these things
Act  Now a number of signs and wonders were done among the people by the hands of the Apostles and they were all together in Solomons covered way
Act  The others in fear kept back from joining them but the people made much of them
Act  And a great number of men and women had faith and were joined to the Lord
Act  And they even took into the streets people who were ill and put them on beds so that when Peter went by some of them might be in his shade
Act  And numbers of people came together from the towns round about Jerusalem with those who were ill and those who were troubled with unclean spirits and they were all made well
Act  But the high priest and those who were with him the Sadducees were full of envy
Act  And they took the Apostles and put them in the common prison
Act  But in the night an angel of the Lord opening the doors of the prison took them out and said
Act  Go take your place in the Temple and give the people all the teaching about this Life
Act  And hearing this they went into the Temple at dawn and were teaching But the high priest and those who were with him got together the Sanhedrin and the representatives of the children of Israel and sent to the prison to get them
Act  But the men who were sent saw that they were not in the prison and came back with the news
Act  Saying The doors of the prison were safely shut and the keepers were at the doors but when they were open there was nobody inside
Act  Now at these words the captain of the Temple and the chief priests were greatly troubled about what might be the end of this business
Act  And someone came and said to them The men whom you put in prison are in the Temple teaching the people
Act  Then the captain and some of the police went and took them but not violently for fear that they might be stoned by the people
Act  And they took them into the Sanhedrin and the high priest said to them
Act  We gave you very clear orders not to give teaching in this name and now Jerusalem is full of your teaching and you are attempting to make us responsible for this mans death
Act  But Peter and the Apostles answering said We have to do the orders of God not of man
Act  The God of our fathers gave Jesus back to life whom you had put to death hanging him on a tree
Act  Him God has put on high at his right hand as a Ruler and a Saviour to give to Israel a change of heart and forgiveness of sins
Act  And we are witnesses of these things and so is the Holy Spirit whom God has given to those who keep his laws
Act  But when these words came to their ears they were cut to the heart and had a mind to put them to death
Act  But one of the Sanhedrin a Pharisee named Gamaliel a man of learning in the law of whom all the people had a high opinion got up and made a suggestion for the men to be put outside for a little time
Act  And he said to them Men of Israel take care what you do about these men
Act  For before this there was Theudas who said he was someone important to whom about four hundred men gave their support he was put to death and his band was broken up and came to nothing
Act  After this man there was Judas of Galilee at the time of the numbering and some of the people went after him he was put to death and all his supporters were put to flight
Act  And now I say to you Do nothing to these men but let them be for if this teaching or this work is of men it will come to nothing
Act  But if it is of God you will not be able to overcome them and you are in danger of fighting against God
Act  And he seemed to them to be right and they sent for the Apostles and after having them whipped and giving them orders to give no teaching in the name of Jesus they let them go
Act  So they went away from the Sanhedrin happy to undergo shame for the Name
Act  And every day in the Temple and privately they went on teaching and preaching Jesus as the Christ
Act  Now in those days when the number of the disciples was increasing protests were made by the Greek Jews against the Hebrews because their widows were not taken care of in the distribution of food every day
Act  And the Apostles sent for all the disciples and said It is not right for us to give up preaching the word of God in order to make distribution of food
Act  Take then from among you seven men of good name full of the Spirit and of wisdom to whom we may give control of this business
Act  Then we will give all our time to prayer and the teaching of the word
Act  And this saying was pleasing to all of them and they made selection of Stephen a man full of faith and of the Holy Spirit and Philip and Prochorus and Nicanor and Timon and Parmenas and Nicolas of Antioch who had become a Jew
Act  These they took to the Apostles who after prayer put their hands on them
Act  And the word of God was increasing in power and the number of the disciples in Jerusalem became very great and a great number of priests were in agreement with the faith
Act  And Stephen full of grace and power did great wonders and signs among the people
Act  But some of those who were of the Synagogue named that of the Libertines and some of the men of Cyrene and of Alexandria and those from Cilicia and Asia had arguments with Stephen
Act  But they were not able to get the better of him for his words were full of wisdom and of the Spirit
Act  Then they got men to say He has said evil against Moses and against God in our hearing
Act  And the people with the rulers and the scribes were moved against him and they came and took him before the Sanhedrin
Act  And they got false witnesses who said This man is for ever saying things against this holy place and against the law
Act  For he has said in our hearing that this Jesus of Nazareth will put this place to destruction and make changes in the rules which were handed down to us by Moses
Act  And all those who were in the Sanhedrin looking at him saw that his face was like the face of an angel
Act  Then the high priest said Are these things true
Act  And he said My brothers and fathers give hearing The God of glory came to our father Abraham when he was in Mesopotamia before he was living in Haran
Act  And said to him Go out of your land and away from your family and come into the land to which I will be your guide
Act  Then he came out of the land of the Chaldaeans and went into Haran and from there when his father was dead he was guided by God into this land where you are living now
Act  And God gave him no heritage in it not even enough to put his foot on but he gave him an undertaking that he would give it to him and to his children after him though he had no child at that time
Act  And God said that his seed would be living in a strange land and that they would make them servants and be cruel to them for four hundred years
Act  And I will be the judge said God of that nation which made them servants and after that they will come out and give me worship in this place
Act  And he made with him the agreement of which circumcision was the sign And so Abraham had a son Isaac and gave him circumcision on the eighth day and Isaac had a son Jacob and Jacob was the father of the twelve heads of the families of Israel
Act  And the brothers moved with envy against Joseph gave him to the Egyptians for money but God was with him
Act  And made him free from all his troubles and gave him wisdom and the approval of Pharaoh king of Egypt who made him ruler over Egypt and all his house
Act  Now there was no food to be had in all Egypt and Canaan and there was great trouble and our fathers were not able to get food
Act  But Jacob hearing that there was grain in Egypt sent out our fathers the first time
Act  And the second time his brothers had a meeting with Joseph and Pharaoh had knowledge of Josephs family
Act  Then Joseph sent for Jacob his father and all his family seventyfive persons
Act  And Jacob went down to Egypt and came to his end there and so did our fathers
Act  And they were taken over to Shechem and put to rest in the place which Abraham got for a price in silver from the sons of Hamor in Shechem
Act  But when the time was near for putting into effect the undertaking which God had given to Abraham the people were increasing in Egypt
Act  Till another king came to power who had no knowledge of Joseph
Act  He having evil designs against our nation was cruel to our fathers and they were forced to put out their young children so that they might not go on living
Act  At which time Moses came to birth and he was very beautiful and he was kept for three months in his fathers house
Act  And when he was put out Pharaohs daughter took him and kept him as her son
Act  And Moses was trained in all the wisdom of Egypt and was great in his words and works
Act  But when he was almost forty years old it came into his heart to go and see his brothers the children of Israel
Act  And seeing one of them being attacked he went to his help and gave the Egyptian a deathblow
Act  And he was hoping that his brothers would see that God had sent him to be their saviour but they did not see
Act  And the day after he came to them while they were having a fight and would have made peace between them saying Sirs you are brothers why do you do wrong to one another
Act  But the man who was doing wrong to his neighbour pushing him away said Who made you a ruler and a judge over us
Act  Will you put me to death as you did the Egyptian yesterday
Act  And at these words Moses went in flight to the land of Midian and was living there for a time and had two sons
Act  At the end of forty years an angel came to him in the waste land of Sinai in the flame of a burning thorntree
Act  And Moses seeing it was full of wonder and when he came up to have a nearer view of it the voice of the Lord came to him saying
Act  I am the God of your fathers the God of Abraham and of Isaac and of Jacob And Moses shaking with fear kept his eyes from looking at it
Act  And the Lord said Take off the shoes from your feet for the place where you are is holy
Act  Truly I have seen the sorrows of my people in Egypt and their cries have come to my ears and I have come down to make them free and now come I will send you to Egypt
Act  This Moses whom they would not have saying Who made you a ruler and a judge him God sent to be a ruler and a saviour by the hand of the angel whom he saw in the thorntree
Act  This man took them out having done wonders and signs in Egypt and in the Red Sea and in the waste land for forty years
Act  This is the same Moses who said to the children of Israel God will give you a prophet from among your brothers like me
Act  This is the man who was in the church in the waste land with the angel who was talking to him in Sinai and with our fathers and to him were given the living words of God so that he might give them to you
Act  By whom our fathers would not be controlled but they put him on one side turning back in their hearts to Egypt
Act  And saying to Aaron Make us gods to go before us as for this Moses who took us out of the land of Egypt we have no idea what has become of him
Act  And they made the image of a young ox in those days and made an offering to it and had joy in the work of their hands
Act  But God was turned from them and let them give worship to the stars of heaven as it says in the book of the prophets Did you make offerings to me of sheep and oxen for forty years in the waste land O house of Israel
Act  And you took up the tent of Moloch and the star of the god Rephan images which you made to give worship to them and I will take you away farther than Babylon
Act  Our fathers had the Tent of witness in the waste land as God gave orders to Moses to make it after the design which he had seen
Act  Which our fathers in their turn took with them when with Joshua they came into the heritage of the nations whom God was driving out before the face of our fathers till the time of David
Act  Who was pleasing to God and he had a desire to make a holy tent for the God of Jacob
Act  But Solomon was the builder of his house
Act  But still the Most High has not his restingplace in houses made with hands as the prophet says
Act  Heaven is the seat of my power and earth is a restingplace for my feet what sort of house will you make for me says the Lord or what is my place of rest
Act  Did not my hand make all these things
Act  You whose hearts are hard and whose ears are shut to me you are ever working against the Holy Spirit as your fathers did so do you
Act  Which of the prophets was not cruelly attacked by your fathers and they put to death those who gave them the news of the coming of the Upright One whom you have now given up and put to death
Act  You to whom the law was given as it was ordered by angels and who have not kept it
Act  Hearing these things they were cut to the heart and moved with wrath against him
Act  But he was full of the Holy Spirit and looking up to heaven he saw the glory of God and Jesus at the right hand of God
Act  And he said Now I see heaven open and the Son of man at the right hand of God
Act  But with loud cries and stopping their ears they made an attack on him all together
Act  Driving him out of the town and stoning him and the witnesses put their clothing at the feet of a young man named Saul
Act  And Stephen while he was being stoned made prayer to God saying Lord Jesus take my spirit
Act  And going down on his knees he said in a loud voice Lord do not make them responsible for this sin And when he had said this he went to his rest
Act  And Saul gave approval to his death Now at that time a violent attack was started against the church in Jerusalem and all but the Apostles went away into all parts of Judaea and Samaria
Act  And Godfearing men put Stephens body in its last restingplace making great weeping over him
Act  But Saul was burning with hate against the church going into every house and taking men and women and putting them in prison
Act  But those who had gone in flight went everywhere preaching the word
Act  And Philip went down to Samaria and was teaching them about Christ
Act  And all the people gave attention to the words which Philip said when they saw the signs which he did
Act  For unclean spirits came out from those who had them crying with a loud voice and a number of those who were ill and broken in body were made well
Act  And there was much joy in that town
Act  But there was a certain man named Simon who in the past had been a wonderworker and a cause of surprise to the people of Samaria saying that he himself was a great man
Act  To whom they all gave attention from the smallest to the greatest saying This man is that power of God which is named Great
Act  And they gave attention to him because for a long time his wonderworking powers had kept them under his control
Act  But when they had faith in the good news given by Philip about the kingdom of God and the name of Jesus Christ a number of men and women had baptism
Act  And Simon himself had faith and having had baptism he went with Philip and seeing the signs and the great wonders which he did he was full of surprise
Act  Now when the Apostles at Jerusalem had news that the people of Samaria had taken the word of God into their hearts they sent to them Peter and John
Act  Who when they came there made prayer for them that the Holy Spirit might be given to them
Act  For up to that time he had not come on any of them only baptism had been given to them in the name of the Lord Jesus
Act  Then they put their hands on them and the Holy Spirit came on them
Act  Now when Simon saw that the Holy Spirit was given through the touch of the Apostles hands he made them an offering of money saying
Act  Give me this power so that when I put my hands on anyone he may get the Holy Spirit
Act  But Peter said May your money come to destruction with you because you had the idea that what is freely given by God may be got for a price
Act  You have no part in this business because your heart is not right before God
Act  Let your heart be changed and make prayer to God that you may have forgiveness for your evil thoughts
Act  For I see that you are prisoned in bitter envy and the chains of sin
Act  And Simon answering said Make prayer for me to the Lord so that these things which you have said may not come on me
Act  So they having given their witness and made clear the word of the Lord went back to Jerusalem giving the good news on their way in a number of the small towns of Samaria
Act  But an angel of the Lord said to Philip Get up and go to the south to the road which goes from Jerusalem to Gaza through the waste land
Act  And he went and there was a man of Ethiopia a servant of great authority under Candace queen of the Ethiopians and controller of all her property who had come up to Jerusalem for worship
Act  He was going back seated in his carriage and was reading the book of the prophet Isaiah
Act  And the Spirit said to Philip Go near and get on his carriage
Act  And Philip running up to him saw that he was reading Isaiah the prophet and said to him Is the sense of what you are reading clear to you
Act  And he said How is that possible when I have no guide And he made Philip get up by his side
Act  Now the place in the book where he was reading was this He was taken like a sheep to be put to death and as a lamb is quiet when its wool is being cut so he made no sound
Act  Being of low degree his cause was not given a hearing who has knowledge of his family for his life is cut off from the earth
Act  And the Ethiopian said to Philip About whom are these words said by the prophet about himself or some other
Act  So Philip starting from this writing gave him the good news about Jesus
Act  And while they were going on their way they came to some water and the Ethiopian said See here is water why may I not have baptism
Act  
Act  And he gave orders for the carriage to be stopped and the two of them went down into the water and Philip gave him baptism
Act  And when they came up out of the water the Spirit of the Lord took Philip away and the Ethiopian saw him no more for he went on his way full of joy
Act  But Philip came to Azotus and went through all the towns preaching the good news till he came to Caesarea
Act  But Saul still burning with desire to put to death the disciples of the Lord went to the high priest
Act  And made a request for letters from him to the Synagogues of Damascus so that if there were any of the Way there men or women he might take them as prisoners to Jerusalem
Act  And while he was journeying he came near Damascus and suddenly he saw a light from heaven shining round him
Act  And he went down on the earth and a voice said to him Saul Saul why are you attacking me so cruelly
Act  And he said Who are you Lord And he said I am Jesus whom you are attacking
Act  But get up and go into the town and it will be made clear to you what you have to do
Act  And the men who were with him were not able to say anything hearing the voice but seeing no one
Act  And Saul got up from the earth and when his eyes were open he saw nothing and he was guided by the hand into Damascus
Act  And for three days he was not able to see and he took no food or drink
Act  Now there was a certain disciple at Damascus named Ananias and the Lord said to him in a vision Ananias and he said Here I am Lord
Act  And the Lord said to him Get up and go to the street which is named Straight and make search at the house of Judas for one named Saul of Tarsus for he is at prayer
Act  And he has seen a man named Ananias coming in and putting his hands on him so that he may be able to see
Act  But Ananias said Lord I have had accounts of this man from a number of people how much evil he has done to your saints at Jerusalem
Act  And here he has authority from the chief priests to make prisoners all who give worship to your name
Act  But the Lord said Go without fear for he is a special vessel for me to give to the Gentiles and kings and to the children of Israel the knowledge of my name
Act  For I will make clear to him what troubles he will have to undergo for me
Act  And Ananias went out and came to the house and putting his hands on him said Brother Saul the Lord Jesus whom you saw when you were on your journey has sent me so that you may be able to see and be full of the Holy Spirit
Act  And straight away it seemed as if a veil was taken from his eyes and he was able to see and he got up and had baptism
Act  And when he had taken food his strength came back And for some days he kept with the disciples who were in Damascus
Act  And straight away in the Synagogues he was preaching Jesus as the Son of God
Act  And all those hearing him were full of wonder and said Is not this the man who in Jerusalem was attacking all the worshippers of this name and he had come here so that he might take them as prisoners before the chief priests
Act  But Saul went on increasing in power and the Jews in Damascus were not able to give answers to the arguments by which he made it clear that Jesus was the Christ
Act  Then after some days the Jews made an agreement together to put him to death
Act  But Saul got knowledge of their design And they kept watch day and night on the roads out of the town so that they might put him to death
Act  But his disciples took him by night and let him down from the wall in a basket
Act  And when he came to Jerusalem he made an attempt to be joined to the disciples but they were all in fear of him not taking him for a disciple
Act  But Barnabas took him to the Apostles and gave them an account of how he had seen the Lord on the road and had given hearing to his words and how at Damascus he had been preaching in the name of Jesus without fear
Act  And he was with them going in and out at Jerusalem
Act  Preaching in the name of the Lord without fear and he had discussions with the Greek Jews but they were working for his death
Act  And when the brothers had knowledge of it they took him to Caesarea and sent him to Tarsus
Act  And so the church through all Judaea and Galilee and Samaria had peace and was made strong and living in the fear of the Lord and in the comfort of the Holy Spirit was increased greatly
Act  And it came about that while Peter was going through all parts of the country he came to the saints who were living at Lydda
Act  And there was a certain man there named Aeneas who for eight years had been in bed without power of moving
Act  And Peter said to him Aeneas Jesus Christ makes you well get up and make your bed And straight away he got up
Act  And all those living in Lydda and Sharon saw him and were turned to the Lord
Act  Now there was at Joppa a certain disciple named Tabitha that is Dorcas this woman was given to good works and acts of mercy at all times
Act  And it came about in those days that she got ill and came to her death and when she had been washed they put her in a room which was high up
Act  And because Lydda was near Joppa the disciples having knowledge that Peter was there sent two men to him requesting him to come to them straight away
Act  And Peter went with them And when he had come they took him into the room and all the widows were there weeping and putting before him the coats and clothing which Dorcas had made while she was with them
Act  But Peter made them all go outside and went down on his knees in prayer and turning to the body he said Tabitha get up And opening her eyes she saw Peter and got up
Act  And he took her hand lifting her up and sending for the saints and widows he gave her to them living
Act  And news of it went all through Joppa and a number of people had faith in the Lord
Act  And he was living in Joppa for some time with Simon a leatherworker
Act  Now there was a certain man in Caesarea named Cornelius the captain of the Italian band of the army
Act  A seriousminded man fearing God with all his family he gave much money to the poor and made prayer to God at all times
Act  He saw in a vision clearly at about the ninth hour of the day an angel of the Lord coming to him and saying to him Cornelius
Act  And he looking on him in fear said What is it Lord And he said to him Your prayers and your offerings have come up to God and he has kept them in mind
Act  Now send men to Joppa and get one Simon named Peter
Act  Who is living with Simon a leatherworker whose house is by the sea
Act  And when the angel who said these words to him had gone away he sent for two of his houseservants and a Godfearing man of the army one of those who were waiting on him at all times
Act  And having given them an account of everything he sent them to Joppa
Act  Now the day after when they were on their journey and were near the town Peter went up to the top of the house for prayer about the sixth hour
Act  And he was in need of food but while they were getting it ready a deep sleep came on him
Act  And he saw the heavens opening and a vessel coming down like a great cloth let down on the earth
Act  In which were all sorts of beasts and birds
Act  And a voice came to him saying Come Peter take them for food
Act  But Peter said No Lord for I have never taken food which is common or unclean
Act  And the voice came to him a second time What God has made clean do not you make common
Act  And this was done three times and then the vessel was taken back into heaven
Act  Now while Peter was in doubt as to the purpose of this vision the men who were sent by Cornelius having made search for Simons house came to the door
Act  To see if Simon named Peter was living there
Act  And while Peter was turning the vision over in his mind the Spirit said to him See three men are looking for you
Act  Go down then and go with them doubting nothing for I have sent them
Act  And Peter went down to the men and said I am the man you are looking for why have you come
Act  And they said Cornelius a captain an upright and Godfearing man respected by all the nation of the Jews had word from God by an angel to send for you to his house and to give hearing to your words
Act  So he took them in for the night And the day after he went with them taking some of the brothers from Joppa with him
Act  And the day after that they came to Caesarea And Cornelius was waiting for them having got together his relations and his near friends
Act  And when Peter came in Cornelius came to him and falling down at his feet gave him worship
Act  But Peter lifting him up said Get up for I am a man as you are
Act  And saying these words he went in and saw that a great number of people had come together
Act  And he said to them You yourselves have knowledge that it is against the law for a man who is a Jew to be in the company of one who is of another nation but God has made it clear to me that no man may be named common or unclean
Act  And so I came without question when I was sent for What then is your purpose in sending for me
Act  And Cornelius said Four days from now I was in my house in prayer at the ninth hour and I saw before me a man in shining clothing
Act  Who said Cornelius your prayer has come to the ears of God and your offerings are kept in his memory
Act  Send then to Joppa and get Simon named Peter to come to you he is living in the house of Simon a leatherworker by the sea
Act  So straight away I sent for you and you have done well to come And now we are all present before God ready to give attention to all the things which the Lord has given you to say
Act  Then Peter said Truly I see clearly that God is no respecter of persons
Act  But in every nation the man who has fear of him and does righteousness is pleasing to him
Act  The word which he sent to the children of Israel giving the good news of peace through Jesus Christ who is Lord of all
Act  That word you yourselves have knowledge of which was made public through all Judaea starting from Galilee after the baptism of which John was the preacher
Act  About Jesus of Nazareth how God gave the Holy Spirit to him with power and how he went about doing good and making well all who were troubled by evil spirits for God was with him
Act  And we are witnesses of all the things which he did in the country of the Jews and in Jerusalem whom they put to death hanging him on a tree
Act  On the third day God gave him back to life and let him be seen
Act  Not by all the people but by witnesses marked out before by God even by us who took food and drink with him after he came back from the dead
Act  And he gave us orders to give news of this to the people and to give public witness that this is he whom God has made judge of the living and the dead
Act  To him all the prophets give witness that through his name everyone who has faith in him will have forgiveness of sins
Act  While Peter was saying these words the Holy Spirit came on all those who were hearing the word
Act  And the Jews of the faith who had come with Peter were full of wonder because the Holy Spirit was given to the Gentiles
Act  And they were talking in tongues and giving glory to God Then Peter said
Act  Will any man say that these may not have baptism who have been given the Holy Spirit as we have
Act  And he gave orders for them to have baptism in the name of Jesus Christ Then they kept him with them for some days
Act  Now the Apostles and the brothers who were in Judaea had news that the word of God had been given to the Gentiles
Act  And when Peter came to Jerusalem those who kept the rule of circumcision had an argument with him
Act  Saying You went to men without circumcision and took food with them
Act  But Peter gave them an account of it all in order saying to them
Act  I was in the town of Joppa at prayer and falling into a deep sleep I saw in a vision a vessel like a great cloth let down from heaven and it came down to me
Act  And looking on it with attention I saw in it all sorts of beasts and birds
Act  And a voice came to my ears saying Come Peter take them for food
Act  But I said No Lord for nothing common or unclean has ever come into my mouth
Act  But the voice coming a second time from heaven said What God has made clean do not you make common
Act  And this was done three times and they were all taken up again into heaven
Act  And at that minute three men sent from Caesarea came to the house where we were
Act  And the Spirit gave me orders to go with them doubting nothing And these six brothers came with me and we went into that mans house
Act  And he gave us an account of how he had seen the angel in his house saying Send to Joppa and get Simon named Peter to come to you
Act  Who will say words to you through which you and all your family may get salvation
Act  And while I was talking to them the Holy Spirit came on them as on us at first
Act  And the words of the Lord came into my mind how he said The baptism of John was with water but you will have baptism with the Holy Spirit
Act  If then God gave them when they had faith in the Lord Jesus Christ the same as he gave to us who was I to go against God
Act  And hearing these things they said nothing more but gave glory to God saying Then to the Gentiles as to us has God given a change of heart so that they may have life
Act  Then those who had gone away at the time of the trouble about Stephen went as far as Phoenicia and Cyprus preaching to the Jews only
Act  But some of them men of Cyprus and Cyrene when they came to Antioch gave the good news about the Lord Jesus to the Greeks
Act  And the power of the Lord was with them and a great number had faith and were turned to the Lord
Act  And news of them came to the ears of the church at Jerusalem and they sent Barnabas as far as Antioch
Act  Who when he came and saw the grace of God was glad and he made clear to them the need of keeping near the Lord with all the strength of their hearts
Act  For he was a good man and full of the Holy Spirit and of faith and a great number were joined to the Lord
Act  Then he went on to Tarsus looking for Saul
Act  And when he had come across him he took him to Antioch And they were with the church there for a year teaching the people and the disciples were first given the name of Christians in Antioch
Act  Now in those days prophets came from Jerusalem to Antioch
Act  And one of them named Agabus said publicly through the Spirit that there would be serious need of food all over the earth which came about in the time of Claudius
Act  And the disciples everyone as he was able made a decision to send help to the brothers living in Judaea
Act  Which they did sending it to the rulers of the church by the hand of Barnabas and Saul
Act  Now about that time Herod the king made cruel attacks on the Christians
Act  And he put James the brother of John to death with the sword
Act  And when he saw that this was pleasing to the Jews he went on to take Peter in addition This was at the time of the feast of unleavened bread
Act  And having taken him he put him in prison with four bands of armed men to keep watch over him his purpose being to take him out to the people after the Passover
