Act  So Peter was kept in prison but the church made strong prayer to God for him
Act  And when Herod was about to take him out the same night Peter was sleeping in chains between two armed men and the watchmen were keeping watch before the door of the prison
Act  And a great light was seen shining in the room and an angel of the Lord came to Peter and touching him on his side so that he came out of his sleep said Get up quickly And his chains came off his hands
Act  Then the angel said Put on your shoes and get ready to go And he did so And he said Put your coat round you and come with me
Act  And he went out after him and he was not certain if what was done by the angel was a fact for it seemed to him that he was seeing a vision
Act  And when they had gone past the first and second watchmen they came to the iron door into the town which came open by itself and they went out and down one street and then the angel went away
Act  And when Peter came to his senses he said Now truly I am certain that the Lord has sent his angel and taken me out of the hands of Herod against all the hopes of the Jews
Act  And when he became clear about this he went to the house of Mary the mother of John named Mark where a number of them had come together for prayer
Act  And he gave a blow on the door and a young girl came to it named Rhoda
Act  And hearing the voice of Peter in her joy she went running without opening the door to say that Peter was outside
Act  And they said to her You are off your head But still she said with decision that it was so And they said It is his angel
Act  But Peter went on giving blows on the door and when it was open and they saw him they were full of wonder
Act  But he made a sign to them with his hand to be quiet and gave them an account of how the Lord had taken him out of prison And he said Give the news to James and the brothers And then he went away
Act  Now when it was day the armed men were greatly troubled about what had become of Peter
Act  And Herod when he sent for him and he was not there after questioning the watchmen gave orders that they were to be put to death Then he went down from Judaea to Caesarea for a time
Act  Now he was very angry with the people of Tyre and Sidon and they came to him all together and having made friends with Blastus the controller of the kings house they made a request for peace because their country was dependent on the kings country for its food
Act  And on the day which had been fixed Herod dressed in his robes and seated in his place made a public statement to them
Act  And the people with loud cries said It is the voice of a god not of a man
Act  And straight away the angel of the Lord sent a disease on him because he did not give the glory to God and his flesh was wasted away by worms and so he came to his end
Act  But the word of the Lord went on increasing
Act  And Barnabas and Saul came back from Jerusalem when their work was ended taking with them John named Mark
Act  Now there were at Antioch in the church there prophets and teachers Barnabas and Symeon who was named Niger and Lucius of Cyrene and Manaen a relation of Herod the king and Saul
Act  And while they were doing the Lords work and going without food the Holy Spirit said Let Barnabas and Saul be given to me for the special work for which they have been marked out by me
Act  Then after prayer and going without food they put their hands on them and sent them away
Act  So being sent out by the Holy Spirit they went down to Seleucia and from there they went by ship to Cyprus
Act  And at Salamis they were preaching the word of God in the Synagogues of the Jews and John was with them helping them
Act  And when they had gone through all the island to Paphos they came across a certain wonderworker and false prophet a Jew whose name was BarJesus
Act  Who was with the ruler Sergius Paulus an able man This man sent for Barnabas and Saul desiring to have knowledge of the word of God
Act  But Elymas the wonderworker for that is the sense of his name put himself against them with the purpose of turning the ruler from the faith
Act  But Saul whose other name is Paul being full of the Holy Spirit looking hard at him said
Act  O you who are full of false tricks and evil ways a son of the Evil One hating all righteousness will you for ever be turning people from the right ways of the Lord
Act  And now see the hand of the Lord is on you and you will be blind and not able to see the sun for a time And straight away a dark mist came down on him and he went about looking for a guide
Act  Then the ruler when he saw what was done had faith being full of wonder at the teaching of the Lord
Act  Then Paul and those who were with him went by ship from Paphos and came to Perga in Pamphylia and there John went away from them and came back to Jerusalem
Act  But they going through from Perga came to Antioch in Pisidia and they went into the Synagogue on the Sabbath and were seated
Act  And after the reading of the law and the prophets the rulers of the Synagogue sent to them saying Brothers if you have a word of comfort for the people say on
Act  And Paul getting up and making a sign with his hand said Men of Israel and you who have the fear of God give ear
Act  The God of this people Israel made selection of our fathers lifting the people up from their low condition when they were living in the land of Egypt and with a strong arm took them out of it
Act  And for about forty years he put up with their ways in the waste land
Act  And having put to destruction seven nations in the land of Canaan he gave them the land for their heritage for about four hundred and fifty years
Act  And after these things he gave them judges till the time of Samuel the prophet
Act  Then at their request for a king God gave them Saul the son of Kish a man of the family of Benjamin who was their king for forty years
Act  And having put him on one side he made David their king to whom he gave witness saying I have taken David the son of Jesse a man dear to my heart who will do all my pleasure
Act  From this mans seed has God given to Israel a Saviour even Jesus as he gave his word
Act  For whose coming John made ready the way by preaching to all the people of Israel the baptism which goes with a change of heart
Act  And when John was completing his work he said What do I seem to you to be I am not he but one is coming after me whose shoes I am not good enough to undo
Act  My brothers children of the family of Abraham and those among you who have the fear of God to us the word of this salvation is sent
Act  For the men of Jerusalem and their rulers having no knowledge of him or of the sayings of the prophets which come to their ears every Sabbath day gave effect to them by judging him
Act  And though no cause of death was seen in him they made a request to Pilate that he might be put to death
Act  And when they had done all the things said in the Writings about him they took him down from the tree and put him in the place of the dead
Act  But God gave him back from the dead
Act  And for a number of days he was seen by those who came with him from Galilee to Jerusalem who are now his witnesses before the people
Act  And we are giving you the good news of the undertaking made to the fathers
Act  Which God has now put into effect for our children by sending Jesus as it says in the second Psalm You are my Son this day I have given you being
Act  And about his coming back from the dead never again to go to destruction he has said these words I will give you the holy and certain mercies of David
Act  Because he says in another Psalm You will not let your Holy One see destruction
Act  Now David having done Gods work for his generation went to sleep and was put with his fathers and his body came to destruction
Act  But he who was lifted up by God did not see destruction
Act  And so let it be clear to you my brothers that through this man forgiveness of sins is offered to you
Act  And through him everyone who has faith is made free from all those things from which the law of Moses was not able to make you free
Act  So take care that these words of the prophets do not come true for you
Act  See you doubters have wonder and come to your end for I will do a thing in your days to which you will not give belief even if it is made clear to you
Act  And when they went out they made a request that these words might be said to them again on the Sabbath after
Act  Now when the meeting was ended a number of the Jews and of the Godfearing Gentiles who had become Jews went after Paul and Barnabas who put before them how important it was to keep on in the grace of God
Act  And on the Sabbath after almost all the town came together to give hearing to the word of God
Act  But when the Jews saw such a great number of people they were full of envy and said evil words against Pauls preaching
Act  Then Paul and Barnabas without fear said It was necessary for the word of God to be given to you first but because you will have nothing to do with it and have no desire for eternal life it will now be offered to the Gentiles
Act  For so the Lord has given us orders saying I have given you for a light to the Gentiles so that you may be for salvation to the ends of the earth
Act  And the Gentiles hearing this were glad and gave glory to the word of God and those marked out by God for eternal life had faith
Act  And the word of the Lord went through all the country
Act  But the Jews working up the feelings of the Godfearing women of high position and of the chief men of the town got an attack started against Paul and Barnabas driving them out of those parts
Act  But they shaking off the dust of that place from their feet came to Iconium
Act  And the disciples were full of joy and of the Holy Spirit
Act  Now in Iconium they went together to the Synagogue of the Jews and gave such teaching that a great number of Jews and Greeks had faith
Act  But those Jews who had not the faith made the minds of the Gentiles bitter against the brothers
Act  So they kept there for a long time taking heart in the Lord who gave witness to the word of his grace by causing signs and wonders to be done by their hands
Act  But there was a division among the people of the town some were on the side of the Jews and some on the side of the Apostles
Act  And when a violent attempt was made by the Gentiles and the Jews with their rulers to make an attack on them and have them stoned
Act  Having got news of it they went in flight to the towns of Lycaonia Lystra and Derbe and the country round about
Act  And went on preaching the good news there
Act  And at Lystra there was a certain man who from birth had been without the use of his feet never having had the power of walking
Act  This man was giving ear to the preaching of Paul who looking at him and seeing that he had faith to be made well
Act  Said in a loud voice Get up on your feet And jumping up he went walking about
Act  And when the people saw what Paul had done they said in a loud voice in the language of Lycaonia The gods have come down to us in the form of men
Act  And they gave the name of Jupiter to Barnabas and to Paul that of Mercury because he was the chief talker
Act  And the priest of the image of Jupiter which was before the town took oxen and flowers to the doors of the town and was about to make an offering with the people
Act  But when this came to the ears of the Apostles Paul and Barnabas they went running out among the people parting their clothing and crying out
Act  Good people why are you doing these things We are men with the same feelings as you and we give you the good news so that you may be turned away from these foolish things to the living God who made the heaven and the earth and the sea and all things in them
Act  Who in the past let all nations go in the ways which seemed good to them
Act  But he was not without witness because he did good and gave you rain from heaven and times of fruit making your hearts full of food and joy
Act  And even with these words it was hard for them to keep the people from making an offering to them
Act  But some Jews came to that place from Antioch and Iconium and got control over the people and after stoning Paul they had him pulled out of the town taking him for dead
Act  But when the disciples came round him he got up and went into the town and the day after he went away with Barnabas to Derbe
Act  And having made a number of disciples through the preaching of the good news in that town they went back to Lystra and Iconium and Antioch
Act  Making strong the souls of the disciples saying to them that they were to keep the faith and that we have to go through troubles of all sorts to come into the kingdom of God
Act  And when they had made selection of some to be rulers in every church and had given themselves to prayer and kept themselves from food they put them into the care of the Lord in whom they had faith
Act  And they went through Pisidia and came to Pamphylia
Act  And after preaching the word in Perga they went down to Attalia
Act  And from there they went by ship to Antioch where they had been handed over to the grace of God for the work which they had not done
Act  And when they came there and had got the church together they gave them an account of all the things which God had done through them and how he had made open a door of faith to the Gentiles
Act  And they were with the disciples there for a long time
Act  Now certain men came down from Judaea teaching the brothers and saying that without circumcision after the rule of Moses there is no salvation
Act  And after Paul and Barnabas had had no little argument and discussion with them the brothers made a decision to send Paul and Barnabas and certain others of them to the Apostles and the rulers of the church at Jerusalem about this question
Act  So they being sent on their way by the church went through Phoenicia and Samaria giving news of the salvation of the Gentiles to the great joy of all the brothers
Act  And when they came to Jerusalem they had a meeting with the church and the Apostles and the rulers and they gave an account of all the things which God had done through them
Act  But some of the Pharisees who were of the faith got up and said It is necessary for these to have circumcision and to keep the law of Moses
Act  And the Apostles and the rulers of the church came together and gave thought to the question
Act  And when there had been much discussion Peter got up and said to them My brothers you have knowledge that some time back it was Gods pleasure that by my mouth the good news might be given to the Gentiles so that they might have faith
Act  And God the searcher of hearts was a witness to them giving them the Holy Spirit even as he did to us
Act  Making no division between them and us but making clean their hearts by faith
Act  Why then are you testing God by putting on the neck of the disciples a yoke so hard that not even our fathers or we were strong enough for it
Act  But we have faith that we will get salvation through the grace of the Lord Jesus in the same way as they
Act  And all the people were quiet while Barnabas and Paul gave an account of the signs and wonders which God had done among the Gentiles by them
Act  And when they had come to an end James answering said My brothers give ear to me
Act  Symeon has given an account of how God was first pleased to take from among the Gentiles a people for himself
Act  And this is in agreement with the words of the prophets as it is said
Act  After these things I will come back and will put up the tent of David which has been broken down building up again its broken parts and making it complete
Act  So that the rest of men may make search for the Lord and all the Gentiles on whom my name is named
Act  Says the Lord who has made these things clear from the earliest times
Act  For this reason my decision is that we do not put trouble in the way of those who from among the Gentiles are turned to God
Act  But that we give them orders to keep themselves from things offered to false gods and from the evil desires of the body and from the flesh of animals put to death in ways against the law and from blood
Act  For Moses from times long past has his preachers in every town reading his law in the Synagogues every Sabbath
Act  Then it seemed good to the Apostles and the rulers and all the church to send men from among them to Antioch with Paul and Barnabas Judas named Barsabbas and Silas chief men among the brothers
Act  And they sent a letter by them saying The Apostles and the older brothers to the brothers who are of the Gentiles in Antioch and Syria and Cilicia may joy be with you
Act  Because we have knowledge that some who went from us have been troubling you with their words putting your souls in doubt to whom we gave no such order
Act  It seemed good to us having come to an agreement together to send these men to you with our well loved Barnabas and Paul
Act  Men who have given up their lives for the name of our Lord Jesus Christ
Act  And so we have sent Judas and Silas who will say the same things to you themselves by word of mouth
Act  For it seemed good to the Holy Spirit and to us to put on you nothing more than these necessary things
Act  To keep from things offered to false gods and from blood and from things put to death in ways which are against the law and from the evil desires of the body if you keep yourselves from these you will do well May you be happy
Act  So they being sent away came down to Antioch and having got the people together they gave them the letter
Act  And after reading it they were glad of its comfort
Act  And Judas and Silas who themselves were prophets gave teaching to the brothers and made them strong in the faith
Act  And when they had been there for some time they were sent back in peace by the brothers to those who had sent them
Act  
Act  But Paul and Barnabas kept on in Antioch teaching and preaching the word of God with a number of others
Act  And after some days Paul said to Barnabas Let us go back and see the brothers in every town where we have given the word of God and see how they are
Act  And Barnabas had a desire to take with them John named Mark
Act  But Paul was of the opinion that it was not right to take with them one who had gone away from them in Pamphylia and had not gone on with the work
Act  And there was a sharp argument between them so that they were parted from one another and Barnabas took Mark with him and went by ship to Cyprus
Act  But Paul took Silas and went away with the blessing of the brothers
Act  And he went through Syria and Cilicia making the churches stronger in the faith
Act  And he came to Derbe and Lystra and there was a certain disciple there named Timothy whose mother was one of the Jews of the faith but his father was a Greek
Act  Of whom the brothers at Lystra and Iconium had a high opinion
Act  Paul had a desire for him to go with him and he gave him circumcision because of the Jews who were in those parts for they all had knowledge that his father was a Greek
Act  And on their way through the towns they gave them the rules which had been made by the Apostles and the rulers of the church at Jerusalem so that they might keep them
Act  So the churches were made strong in the faith and were increased in number every day
Act  And after they had gone through the land of Phrygia and Galatia the Holy Spirit did not let them take the word into Asia
Act  And having come to Mysia they made an attempt to go into Bithynia but the Spirit of Jesus did not let them
Act  And going past Mysia they came down to Troas
Act  And Paul had a vision in the night a man of Macedonia came requesting him and saying Come over into Macedonia and give us help
Act  And when he had seen the vision straight away we made the decision to go into Macedonia for it seemed certain to us that God had sent us to give the good news to them
Act  So from Troas we went straight by ship to Samothrace and the day after to Neapolis
Act  And from there to Philippi which is the most important town of Macedonia and a Roman colony and we were there for some days
Act  And on the Sabbath we went outside the town by the river where we had an idea that there would be a place of prayer and being seated we had talk with the women who had come together
Act  And a certain woman named Lydia a trader in purple cloth of the town of Thyatira and a Godfearing woman gave ear to us whose heart the Lord made open to give attention to the things which Paul was saying
Act  And when she and her family had had baptism she made a request to us saying If it seems to you that I am true to the Lord come into my house and be my guests And she made us come
Act  And when we were going to the place of prayer we came across a girl with a spirit which gave knowledge of the future whose masters made great profit from her power
Act  She came after Paul and us crying out and saying These men are the servants of the Most High God who are giving you news of the way of salvation
Act  And this she did on a number of days But Paul was greatly troubled and turning said to the spirit I give you orders in the name of Jesus Christ to come out of her And it came out that very hour
Act  But when her masters saw that their hope of profit was gone they took Paul and Silas pulling them into the marketplace before the rulers
Act  And when they had taken them before the authorities they said These men who are Jews are greatly troubling our town
Act  Teaching rules of living which it is not right for us to have or to keep being Romans
Act  And the people made an attack on them all together and the authorities took their clothing off them and gave orders for them to be whipped
Act  And when they had given them a great number of blows they put them in prison giving orders to the keeper of the prison to keep them safely
Act  And he having such orders put them into the inner prison with chains on their feet
Act  But about the middle of the night Paul and Silas were making prayers and songs to God in the hearing of the prisoners
Act  And suddenly there was an earthshock so that the base of the prison was moved and all the doors came open and everyones chains came off
Act  And the keeper coming out of his sleep and seeing the prison doors open took his sword and was about to put himself to death fearing that the prisoners had got away
Act  But Paul said in a loud voice Do yourself no damage for we are all here
Act  And he sent for lights and came rushing in and shaking with fear went down on his face before Paul and Silas
Act  And took them out and said Sirs what have I to do to get salvation
Act  And they said Have faith in the Lord Jesus and you and your family will have salvation
Act  And they gave the word of the Lord to him and to all who were in his house
Act  And that same hour of the night he took them and when he had given attention to their wounds he and all his family had baptism straight away
Act  And he took them into his house and gave them food and he was full of joy having faith in God with all his family
Act  But when it was day the authorities sent the police saying Let these men go
Act  And the keeper said to Paul The authorities have given orders to let you go come out now and go in peace
Act  But Paul said to them They have given us who are Romans a public whipping without judging us and have put us in prison Will they now send us out secretly no truly let them come themselves and take us out
Act  And the police gave an account of these words to the authorities and they were full of fear on hearing that they were Romans
Act  Then they came and made prayers to them requesting them when they had taken them out to go away from the town
Act  And they came out of the prison and went to the house of Lydia and when they had seen the brothers they gave them comfort and went away
Act  Now when they had gone through Amphipolis and Apollonia they came to Thessalonica where there was a Synagogue of the Jews
Act  And Paul as he generally did went in to them and on three Sabbath days had discussions with them from the holy Writings
Act  Saying to them clearly and openly that Christ had to be put to death and come back to life again and that this Jesus whom he said I am preaching to you is the Christ
Act  And some of them had faith and were joined to Paul and Silas and a number of the Godfearing Greeks and some of the chief women
Act  But the Jews being moved with envy took with them certain low persons from among the common people and getting together a great number of people made an outcry in the town attacking the house of Jason with the purpose of taking them out to the people
Act  And when they were not able to get them they took Jason and some of the brothers by force before the rulers of the town crying These men who have made trouble all over the world have now come here
Act  Whom Jason has taken into his house and they are acting against the orders of Caesar saying that there is another king Jesus
Act  And hearing these things the people and the rulers of the town were troubled
Act  And having made Jason and the others give an undertaking to keep the peace they let them go
Act  And the brothers straight away sent Paul and Silas away by night to Beroea and they when they came there went to the Synagogue of the Jews
Act  Now these were more noble than the Jews of Thessalonica for they gave serious attention to the word searching in the holy Writings every day to see if these things were so
Act  And a number of them had faith and no small number of the Greek women of high position and of the men
Act  But when the Jews of Thessalonica had news that Paul was preaching the word at Beroea they came there troubling the people and working them up
Act  So the brothers sent Paul straight away to the sea but Silas and Timothy kept there still
Act  But those who went with Paul took him as far as Athens and then went away with orders from him to Silas and Timothy to come to him quickly
Act  Now while Paul was waiting for them at Athens his spirit was troubled for he saw all the town full of images of the gods
Act  So he had discussions in the Synagogue with the Jews and Godfearing Gentiles and every day in the marketplace with those who were there
Act  And some of those who were supporters of the theories of the Epicureans and the Stoics had a meeting with him And some said What is this talker of foolish words saying And others He seems to be a preacher of strange gods because he was preaching of Jesus and his coming back from the dead
Act  And they took him to Mars Hill saying Will you make clear to us what is this new teaching of yours
Act  For you seem to us to say strange things and we have a desire to get the sense of them
Act  Now all the Athenians and the men from other lands who come there were giving all their time to talking or hearing of anything new
Act  And Paul got to his feet on Mars Hill and said O men of Athens I see that you are overmuch given to fear of the gods
Act  For when I came by I was looking at the things to which you give worship and I saw an altar with this writing on it TO THE GOD OF WHOM THERE IS NO KNOWLEDGE Now what you without knowledge give worship to I make clear to you
Act  The God who made the earth and everything in it he being Lord of heaven and earth is not housed in buildings made with hands
Act  And he is not dependent on the work of mens hands as if he had need of anything for he himself gives to all life and breath and all things
Act  And he has made of one blood all the nations of men living on all the face of the earth ordering their times and the limits of their lands
Act  So that they might make search for God in order if possible to get knowledge of him and make discovery of him though he is not far from every one of us
Act  For in him we have life and motion and existence as certain of your verse writers have said For we are his offspring
Act  If then we are the offspring of God it is not right for us to have the idea that God is like gold or silver or stone formed by the art or design of man
Act  Those times when men had no knowledge were overlooked by God but now he gives orders to all men in every place to undergo a change of heart
Act  Because a day has been fixed in which all the world will be judged in righteousness by the man who has been marked out by him for this work of which he has given a sign to all men by giving him back from the dead
Act  Now on hearing about the coming back from death some of them made sport of it but others said Let us go more fully into this another time
Act  And so Paul went away from among them
Act  But some men gave him their support among whom was Dionysius the Areopagite and a woman named Damaris and others with them
Act  After these things he went away from Athens and came to Corinth
Act  And there he came across a certain Jew named Aquila a man of Pontus by birth who not long before had come from Italy with his wife Priscilla because Claudius had given orders that all Jews were to go away from Rome and he came to them
Act  And because he was of the same trade he was living with them and they did their work together for by trade they were tentmakers
Act  And every Sabbath he had discussions in the Synagogue turning Jews and Greeks to the faith
Act  And when Silas and Timothy came down from Macedonia Paul was completely given up to the word preaching to the Jews that the Christ was Jesus
Act  And when they put themselves against him and said evil words he said shaking his clothing Your blood be on your heads I am clean from now I will go to the Gentiles
Act  And moving from there he went into the house of a man named Titus Justus a Godfearing man whose house was very near the Synagogue
Act  And Crispus the ruler of the Synagogue with all his family had faith in the Lord and a great number of the people of Corinth hearing the word had faith and were given baptism
Act  And the Lord said to Paul in the night in a vision Have no fear and go on preaching
Act  For I am with you and no one will make an attack on you to do you damage for I have a number of people in this town
Act  And he was there for a year and six months teaching the word of God among them
Act  But when Gallio was ruler of Achaia all the Jews together made an attack on Paul and took him to the judges seat
Act  Saying This man is teaching the people to give worship to God in a way which is against the law
Act  But when Paul was about to say something Gallio said to the Jews If this was anything to do with wrongdoing or crime there would be a reason for me to give you a hearing
Act  But if it is a question of words or names or of your law see to it yourselves I will not be a judge of such things
Act  And he sent them away from the judges seat
Act  And they all made an attack on Sosthenes the ruler of the Synagogue and gave him blows before the judges seat but Gallio gave no attention to these things
Act  And Paul after waiting some days went away from the brothers and went by ship to Syria Priscilla and Aquila being with him and he had had his hair cut off in Cenchrea for he had taken an oath
Act  And they came down to Ephesus and he left them there and he himself went into the Synagogue and had a discussion with the Jews
Act  And being requested by them to be there for a longer time he said No
Act  And went from them saying I will come back to you if God lets me and he took ship from Ephesus
Act  And when he had come to land at Caesarea he went to see the church and then went down to Antioch
Act  And having been there for some time he went through the country of Galatia and Phrygia in order making the disciples strong in the faith
Act  Now a certain Jew named Apollos an Alexandrian by birth and a man of learning came to Ephesus and he had great knowledge of the holy Writings
Act  This man had been trained in the way of the Lord and burning in spirit he gave himself up to teaching the facts about Jesus though he had knowledge only of Johns baptism
Act  And he was preaching in the Synagogue without fear But Priscilla and Aquila hearing his words took him in and gave him fuller teaching about the way of God
Act  And when he had a desire to go over into Achaia the brothers gave him help and sent letters to the disciples requesting them to take him in among them and when he had come he gave much help to those who had faith through grace
Act  For he overcame the Jews in public discussion making clear from the holy Writings that the Christ was Jesus
Act  And it came about that while Apollos was at Corinth Paul having gone through the higher country came to Ephesus where there were certain disciples
Act  And he said to them Did you get the Holy Spirit when you had faith And they said to him No we have had no knowledge of the Holy Spirit
Act  And he said What sort of baptism did you have And they said The baptism of John
Act  And Paul said John gave a baptism which goes with a change of heart saying to the people that they were to have faith in him who was coming after him that is in Jesus
Act  And hearing this they had baptism in the name of the Lord Jesus
Act  And when Paul had put his hands on them the Holy Spirit came on them and they had the power of talking in tongues and acting like prophets
Act  And there were about twelve of these men
Act  And he went into the Synagogue and for three months he was preaching there without fear reasoning and teaching about the kingdom of God
Act  But because some of the people were hardhearted and would not give hearing saying evil words about the Way before the people he went away from them and kept the disciples separate reasoning every day in the school of Tyrannus
Act  And this went on for two years so that all those who were living in Asia had knowledge of the word of the Lord Greeks as well as Jews
Act  And God did special works of power by the hands of Paul
Act  So that bits of linen and clothing from his body were taken to people who were ill and their diseases went away from them and the evil spirits went out
Act  But some of the Jews who went from place to place driving out evil spirits took it on themselves to make use of the name of the Lord Jesus over those who had evil spirits saying I give you orders by Jesus whom Paul is preaching
Act  And there were seven sons of a man named Sceva a Jew and a chief priest who did this
Act  And the evil spirit answering said to them I have knowledge of Jesus and of Paul but who are you
Act  And the man in whom the evil spirit was jumping on them was stronger than the two of them and overcame them so that they went running from that house wounded and without their clothing
Act  And this came to the ears of all those Jews and Greeks who were living at Ephesus and fear came on them all and the name of the Lord Jesus was made great
Act  And a number of those who had faith came and made a public statement of their sins and all their acts
Act  And a great number of those who were experts in strange arts took their books and put them on the fire in front of everyone and when the books were valued they came to fifty thousand bits of silver
Act  So the word of the Lord was increased very greatly and was full of power
Act  Now after these things were ended Paul came to a decision that when he had gone through Macedonia and Achaia he would go to Jerusalem saying After I have been there I have a desire to see Rome
Act  And having sent two of his helpers Timothy and Erastus into Macedonia he himself went on living in Asia for a time
Act  And about that time a great outcry took place about the Way
Act  For there was a certain man named Demetrius a silverworker who made silver boxes for the images of Diana and gave no small profit to the workmen
Act  Whom he got together with other workmen of the same trade and said to them Men it is clear that from this business we get our wealth
Act  And you see for it has come to your ears that not only at Ephesus but almost all through Asia this Paul has been teaching numbers of people and turning them away saying that those are not gods who are made by mens hands
Act  And there is danger not only that our trade may be damaged in the opinion of men but that the holy place of the great goddess Diana may be no longer honoured and that she to whom all Asia and the world give worship will be put down from her high position
Act  And hearing this they were very angry crying out and saying Great is Diana of Ephesus
Act  And the town was full of noise and trouble and they all came running into the theatre having taken by force Gaius and Aristarchus men of Macedonia who were journeying in company with Paul
Act  And when Paul was about to go in to the people the disciples did not let him
Act  And some of the rulers of Asia being his friends sent to him requesting him seriously not to put himself in danger by going into the theatre
Act  And some said one thing and some another for there was no order in the meeting and most of them had no idea why they had come together
Act  Then they took Alexander out from among the people the Jews putting him forward And Alexander making a sign with his hand was about to make a statement to the people in answer
Act  But when they saw that he was a Jew all of them with one voice went on crying out for about two hours Great is Diana of Ephesus
Act  And when the chief secretary had got the people quiet he said Men of Ephesus is any man without knowledge that the town of Ephesus is the keeper of the holy place of the great Diana who was sent down from Jupiter
Act  So then because these things may not be doubted it would be better for you to be quiet and do nothing unwise
Act  For you have taken these men who are not doing damage to the holy place or talking against our goddess
Act  If then Demetrius and the workmen who are with him have a protest to make against any man the law is open to them and there are judges let them put up a cause at law against one another
Act  But if any other business is in question let it be taken up in the regular meeting
Act  For truly we are in danger of being made responsible for this days trouble there being no cause for it and we are not able to give any reason for this coming together
Act  And when he had said this he sent the meeting away
Act  And after the noise had come to an end Paul having sent for the disciples and given them comfort went away from them to Macedonia
Act  And when he had gone through those parts and given them much teaching he came into Greece
Act  And when he had been there three months because the Jews had made a secret design against him when he was about to take ship for Syria he made a decision to go back through Macedonia
Act  And Sopater of Beroea the son of Pyrrhus and Aristarchus and Secundus of Thessalonica and Gaius of Derbe and Timothy and Tychicus and Trophimus of Asia went with him as far as Asia
Act  But these had gone before and were waiting for us at Troas
Act  And we went away from Philippi by ship after the days of unleavened bread and came to them at Troas in five days and we were there for seven days
Act  And on the first day of the week when we had come together for the holy meal Paul gave them a talk for it was his purpose to go away on the day after and he went on talking till after the middle of the night
Act  And there were a number of lights in the room where we had come together
Act  And a certain young man named Eutychus who was seated in the window went into a deep sleep and while Paul went on talking being overcome by sleep he had a fall from the third floor and was taken up dead
Act  And Paul went down and falling on him took him in his arms and said Do not be troubled for his life is in him
Act  And when he had gone up and had taken the broken bread he went on talking to them for a long time even till dawn and then he went away
Act  And they took the boy in living and were greatly comforted
Act  But we going before him by ship went to Assos with the purpose of taking Paul in there for so he had given orders because he himself was coming by land
Act  And when he came up with us at Assos we took him in the ship and went on to Mitylene
Act  And going from there by sea we came on the day after opposite Chios and touching at Samos on the day after that we came on the third day to Miletus
Act  For Pauls purpose was to go past Ephesus so that he might not be kept in Asia for he was going quickly in order if possible to be at Jerusalem on the day of Pentecost
Act  And from Miletus he sent to Ephesus for the rulers of the church
Act  And when they had come he said to them You yourselves have seen what my life has been like all the time from the day when I first came into Asia
Act  Doing the Lords work without pride through all the sorrow and troubles which came on me because of the evil designs of the Jews
Act  And how I kept back nothing which might be of profit to you teaching you publicly and privately
Act  Preaching to Jews and to Greeks the need for a turning of the heart to God and faith in the Lord Jesus Christ
Act  And now as you see I am going to Jerusalem a prisoner in spirit having no knowledge of what will come to me there
Act  Only that the Holy Spirit makes clear to me in every town that prison and pains are waiting for me
Act  But I put no value on my life if only at the end of it I may see the work complete which was given to me by the Lord Jesus to be a witness of the good news of the grace of God
Act  And now I am conscious that you among whom I have gone about preaching the kingdom will not see my face again
Act  And so I say to you this day that I am clean from the blood of all men
Act  For I have not kept back from you anything of the purpose of God
Act  Give attention to yourselves and to all the flock which the Holy Spirit has given into your care to give food to the church of God for which he gave his blood
Act  I am conscious that after I am gone evil wolves will come in among you doing damage to the flock
Act  And from among yourselves will come men who will give wrong teaching turning away the disciples after them
Act  So keep watch having in mind that for three years without resting I was teaching every one of you day and night with weeping
Act  And now I give you into the care of God and the word of his grace which is able to make you strong and to give you your heritage among all the saints
Act  I have had no desire for any mans silver or gold or clothing
Act  You yourselves have seen that with these hands I got what was necessary for me and those who were with me
Act  In all things I was an example to you of how in your lives you are to give help to the feeble and keep in memory the words of the Lord Jesus how he himself said There is a greater blessing in giving than in getting
Act  And having said these words he went down on his knees in prayer with them all
Act  And they were all weeping falling on Pauls neck and kissing him
Act  Being sad most of all because he had said that they would not see his face again And so they went with him to the ship
Act  And after parting from them we put out to sea and came straight to Cos and the day after to Rhodes and from there to Patara
Act  And as there was a ship going to Phoenicia we went in it
Act  And when we had come in view of Cyprus going past it on our left we went on to Syria and came to land at Tyre for there the goods which were in the ship had to be taken out
Act  And meeting the disciples we were there for seven days and they gave Paul orders through the Spirit not to go up to Jerusalem
Act  And when these days came to an end we went on our journey and they all with their wives and children came with us on our way till we were out of the town and after going on our knees in prayer by the sea
Act  We said our last words to one another and got into the ship and they went back to their houses
Act  And journeying by ship from Tyre we came to Ptolemais and there we had talk with the brothers and were with them for one day
Act  And on the day after we went away and came to Caesarea where we were guests in the house of Philip the preacher who was one of the seven
Act  And he had four daughters virgins who were prophets
Act  And while we were waiting there for some days a certain prophet named Agabus came down from Judaea
Act  And he came to us and took the band of Pauls clothing and putting it round his feet and hands said The Holy Spirit says these words So will the Jews do to the man who is the owner of this band and they will give him up into the hands of the Gentiles
Act  And hearing these things we and those who were living in that place made request to him not to go to Jerusalem
Act  Then Paul said What are you doing weeping and wounding my heart for I am ready not only to be a prisoner but to be put to death at Jerusalem for the name of the Lord Jesus
Act  And as he might not be moved we did no more saying Let the purpose of God be done
Act  And after these days we got ready and went up to Jerusalem
Act  And some of the disciples from Caesarea went with us taking a certain Mnason of Cyprus one of the early disciples in whose house we were to be living
Act  And when we came to Jerusalem the brothers were pleased to see us
Act  And on the day after Paul went with us to James and all the rulers of the church were present
Act  And when he had said how glad he was to see them he gave them a detailed account of the things which God had done through his work among the Gentiles
Act  And hearing it they gave praise to God and they said to him You see brother what thousands there are among the Jews who have the faith and they all have a great respect for the law
Act  And they have had news of you how you have been teaching all the Jews among the Gentiles to give up the law of Moses and not to give circumcision to their children and not to keep the old rules
Act  What then is the position They will certainly get news that you have come
Act  Do this then which we say to you We have four men who have taken an oath
Act  Go with these and make yourself clean with them and make the necessary payments for them so that they may be free from their oath and everyone will see that the statements made about you are not true but that you put yourself under rule and keep the law
Act  But as to the Gentiles who have the faith we sent a letter giving our decision that they were to keep themselves from offerings made to false gods and from blood and from the flesh of animals put to death in ways against the law and from the evil desires of the body
Act  Then Paul took the men and on the day after making himself clean with them he went into the Temple giving out the statement that the days necessary for making them clean were complete till the offering was made for every one of them
Act  And when the seven days were almost ended the Jews from Asia seeing him in the Temple got the people together and put their hands on him
Act  Crying out Men of Israel come to our help this is the man who is teaching all men everywhere against the people and the law and this place and in addition he has taken Greeks into the Temple and made this holy place unclean
Act  For they had seen him before in the town with Trophimus of Ephesus and had the idea that Paul had taken him with him into the Temple
Act  And all the town was moved and the people came running together and put their hands on Paul pulling him out of the Temple and then the doors were shut
Act  And while they were attempting to put him to death news came to the chief captain of the band that all Jerusalem was out of control
Act  And straight away he took some armed men and went quickly down to them and the Jews seeing them gave no more blows to Paul
Act  Then the chief captain came near and took him and gave orders for him to be put in chains questioning them as to who he was and what he had done
Act  And some said one thing and some another among the people and as he was not able to get a knowledge of the facts because of the noise he gave orders for Paul to be taken into the army building
Act  And when he came on to the steps he was lifted up by the armed men because of the force of the people
Act  For a great mass of people came after them crying out Away with him
Act  And when Paul was about to be taken into the building he said to the chief captain May I say something to you And he said Have you a knowledge of Greek
Act  Are you by chance the Egyptian who before this got the people worked up against the government and took four thousand men of the Assassins out into the waste land
Act  But Paul said I am a Jew of Tarsus in Cilicia which is not an unimportant town I make a request to you to let me say a word to the people
Act  And when he let him do so Paul from the steps made a sign with his hand to the people and when they were all quiet he said to them in the Hebrew language
Act  My brothers and fathers give ear to the story of my life which I now put before you
Act  And hearing him talking in the Hebrew language they became the more quiet and he said
Act  I am a Jew of Tarsus in Cilicia by birth but I had my education in this town at the feet of Gamaliel being trained in the keeping of every detail of the law of our fathers given up to the cause of God with all my heart as you are today
Act  And I made attacks on this Way even to death taking men and women and putting them in prison
Act  Of which the high priest will be a witness and all the rulers from whom I had letters to the brothers and I went into Damascus to take those who were there as prisoners to Jerusalem for punishment
Act  And it came about that while I was on my journey coming near to Damascus about the middle of the day suddenly I saw a great light from heaven shining round me
Act  And when I went down on the earth a voice came to my ears saying to me Saul Saul why are you attacking me so cruelly
Act  And I answering said Who are you Lord And he said to me I am Jesus of Nazareth whom you are attacking
Act  And those who were with me saw the light but the voice of him who was talking to me came not to their ears
Act  And I said What have I to do Lord And the Lord said to me Get up and go into Damascus and it will be made clear to you what you have to do
Act  And because I was unable to see because of the glory of that light those who were with me took me by the hand and so I came to Damascus
Act  And one Ananias a Godfearing man who kept the law and of whom all the Jews in that place had a high opinion
Act  Came to my side and said Brother Saul let your eyes be open And in that very hour I was able to see him
Act  And he said You have been marked out by the God of our fathers to have knowledge of his purpose and to see the Upright One and to give ear to the words of his mouth
Act  For you will be a witness for him to all men of what you have seen and of what has come to your ears
Act  And now why are you waiting get up and have baptism for the washing away of your sins giving worship to his name
Act  And it came about that when I had come back to Jerusalem while I was at prayer in the Temple my senses became more than naturally clear
Act  And I saw him saying to me Go out of Jerusalem straight away because they will not give hearing to your witness about me
Act  And I said Lord they themselves have knowledge that I went through the Synagogues putting in prison and whipping all those who had faith in you
Act  And when Stephen your witness was put to death I was there giving approval and looking after the clothing of those who put him to death
Act  And he said to me Go for I will send you far away to the Gentiles
Act  And they gave him a hearing as far as this word then with loud voices they said Away with this man from the earth it is not right for him to be living
Act  And while they were crying out and pulling off their clothing and sending dust into the air
Act  The chief captain gave orders for him to be taken into the army building saying that he would put him to the test by whipping so that he might have knowledge of the reason why they were crying out so violently against him
Act  And when they had put leather bands round him Paul said to the captain who was present Is it the law for you to give blows to a man who is a Roman and has not been judged
Act  And hearing this the man went to the chief captain and gave him an account of it saying What are you about to do for this man is a Roman
Act  And the chief captain came to him and said Give me an answer are you a Roman And he said Yes
Act  And the chief captain said I got Roman rights for myself at a great price And Paul said But I had them by birth
Act  Then those who were about to put him to the test went away and the chief captain was in fear seeing that he was a Roman and that he had put chains on him
Act  But on the day after desiring to have certain knowledge of what the Jews had to say against him he made him free and gave orders for the chief priests and all the Sanhedrin to come together and he took Paul and put him before them
Act  And Paul looking fixedly at the Sanhedrin said My brothers my life has been upright before God till this day
Act  And the high priest Ananias gave orders to those who were near him to give him a blow on the mouth
Act  Then Paul said to him God will give blows to you you whitewashed wall are you here to be my judge by law and by your orders am I given blows against the law
Act  And those who were near said Do you say such words against Gods high priest
Act  And Paul said Brother I had no idea that he was the high priest for it has been said You may not say evil about the ruler of your people
Act  But when Paul saw that half of them were Sadducees and the rest Pharisees he said in the Sanhedrin Brothers I am a Pharisee and the son of Pharisees I am here to be judged on the question of the hope of the coming back from the dead
Act  And when he had said this there was an argument between the Pharisees and the Sadducees and a division in the meeting
Act  For the Sadducees say that there is no coming back from the dead and no angels or spirits but the Pharisees have belief in all these
Act  And there was a great outcry and some of the scribes on the side of the Pharisees got up and took part in the discussion saying We see no evil in this man what if he has had a revelation from an angel or a spirit
Act  And when the argument became very violent the chief captain fearing that Paul would be pulled in two by them gave orders to the armed men to take him by force from among them and take him into the army building
Act  And the night after the Lord came to his side and said Be of good heart for as you have been witnessing for me in Jerusalem so will you be my witness in Rome
Act  And when it was day the Jews came together and put themselves under an oath that they would take no food or drink till they had put Paul to death
Act  And more than forty of them took this oath
Act  And they came to the chief priests and the rulers and said We have taken a great oath to take no food till we have put Paul to death
Act  So now will you and the Sanhedrin make a request to the military authorities to have him sent down to you as if you were desiring to go into the business in greater detail and we before ever he gets to you will be waiting to put him to death
Act  But Pauls sisters son had word of their design and he came into the army building and gave news of it to Paul
Act  And Paul sent for a captain and said Take this young man to your chief for he has news for him
Act  So he took him to the chief captain and said Paul the prisoner made a request to me to take this young man to you for he has something to say to you
Act  And the chief took him by the hand and going on one side said to him privately What is it you have to say to me
Act  And he said The Jews are in agreement together to make a request to you for Paul to be taken on the day after this into the Sanhedrin to be questioned in greater detail
Act  But do not give way to them for more than forty of them are waiting for him having taken an oath not to take food or drink till they have put him to death and now they are ready waiting for your order
Act  So the chief captain let the young man go saying to him Do not say to anyone that you have given me word of these things
Act  And he sent for two captains and said Make ready two hundred men with seventy horsemen and two hundred spearmen to go to Caesarea at the third hour of the night
Act  And get beasts so that they may put Paul on them and take him safely to Felix the ruler
Act  And he sent a letter in these words
Act  Claudius Lysias to the most noble ruler Felix peace be with you
Act  This man was taken by the Jews and was about to be put to death by them when I came on them with the army and took him out of danger having knowledge that he was a Roman
Act  And desiring to get at the reason for their attack on him I took him down to their Sanhedrin
Act  Then it became clear to me that it was a question of their law and that nothing was said against him which might be a reason for prison or death
Act  And when news was given to me that a secret design was being made against the man I sent him straight away to you giving orders to those who are against him to make their statements before you
Act  So the armed men as they were ordered took Paul and came by night to Antipatris
Act  But on the day after they sent the horsemen on with him and went back to their place
Act  And they when they came to Caesarea gave the letter to the ruler and took Paul before him
Act  And after reading it he said What part of the country do you come from And hearing that he was from Cilicia
Act  I will give hearing to your cause he said when those who are against you have come And he gave orders for him to be kept in Herods Praetorium
Act  And after five days the high priest Ananias came with certain of the rulers and an expert talker one Tertullus and they made a statement to Felix against Paul
Act  And when he had been sent for Tertullus starting his statement said Because by you we are living in peace and through your wisdom wrongs are put right for this nation
Act  In all things and in all places we are conscious of our great debt to you most noble Felix
Act  But so that I may not make you tired I make a request to you of your mercy to give hearing to a short statement
Act  For this man in our opinion is a cause of trouble a maker of attacks on the government among Jews through all the empire and a chief mover in the society of the Nazarenes
Act  Who in addition was attempting to make the Temple unclean whom we took
Act  
Act  And from whom you will be able by questioning him yourself to get knowledge of all the things which we say against him
Act  And the Jews were in agreement with his statement saying that these things were so
Act  Then when the ruler had given him a sign to make his answer Paul said Because I have knowledge that you have been a judge over this nation for a number of years I am glad to make my answer
Act  Seeing that you are able to make certain of the fact that it is not more than twelve days from the time when I came up to Jerusalem for worship
Act  And they have not seen me in argument with any man in the Temple or working up the feelings of the people in the Synagogues or in the town
Act  And they are not able to give facts in support of the things which they say against me now
Act  But this I will say openly to you that I do give worship to the God of our fathers after that Way which to them is not the true religion but I have belief in all the things which are in the law and in the books of the prophets
Act  Hoping in God for that which they themselves are looking for that there will be a coming back from the dead for upright men and wrongdoers
Act  And in this I do my best at all times to have no reason for shame before God or men
Act  Now after a number of years I came to give help and offerings to my nation
Act  And having been made clean I was in the Temple but not with a great number of people and not with noise but there were certain Jews from Asia
Act  And it would have been better if they had come here to make a statement if they have anything against me
Act  Or let these men here present say what wrongdoing was seen in me when I was before the Sanhedrin
Act  But only this one thing which I said among them in a loud voice I am this day being judged on the question of the coming back from the dead
Act  But Felix who had a more detailed knowledge of the Way put them off saying When Lysias the chief captain comes down I will give attention to your business
Act  And he gave orders to the captain to keep Paul under his control and to let him have everything he had need of and not to keep his friends from coming to see him
Act  But after some days Felix came with Drusilla his wife who was of the Jews by birth and sent for Paul and gave hearing to him about faith in Christ Jesus
Act  And while he was talking about righteousness and selfcontrol and the judging which was to come Felix had great fear and said Go away for the present and when the right time comes I will send for you
Act  For he was hoping that Paul would give him money so he sent for him more frequently and had talk with him
Act  But after two years Porcius Festus took the place of Felix who desiring to have the approval of the Jews kept Paul in chains
Act  So Festus having come into that part of the country which was under his rule after three days went up to Jerusalem from Caesarea
Act  And the chief priests and the chief men of the Jews made statements against Paul
Act  Requesting Festus to give effect to their design against him and send him to Jerusalem when they would be waiting to put him to death on the way
Act  But Festus in answer said that Paul was being kept in prison at Caesarea and that in a short time he himself was going there
Act  So he said let those who have authority among you go with me and if there is any wrong in the man let them make a statement against him
Act  And when he had been with them not more than eight or ten days he went down to Caesarea and on the day after he took his place on the judges seat and sent for Paul
Act  And when he came the Jews who had come down from Jerusalem came round him and made all sorts of serious statements against him which were not supported by the facts
Act  Then Paul in his answer to them said I have done no wrong against the law of the Jews or against the Temple or against Caesar
Act  But Festus desiring to get the approval of the Jews said to Paul Will you go up to Jerusalem and be judged before me there in connection with these things
Act  And Paul said I am before the seat of Caesars authority where it is right for me to be judged I have done no wrong to the Jews as you are well able to see
Act  If then I am a wrongdoer and there is a cause of death in me I am ready for death if it is not as they say against me no man may give me up to them Let my cause come before Caesar
Act  Then Festus having had a discussion with the Jews made answer You have said Let my cause come before Caesar to Caesar you will go
Act  Now when some days had gone by King Agrippa and Bernice came to Caesarea and went to see Festus
Act  And as they were there for some days Festus gave them Pauls story saying There is a certain man here who was put in prison by Felix
Act  Against whom the chief priests and the rulers of the Jews made a statement when I was at Jerusalem requesting me to give a decision against him
Act  To whom I gave answer that it is not the Roman way to give a man up till he has been face to face with those who are attacking him and has had a chance to give an answer to the statements made against him
Act  So when they had come together here straight away on the day after I took my place on the judges seat and sent for the man
Act  But when they got up they said nothing about such crimes as I had in mind
Act  But had certain questions against him in connection with their religion and about one Jesus now dead who Paul said was living
Act  And as I had not enough knowledge for the discussion of these things I made the suggestion to him to go to Jerusalem and be judged there
Act  But when Paul made a request that he might be judged by Caesar I gave orders for him to be kept till I might send him to Caesar
Act  And Agrippa said to Festus I have a desire to give the man a hearing myself Tomorrow he said you may give him a hearing
Act  So on the day after when Agrippa and Bernice in great glory had come into the public place of hearing with the chief of the army and the chief men of the town at the order of Festus Paul was sent for
Act  And Festus said King Agrippa and all those who are present here with us you see this man about whom all the Jews have made protests to me at Jerusalem and in this place saying that it is not right for him to be living any longer
Act  But in my opinion there is no cause of death in him and as he himself has made a request to be judged by Caesar I have said that I would send him
Act  But I have no certain account of him to send to Caesar So I have sent for him to come before you and specially before you King Agrippa so that after the business has been gone into I may have something to put in writing
Act  For it seems to me against reason to send a prisoner without making clear what there is against him
Act  And Agrippa said to Paul You may put your cause before us Then Paul stretching out his hand made his answer saying
Act  In my opinion I am happy King Agrippa to be able to give my answer before you today to all these things which the Jews say against me
Act  The more so because you are expert in all questions to do with the Jews and their ways so I make my request to you to give me a hearing to the end
Act  All the Jews have knowledge of my way of life from my early years as it was from the start among my nation and at Jerusalem
Act  And they are able to say if they would give witness that I was living as a Pharisee in that division of our religion which is most regular in the keeping of the law
Act  And now I am here to be judged because of the hope given by Gods word to our fathers
Act  For the effecting of which our twelve tribes have been working and waiting night and day with all their hearts And in connection with this hope I am attacked by the Jews O king
Act  Why in your opinion is it outside belief for God to make the dead come to life again
Act  For I truly was of the opinion that it was right for me to do a number of things against the name of Jesus of Nazareth
Act  And this I did in Jerusalem and numbers of the saints I put in prison having had authority given to me from the chief priests and when they were put to death I gave my decision against them
Act  And I gave them punishment frequently in all the Synagogues forcing them to say things against God and burning with passion against them I went after them even into faraway towns
Act  Then when I was journeying to Damascus with the authority and orders of the chief priests
Act  In the middle of the day on the road I saw a light from heaven brighter than the sun shining round me and those who were journeying with me
Act  And when we had all gone down on the earth a voice came to me saying in the Hebrew language Saul Saul why are you attacking me so cruelly It is hard for you to go against the impulse which is driving you
Act  And I said Who are you Lord And the Lord said I am Jesus whom you are attacking
Act  But get up on your feet for I have come to you for this purpose to make you a servant and a witness of the things in which you have seen me and of those in which you will see me
Act  And I will keep you safe from the people and from the Gentiles to whom I send you
Act  To make their eyes open turning them from the dark to the light and from the power of Satan to God so that they may have forgiveness of sins and a heritage among those who are made holy by faith in me
Act  So then King Agrippa I did not go against the vision from heaven
Act  But I went about first to those in Damascus and Jerusalem and through all the country of Judaea and then to the Gentiles preaching a change of heart so that they being turned to God might give in their works the fruits of a changed heart
Act  For this reason the Jews took me in the Temple and made an attempt to put me to death
Act  And so by Gods help I am here today witnessing to small and great saying nothing but what the prophets and Moses said would come about
Act  That the Christ would go through pain and being the first to come back from the dead would give light to the people and to the Gentiles
Act  And when he made his answer in these words Festus said in a loud voice Paul you are off your head your great learning has made you unbalanced
Act  Then Paul said I am not off my head most noble Festus but my words are true and wise
Act  For the king has knowledge of these things to whom I am talking freely being certain that all this is common knowledge to him for it has not been done in secret
Act  King Agrippa have you faith in the prophets I am certain that you have
Act  And Agrippa said to Paul A little more and you will be making me a Christian
Act  And Paul said It is my prayer to God that in little or great measure not only you but all those hearing me today might be even as I am but for these chains
Act  And the king and the ruler and Bernice and those who were seated with them got up
Act  And when they had gone away they said to one another This man has done nothing which might give cause for death or prison
Act  And Agrippa said to Festus This man might have been made free if he had not put his cause before Caesar
Act  And when the decision had been made that we were to go by sea to Italy they gave Paul and certain other prisoners into the care of a captain named Julius of the Augustan band
Act  And we went to sea in a ship of Adramyttium which was sailing to the sea towns of Asia Aristarchus a Macedonian of Thessalonica being with us
Act  And on the day after we came to Sidon and Julius was kind to Paul and let him go to see his friends and take a rest
Act  And sailing again from there we went on under cover of Cyprus because the wind was against us
Act  And having gone across the sea off Cilicia and Pamphylia we came to Myra in Lycia
Act  And there the captain came across a ship of Alexandria sailing for Italy and put us in it
Act  And when we had gone on slowly for a long time and had had hard work getting across to Cnidus for the wind was against us we went under cover of Crete in the direction of Salmone
Act  And sailing down the side of it as well as we were able we came to a certain place named Fair Havens near which was the town of Lasea
Act  And as a long time had gone by and the journey was now full of danger because it was late in the year Paul put the position before them
Act  Saying Friends I see that this journey will be one of great damage and loss not only to the goods and the ship but to ourselves
Act  But the captain gave more attention to the master and the owner of the ship than to what Paul said
Act  And as the harbour was not a good one in which to be for the winter the greater number of them were for going out to sea in order if possible to put in for the winter at Phoenix a harbour of Crete looking to the northeast and southeast
Act  And when the south wind came softly being of the opinion that their purpose might be effected they let the ship go and went sailing down the side of Crete very near to the land
Act  But after a little time a very violent wind named Euraquilo came down from it with great force
Act  And when the ship got into the grip of it and was not able to make headway into the wind we gave way and went before it
Act  And sailing near the side of a small island named Cauda we were able though it was hard work to make the ships boat safe
Act  And having got it up they put cords under and round the ship but fearing that they might be pushed on to the Syrtis they let down the sails and so went running before the wind
Act  And still fighting the storm with all our strength the day after they made a start at getting the goods out of the ship
Act  And on the third day they let all the sailing apparatus go over the side
Act  And as we had not seen the sun or stars for a long time and a great storm was on us all hope of salvation was gone
Act  And when they had been without food for a long time Paul got up among them and said Friends it would have been better if you had given attention to me and not gone sailing out from Crete to undergo this damage and loss
Act  But now I say to you be of good heart for there will be no loss of life but only of the ship
Act  For this night there came to my side an angel of the God who is my Master and whose servant I am
Act  Saying Have no fear Paul for you will come before Caesar and God has given to you all those who are sailing with you
Act  And so O men be of good heart for I have faith in God that it will be as he said to me
Act  But we will be sent on to a certain island
Act  But when the fourteenth day came while we were going here and there in the Adriatic sea about the middle of the night the sailors had an idea that they were getting near land
Act  And they let down the lead and saw that the sea was a hundred and twenty feet deep and after a little time they did it again and it was ninety feet
Act  Then fearing that by chance we might come on to the rocks they let down four hooks from the back of the ship and made prayers for the coming of day
Act  Then the sailors made attempts secretly to get away from the ship letting down a boat as if they were about to put down hooks from the front of the ship
Act  But Paul said to the captain and his men If you do not keep these men in the ship you will not be safe
Act  Then the armed men cutting the cords of the boat let her go
Act  And when dawn was near Paul gave them all orders to take food saying This is the fourteenth day you have been waiting and taking no food
Act  So I make request to you to take food for this is for your salvation not a hair from the head of any of you will come to destruction
Act  And when he had said this and had taken bread he gave praise to God before them all and took a meal of the broken bread
Act  Then they all took heart and did the same
Act  And we were in the ship two hundred and seventysix persons
Act  And when they had had enough food they made the weight of the ship less turning the grain out into the sea
Act  And when it was day they had no knowledge of the land but they saw an inlet of the sea with a floor of sand and they had the idea of driving the ship up on to it if possible
Act  So cutting away the hooks and letting them go into the sea and freeing the cords of the guidingblades and lifting up the sail to the wind they went in the direction of the inlet
Act  And coming to a point between two seas they got the ship to land and the front part was fixed in the sand and not able to be moved but the back part was broken by the force of the waves
Act  Then the armed men were for putting the prisoners to death so that no one would get away by swimming
Act  But the captain desiring to keep Paul safe kept them from their purpose and gave orders that those who had knowledge of swimming were to go off the ship and get first to land
Act  And the rest some on boards and some on things from the ship And so it came about that they all got safe to land
Act  And when we were safe we made the discovery that the island was named Melita
Act  And the simple people living there were uncommonly kind to us for they made a fire for us and took us in because it was raining and cold
Act  But when Paul had got some sticks together and put them on the fire a snake came out because of the heat and gave him a bite on the hand
Act  And when the people saw it hanging on his hand they said to one another Without doubt this man has put someone to death and though he has got safely away from the sea God will not let him go on living
Act  But shaking off the beast into the fire he got no damage
Act  But they had the idea that they would see him becoming ill or suddenly falling down dead but after waiting a long time and seeing that no damage came to him changing their opinion they said he was a god
Act  Now near that place there was some land the property of the chief man of the island who was named Publius who very kindly took us into his house as his guests for three days
Act  And the father of Publius was ill with a disease of the stomach to whom Paul went and put his hands on him with prayer and made him well
Act  And when this took place all the others in the island who had diseases came and were made well
Act  Then they gave us great honour and when we went away they put into the ship whatever things we were in need of
Act  And after three months we went to sea in a ship of Alexandria sailing under the sign of the Dioscuri which had been at the island for the winter
Act  And going into the harbour at Syracuse we were waiting there for three days
Act  And from there going about in a curve we came to Rhegium and after one day a south wind came up and on the day after we came to Puteoli
Act  Where we came across some of the brothers who kept us with them for seven days and so we came to Rome
Act  And the brothers when they had news of us came out from town as far as Appii Forum and the Three Taverns to have a meeting with us and Paul seeing them gave praise to God and took heart
Act  And when we came into Rome they let Paul have a house for himself and the armed man who kept watch over him
Act  Then after three days he sent for the chief men of the Jews and when they had come together he said to them My brothers though I had done nothing against the people or the ways of our fathers I was given a prisoner from Jerusalem into the hands of the Romans
Act  Who when they had put questions to me were ready to let me go free because there was no cause of death in me
Act  But when the Jews made protest against it I had to put my cause into Caesars hands not because I have anything to say against my nation
Act  But for this reason I sent for you to see and have talk with you for because of the hope of Israel I am in these chains
Act  And they said to him We have not had letters from Judaea about you and no one of the brothers has come to us here to give an account or say any evil about you
Act  But we have a desire to give hearing to your opinion for as to this form of religion we have knowledge that in all places it is attacked
Act  And when a day had been fixed they came to his house in great numbers and he gave them teaching giving witness to the kingdom of God and having discussions with them about Jesus from the law of Moses and from the prophets from morning till evening
Act  And some were in agreement with what he said but some had doubts
Act  And they went away for there was a division among them after Paul had said this one thing Well did the Holy Spirit say by the prophet Isaiah to your fathers
Act  Go to this people and say Though you give ear you will not get knowledge and seeing you will see but the sense will not be clear to you
Act  For the heart of this people has become fat and their ears are slow in hearing and their eyes are shut for fear that they might see with their eyes and give hearing with their ears and become wise in their hearts and be turned again to me so that I might make them well
Act  Be certain then that the salvation of God is sent to the Gentiles and they will give hearing
Act  
Act  And for the space of two years Paul was living in the house of which he had the use and had talk with all those who went in to see him
