Act  Preaching the kingdom of God and teaching about the Lord Jesus Christ without fear and no orders were given that he was not to do so
Rom  Paul a servant of Jesus Christ an Apostle by the selection of God given authority as a preacher of the good news
Rom  Of which God had given word before by his prophets in the holy Writings
Rom  About his Son who in the flesh came from the family of David
Rom  But was marked out as Son of God in power by the Holy Spirit through the coming to life again of the dead Jesus Christ our Lord
Rom  Through whom grace has been given to us sending us out to make disciples to the faith among all nations for his name
Rom  Among whom you in the same way have been marked out to be disciples of Jesus Christ
Rom  To all those who are in Rome loved by God marked out as saints Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Rom  First of all I give praise to my God through Jesus Christ for you all because news of your faith has gone into all the world
Rom  For God is my witness whose servant I am in spirit in the good news of his Son that you are at all times in my memory and in my prayers
Rom  And that I am ever making prayers that God will give me a good journey to you
Rom  For I have a strong desire to see you and to give you some grace of the spirit so that you may be made strong
Rom  That is to say that all of us may be comforted together by the faith which is in you and in me
Rom  You may be certain my brothers that it has frequently been in my mind to come to you but till now I was kept from it so that I might have some fruit from you in the same way as I have had it from the other nations
Rom  I have a debt to Greeks and to the nations outside to the wise and to those who have no learning
Rom  For which reason I have the desire as far as I am able to give the knowledge of the good news to you who are in Rome
Rom  For I have no feeling of shame about the good news because it is the power of God giving salvation to everyone who has faith to the Jew first and then to the Greek
Rom  For in it there is the revelation of the righteousness of God from faith to faith as it is said in the holy Writings The man who does righteousness will be living by his faith
Rom  For there is a revelation of the wrath of God from heaven against all the wrongdoing and evil thoughts of men who keep down what is true by wrongdoing
Rom  Because the knowledge of God may be seen in them God having made it clear to them
Rom  For from the first making of the world those things of God which the eye is unable to see that is his eternal power and existence are fully made clear he having given the knowledge of them through the things which he has made so that men have no reason for wrongdoing
Rom  Because having the knowledge of God they did not give glory to God as God and did not give praise but their minds were full of foolish things and their hearts being without sense were made dark
Rom  Seeming to be wise they were in fact foolish
Rom  And by them the glory of the eternal God was changed and made into the image of man who is not eternal and of birds and beasts and things which go on the earth
Rom  For this reason God gave them up to the evil desires of their hearts working shame in their bodies with one another
Rom  Because by them the true word of God was changed into that which is false and they gave worship and honour to the thing which is made and not to him who made it to whom be blessing for ever So be it
Rom  For this reason God gave them up to evil passions and their women were changing the natural use into one which is unnatural
Rom  And in the same way the men gave up the natural use of the woman and were burning in their desire for one another men doing shame with men and getting in their bodies the right reward of their evildoing
Rom  And because they had not the mind to keep God in their knowledge God gave them up to an evil mind to do those things which are not right
Rom  Being full of all wrongdoing evil desire for the goods of others hate envy putting to death fighting deceit cruel ways evil talk and false statements about others
Rom  Hated by God full of pride without respect full of loud talk given to evil inventions not honouring father or mother
Rom  Without knowledge not true to their undertakings unkind having no mercy
Rom  Who though they have knowledge of the law of God that the fate of those who do these things is death not only go on doing these things themselves but give approval to those who do them
Rom  So you have no reason whoever you are for judging for in judging another you are judging yourself for you do the same things
Rom  And we are conscious that God is a true judge against those who do such things
Rom  But you who are judging another for doing what you do yourself are you hoping that Gods decision will not take effect against you
Rom  Or is it nothing to you that God had pity on you waiting and putting up with you for so long not seeing that in his pity Gods desire is to give you a change of heart
Rom  But by your hard and unchanged heart you are storing up wrath for yourself in the day of the revelation of Gods judging in righteousness
Rom  Who will give to every man his right reward
Rom  To those who go on with good works in the hope of glory and honour and salvation from death he will give eternal life
Rom  But to those who from a love of competition are not guided by what is true will come the heat of his wrath
Rom  Trouble and sorrow on all whose works are evil to the Jew first and then to the Greek
Rom  But glory and honour and peace to all whose works are good to the Jew first and then to the Greek
Rom  For one man is not different from another before God
Rom  All those who have done wrong without the law will get destruction without the law and those who have done wrong under the law will have their punishment by the law
Rom  For it is not the hearers of the law who will be judged as having righteousness before God but only the doers
Rom  For when the Gentiles without the law have a natural desire to do the things in the law they are a law to themselves
Rom  Because the work of the law is seen in their hearts their sense of right and wrong giving witness to it while their minds are at one time judging them and at another giving them approval
Rom  In the day when God will be a judge of the secrets of men as it says in the good news of which I am a preacher through Jesus Christ
Rom  But as for you who have the name of Jew and are resting on the law and take pride in God
Rom  And have knowledge of his desires and are a judge of the things which are different having the learning of the law
Rom  In the belief that you are a guide to the blind a light to those in the dark
Rom  A teacher of the foolish having in the law the form of knowledge and of what is true
Rom  You who give teaching to others do you give it to yourself you who say that a man may not take what is not his do you take what is not yours
Rom  You who say that a man may not be untrue to his wife are you true to yours you who are a hater of images do you do wrong to the house of God
Rom  You who take pride in the law are you doing wrong to the honour of God by behaviour which is against the law
Rom  For the name of God is shamed among the Gentiles because of you as it is said in the holy Writings
Rom  It is true that circumcision is of use if you keep the law but if you go against the law it is as if you had it not
Rom  If those who have not circumcision keep the rules of the law will it not be credited to them as circumcision
Rom  And they by their keeping of the law without circumcision will be judges of you by whom the law is broken though you have the letter of the law and circumcision
Rom  The true Jew is not one who is only so publicly and circumcision is not that which may be seen in the flesh
Rom  But he is a Jew who is a secret one whose circumcision is of the heart in the spirit and not in the letter whose praise is not from men but from God
Rom  How then is the Jew better off or what profit is there in circumcision
Rom  Much in every way first of all because the words of God were given to them
Rom  And if some have no faith will that make the faith of God without effect
Rom  In no way but let God be true though every man is seen to be untrue as it is said in the Writings That your words may be seen to be true and you may be seen to be right when you are judged
Rom  But if the righteousness of God is supported by our wrongdoing what is to be said is it wrong for God to be angry as men may say
Rom  In no way because if it is so how is God able to be the judge of all the world
Rom  But if because I am untrue God being seen to be true gets more glory why am I to be judged as a sinner
Rom  Let us not do evil so that good may come a statement which we are falsely said by some to have made because such behaviour will have its right punishment
Rom  What then are we worse off than they In no way because we have before made it clear that Jews as well as Greeks are all under the power of sin
Rom  As it is said in the holy Writings There is not one who does righteousness
Rom  Not one who has the knowledge of what is right not one who is a searcher after God
Rom  They have all gone out of the way there is no profit in any of them there is not one who does good not so much as one
Rom  Their throat is like an open place of death with their tongues they have said what is not true the poison of snakes is under their lips
Rom  Whose mouth is full of curses and bitter words
Rom  Their feet are quick in running after blood
Rom  Destruction and trouble are in their ways
Rom  And of the way of peace they have no knowledge
Rom  There is no fear of God before their eyes
Rom  Now we have knowledge that what the law says is for those who are under the law so that every mouth may be stopped and all men may be judged by God
Rom  Because by the works of the law no man is able to have righteousness in his eyes for through the law comes the knowledge of sin
Rom  But now without the law there is a revelation of the righteousness of God to which witness is given by the law and the prophets
Rom  That is the righteousness of God through faith in Jesus Christ to all those who have faith and one man is not different from another
Rom  For all have done wrong and are far from the glory of God
Rom  And they may have righteousness put to their credit freely by his grace through the salvation which is in Christ Jesus
Rom  Whom God has put forward as the sign of his mercy through faith by his blood to make clear his righteousness when in his pity God let the sins of earlier times go without punishment
Rom  And to make clear his righteousness now so that he might himself be upright and give righteousness to him who has faith in Jesus
Rom  What reason then is there for pride It is shut out By what sort of law of works No but by a law of faith
Rom  For this reason then a man may get righteousness by faith without the works of the law
Rom  Or is God the God of Jews only is he not in the same way the God of Gentiles Yes of Gentiles
Rom  If God is one and he will give righteousness because of faith to those who have circumcision and through faith to those who have not circumcision
Rom  Do we then through faith make the law of no effect in no way but we make it clear that the law is important
Rom  What then may we say that Abraham our father after the flesh has got
Rom  For if Abraham got righteousness by works he has reason for pride but not before God
Rom  But what does it say in the holy Writings And Abraham had faith in God and it was put to his account as righteousness
Rom  Now the reward is credited to him who does works not as of grace but as a debt
Rom  But to him who without working has faith in him who gives righteousness to the evildoer his faith is put to his account as righteousness
Rom  As David says that there is a blessing on the man to whose account God puts righteousness without works saying
Rom  Happy are those who have forgiveness for their wrongdoing and whose sins are covered
Rom  Happy is the man against whom no sin is recorded by the Lord
Rom  Is this blessing then for the circumcision only or in the same way for those who have not circumcision for we say that the faith of Abraham was put to his account as righteousness
Rom  How then was it judged when he had circumcision or when he had it not Not when he had it but when he did not have it
Rom  And he was given the sign of circumcision as a witness of the faith which he had before he underwent circumcision so that he might be the father of all those who have faith though they have not circumcision and so that righteousness might be put to their account
Rom  And the father of circumcision to those who not only are of the circumcision but who keep to the way of that faith which our father Abraham had before he underwent circumcision
Rom  For Gods word that the earth would be his heritage was given to Abraham not through the law but through the righteousness of faith
Rom  For if they who are of the law are the people who get the heritage then faith is made of no use and the word of God has no power
Rom  For the outcome of the law is wrath but where there is no law it will not be broken
Rom  For this reason it is of faith so that it may be through grace and so that the word of God may be certain to all the seed not only to that which is of the law but to that which is of the faith of Abraham who is the father of us all
Rom  As it is said in the holy Writings I have made you a father of a number of nations before him in whom he had faith that is God who gives life to the dead and to whom the things which are not are as if they were
Rom  Who without reason for hope in faith went on hoping so that he became the father of a number of nations as it had been said So will your seed be
Rom  And not being feeble in faith though his body seemed to him little better than dead he being about a hundred years old and Sarah was no longer able to have children
Rom  Still he did not give up faith in the undertaking of God but was made strong by faith giving glory to God
Rom  And being certain that God was able to keep his word
Rom  For which reason it was put to his account as righteousness
Rom  Now it was not because of him only that this was said
Rom  But for us in addition to whose account it will be put if we have faith in him who made Jesus our Lord come back again from the dead
Rom  Who was put to death for our evildoing and came to life again so that we might have righteousness
Rom  For which reason because we have righteousness through faith let us be at peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ
Rom  Through whom in the same way we have been able by faith to come to this grace in which we now are and let us have joy in hope of the glory of God
Rom  And not only so but let us have joy in our troubles in the knowledge that trouble gives us the power of waiting
Rom  And waiting gives experience and experience hope
Rom  And hope does not put to shame because our hearts are full of the love of God through the Holy Spirit which is given to us
Rom  For when we were still without strength at the right time Christ gave his life for evildoers
Rom  Now it is hard for anyone to give his life even for an upright man though it might be that for a good man someone would give his life
Rom  But God has made clear his love to us in that when we were still sinners Christ gave his life for us
Rom  Much more if we now have righteousness by his blood will salvation from the wrath of God come to us through him
Rom  For if when we were haters of God the death of his Son made us at peace with him much more now that we are his friends will we have salvation through his life
Rom  And not only so but we have joy in God through our Lord Jesus Christ through whom we are now at peace with God
Rom  For this reason as through one man sin came into the world and death because of sin and so death came to all men because all have done evil
Rom  Because till the law came sin was in existence but sin is not put to the account of anyone when there is no law to be broken
Rom  But still death had power from Adam till Moses even over those who had not done wrong like Adam who is a picture of him who was to come
Rom  But the free giving of God is not like the wrongdoing of man For if by the wrongdoing of one man death came to numbers of men much more did the grace of God and the free giving by the grace of one man Jesus Christ come to men
Rom  And the free giving has not the same effect as the sin of one for the effect of one mans sin was punishment by the decision of God but the free giving had power to give righteousness to wrongdoers in great number
Rom  For if by the wrongdoing of one death was ruling through the one much more will those to whom has come the wealth of grace and the giving of righteousness be ruling in life through the one even Jesus Christ
Rom  So then as the effect of one act of wrongdoing was that punishment came on all men even so the effect of one act of righteousness was righteousness of life for all men
Rom  Because as numbers of men became sinners through the wrongdoing of one man even so will great numbers get righteousness through the keeping of the word of God by one man
Rom  And the law came in addition to make wrongdoing worse but where there was much sin there was much more grace
Rom  That as sin had power in death so grace might have power through righteousness to eternal life through Jesus Christ our Lord
Rom  What may we say then are we to go on in sin so that there may be more grace
Rom  In no way How may we who are dead to sin be living in it any longer
Rom  Or are you without the knowledge that all we who had baptism into Christ Jesus had baptism into his death
Rom  We have been placed with him among the dead through baptism into death so that as Christ came again from the dead by the glory of the Father we in the same way might be living in new life
Rom  For if we have been made like him in his death we will in the same way be like him in his coming to life again
Rom  Being conscious that our old man was put to death on the cross with him so that the body of sin might be put away and we might no longer be servants to sin
Rom  Because he who is dead is free from sin
Rom  But if we are dead with Christ we have faith that we will be living with him
Rom  Having knowledge that because Christ has come back from the dead he will never again go down to the dead death has no more power over him
Rom  For his death was a death to sin but his life now is a life which he is living to God
Rom  Even so see yourselves as dead to sin but living to God in Christ Jesus
Rom  For this cause do not let sin be ruling in your body which is under the power of death so that you give way to its desires
Rom  And do not give your bodies to sin as the instruments of wrongdoing but give yourselves to God as those who are living from the dead and your bodies as instruments of righteousness to God
Rom  For sin may not have rule over you because you are not under law but under grace
Rom  What then are we to go on in sin because we are not under law but under grace Let it not be so
Rom  Are you not conscious that you are the servants of him to whom you give yourselves to do his desire if to sin the end being death or if to do the desire of God the end being righteousness
Rom  But praise be to God that though you were the servants of sin you have now given yourselves freely to that form of teaching under which you were placed
Rom  And being made free from sin you have been made the servants of righteousness
Rom  I am using words in the way of men because your flesh is feeble as you gave your bodies as servants to what is unclean and to evil to do evil so now give them as servants to righteousness to do what is holy
Rom  When you were servants of sin you were free from righteousness
Rom  What fruit had you at that time in the things which are now a shame to you for the end of such things is death
Rom  But now being free from sin and having been made servants to God you have your fruit in that which is holy and the end is eternal life
Rom  For the reward of sin is death but what God freely gives is eternal life in Jesus Christ our Lord
Rom  Is it not clear my brothers I am using an argument to those who have knowledge of the law that the law has power over a man as long as he is living
Rom  For the woman who has a husband is placed by the law under the power of her husband as long as he is living but if her husband is dead she is free from the law of the husband
Rom  So if while the husband is living she is joined to another man she will get the name of one who is untrue to her husband but if the husband is dead she is free from the law so that she is not untrue even if she takes another man
Rom  In the same way my brothers you were made dead to the law through the body of Christ so that you might be joined to another even to him who came again from the dead so that we might give fruit to God
Rom  For when we were in the flesh the evil passions which came into being through the law were working in our bodies to give the fruit of death
Rom  But now we are free from the law having been made dead to that which had power over us so that we are servants in the new way of the spirit not in the old way of the letter
Rom  What then is to be said is the law sin in no way But I would not have had knowledge of sin but for the law for I would not have been conscious of desire if the law had not said You may not have a desire for what is anothers
Rom  But sin taking its chance through that which was ordered by the law was working in me every form of desire because without the law sin is dead
Rom  And there was a time when I was living without the law but when the law gave its orders sin came to life and put me to death
Rom  And I made the discovery that the law whose purpose was to give life had become a cause of death
Rom  For I was tricked and put to death by sin which took its chance through the law
Rom  But the law is holy and its orders are holy upright and good
Rom  Was then that which is good death to me In no way But the purpose was that sin might be seen to be sin by working death to me through that which is good so that through the orders of the law sin might seem much more evil
Rom  For we are conscious that the law is of the spirit but I am of the flesh given into the power of sin
Rom  And I have no clear knowledge of what I am doing for that which I have a mind to do I do not but what I have hate for that I do
Rom  But if I do that which I have no mind to do I am in agreement with the law that the law is good
Rom  So it is no longer I who do it but the sin living in me
Rom  For I am conscious that in me that is in my flesh there is nothing good I have the mind but not the power to do what is right
Rom  For the good which I have a mind to do I do not but the evil which I have no mind to do that I do
Rom  But if I do what I have no mind to do it is no longer I who do it but the sin living in me
Rom  So I see a law that though I have a mind to do good evil is present in me
Rom  In my heart I take pleasure in the law of God
Rom  But I see another law in my body working against the law of my mind and making me the servant of the law of sin which is in my flesh
Rom  How unhappy am I who will make me free from the body of this death
Rom  I give praise to God through Jesus Christ our Lord So with my mind I am a servant to the law of God but with my flesh to the law of sin
Rom  For this cause those who are in Christ Jesus will not be judged as sinners
Rom  For the law of the Spirit of life in Christ Jesus has made me free from the law of sin and death
Rom  For what the law was not able to do because it was feeble through the flesh God sending his Son in the image of the evil flesh and as an offering for sin gave his decision against sin in the flesh
Rom  So that what was ordered by the law might be done in us who are living not in the way of the flesh but in the way of the Spirit
Rom  For those who are living in the way of the flesh give their minds to the things of the flesh but those who go in the way of the Spirit to the things of the Spirit
Rom  For the mind of the flesh is death but the mind of the Spirit is life and peace
Rom  Because the mind of the flesh is opposite to God it is not under the law of God and is not able to be
Rom  So that those who are in the flesh are not able to give pleasure to God
Rom  You are not in the flesh but in the Spirit if the Spirit of God is in you But if any man has not the Spirit of Christ he is not one of his
Rom  And if Christ is in you the body is dead because of sin but the Spirit is life because of righteousness
Rom  But if the Spirit of him who made Jesus come again from the dead is in you he who made Christ Jesus come again from the dead will in the same way through his Spirit which is in you give life to your bodies which now are under the power of death
Rom  So then my brothers we are in debt not to the flesh to be living in the way of the flesh
Rom  For if you go in the way of the flesh death will come on you but if by the Spirit you put to death the works of the body you will have life
Rom  And all those who are guided by the Spirit of God are sons of God
Rom  For you did not get the spirit of servants again to put you in fear but the spirit of sons was given to you by which we say Abba Father
Rom  The Spirit is witness with our spirit that we are children of God
Rom  And if we are children we have a right to a part in the heritage a part in the things of God together with Christ so that if we have a part in his pain we will in the same way have a part in his glory
Rom  I am of the opinion that there is no comparison between the pain of this present time and the glory which we will see in the future
Rom  For the strong desire of every living thing is waiting for the revelation of the sons of God
Rom  For every living thing was put under the power of change not by its desire but by him who made it so in hope
Rom  That all living things will be made free from the power of death and will have a part with the free children of God in glory
Rom  For we are conscious that all living things are weeping and sorrowing in pain together till now
Rom  And not only so but we who have the first fruits of the Spirit even we have sorrow in our minds waiting for the time when we will take our place as sons that is the salvation of our bodies
Rom  For our salvation is by hope but hope which is seen is not hope for who is hoping for what he sees
Rom  But if we have hope for that which we see not then we will be able to go on waiting for it
Rom  And in the same way the Spirit is a help to our feeble hearts for we are not able to make prayer to God in the right way but the Spirit puts our desires into words which are not in our power to say
Rom  And he who is the searcher of hearts has knowledge of the mind of the Spirit because he is making prayers for the saints in agreement with the mind of God
Rom  And we are conscious that all things are working together for good to those who have love for God and have been marked out by his purpose
Rom  Because those of whom he had knowledge before they came into existence were marked out by him to be made like his Son so that he might be the first among a band of brothers
Rom  And those who were marked out by him were named and those who were named were given righteousness and to those to whom he gave righteousness in the same way he gave glory
Rom  What may we say about these things If God is for us who is against us
Rom  He who did not keep back his only Son but gave him up for us all will he not with him freely give us all things
Rom  Who will say anything against the saints of God It is God who makes us clear from evil
Rom  Who will give a decision against us It is Christ Jesus who not only was put to death but came again from the dead who is now at the right hand of God taking our part
Rom  Who will come between us and the love of Christ Will trouble or pain or cruel acts or the need of food or of clothing or danger or the sword
Rom  As it is said in the holy Writings Because of you we are put to death every day we are like sheep ready for destruction
Rom  But we are able to overcome all these things and more through his love
Rom  For I am certain that not death or life or angels or rulers or things present or things to come or powers
Rom  Or things on high or things under the earth or anything which is made will be able to come between us and the love of God which is in Christ Jesus our Lord
Rom  I say what is true in Christ and not what is false my mind giving witness with me in the Holy Spirit
Rom  That I am full of sorrow and pain without end
Rom  For I have a desire to take on myself the curse for my brothers my family in the flesh
Rom  Who are Israelites who have the place of sons and the glory and the agreements with God and the giving of the law and the worship and the hope offered by God
Rom  Whose are the fathers and of whom came Christ in the flesh who is over all God to whom be blessing for ever So be it
Rom  But it is not as if the word of God was without effect For they are not all Israel who are of Israel
Rom  And they are not all children because they are the seed of Abraham but In Isaac will your seed be named
Rom  That is it is not the children of the flesh but the children of Gods undertaking who are named as the seed
Rom  For this is the word of Gods undertaking At this time will I come and Sarah will have a son
Rom  And not only so but Rebecca being about to have a child by our father Isaac
Rom  Before the children had come into existence or had done anything good or bad in order that Gods purpose and his selection might be effected not by works but by him whose purpose it is
Rom  It was said to her The older will be the servant of the younger
Rom  Even as it is said I had love for Jacob but for Esau I had hate
Rom  What may we say then is God not upright let it not be said
Rom  For he says to Moses I will have mercy on whom I will have mercy and pity on whom I will have pity
Rom  So then it is not by the desire or by the attempt of man but by the mercy of God
Rom  For the holy Writings say to Pharaoh For this same purpose did I put you on high so that I might make my power seen in you and that there might be knowledge of my name through all the earth
Rom  So then at his pleasure he has mercy on a man and at his pleasure he makes the heart hard
Rom  But you will say to me Why does he still make us responsible who is able to go against his purpose
Rom  But O man who are you to make answer against God May the thing which is made say to him who made it Why did you make me so
Rom  Or has not the potter the right to make out of one part of his earth a vessel for honour and out of another a vessel for shame
Rom  What if God desiring to let his wrath and his power be seen for a long time put up with the vessels of wrath which were ready for destruction
Rom  And to make clear the wealth of his glory to vessels of mercy which he had before made ready for glory
Rom  Even us who were marked out by him not only from the Jews but from the Gentiles
Rom  As he says in Hosea They will be named my people who were not my people and she will be loved who was not loved
Rom  And in the place where it was said to them You are not my people there they will be named the sons of the living God
Rom  And Isaiah says about Israel Even if the number of the children of Israel is as the sand of the sea only a small part will get salvation
Rom  For the Lord will give effect to his word on the earth putting an end to it and cutting it short
Rom  And as Isaiah had said before If the Lord of armies had not given us a seed we would have been like Sodom and Gomorrah
Rom  What then may we say That the nations who did not go after righteousness have got righteousness even the righteousness which is of faith
Rom  But Israel going after a law of righteousness did not get it
Rom  Why Because they were not searching for it by faith but by works They came up against the stone which was in the way
Rom  As it is said See I am putting in Zion a stone causing a fall and a rock in the way but he who has faith in him will not be put to shame
Rom  Brothers my hearts desire and my prayer to God for them is that they may get salvation
Rom  For I give witness of them that they have a strong desire for God but not with knowledge
Rom  Because not having knowledge of Gods righteousness and desiring to give effect to their righteousness they have not put themselves under the righteousness of God
Rom  For Christ is the end of the law for righteousness to everyone who has faith
Rom  For Moses says that the man who does the righteousness which is of the law will get life by it
Rom  But the righteousness which is of faith says these words Say not in your heart Who will go up to heaven that is to make Christ come down
Rom  Or Who will go down into the deep that is to make Christ come again from the dead
Rom  But what does it say The word is near you in your mouth and in your heart that is the word of faith of which we are the preachers
Rom  Because if you say with your mouth that Jesus is Lord and have faith in your heart that God has made him come back from the dead you will have salvation
Rom  For with the heart man has faith to get righteousness and with the mouth he says that Jesus is Lord to get salvation
Rom  Because it is said in the holy Writings Whoever has faith in him will not be shamed
Rom  And the Jew is not different from the Greek for there is the same Lord of all who is good to all who have hope in his name
Rom  Because Whoever will give worship to the name of the Lord will get salvation
Rom  But how will they give worship to him in whom they have no faith and how will they have faith in him of whom they have not had news and how will they have news without a preacher
Rom  And how will there be preachers if they are not sent As it is said How beautiful are the feet of those who give the glad news of good things
Rom  But they have not all given ear to the good news For Isaiah says Lord who has had faith in our word
Rom  So faith comes by hearing and hearing by the word of Christ
Rom  But I say Did not the word come to their ears Yes certainly Their sound has gone out into all the earth and their words to the ends of the world
Rom  But I say Had Israel no knowledge First Moses says You will be moved to envy by that which is not a nation and by a foolish people I will make you angry
Rom  And Isaiah says without fear Those who were not searching for me made discovery of me and I was seen by those whose hearts were turned away from me
Rom  But about Israel he says All the day my hands have been stretched out to a people whose hearts were turned away and who put themselves against my word
Rom  So I say Has God put his people on one side Let there be no such thought For I am of Israel of the seed of Abraham of the tribe of Benjamin
Rom  God has not put away the people of his selection Or have you no knowledge of what is said about Elijah in the holy Writings how he says words to God against Israel
Rom  Lord they have put your prophets to death and made waste your altars and now I am the last and they are searching for me to take away my life
Rom  But what answer does God make to him I have still seven thousand men whose knees have not been bent to Baal
Rom  In the same way there are at this present time some who are marked out by the selection of grace
Rom  But if it is of grace then it is no longer of works or grace would not be grace
Rom  What then That which Israel was searching for he did not get but those of the selection got it and the rest were made hard
Rom  As it was said in the holy Writings God gave them a spirit of sleep eyes which might not see and ears which have no hearing to this day
Rom  And David says Let their table be made a net for taking them and a stone in their way and a punishment
Rom  Let their eyes be made dark so that they may not see and let their back be bent down at all times
Rom  So I say Were their steps made hard in order that they might have a fall In no way but by their fall salvation has come to the Gentiles so that they might be moved to envy
Rom  Now if their fall is the wealth of the world and their loss the wealth of the Gentiles how much greater will be the glory when they are made full
Rom  But I say to you Gentiles in so far as I am the Apostle of the Gentiles I make much of my position
Rom  If in any way those who are of my flesh may be moved to envy so that some of them may get salvation by me
Rom  For if by their putting away the rest of men have been made friends with God what will their coming back again be but life from the dead
Rom  And if the firstfruit is holy so is the mass and if the root is holy so are the branches
Rom  But if some of the branches were broken off and you an olivetree of the fields were put in among them and were given a part with them in the root by which the olivetree is made fertile
Rom  Do not be uplifted in pride over the branches because it is not you who are the support of the root but it is by the root that you are supported
Rom  You will say Branches were broken off so that I might be put in
Rom  Truly because they had no faith they were broken off and you have your place by reason of your faith Do not be lifted up in pride but have fear
Rom  For if God did not have mercy on the natural branches he will not have mercy on you
Rom  See then that God is good but his rules are fixed to those who were put away he was hard but to you he has been good on the condition that you keep in his mercy if not you will be cut off as they were
Rom  And they if they do not go on without faith will be united to the tree again because God is able to put them in again
Rom  For if you were cut out of a field olivetree and against the natural use were united to a good olivetree how much more will these the natural branches be united again with the olivetree which was theirs
Rom  For it is my desire brothers that this secret may be clear to you so that you may not have pride in your knowledge that Israel has been made hard in part till all the Gentiles have come in
Rom  And so all Israel will get salvation as it is said in the holy Writings There will come out of Zion the One who makes free by him wrongdoing will be taken away from Jacob
Rom  And this is my agreement with them when I will take away their sins
Rom  As far as the good news is in question they are cut off from God on account of you but as far as the selection is in question they are loved on account of the fathers
Rom  Because Gods selection and his mercies may not be changed
Rom  For as you in time past were not under the rule of God but now have got mercy through their turning away
Rom  So in the same way these have gone against the orders of God so that by the mercy given to you they may now get mercy
Rom  For God has let them all go against his orders so that he might have mercy on them all
Rom  O how deep is the wealth of the wisdom and knowledge of God no one is able to make discovery of his decisions and his ways may not be searched out
Rom  Who has knowledge of the mind of the Lord or who has taken part in his purposes
Rom  Or who has first given to him and it will be given back to him again
Rom  For of him and through him and to him are all things To him be the glory for ever So be it
Rom  For this reason I make request to you brothers by the mercies of God that you will give your bodies as a living offering holy pleasing to God which is the worship it is right for you to give him
Rom  And let not your behaviour be like that of this world but be changed and made new in mind so that by experience you may have knowledge of the good and pleasing and complete purpose of God
Rom  But I say to every one of you through the grace given to me not to have an overhigh opinion of himself but to have wise thoughts as God has given to every one a measure of faith
Rom  For as we have a number of parts in one body but all the parts have not the same use
Rom  So we though we are a number of persons are one body in Christ and are dependent on one another
Rom  And having different qualities by reason of the grace given to us such as the quality of a prophet let it be made use of in relation to the measure of our faith
Rom  Or the position of a Deacon of the church let a man give himself to it or he who has the power of teaching let him make use of it
Rom  He who has the power of comforting let him do so he who gives let him give freely he who has the power of ruling let him do it with a serious mind he who has mercy on others let it be with joy
Rom  Let love be without deceit Be haters of what is evil keep your minds fixed on what is good
Rom  Be kind to one another with a brothers love putting others before yourselves in honour
Rom  Be not slow in your work but be quick in spirit as the Lords servants
Rom  Being glad in hope quiet in trouble at all times given to prayer
Rom  Giving to the needs of the saints ready to take people into your houses
Rom  Give blessing and not curses to those who are cruel to you
Rom  Take part in the joy of those who are glad and in the grief of those who are sorrowing
Rom  Be in harmony with one another Do not have a high opinion of yourselves but be in agreement with common people Do not give yourselves an air of wisdom
Rom  Do not give evil for evil to any man Let all your business be well ordered in the eyes of all men
Rom  As far as it is possible for you be at peace with all men
Rom  Do not give punishment for wrongs done to you dear brothers but give way to the wrath of God for it is said in the holy Writings Punishment is mine I will give reward says the Lord
Rom  But if one who has hate for you is in need of food or of drink give it to him for in so doing you will put coals of fire on his head
Rom  Do not let evil overcome you but overcome evil by good
Rom  Let everyone put himself under the authority of the higher powers because there is no power which is not of God and all powers are ordered by God
Rom  For which reason everyone who puts himself against the authority puts himself against the order of God and those who are against it will get punishment for themselves
Rom  For rulers are not a cause of fear to the good work but to the evil If you would have no fear of the authority do good and you will have praise
Rom  For he is the servant of God to you for good But if you do evil have fear for the sword is not in his hand for nothing he is Gods servant making Gods punishment come on the evildoer
Rom  So put yourselves under the authority not for fear of wrath but because you have the knowledge of what is right
Rom  For the same reason make payment of taxes because the authority is Gods servant to take care of such things at all times
Rom  Give to all what is their right taxes to him whose they are payment to him whose right it is fear to whom fear honour to whom honour is to be given
Rom  Be in debt for nothing but to have love for one another for he who has love for his neighbour has kept all the law
Rom  And this Do not be untrue in married life Do not put to death Do not take what is anothers Do not have desire for what is anothers and if there is any other order it is covered by this word Have love for your neighbour as for yourself
Rom  Love does no wrong to his neighbour so love makes the law complete
Rom  See then that the time has come for you to be awake from sleep for now is your salvation nearer than when you first had faith
Rom  The night is far gone and the day is near so let us put off the works of the dark arming ourselves with light
Rom  With right behaviour as in the day not in pleasuremaking and drinking not in bad company and unclean behaviour not in fighting and envy
Rom  But put on the Lord Jesus Christ and do not give thought to the flesh to do its desires
Rom  Do not put on one side him who is feeble in faith and do not put him in doubt by your reasonings
Rom  One man has faith to take all things as food another who is feeble in faith takes only green food
Rom  Let not him who takes food have a low opinion of him who does not and let not him who does not take food be a judge of him who does for he has Gods approval
Rom  Who are you to make yourself a judge of another mans servant it is to his master that he is responsible for good or bad Yes his place will be safe because the Lord is able to keep him from falling
Rom  This man puts one day before another to that man they are the same Let every man be certain in his mind
Rom  He who keeps the day keeps it to the Lord and he who takes food takes it as to the Lord for he gives praise to God and he who does not take food to the Lord he takes it not and gives praise to God
Rom  For every mans life and every mans death has a relation to others as well as to himself
Rom  As long as we have life we are living to the Lord or if we give up our life it is to the Lord so if we are living or if our life comes to an end we are the Lords
Rom  And for this purpose Christ went into death and came back again that he might be the Lord of the dead and of the living
Rom  But you why do you make yourself your brothers judge or again why have you no respect for your brother because we will all have to take our place before God as our judge
Rom  For it is said in the holy Writings By my life says the Lord to me every knee will be bent and every tongue will give worship to God
Rom  So every one of us will have to give an account of himself to God
Rom  Then let us not be judges of one another any longer but keep this in mind that no man is to make it hard for his brother or give him cause for doubting
Rom  I am conscious of this and am certain in the Lord Jesus that nothing is unclean in itself but for the man in whose opinion it is unclean for him it is unclean
Rom  And if because of food your brother is troubled then you are no longer going on in the way of love Do not let your food be destruction to him for whom Christ went into death
Rom  Let it not be possible for men to say evil about your good
Rom  For the kingdom of God is not food and drink but righteousness and peace and joy in the Holy Spirit
Rom  And he who in these things is Christs servant is pleasing to God and has the approval of men
Rom  So then let us go after the things which make peace and the things by which we may be a help to one another
Rom  Do not let the work of God come to nothing on account of food All things are certainly clean but it is evil for that man who by taking food makes it hard for another
Rom  It is better not to take meat or wine or to do anything which might be a cause of trouble to your brother
Rom  The faith which you have have it to yourself before God Happy is the man who is not judged by that to which he gives approval
Rom  But he who is in doubt is judged if he takes food because he does it not in faith and whatever is not of faith is sin
Rom  We who are strong have to be a support to the feeble and not give pleasure to ourselves
Rom  Let every one of us give pleasure to his neighbour for his good to make him strong
Rom  For Christ did not give pleasure to himself but as it is said The bitter words of those who were angry with you came on me
Rom  Now those things which were put down in writing before our time were for our learning so that through quiet waiting and through the comfort of the holy Writings we might have hope
Rom  Now may the God who gives comfort and strength in waiting make you of the same mind with one another in harmony with Christ Jesus
Rom  So that with one mouth you may give glory to the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ
Rom  So then take one another to your hearts as Christ took us to the glory of God
Rom  Now I say that Christ has been made a servant of the circumcision to give effect to the undertakings given by God to the fathers
Rom  And so that the Gentiles might give glory to God for his mercy as it is said For this reason I will give praise to you among the Gentiles and I will make a song to your name
Rom  And again he says Take part you Gentiles in the joy of his people
Rom  And again Give praise to the Lord all you Gentiles and let all the nations give praise to him
Rom  And again Isaiah says There will be the root of Jesse and he who comes to be the ruler over the Gentiles in him will the Gentiles put their hope
Rom  Now may the God of hope make you full of joy and peace through faith so that all hope may be yours in the power of the Holy Spirit
Rom  And I myself am certain of you brothers that you are full of what is good complete in all knowledge able to give direction to one another
Rom  But I have in some measure less fear in writing to you to put these things before you again because of the grace which was given to me by God
Rom  To be a servant of Christ Jesus to the Gentiles doing the work of a priest in the good news of God so that the offering of the Gentiles might be pleasing to God being made holy by the Holy Spirit
Rom  So I have pride in Christ Jesus in the things which are Gods
Rom  And I will keep myself from talking of anything but those things which Christ has done by me to put the Gentiles under his rule in word and in act
Rom  By signs and wonders in the power of the Holy Spirit so that from Jerusalem and round about as far as Illyricum I have given all the good news of Christ
Rom  Making it my purpose not to take the good news where Christ was named so that my work might not be resting on that of others
Rom  But as it is said in the holy Writings They will see to whom the news of him had not been given and those to whose ears it had not come will have knowledge
Rom  For which reason I was frequently kept from coming to you
Rom  But now having no longer any place in these parts and having had for a number of years a great desire to come to you
Rom  Whenever I go to Spain for it is my hope to see you on my way and to be sent on there by you if first I may in some measure have been comforted by your company
Rom  But now I go to Jerusalem taking help for the saints
Rom  For it has been the good pleasure of those of Macedonia and Achaia to send a certain amount of money for the poor among the saints at Jerusalem
Rom  Yes it has been their good pleasure and they are in their debt For if the Gentiles have had a part in the things of the Spirit which were theirs it is right for them in the same way to give them help in the things of the flesh
Rom  So when I have done this and have given them this fruit of love I will go on by you into Spain
Rom  And I am certain that when I come I will be full of the blessing of Christ
Rom  Now I make request to you brothers by our Lord Jesus Christ and by the love of the Spirit that you will be working together with me in your prayers to God for me
Rom  So that I may be kept safe from those in Judaea who have not put themselves under the rule of God and that the help which I am taking for Jerusalem may be pleasing to the saints
Rom  So that I may come to you in joy by the good pleasure of God and have rest with you
Rom  Now may the God of peace be with you all So be it
Rom  It is my desire to say a good word for Phoebe who is a servant of the church in Cenchreae
Rom  That you will take her in kindly after the way of the saints as one who is the Lords and give her help in anything in which she may have need of you because she has been a help to a great number and to myself
Rom  Give my love to Prisca and Aquila workers with me in Christ Jesus
Rom  Who for my life put their necks in danger to whom not only I but all the churches of the Gentiles are in debt
Rom  And say a kind word to the church which is in their house Give my love to my dear Epaenetus who is the first fruit of Asia to Christ
Rom  Give my love to Mary who gave much care to you
Rom  Give my love to Andronicus and Junia my relations who were in prison with me who are noted among the Apostles and who were in Christ before me
Rom  Give my love to Ampliatus who is dear to me in the Lord
Rom  Give my love to Urbanus a worker in Christ with us and to my dear Stachys
Rom  Give my love to Apelles who has the approval of Christ Say a kind word to those who are of the house of Aristobulus
Rom  Give my love to Herodion my relation Say a kind word to those of the house of Narcissus who are in the Lord
Rom  Give my love to Tryphaena and Tryphosa workers in the Lord Give my love to my dear Persis who did much work in the Lord
Rom  Give my love to Rufus one of the Lords selection and to his mother and mine
Rom  Give my love to Asyncritus Phlegon Hermes Patrobas Hermas and the brothers who are with them
Rom  Give my love to Philologus and Julia Nereus and his sister and Olympas and all the saints who are with them
Rom  Give one another a holy kiss All the churches of Christ send their love to you
Rom  Now it is my desire brothers that you will take note of those who are causing division and trouble among you quite against the teaching which was given to you and keep away from them
Rom  For such people are not servants of the Lord Christ but of their stomachs and by their smooth and wellsaid words the hearts of those who have no knowledge of evil are tricked
Rom  For all have knowledge of how you do what you are ordered For this reason I have joy in you but it is my desire that you may be wise in what is good and without knowledge of evil
Rom  And the God of peace will be crushing Satan under your feet before long The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you
Rom  Timothy who is working with me sends his love to you so do Lucius and Jason and Sosipater my relations
Rom  I Tertius who have done the writing of this letter send love in the Lord
Rom  Gaius with whom I am living whose house is open to all the church sends his love so does Erastus the manager of the accounts of the town and Quartus the brother
Rom  
Rom  Now to him who is able to make you strong in agreement with the good news which I gave you and the preaching of Jesus Christ in the light of the revelation of that secret which has been kept through times eternal
Rom  But is now made clear and by the writings of the prophets by the order of the eternal God the knowledge of it has been given to all the nations so that they may come under the rule of the faith
Rom  To the only wise God through Jesus Christ be the glory for ever So be it
Co  Paul an Apostle of Jesus Christ by the purpose of God and Sosthenes the brother
Co  To the church of God which is in Corinth to those who have been made holy in Christ Jesus saints by the selection of God with all those who in every place give honour to the name of our Lord Jesus Christ their Lord and ours
Co  Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Co  I give praise to my God for you at all times because of the grace of God which has been given to you in Christ Jesus
Co  So that in him you have wealth in all things in word and in knowledge of every sort
Co  Even as the witness of the Christ has been made certain among you
Co  So that having every grace you are living in the hope of the revelation of our Lord Jesus Christ
Co  Who will give you strength to the end to be free from all sin in the day of our Lord Jesus Christ
Co  God is true through whom you have been given a part with his Son Jesus Christ our Lord
Co  Now I make request to you my brothers in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ that you will all say the same thing and that there may be no divisions among you so that you may be in complete agreement in the same mind and in the same opinion
Co  Because it has come to my knowledge through those of the house of Chloe that there are divisions among you my brothers
Co  That is that some of you say I am of Paul some say I am of Apollos some say I am of Cephas and some say I am Christs
Co  Is there a division in Christ was Paul nailed to the cross for you or were you given baptism in the name of Paul
Co  I give praise to God that not one of you had baptism from me but Crispus and Gaius
Co  So that no one may be able to say that you had baptism in my name
Co  And I gave baptism to the house of Stephanas but I am not certain that any others had baptism from me
Co  For Christ sent me not to give baptism but to be a preacher of the good news not with wise words for fear that the cross of Christ might be made of no value
Co  For the word of the cross seems foolish to those who are on the way to destruction but to us who are on the way to salvation it is the power of God
Co  As it says in the holy Writings I will put an end to the wisdom of the wise and will put on one side the designs of those who have knowledge
Co  Where is the wise where is he who has knowledge of the law where is the man of this world who has a love of discussion has not God made foolish the wisdom of this world
Co  For because by the purpose of God the world with all its wisdom had not the knowledge of God it was Gods pleasure by so foolish a thing as preaching to give salvation to those who had faith in him
Co  Seeing that the Jews make request for signs and the Greeks are looking for knowledge
Co  But we give the good news of Christ on the cross a hard thing to the Jews and a foolish thing to the Gentiles
Co  But to those of Gods selection Jews and Greeks Christ is the power and the wisdom of God
Co  Because what seems foolish in God is wiser than men and what seems feeble in God is stronger than men
Co  For you see Gods design for you my brothers that he has not taken a great number of the wise after the flesh not the strong not the noble
Co  But God made selection of the foolish things of this world so that he might put the wise to shame and the feeble things that he might put to shame the strong
Co  And the low things of the world and the things without honour did God make selection of yes even the things which are not so that he might make as nothing the things which are
Co  So that no flesh might have glory before God
Co  But God has given you a place in Christ Jesus through whom God has given us wisdom and righteousness and salvation and made us holy
Co  So that as it is said in the holy Writings Whoever has a desire for glory let his glory be in the Lord
Co  And when I came to you my brothers I did not come with wise words of knowledge putting before you the secret of God
Co  For I had made the decision to have knowledge of nothing among you but only of Jesus Christ on the cross
Co  And I was with you without strength in fear and in doubt
Co  And in my preaching there were no honeyed words of wisdom but I was dependent on the power of the Spirit to make it clear to you
Co  So that your faith might be based not on mans wisdom but on the power of God
Co  But still we have wisdom for those who are complete in knowledge though not the wisdom of this world and not of the rulers of this world who are coming to nothing
Co  But we give the news of the secret wisdom of God which he had kept in store before the world came into existence for our glory
Co  Of which not one of the rulers of this world had knowledge for if they had they would not have put the Lord of glory on the cross
Co  But as it says in the holy Writings Things which the eye saw not and which had not come to the ears or into the heart of man such things as God has made ready for those who have love for him
Co  But God has given us the revelation of these things through his Spirit for the Spirit makes search into all things even the deep things of God
Co  For who has knowledge of the things of a man but the spirit of the man which is in him in the same way no one has knowledge of the things of God but the Spirit of God
Co  But we have not the spirit of the world but the Spirit which comes from God so that we may have knowledge of the things which are freely given to us by God
Co  And these are the things which we say not in the language of mans wisdom but in words given to us by the Spirit judging the things of the spirit by the help of the Spirit
Co  For the natural man is not able to take in the things of the Spirit of God for they seem foolish to him and he is not able to have knowledge of them because such knowledge comes only through the Spirit
Co  But he who has the Spirit though judging all things is himself judged by no one
Co  For who has knowledge of the mind of the Lord so as to be his teacher But we have the mind of Christ
Co  And the teaching I gave you my brothers was such as I was able to give not to those who have the Spirit but to those who are still in the flesh even to children in Christ
Co  I gave you milk and not meat because you were then unable to take it and even now you are not able
Co  Because you are still in the flesh for when there is envy and division among you are you not still walking after the way of the flesh even as natural men
Co  For when one says I am of Paul and another says I am of Apollos are you not talking like natural men
Co  What then is Apollos and what is Paul They are but servants who gave you the good news as God gave it to them
Co  I did the planting Apollos did the watering but God gave the increase
Co  So then the planter is nothing and the waterer is nothing but God who gives the increase
Co  Now the planter and the waterer are working for the same end but they will have their separate rewards in the measure of their work
Co  For we are workers with God you are Gods planting Gods building
Co  In the measure of the grace given to me I as a wise masterbuilder have put the base in position and another goes on building on it But let every man take care what he puts on it
Co  For there is no other base for the building but that which has been put down which is Jesus Christ
Co  But on the base a man may put gold silver stones of great price wood dry grass cut stems
Co  Every mans work will be made clear in that day because it will be tested by fire and the fire itself will make clear the quality of every mans work
Co  If any mans work comes through the test he will have a reward
Co  If the fire puts an end to any mans work it will be his loss but he will get salvation himself though as by fire
Co  Do you not see that you are Gods holy house and that the Spirit of God has his place in you
Co  If anyone makes the house of God unclean God will put an end to him for the house of God is holy and you are his house
Co  Let no man have a false idea If any man seems to himself to be wise among you let him become foolish so that he may be wise
Co  For the wisdom of this world is foolish before God As it is said in the holy Writings He who takes the wise in their secret designs
Co  And again The Lord has knowledge of the reasonings of the wise that they are nothing
Co  So let no one take pride in men For all things are yours
Co  Paul or Apollos or Cephas or the world or life or death or things present or things to come all are yours
Co  And you are Christs and Christ is Gods
Co  Let us be judged as servants of Christ and as those who are responsible for the secret things of God
Co  And it is right for such servants to be safe persons
Co  But it is a small thing to me that I am judged by you or by mans judging I am not even a judge of myself
Co  For I am not conscious of any wrong in myself but this does not make me clear for it is the Lord who is my judge
Co  For this reason let there be no judging before the time till the Lord comes who will make clear the secret things of the dark and the designs of the heart and then will every man have his praise from God
Co  My brothers it is because of you that I have taken Apollos and myself as examples of these things so that in us you might see that it is not wise to go farther than what is in the holy Writings so that no one of you may be lifted up against his brother
Co  For who made you better than your brother or what have you that has not been given to you but if it has been given to you what cause have you for pride as if it had not been given to you
Co  For even now you are full even now you have wealth you have been made kings without us truly I would be glad if you were kings so that we might be kings with you
Co  For it seems to me that God has put us the Apostles last of all as men whose fate is death for we are put on view to the world and to angels and to men
Co  We are made to seem foolish for Christ but you are wise in Christ we are feeble but you are strong you have glory but we have shame
Co  Even to this hour we are without food drink and clothing we are given blows and have no certain restingplace
Co  And with our hands we do the hardest work when they give us curses we give blessings when we undergo punishment we take it quietly
Co  When evil things are said about us we give gentle answers we are made as the unclean things of the world as that for which no one has any use even till now
Co  I am not saying these things to put you to shame but so that as my dear children you may see what is right
Co  For even if you had ten thousand teachers in Christ you have not more than one father for in Christ Jesus I have given birth to you through the good news
Co  So my desire is that you take me as your example
Co  For this cause I have sent Timothy to you who is my dear and true child in the Lord he will make clear to you my ways in Christ even as I am teaching everywhere in every church
Co  Now some are full of pride as if I was not coming to you
Co  But I will come to you in a short time if it is pleasing to the Lord and I will take note not of the word of those who are full of pride but of the power
Co  For the kingdom of God is not in word but in power
Co  What is your desire is my coming to be with punishment or is it to be in love and a gentle spirit
Co  It is said in fact that there is among you a sin of the flesh such as is not seen even among the Gentiles that one of you has his fathers wife
Co  And in place of feeling sorrow you are pleased with yourselves so that he who has done this thing has not been sent away from among you
Co  For I myself being present in spirit though not in body have come to a decision about him who has done this thing
Co  In the name of our Lord Jesus when you have come together with my spirit with the power of our Lord Jesus
Co  That this man is to be handed over to Satan for the destruction of the flesh so that his spirit may have forgiveness in the day of the Lord Jesus
Co  This pride of yours is not good Do you not see that a little leaven makes a change in all the mass
Co  Take away then the old leaven so that you may be a new mass even as you are without leaven For Christ has been put to death as our Passover
Co  Let us then keep the feast not with old leaven and not with the leaven of evil thoughts and acts but with the unleavened bread of true thoughts and right feelings
Co  In my letter I said to you that you were not to keep company with those who go after the desires of the flesh
Co  But I had not in mind the sinners who are outside the church or those who have a desire for and take the property of others or those who give worship to images for it is not possible to keep away from such people without going out of the world completely
Co  But the sense of my letter was that if a brother had the name of being one who went after the desires of the flesh or had the desire for other peoples property or was in the way of using violent language or being the worse for drink or took by force what was not his you might not keep company with such a one or take food with him
Co  For it is no business of mine to be judging those who are outside but it is yours to be judging those who are among you
Co  As for those who are outside God is their judge So put away the evil man from among you
Co  How is it that if any one of you has a cause at law against another he takes it before a Gentile judge and not before the saints
Co  Is it not certain that the saints will be the judges of the world if then the world will be judged by you are you unable to give a decision about the smallest things
Co  Is it not certain that we are to be the judges of angels how much more then of the things of this life
Co  If then there are questions to be judged in connection with the things of this life why do you put them in the hands of those who have no position in the church
Co  I say this to put you to shame Is there not among you one wise man who may be able to give a decision between his brothers
Co  But a brother who has a cause at law against another takes it before Gentile judges
Co  More than this it is not to your credit to have causes at law with one another at all Why not put up with wrong why not undergo loss
Co  So far from doing this you yourselves do wrong and take your brothers property
Co  Have you not knowledge that evildoers will have no part in the kingdom of God Have no false ideas about this no one who goes after the desires of the flesh or gives worship to images or is untrue when married or is less than a man or makes a wrong use of men
Co  Or is a thief or the worse for drink or makes use of strong language or takes by force what is not his will have any part in the kingdom of God
Co  And such were some of you but you have been washed you have been made holy you have been given righteousness in the name of the Lord Jesus Christ and in the Spirit of our God
Co  I am free to do all things but not all things are wise I am free to do all things but I will not let myself come under the power of any
Co  Food is for the stomach and the stomach for food and God will put an end to them together But the body is not for the desires of the flesh but for the Lord and the Lord for the body
Co  And God who made the Lord Jesus come back from the dead will do the same for us by his power
Co  Do you not see that your bodies are part of the body of Christ how then may I take what is a part of the body of Christ and make it a part of the body of a loose woman such a thing may not be
Co  Or do you not see that he who is joined to a loose woman is one body with her for God has said The two of them will become one flesh
Co  But he who is united to the Lord is one spirit
Co  Keep away from the desires of the flesh Every sin which a man does is outside of the body but he who goes after the desires of the flesh does evil to his body
Co  Or are you not conscious that your body is a house for the Holy Spirit which is in you and which has been given to you by God and you are not the owners of yourselves
Co  For a payment has been made for you let God be honoured in your body
Co  Now as to the things in your letter to me It is good for a man to have nothing to do with a woman
Co  But because of the desires of the flesh let every man have his wife and every woman her husband
Co  Let the husband give to the wife what is right and let the wife do the same to the husband
Co  The wife has not power over her body but the husband and in the same way the husband has not power over his body but the wife
Co  Do not keep back from one another what is right but only for a short time and by agreement so that you may give yourselves to prayer and come together again so that Satan may not get the better of you through your loss of selfcontrol
Co  But this I say as my opinion and not as an order of the Lord
Co  It is my desire that all men might be even as I am But every man has the power of his special way of life given him by God one in this way and one in that
Co  But I say to the unmarried and to the widows It is good for them to be even as I am
Co  But if they have not selfcontrol let them get married for married life is better than the burning of desire
Co  But to the married I give orders though not I but the Lord that the wife may not go away from her husband
Co  Or if she goes away from him let her keep unmarried or be united to her husband again and that the husband may not go away from his wife
Co  But to the rest I say and not the Lord If a brother has a wife who is not a Christian and it is her desire to go on living with him let him not go away from her
Co  And if a woman has a husband who is not a Christian and it is his desire to go on living with her let her not go away from her husband
Co  For the husband who has not faith is made holy through his Christian wife and the wife who is not a Christian is made holy through the brother if not your children would be unholy but now are they holy
Co  But if the one who is not a Christian has a desire to go away let it be so the brother or the sister in such a position is not forced to do one thing or the other but it is Gods pleasure that we may be at peace with one another
Co  For how may you be certain O wife that you will not be the cause of salvation to your husband or you O husband that you may not do the same for your wife
Co  Only as the Lord has given to a man and as is the purpose of God for him so let him go on living And these are my orders for all the churches
Co  If any man who is a Christian has had circumcision let him keep so and if any man who is a Christian has not had circumcision let him make no change
Co  Circumcision is nothing and its opposite is nothing but only doing the orders of God is of value
Co  Let every man keep the position in which he has been placed by God
Co  If you were a servant when you became a Christian let it not be a grief to you but if you have a chance to become free make use of it
Co  For he who was a servant when he became a Christian is the Lords free man and he who was free when he became a Christian is the Lords servant
Co  It is the Lord who has made payment for you be not servants of men
Co  My brothers let every man keep in that condition which is the purpose of God for him
Co  Now about virgins I have no orders from the Lord but I give my opinion as one to whom the Lord has given mercy to be true to him
Co  In my opinion then because of the present trouble it is good for a man to keep as he is
Co  If you are married to a wife make no attempt to get free from her if you are free from a wife do not take a wife
Co  If you get married it is not a sin and if an unmarried woman gets married it is not a sin But those who do so will have trouble in the flesh But I will not be hard on you
Co  But I say this my brothers the time is short and from now it will be wise for those who have wives to be as if they had them not
Co  And for those who are in sorrow to give no signs of it and for those who are glad to give no signs of joy and for those who are getting property to be as if they had nothing
Co  And for those who make use of the world not to be using it fully for this worlds way of life will quickly come to an end
Co  But it is my desire for you to be free from cares The unmarried man gives his mind to the things of the Lord how he may give pleasure to the Lord
Co  But the married man gives his attention to the things of this world how he may give pleasure to his wife
Co  And the wife is not the same as the virgin The virgin gives her mind to the things of the Lord so that she may be holy in body and in spirit but the married woman takes thought for the things of the world how she may give pleasure to her husband
Co  Now I say this for your profit not to make things hard for you but because of what is right and so that you may be able to give all your attention to the things of the Lord
Co  But if in any mans opinion he is not doing what is right for his virgin if she is past her best years and there is need for it let him do what seems right to him it is no sin let them be married
Co  But the man who is strong in mind and purpose who is not forced but has control over his desires does well if he comes to the decision to keep her a virgin
Co  So then he who gets married to his virgin does well and he who keeps her unmarried does better
Co  It is right for a wife to be with her husband as long as he is living but when her husband is dead she is free to be married to another but only to a Christian
Co  But it will be better for her to keep as she is in my opinion and it seems to me that I have the Spirit of God
Co  Now about things offered to images we all seem to ourselves to have knowledge Knowledge gives pride but love gives true strength
Co  If anyone seems to himself to have knowledge so far he has not the right sort of knowledge about anything
Co  But if anyone has love for God God has knowledge of him
Co  So then as to the question of taking food offered to images we are certain that an image is nothing in the world and that there is no God but one
Co  For though there are those who have the name of gods in heaven or on earth as there are a number of gods and a number of lords
Co  There is for us only one God the Father of whom are all things and we are for him and one Lord Jesus Christ through whom are all things and we have our being through him
Co  Still all men have not that knowledge but some being used till now to the image are conscious that they are taking food which has been offered to the image and because they are not strong in the faith their minds are troubled
Co  But Gods approval of us is not based on the food we take if we do not take it we are no worse for it and if we take it we are no better
Co  But take care that this power of yours does not give cause for trouble to the feeble
Co  For if a man sees you who have knowledge taking food as a guest in the house of an image will it not give him if he is feeble the idea that he may take food offered to images
Co  And so through your knowledge you are the cause of destruction to your brother for whom Christ underwent death
Co  And in this way doing evil to the brothers and causing trouble to those whose faith is feeble you are sinning against Christ
Co  For this reason if food is a cause of trouble to my brother I will give up taking meat for ever so that I may not be a cause of trouble to my brother
Co  Am I not free am I not an Apostle have I not seen Jesus our Lord are you not my work in the Lord
Co  If to others I am not an Apostle at least I am one to you for the fact that you are Christians is the sign that I am an Apostle
Co  My answer to those who are judging me is this
Co  Have we no right to take food and drink
Co  Have we no right to take about with us a Christian wife like the rest of the Apostles and the brothers of the Lord and Cephas
Co  Or I only and Barnabas have we no right to take a rest from work
Co  Who ever goes to war without looking to someone to be responsible for his payment who puts in vines and does not take the fruit of them or who takes care of sheep without drinking of their milk
Co  Am I talking as a man does not the law say the same
Co  For it says in the law of Moses It is not right to keep the ox from taking the grain when he is crushing it Is it for the oxen that God is giving orders
Co  Or has he us in mind Yes it was said for us because it is right for the ploughman to do his ploughing in hope and for him who is crushing the grain to do his work hoping for a part in the fruits of it
Co  If we have been planting the things of the Spirit for you does it seem a great thing for you to give us a part in your things of this world
Co  If others have a part in this right over you have we not even more But we did not make use of our right so that we might put nothing in the way of the good news of Christ
Co  Do you not see that the servants of the holy things get their living from the Temple and the servants of the altar have their part in the food which is offered on the altar
Co  Even so did the Lord give orders that the preachers of the good news might get their living from the good news
