Co  But I have not made use of any of these things and I am not writing this in the hope that it may be so for me for it would be better for me to undergo death than for any man to make this pride of mine of no effect
Co  For if I am a preacher of the good news I have no cause for pride in this because I am forced to do so for a curse is on me if I do not
Co  But if I do it gladly I have a reward and if not I am under orders to do it
Co  What then is my reward This that when I am giving the good news I may give it without payment not making use of my rights as a preacher of the good news
Co  For though I was free from all men I made myself a servant to all so that more might have salvation
Co  And to the Jews I was as a Jew so that I might give the good news to them to those under the law I was the same not as being myself under the law but so that I might give the good news to those under the law
Co  To those without the law I was as one without the law not as being without law to God but as under law to Christ so that I might give the good news to those without the law
Co  To the feeble I was as one who is feeble so that they might have salvation I have been all things to all men so that some at least might have salvation
Co  And I do all things for the cause of the good news so that I may have a part in it
Co  Do you not see that in a running competition all take part but only one gets the reward So let your minds be fixed on the reward
Co  And every man who takes part in the sports has selfcontrol in all things Now they do it to get a crown which is of this world but we for an eternal crown
Co  So then I am running not uncertainly so I am fighting not as one who gives blows in the air
Co  But I give blows to my body and keep it under control for fear that after having given the good news to others I myself might not have Gods approval
Co  For it is my desire my brothers that you may keep in mind how all our fathers were under the cloud and they all went through the sea
Co  And they all had baptism from Moses in the cloud and in the sea
Co  And they all took the same holy food
Co  And the same holy drink for they all took of the water from the holy rock which came after them and the rock was Christ
Co  But with most of them God was not pleased for they came to their end in the waste land
Co  Now these things were for an example to us so that our hearts might not go after evil things as they did
Co  Then do not go after false gods as some of them did as it is said in the holy Writings After resting and feasting the people got up to take their pleasure
Co  Again let us not give way to the desires of the flesh as some of them did of whom twentythree thousand came to their end in one day
Co  And let us not put the Lord to the test as some of them did and came to their death by snakes
Co  And do not say evil things against the Lord as some of them did and destruction overtook them
Co  Now these things were done as an example and were put down in writing for our teaching on whom the last days have come
Co  So let him who seems to himself to be safe go in fear of a fall
Co  You have been put to no test but such as is common to man and God is true who will not let any test come on you which you are not able to undergo but he will make with the test a way out of it so that you may be able to go through it
Co  For this cause my dear brothers give no worship to false gods
Co  What I am saying is for wise men do you be the judges of it
Co  The cup of blessing which we take does it not give us a part in the blood of Christ and is not the broken bread a taking part in the body of Christ
Co  Because we being a number of persons are one bread we are one body for we all take part in the one bread
Co  See Israel after the flesh do not those who take as food the offerings of the altar take a part in the altar
Co  Do I say then that what is offered to images is anything or that the image is anything
Co  What I say is that the things offered by the Gentiles are offered to evil spirits and not to God and it is not my desire for you to have any part with evil spirits
Co  It is not possible for you at the same time to take the cup of the Lord and the cup of evil spirits you may not take part in the table of the Lord and the table of evil spirits
Co  Or may we be the cause of envy to the Lord are we stronger than he
Co  We are free to do all things but there are things which it is not wise to do We are free to do all things but not all things are for the common good
Co  Let a man give attention not only to what is good for himself but equally to his neighbours good
Co  Whatever meat may be had at the public market take as food without question of right or wrong
Co  For the earth is the Lords and all things in it
Co  If a Gentile makes a feast for you and you are pleased to go as a guest take whatever is put before you without question of right or wrong
Co  But if anyone says to you This food has been used as an offering do not take it on account of him who said it and on account of his sense of right and wrong
Co  Right and wrong I say not for you but for the other man for the fact that I am free is not dependent on another mans sense of right or wrong
Co  But if I give praise to God for the food which I take let no man say evil of me for that reason
Co  So then if it is a question of food or drink or any other thing whatever you do do all to the glory of God
Co  Give no cause of trouble to Jews or to Greeks or to the church of God
Co  Even as I give way to all men in all things not looking for profit for myself but for the good of others that they may get salvation
Co  So take me for your example even as I take Christ for mine
Co  Now I am pleased to see that you keep me in memory in all things and that you give attention to the teaching which was handed down from me to you
Co  But it is important for you to keep this fact in mind that the head of every man is Christ and the head of the woman is the man and the head of Christ is God
Co  Every man who takes part in prayer or gives teaching as a prophet with his head covered puts shame on his head
Co  But every woman who does so with her head unveiled puts shame on her head for it is the same as if her hair was cut off
Co  For if a woman is not veiled let her hair be cut off but if it is a shame to a woman to have her hair cut off let her be veiled
Co  For it is not right for a man to have his head covered because he is the image and glory of God but the woman is the glory of the man
Co  For the man did not come from the woman but the woman from the man
Co  And the man was not made for the woman but the woman for the man
Co  For this reason it is right for the woman to have a sign of authority on her head because of the angels
Co  But the woman is not separate from the man and the man is not separate from the woman in the Lord
Co  For as the woman is from the man so the man is through the woman but all things are from God
Co  Be judges yourselves of the question does it seem right for a woman to take part in prayer unveiled
Co  Does it not seem natural to you that if a man has long hair it is a cause of shame to him
Co  But if a woman has long hair it is a glory to her for her hair is given to her for a covering
Co  But if any man will not be ruled in this question this is not our way of doing things and it is not done in the churches of God
Co  But in giving you this order there is one thing about which I am not pleased it is that when you come together it is not for the better but for the worse
Co  For first of all it has come to my ears that when you come together in the church there are divisions among you and I take the statement to be true in part
Co  For divisions are necessary among you in order that those who have Gods approval may be clearly seen among you
Co  But now when you come together it is not possible to take the holy meal of the Lord
Co  For when you take your food everyone takes his meal before the other and one has not enough food and another is the worse for drink
Co  What have you not houses to take your meals in or have you no respect for the church of God putting the poor to shame What am I to say to you am I to give you praise certainly not
Co  For it was handed down to me from the Lord as I gave it to you that the Lord Jesus on the night when Judas was false to him took bread
Co  And when it had been broken with an act of praise he said This is my body which is for you do this in memory of me
Co  In the same way with the cup after the meal he said This cup is the new testament in my blood do this whenever you take it in memory of me
Co  For whenever you take the bread and the cup you give witness to the Lords death till he comes
Co  If then anyone takes the bread or the cup of the Lord in the wrong spirit he will be responsible for the body and blood of the Lord
Co  But let no man take of the bread and the cup without testing himself
Co  For a man puts himself in danger if he takes part in the holy meal without being conscious that it is the Lords body
Co  For this cause a number of you are feeble and ill and a number are dead
Co  But if we were true judges of ourselves punishment would not come on us
Co  But if punishment does come it is sent by the Lord so that we may be safe when the world is judged
Co  So then my brothers when you come together to the holy meal of the Lord let there be waiting for one another
Co  If any man is in need of food let him take his meal in his house so that you may not come together to your damage And the rest I will put in order when I come
Co  But about the things of the spirit my brothers it is not right for you to be without teaching
Co  You are conscious that when you were Gentiles in whatever way you were guided you went after images without voice or power
Co  So it is my desire for you to be clear about this that no one is able to say by the Spirit of God that Jesus is cursed and no one is able to say that Jesus is Lord but by the Holy Spirit
Co  Now there are different qualities given to men but the same Spirit
Co  And there are different sorts of servants but the same Lord
Co  And there are different operations but the same God who is working all things in all
Co  But to every man some form of the Spirits working is given for the common good
Co  For to one are given words of wisdom through the Spirit and to another words of knowledge through the same Spirit
Co  To another faith in the same Spirit and to another the power of taking away disease by the one Spirit
Co  And to another the power of working wonders and to another the prophets word and to another the power of testing spirits to another different sorts of tongues and to another the power of making clear the sense of the tongues
Co  But all these are the operations of the one and the same Spirit giving to every man separately as his pleasure is
Co  For as the body is one and has a number of parts and all the parts make one body so is Christ
Co  For through the baptism of the one Spirit we were all formed into one body Jews or Greeks servants or free men and were all made full of the same Spirit
Co  For the body is not one part but a number of parts
Co  If the foot says Because I am not the hand I am not a part of the body it is no less a part of the body
Co  And if the ear says Because I am not the eye I am not a part of the body it is a part of the body all the same
Co  If all the body was an eye where would be the hearing if all was hearing where would be the smelling
Co  But now God has put every one of the parts in the body as it was pleasing to him
Co  And if they were all one part where would the body be
Co  But now they are all different parts but one body
Co  And the eye may not say to the hand I have no need of you or again the head to the feet I have no need of you
Co  No those parts which seem to be feeble are the more necessary
Co  And to those parts of the body which seem to have less honour we give all the more honour and to those parts of the body which are a cause of shame to us we give the greater respect
Co  But those parts of the body which are beautiful have no need of such care and so the body has been joined together by God in such a way as to give more honour to those parts which had need of it
Co  So that there might be no division in the body but all the parts might have the same care for one another
Co  And if there is pain in one part of the body all the parts will be feeling it or if one part is honoured all the parts will be glad
Co  Now you are the body of Christ and every one of you the separate parts of it
Co  And God has put some in the church first Apostles second prophets third teachers then those with wonderworking powers then those with the power of taking away disease helpers wise guides users of strange tongues
Co  Are all Apostles are all prophets are all teachers have all the power of working wonders
Co  Are all able to take away disease have all the power of tongues are all able to give their sense
Co  But let your desires be turned to the more important things given by the Spirit And now I am pointing out to you an even better way
Co  If I make use of the tongues of men and of angels and have not love I am like sounding brass or a loudtongued bell
Co  And if I have a prophets power and have knowledge of all secret things and if I have all faith by which mountains may be moved from their place but have not love I am nothing
Co  And if I give all my goods to the poor and if I give my body to be burned but have not love it is of no profit to me
Co  Love is never tired of waiting love is kind love has no envy love has no high opinion of itself love has no pride
Co  Loves ways are ever fair it takes no thought for itself it is not quickly made angry it takes no account of evil
Co  It takes no pleasure in wrongdoing but has joy in what is true
Co  Love has the power of undergoing all things having faith in all things hoping all things
Co  Though the prophets word may come to an end tongues come to nothing and knowledge have no more value love has no end
Co  For our knowledge is only in part and the prophets word gives only a part of what is true
Co  But when that which is complete is come then that which is in part will be no longer necessary
Co  When I was a child I made use of a childs language I had a childs feelings and a childs thoughts now that I am a man I have put away the things of a child
Co  For now we see things in a glass darkly but then face to face now my knowledge is in part then it will be complete even as Gods knowledge of me
Co  But now we still have faith hope love these three and the greatest of these is love
Co  Go after love still desiring to have the things which the Spirit gives but most of all that you may have the prophets power
Co  For he who makes use of tongues is not talking to men but to God because no one has the sense of what he is saying but in the Spirit he is talking of secret things
Co  But the word of the prophet gives men knowledge and comfort and strength
Co  He who makes use of tongues may do good to himself but he who gives the prophets word does good to the church
Co  Now though it is my desire for you all to have the power of tongues it would give me more pleasure to be hearing the prophets word from you for this is a greater thing than using tongues if the sense is not given at the same time for the good of the church
Co  But now my brothers if I come to you using tongues what profit will it be to you if I do not give you a revelation or knowledge or the word of the prophet or teaching
Co  Even things without life having a voice such as a musicpipe or other instrument if they do not give out different sounds who may be certain what is being played
Co  For if the warhorn gives out an uncertain note who will get ready for the fight
Co  So if you in using a strange tongue say words which have no sense how will anyone take in what you are saying for you will be talking to the air
Co  There are it may be a number of different voices in the world and no voice is without sense
Co  But if the sense of the voice is not clear to me I am like a man from a strange country to him who is talking and he will be the same to me
Co  So if you are desiring the things which the Spirit gives let your minds be turned first to the things which are for the good of the church
Co  For this reason let the man who has the power of using tongues make request that he may at the same time be able to give the sense
Co  For if I make use of tongues in my prayers my spirit makes the prayer but not my mind
Co  What then let my prayer be from the spirit and equally from the mind let my song be from the spirit and equally from mind
Co  For if you give a blessing with the spirit how will the man who has no knowledge say So be it after your prayer seeing that he has not taken in what you are saying
Co  For your giving of the blessing is certainly well done but of no profit to the man without knowledge
Co  I give praise to God that I am able to make use of tongues more than you all
Co  But in the church it would be better for me to make use of five words of which the sense was clear so that others might have profit than ten thousand words in a strange tongue
Co  My brothers do not be children in mind in evil be as little children but in mind be of full growth
Co  In the law it is said By men of other tongues and by strange lips will my words come to this people and not even so will they give ear to me says the Lord
Co  For this reason tongues are for a sign not to those who have faith but to those who have not but the prophets word is for those who have faith and not for the rest who have not
Co  If then the church has come together and all are using tongues and there come in men without knowledge or faith will they not say that you are unbalanced
Co  But if all are teaching as prophets and a man without faith or knowledge comes in he is tested by all he is judged by all
Co  The secrets of his heart are made clear and he will go down on his face and give worship to God saying that God is truly among you
Co  What is it then my brothers when you come together everyone has a holy song or a revelation or a tongue or is giving the sense of it Let everything be done for the common good
Co  If any man makes use of a tongue let it not be more than two or at the most three and in turn and let someone give the sense
Co  But if there is no one to give the sense let him keep quiet in the church and let his words be to himself and to God
Co  And let the prophets give their words but not more than two or three and let the others be judges of what they say
Co  But if a revelation is given to another who is seated near let the first be quiet
Co  For you may all be prophets in turn so that all may get knowledge and comfort
Co  And the spirits of the prophets are controlled by the prophets
Co  For God is not a God whose ways are without order but a God of peace as in all the churches of the saints
Co  Let women keep quiet in the churches for it is not right for them to be talking but let them be under control as it says in the law
Co  And if they have a desire for knowledge about anything let them put questions to their husbands privately for talking in the church puts shame on a woman
Co  What was it from you that the word of God went out or did it only come in to you
Co  If any man seems to himself to be a prophet or to have the Spirit let him take note of the things which I am writing to you as being the word of the Lord
Co  But if any man is without knowledge let him be so
Co  So then my brothers let it be your chief desire to be prophets but let no one be stopped from using tongues
Co  Let all things be done in the right and ordered way
Co  Now I am going to make clear to you my brothers what the good news was which I gave to you and which you took and on which your faith is based
Co  By which you have salvation that is to say the form in which it was given to you if it is fixed in your minds and if your faith in it is not without effect
Co  For I gave to you first of all what was handed down to me how Christ underwent death for our sins as it says in the Writings
Co  And he was put in the place of the dead and on the third day he came back from the dead as it says in the Writings
Co  And he was seen by Cephas then by the twelve
Co  Then by more than five hundred brothers at the same time most of whom are still living but some are sleeping
Co  Then he was seen by James then by all the Apostles
Co  And last of all as by one whose birth was out of the right time he was seen by me
Co  For I am the least of the Apostles having no right to be named an Apostle because of my cruel attacks on the church of God
Co  But by the grace of God I am what I am and his grace which was given to me has not been for nothing for I did more work than all of them though not I but the grace of God which was with me
Co  If then it is I who am the preacher or they this is our word and to this you have given your faith
Co  Now if the good news says that Christ came back from the dead how do some of you say that there is no coming back from the dead
Co  But if there is no coming back from the dead then Christ has not come back from the dead
Co  And if Christ did not come again from the dead then our good news and your faith in it are of no effect
Co  Yes and we are seen to be false witnesses of God because we gave witness of God that by his power Christ came again from the dead which is not true if there is no coming back from the dead
Co  For if it is not possible for the dead to come to life again then Christ has not come to life again
Co  And if that is so your faith is of no effect you are still in your sins
Co  And in addition the dead in Christ have gone to destruction
Co  If in this life only we have hope in Christ we are of all men most unhappy
Co  But now Christ has truly come back from the dead the firstfruits of those who are sleeping
Co  For as by man came death so by man there is a coming back from the dead
Co  For as in Adam death comes to all so in Christ will all come back to life
Co  But every man in his right order Christ the firstfruits then those who are Christs at his coming
Co  Then comes the end when he will give up the kingdom to God even the Father when he will have put an end to all rule and to all authority and power
Co  For his rule will go on till he has put all those who are against him under his feet
Co  The last power to come to an end is death
Co  For as it says He has put all things under his feet But when he says All things are put under him it is clear that it is not said about him who put all things under him
Co  And when all things have been put under him then will the Son himself be under him who put all things under him so that God may be all in all
Co  Again what will they do who are given baptism for the dead if the dead do not come back at all why are people given baptism for them
Co  And why are we in danger every hour
Co  Yes truly by your pride in me my brothers in Christ Jesus our Lord my life is one long death
Co  If after the way of men I was fighting with beasts at Ephesus what profit is it to me If the dead do not come to life again let us take our pleasure in feasting for tomorrow we come to an end
Co  Do not be tricked by false words evil company does damage to good behaviour
Co  Be awake to righteousness and keep yourselves from sin for some have no knowledge of God I say this to put you to shame
Co  But someone will say How do the dead come back and with what sort of body do they come
Co  Foolish man it is necessary for the seed which you put into the earth to undergo death in order that it may come to life again
Co  And when you put it into the earth you do not put in the body which it will be but only the seed of grain or some other sort of plant
Co  But God gives it a body as it is pleasing to him and to every seed its special body
Co  All flesh is not the same flesh but there is one flesh of men another of beasts another of birds and another of fishes
Co  And there are bodies of heaven and bodies of earth but the glory of the one is different from that of the other
Co  There is one glory of the sun and another glory of the moon and another glory of the stars for the glory of one star is different from that of another
Co  So is it with the coming back from the dead It is planted in death it comes again in life
Co  It is planted in shame it comes again in glory feeble when it is planted it comes again in power
Co  It is planted a natural body it comes again as a body of the spirit If there is a natural body there is equally a body of the spirit
Co  And so it is said The first man Adam was a living soul The last Adam is a lifegiving spirit
Co  But that which is natural comes before that which is of the spirit
Co  The first man is from the earth and of the earth the second man is from heaven
Co  Those who are of the earth are like the man who was from the earth and those who are of heaven are like the one from heaven
Co  And in the same way as we have taken on us the image of the man from the earth so we will take on us the image of the one from heaven
Co  Now I say this my brothers that it is not possible for flesh and blood to have a part in the kingdom of God and death may not have a part in life
Co  See I am giving you the revelation of a secret we will not all come to the sleep of death but we will all be changed
Co  In a second in the shutting of an eye at the sound of the last horn for at that sound the dead will come again free for ever from the power of death and we will be changed
Co  For this body which comes to destruction will be made free from the power of death and the man who is under the power of death will put on eternal life
Co  But when this has taken place then that which was said in the Writings will come true Death is overcome by life
Co  O death where is your power O death where are your pains
Co  The pain of death is sin and the power of sin is the law
Co  But praise be to God who gives us strength to overcome through our Lord Jesus Christ
Co  For this cause my dear brothers be strong in purpose and unmoved ever giving yourselves to the work of the Lord because you are certain that your work is not without effect in the Lord
Co  Now about the giving of money for the saints as I gave orders to the churches of Galatia so do you
Co  On the first day of the week let every one of you put by him in store in measure as he has done well in business so that it may not be necessary to get money together when I come
Co  And when I come I will send the men of your selection with letters to take the money you have got together to Jerusalem
Co  And if it is possible for me to go there they will go with me
Co  But I will come to you after I have gone through Macedonia for that is my purpose
Co  But I may be with you for a time or even for the winter so that you may see me on my way wherever I go
Co  For it is not my desire to see you now on my way because it is my hope to be with you for some time if that is the Lords pleasure
Co  But I will be at Ephesus till Pentecost
Co  For a great and important door there is open to me and there are a number of people against me
Co  Now if Timothy comes see that he is with you without fear because he is doing the Lords work even as I am
Co  See then that he has the honour which is right But send him on his way in peace so that he may come to me for I am looking for him with the brothers
Co  But as for Apollos the brother I had a great desire for him to come to you with the brothers but it was not his pleasure to come now but he will come when he has a chance
Co  Be on the watch unmoved in the faith and be strong like men
Co  Let all you do be done in love
Co  Now I make my request to you my brothers for you have knowledge that the house of Stephanas is the firstfruits of Achaia and that they have made themselves the servants of the saints
Co  That you put yourselves under such and under everyone who is helping the Lords work
Co  And I am glad of the coming of Stephanas and Fortunatus and Achaicus for they have done what was needed to make your work complete
Co  For they gave comfort to my spirit and to yours for which cause give respect to such people
Co  The churches of Asia send their love to you So do Aquila and Prisca with the church which is in their house
Co  All the brothers send their love to you Give one another a holy kiss
Co  I Paul send you these words of love in my writing
Co  If any man has not love for the Lord let him be cursed Maran atha our Lord comes
Co  The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you
Co  My love be with you all in Christ Jesus So be it
Co  Paul an Apostle of Jesus Christ by the purpose of God and Timothy the brother to the church of God which is in Corinth with all the saints who are in all Achaia
Co  Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Co  Praise be to the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ the Father of mercies and the God of all comfort
Co  Who gives us comfort in all our troubles so that we may be able to give comfort to others who are in trouble through the comfort with which we ourselves are comforted by God
Co  For as we undergo more of the pain which Christ underwent so through Christ does our comfort become greater
Co  But if we are troubled it is for your comfort and salvation or if we are comforted it is for your comfort which takes effect through your quiet undergoing of the same troubles which we undergo
Co  And our hope for you is certain in the knowledge that as you take part in the troubles so you will take part in the comfort
Co  For it is our desire that you may not be without knowledge of our trouble which came on us in Asia that the weight of it was very great more than our power so that it seemed that we had no hope even of life
Co  Yes we ourselves have had the answer of death in ourselves so that our hope might not be in ourselves but in God who is able to give life to the dead
Co  Who gave us salvation from so great a death on whom we have put our hope that he will still go on to give us salvation
Co  You at the same time helping together by your prayer for us so that for what has been given to us through a number of persons praise may go up to God for us from all of them
Co  For our glory is in this in the knowledge which we have that our way of life in the world and most of all in relation to you has been holy and true in the eyes of God not in the wisdom of the flesh but in the grace of God
Co  For in our letters we say no other things to you but those which you are reading and to which you give agreement and it is my hope will go on doing so to the end
Co  Even as you have been ready in part to say that we are your glory in the same way that you are ours in the day of the Lord Jesus
Co  And being certain of this it was my purpose to come to you before so that you might have a second grace
Co  And by way of Corinth to go into Macedonia and from there to come back again to you so that you might send me on my way to Judaea
Co  If then I had such a purpose did I seem to be changing suddenly or am I guided in my purposes by the flesh saying Yes today and No tomorrow
Co  As God is true our word to you is not Yes and No
Co  For the Son of God Jesus Christ whom we were preaching among you even I and Silvanus and Timothy was not Yes and No but in him is Yes
Co  For he is the Yes to all the undertakings of God and by him all the words of God are made certain and put into effect to the glory of God through us
Co  Now he who makes our faith strong together with you in Christ and has given us of his grace is God
Co  And it is he who has put his stamp on us even the Spirit as the sign in our hearts of the coming glory
Co  But God is my witness that it was in pity for you that I did not come to Corinth at that time
Co  Not that we have authority over your faith but we are helpers of your joy for it is faith which is your support
Co  But it was my decision for myself not to come again to you with sorrow
Co  For if I give you sorrow who then will make me glad but he who is made sad by me
Co  And I said this very thing in my letter for fear that when I came I might have sorrow from those from whom it was right for me to have joy being certain of this that my joy is the joy of you all
Co  For out of much trouble and pain of heart and much weeping I sent my letter to you not to give you sorrow but so that you might see how great is the love which I have to you
Co  But if anyone has been a cause of sorrow he has been so not to me only but in some measure to all of you I say this that I may not be overhard on you
Co  Let it be enough for such a man to have undergone the punishment which the church put on him
Co  So that now on the other hand it is right for him to have forgiveness and comfort from you for fear that his sorrow may be overgreat
Co  For which cause my desire is that you will make your love to him clear by your acts
Co  And for the same reason I sent you a letter so that I might be certain of your desire to do my orders in all things
Co  But if you give forgiveness to anyone I do the same for if I have given forgiveness for anything I have done it because of you in the person of Christ
Co  So that Satan may not get the better of us for we are not without knowledge of his designs
Co  Now when I came to Troas for the good news of Christ and there was an open door for me in the Lord
Co  I had no rest in my spirit because Titus my brother was not there so I went away from them and came into Macedonia
Co  But praise be to God who makes us strong to overcome in Christ and makes clear through us in every place the value of the knowledge of him
Co  For we are a sweet perfume of Christ to God in those who are getting salvation and in those who are going to destruction
Co  To the one it is a perfume of death to death to the other a perfume of life to life And who is enough for such things
Co  For we are not like the great number who make use of the word of God for profit but our words are true as from God being said as before God in Christ
Co  Do we seem to be again attempting to put ourselves in the right or have we need as some have of letters of approval to you or from you
Co  You yourselves are our letter whose writing is in our heart open for every mans reading and knowledge
Co  For you are clearly a letter of Christ the fruit of our work recorded not with ink but with the Spirit of the living God not in stone but in hearts of flesh
Co  And this is the certain faith which we have in God through Christ
Co  Not as if we were able by ourselves to do anything for which we might take the credit but our power comes from God
Co  Who has made us able to be servants of a new agreement not of the letter but of the Spirit for the letter gives death but the Spirit gives life
Co  For if the operation of the law giving death recorded in letters on stone came with glory so that the eyes of the children of Israel had to be turned away from the face of Moses because of its glory a glory which was only for a time
Co  Will not the operation of the Spirit have a much greater glory
Co  For if the operation of the law producing punishment had its glory how much greater will be the operation of the Spirit causing righteousness
Co  For the glory of the first no longer seems to be glory because of the greater glory of that which comes after
Co  For if the order which was for a time had its glory much more will the eternal order have its glory
Co  Having then such a hope we keep nothing back
Co  And are not like Moses who put a veil on his face so that the children of Israel might not see clearly to the end of the present order of things
Co  But their minds were made hard for to this very day at the reading of the old agreement the same veil is still unlifted though it is taken away in Christ
Co  But to this day at the reading of the law of Moses a veil is over their heart
Co  But when it is turned to the Lord the veil will be taken away
Co  Now the Lord is the Spirit and where the Spirit of the Lord is there the heart is free
Co  But we all with unveiled face giving back as in a glass the glory of the Lord are changed into the same image from glory to glory even as from the Lord who is the Spirit
Co  For this reason because we have been made servants of this new order through the mercy given to us we are strong
Co  And we have given up the secret things of shame not walking in false ways and not making use of the word of God with deceit but by the revelation of what is true as before God we have the approval of every mans sense of right and wrong
Co  But if our good news is veiled it is veiled from those who are on the way to destruction
Co  Because the god of this world has made blind the minds of those who have not faith so that the light of the good news of the glory of Christ who is the image of God might not be shining on them
Co  For our preaching is not about ourselves but about Christ Jesus as Lord and ourselves as your servants through Jesus
Co  Seeing that it is God who said Let light be shining out of the dark who has put in our hearts the light of the knowledge of the glory of God in the face of Jesus Christ
Co  But we have this wealth in vessels of earth so that it may be seen that the power comes not from us but from God
Co  Troubles are round us on every side but we are not shut in things are hard for us but we see a way out of them
Co  We are cruelly attacked but not without hope we are made low but we are not without help
Co  In our bodies there is ever the mark of the death of Jesus so that the life of Jesus may be seen in our bodies
Co  For while living we are still being given up to death because of Jesus so that the life of Jesus may be seen in our flesh though it is under the power of death
Co  So then death is working in us but life in you
Co  But having the same spirit of faith as it is said in the Writings The words of my mouth came from the faith in my heart in the same way our words are the outcome of our faith
Co  Because we are certain that he who made the Lord Jesus come back from the dead will do the same for us and will give us a place in his glory with you
Co  For we go through all things on account of you because the greater the number to whom the grace is given the greater is the praise to the glory of God
Co  For which cause we do not give way to weariness but though our outer man is getting feebler our inner man is made new day by day
Co  For our present trouble which is only for a short time is working out for us a much greater weight of glory
Co  While our minds are not on the things which are seen but on the things which are not seen for the things which are seen are for a time but the things which are not seen are eternal
Co  For we are conscious that if this our tent of flesh is taken down we have a building from God a house not made with hands eternal in heaven
Co  For in this we are crying in weariness greatly desiring to be clothed with our house from heaven
Co  So that our spirits may not be unclothed
Co  For truly we who are in this tent do give out cries of weariness for the weight of care which is on us not because we are desiring to be free from the body but so that we may have our new body and death may be overcome by life
Co  Now he who has made us for this very thing is God who has given us the Spirit as a witness of what is to come
Co  So then we are ever without fear and though conscious that while we are in the body we are away from the Lord
Co  For we are walking by faith not by seeing
Co  We are without fear desiring to be free from the body and to be with the Lord
Co  For this reason we make it our purpose in the body or away from it to be wellpleasing to him
Co  For we all have to come before Christ to be judged so that every one of us may get his reward for the things done in the body good or bad
Co  Having in mind then the fear of the Lord we put these things before men but God sees our hearts and it is my hope that we may seem right in your eyes
Co  We are not again requesting your approval but we are giving you the chance of taking pride in us so that you may be able to give an answer to those whose glory is in seeming and not in the heart
Co  For if we are foolish it is to God or if we are serious it is for you
Co  For it is the love of Christ which is moving us because we are of the opinion that if one was put to death for all then all have undergone death
Co  And that he underwent death for all so that the living might no longer be living to themselves but to him who underwent death for them and came back from the dead
Co  For this reason from this time forward we have knowledge of no man after the flesh even if we have had knowledge of Christ after the flesh we have no longer any such knowledge
Co  So if any man is in Christ he is in a new world the old things have come to an end they have truly become new
Co  But all things are of God who has made us at peace with himself through Christ and has given to us the work of making peace
Co  That is that God was in Christ making peace between the world and himself not putting their sins to their account and having given to us the preaching of this news of peace
Co  So we are the representatives of Christ as if God was making a request to you through us we make our request to you in the name of Christ be at peace with God
Co  For him who had no knowledge of sin God made to be sin for us so that we might become the righteousness of God in him
Co  We then working together with God make our request to you not to take the grace of God to no purpose
Co  For he says I have given ear to you at a good time and I have been your helper in a day of salvation see now is the good time now is the day of salvation
Co  Giving no cause for trouble in anything so that no one may be able to say anything against our work
Co  But in everything making it clear that we are the servants of God in quiet strength in troubles in need in sorrow
Co  In blows in prisons in attacks in hard work in watchings in going without food
Co  In a clean heart in knowledge in long waiting in being kind in the Holy Spirit in true love
Co  In the true word in the power of God with the arms of righteousness on the right hand and on the left
Co  By glory and by shame by an evil name and a good name as untrue and still true
Co  Unnoted but still kept fully in mind as near to death but still living as undergoing punishment but not put to death
Co  As full of sorrow but ever glad as poor but giving wealth to others as having nothing but still having all things
Co  Our mouth is open to you O Corinthians our heart is wide
Co  It is not our feelings to you which are narrow but yours to us
Co  Now to give me back payment of the same sort I am talking as to my children let your hearts be wide open to me
Co  Do not keep company with those who have not faith for what is there in common between righteousness and evil or between light and dark
Co  And what agreement is there between Christ and the Evil One or what part has one who has faith with one who has not
Co  And what agreement has the house of God with images for we are a house of the living God even as God has said I will be living among them and walking with them and I will be their God and they will be my people
Co  For which cause Come out from among them and be separate says the Lord and let no unclean thing come near you and I will take you for myself
Co  And will be a Father to you and you will be my sons and daughters says the Lord the Ruler of all
Co  Because God then will give us such rewards dear brothers let us make ourselves clean from all evil of flesh and spirit and become completely holy in the fear of God
Co  Let your hearts be open to us we have done no man wrong no man has been damaged by us we have made no profit out of any man
Co  It is not with the purpose of judging you that I say this for I have said before that you are in our hearts for life and death together
Co  My words to you are without fear I am full of pride on account of you I have great comfort and joy in all our troubles
Co  For even when we had come into Macedonia our flesh had no rest but we were troubled on every side there were fightings outside and fears inside
Co  But God who gives comfort to the poor in spirit gave us comfort by the coming of Titus
Co  And not by his coming only but by the comfort which he had in you while he gave us word of your desire your sorrow your care for me so that I was still more glad
Co  For though my letter gave you pain I have no regret for it now though I had before for I see that the letter gave you pain but only for a time
Co  Now I am glad not that you had sorrow but that your sorrow was the cause of a change of heart for yours was a holy sorrow so that you might undergo no loss by us in anything
Co  For the sorrow which God gives is the cause of salvation through a change of heart in which there is no reason for grief but the sorrow of the world is a cause of death
Co  For you see what care was produced in you by this very sorrow of yours before God what clearing of yourselves what wrath against sin what fear what desire what serious purpose what punishment In everything you have made it clear that you are free from sin in this business
Co  So though I sent you a letter it was not only because of the man who did the wrong or because of him to whom the wrong was done but so that your true care for us might be made clear in the eyes of God
Co  So we have been comforted and we had the greater joy in our comfort because of the joy of Titus for his spirit had been made glad by you all
Co  For I was not put to shame in anything in which I may have made clear to him my pride in you but as we said nothing to you but what was true so the good things which I said to Titus about you were seen by him to be true
Co  And his love to you is the more increased by his memory of you all how you gave way to his authority and how you took him to your hearts with fear and honour
Co  It gives me great joy to see you answering to my good opinion of you in every way
Co  And now we give you news brothers about the grace of God which has been given to the churches of Macedonia
Co  How while they were undergoing every sort of trouble and were in the greatest need they took all the greater joy in being able to give freely to the needs of others
Co  For I give them witness that as they were able and even more than they were able they gave from the impulse of their hearts
Co  Seriously requesting us that they might have a part in this grace of being servants to the needs of the saints
Co  And going even farther than our hope they first gave themselves to the Lord and to us after the purpose of God
Co  So that we made a request to Titus that as he had made a start before so he might make this grace complete in you
Co  And that as you are full of every good thing of faith of the word of knowledge of a ready mind and of love to us so you may be full of this grace in the same way
Co  I am not giving you an order but using the ready mind of others as a test of the quality of your love
Co  For you see the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ how though he had wealth he became poor on your account so that through his need you might have wealth
Co  And in this I give my opinion for it is to your profit who were the first to make a start a year before not only to do this but to make clear that your minds were more than ready to do it
Co  Then make the doing of it complete so that as you had a ready mind you may give effect to it as you are able
Co  For if there is a ready mind a man will have Gods approval in the measure of what he has and not of what he has not
Co  And I am not saying this so that others may get off free while the weight comes on you
Co  But so that things may be equal that from those things of which you have more than enough at the present time their need may be helped and that if you are in any need they may be a help to you in the same way making things equal
Co  As it says in the Writings He who had taken up much had nothing over and he who had little had enough
Co  But praise be to God who puts the same care for you into the heart of Titus
Co  For while he gladly gave ear to our request he was interested enough to go to you from the impulse of his heart
Co  And with him we have sent a brother whose praise in the good news has gone through all the churches
Co  And not only so but he was marked out by the churches to go with us in the grace of this giving which we have undertaken to the glory of the Lord and to make clear that our mind was ready
Co  And so that no man might be able to say anything against us in the business of this giving which has been put into our hands
Co  For the business has been so ordered by us as to have the approval not only of the Lord but of men
Co  And we have sent with them our brother whose ready spirit has been made clear to us at times and in ways without number but it is now all the more so because of the certain faith which he has in you
Co  If any question comes up about Titus he is my brotherworker working with me for you or about the others they are the representatives of the churches to the glory of Christ
Co  Make clear then to them as representatives of the churches the quality of your love and that the things which we have said about you are true
Co  But there is no need for me to say anything in my letter about the giving to the saints
Co  For I have before made clear to those of Macedonia my pride in your ready mind saying to them that Achaia has been ready for a year back and a great number have been moved to do the same by your example
Co  But I have sent the brothers so that the good things we said about you may be seen to be true and that as I said you may be ready
Co  For fear that if any from Macedonia come with me and you are not ready we not to say you might be put to shame in this thing
Co  So it seemed to me wise for the brothers to go before and see that the amount which you had undertaken to give was ready so that it might be a cause for praise and not as if we were making profit out of you
Co  But in the Writings it says He who puts in only a small number of seeds will get in the same and he who puts them in from a full hand will have produce in full measure from them
Co  Let every man do after the purpose of his heart not giving with grief or by force for God takes pleasure in a ready giver
Co  And God is able to give you all grace in full measure so that ever having enough of all things you may be full of every good work
Co  As it is said in the Writings He has sent out far and wide he has given to the poor his righteousness is for ever
Co  And he who gives seed for putting into the field and bread for food will take care of the growth of your seed at the same time increasing the fruits of your righteousness
Co  Your wealth being increased in everything with a simple mind causing praise to God through us
Co  For this work of giving not only takes care of the needs of the saints but is the cause of much praise to God
Co  For when through this work of giving they see what you are they give glory to God for the way in which you have given yourselves to the good news of Christ and for the wealth of your giving to them and to all
Co  While their hearts go out to you in love and in prayer for you because of the great grace of God which is in you
Co  Praise be to God for what he has given which words have no power to say
Co  Now I Paul myself make request to you by the quiet and gentle behaviour of Christ I who am poor in spirit when with you but who say what is in my mind to you without fear when I am away from you
Co  Yes I make my request to you so that when I am with you I may not have to make use of the authority which may be needed against some to whom we seem to be walking after the flesh
Co  For though we may be living in the flesh we are not fighting after the way of the flesh
Co  For the arms with which we are fighting are not those of the flesh but are strong before God for the destruction of high places
Co  Putting an end to reasonings and every high thing which is lifted up against the knowledge of God and causing every thought to come under the authority of Christ
Co  Being ready to give punishment to whatever is against his authority after you have made it clear that you are completely under his control
Co  Give attention to the things which are before you If any man seems to himself to be Christs let him keep in mind that we are as much Christs as he is
Co  For though I might take pride in our authority which the Lord gave for building you up and not for your destruction it will not be a cause of shame to me
Co  That I may not seem to have the desire of causing you fear by my letters
Co  For his letters they say have weight and are strong but in body he is feeble and his way of talking has little force
Co  Let those who say this keep in mind that what we are in word by letters when we are away so will we be in act when we are present
Co  For we will not make comparison of ourselves with some of those who say good things about themselves but these measuring themselves by themselves and making comparison of themselves with themselves are not wise
Co  We will not give glory to ourselves in overgreat measure but after the measure of the rule which God has given us a measure which comes even to you
Co  For we have no need to make ourselves seem more than we are as if our authority did not come as far as to you for we came even as far as you with the good news of Christ
Co  Not taking credit to ourselves for what is not our business that is for the work of others but having hope that with the growth of your faith we may get the credit for an increase which is the effect of our work
Co  So that we may be able to go on and take the good news to countries still farther away than you are and not take credit for another mans work in making things ready to our hand
Co  But whoever has a desire for glory let his glory be in the Lord
Co  For the Lords approval of a man is not dependent on his opinion of himself but on the Lords opinion of him
Co  Put up with me if I am a little foolish but truly you do put up with me
Co  For I have a very great care for you because you have been married by me to one husband and it is my desire to give you completely holy to Christ
Co  But I have a fear that in some way as Eve was tricked by the deceit of the snake your minds may be turned away from their simple and holy love for Christ
Co  For if anyone comes preaching another Jesus from the one whose preachers we are or if you have got a different spirit or a different sort of good news from those which came to you how well you put up with these things
Co  For in my opinion I am in no way less than the most important of the Apostles
Co  But though I am rough in my way of talking I am not so in knowledge as we have made clear to all by our acts among you
Co  Or did I do wrong in making myself low so that you might be lifted up because I gave you the good news of God without reward
Co  I took money from other churches as payment for my work so that I might be your servant
Co  And when I was present with you and was in need I let no man be responsible for me for the brothers when they came from Macedonia gave me whatever was needed and in everything I kept myself from being a trouble to you and I will go on doing so
Co  As the true word of Christ is in me I will let no man take from me this my cause of pride in the country of Achaia
Co  Why because I have no love for you let God be judge
Co  But what I do that I will go on doing so that I may give no chance to those who are looking for one so that in the cause of their pride they may be seen to be the same as we are
Co  For such men are false Apostles workers of deceit making themselves seem like Apostles of Christ
Co  And it is no wonder for even Satan himself is able to take the form of an angel of light
Co  So it is no great thing if his servants make themselves seem to be servants of righteousness whose end will be the reward of their works
Co  I say again Let me not seem foolish to anyone but if I do put up with me as such so that I may take a little glory to myself
Co  What I am now saying is not by the order of the Lord but as a foolish person taking credit to myself as it seems
Co  Seeing that there are those who take credit to themselves after the flesh I will do the same
Co  For you put up with the foolish gladly being wise yourselves
Co  You put up with a man if he makes servants of you if he makes profit out of you if he makes you prisoners if he puts himself in a high place if he gives you blows on the face
Co  I say this by way of shaming ourselves as if we had been feeble But if anyone puts himself forward I am talking like a foolish person I will do the same
Co  Are they Hebrews so am I Are they of Israel so am I Are they the seed of Abraham so am I
Co  Are they servants of Christ I am talking foolishly I am more so I have had more experience of hard work of prisons of blows more than measure of death
Co  Five times the Jews gave me forty blows but one
Co  Three times I was whipped with rods once I was stoned three times the ship I was in came to destruction at sea a night and a day I have been in the water
Co  In frequent travels in dangers on rivers in dangers from outlaws in dangers from my countrymen in dangers from the Gentiles in dangers in the town in dangers in the waste land in dangers at sea in dangers among false brothers
Co  In hard work and weariness in frequent watchings going without food and drink cold and in need of clothing
Co  In addition to all the other things there is that which comes on me every day the care of all the churches
Co  Who is feeble and I am not feeble who is in danger of falling and I am not angry
Co  If I have to take credit to myself I will do so in the things in which I am feeble
Co  The God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ to whom be praise for ever is witness that the things which I say are true
Co  In Damascus the ruler under Aretas the king kept watch over the town of the people of Damascus in order to take me
Co  And being let down in a basket from the wall through a window I got free from his hands
Co  As it is necessary for me to take glory to myself though it is not a good thing I will come to visions and revelations of the Lord
Co  I have knowledge of a man in Christ fourteen years back if he was in the body or out of the body I am not able to say but God only who was taken up to the third heaven
Co  And I have knowledge of such a man if he was in the body or out of the body I am not able to say but God only
Co  How he was taken up into Paradise and words came to his ears which may not be said and which man is not able to say
Co  On account of such a one I will have glory for myself I will take no glory but only in my feeble body
Co  For if I had a desire to take credit to myself it would not be foolish for I would be saying what is true but I will not for fear that I might seem to any man more than he sees me to be or has word from me that I am
Co  And because the revelations were so very great in order that I might not be overmuch lifted up there was given to me a thorn in the flesh one sent from Satan to give me pain
Co  And about this thing I made request to the Lord three times that it might be taken away from me
Co  And he said to me My grace is enough for you for my power is made complete in what is feeble Most gladly then will I take pride in my feeble body so that the power of Christ may be on me
Co  So I take pleasure in being feeble in unkind words in needs in cruel attacks in troubles on account of Christ for when I am feeble then am I strong
Co  I have been forced by you to become foolish though it was right for my praise to have come from you for in no way was I less than the chief of the Apostles though I am nothing
Co  Truly the signs of an Apostle were done among you in quiet strength with wonders and acts of power
Co  For what is there in which you were made less than the other churches but in the one thing that I was not a trouble to you Let me have forgiveness for this wrong
Co  This is now the third time that I am ready to come to you and I will not be a trouble to you my desire is for you not for your property for it is not the childrens business to make store for their fathers but the fathers for the children
Co  And I will gladly give all I have for your souls If I have the more love for you am I to be loved the less
Co  But let it be so that I was not a trouble to you myself but someone may say being false I took you with deceit
Co  Did I make a profit out of you by any of those whom I sent to you
Co  I gave orders to Titus and I sent the brother with him Did Titus make any profit out of you were we not guided by the same Spirit in the same ways
Co  It may seem to you that all this time we have been attempting to put ourselves in the right but we are saying these things before God in Christ For all things dear brothers are for your profit
Co  For I have a fear that when I come you may not be answering to my desire and that I may not be answering to yours that there may be fighting hate angry feeling divisions evil talk about others secrets thoughts of pride outbursts against authority
Co  And that when I come again my God may put me to shame among you and I may have grief for those who have done wrong before and have had no regret for their unclean ways and for the evil desires of the flesh to which they have given way
Co  This is the third time that I am coming to you From the mouth of two or three witnesses will every word be made certain
Co  I said before and still say it before I come as being present for the second time though I am still away from you to those who have done wrong before and to all the others that if I come again I will not have pity
Co  Seeing that you are looking for a sign of Christ giving out his word in me who is not feeble in relation to you but is strong in you
Co  For he was feeble in that he was put to death on the cross but he is living by the power of God And we are feeble in him but we will be living with him through the power of God in relation to you
Co  Make a test of yourselves if you are in the faith make certain of yourselves Or are you not conscious in yourselves that Jesus Christ is in you if you are truly Christs
Co  But it is my hope that you will have no doubt that we are truly Christs
Co  Now our prayer to God is that you may do no evil not in order that it may be put to our credit but so that you may do what is right whatever we may seem
Co  Because we are able to do nothing against what is true but only for it
Co  For we are glad when we are feeble and you are strong and this is our prayer even that you may be made complete
Co  For this cause I am writing these things while I am away so that there may be need for me when I am present to make use of sharp measures by the authority which the Lord has given me for building up and not for destruction
Co  Let this be my last word brothers be glad be complete be comforted be of the same mind be at peace with one another and the God of love and peace will be with you
Co  Give one another a holy kiss
Co  All the saints send their love to you
Co  The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ and the love of God and the harmony of the Holy Spirit be with you all
Gal  Paul an Apostle not from men and not through man but through Jesus Christ and God the Father who made him come back from the dead
Gal  And all the brothers who are with me to the churches of Galatia
Gal  Grace to you and peace from God the Father and our Lord Jesus Christ
Gal  Who gave himself for our sins so that he might make us free from this present evil world after the purpose of our God and Father
Gal  To whom be the glory for ever and ever So be it
Gal  I am surprised that you are being so quickly turned away from him whose word came to you in the grace of Christ to good news of a different sort
Gal  Which is not another sort only there are some who give you trouble desiring to make changes in the good news of Christ
Gal  But even if we or an angel from heaven were to be a preacher to you of good news other than that which we have given you let there be a curse on him
Gal  As we have said before so say I now again If any man is a preacher to you of any good news other than that which has been given to you let there be a curse on him
Gal  Am I now using arguments to men or God or is it my desire to give men pleasure if I was still pleasing men I would not be a servant of Christ
Gal  Because I say to you my brothers that the good news of which I was the preacher is not mans
Gal  For I did not get it from man and I was not given teaching in it but it came to me through revelation of Jesus Christ
Gal  For news has come to you of my way of life in the past in the Jews religion how I was cruel without measure to the church of God and did great damage to it
Gal  And I went farther in the Jews religion than a number of my generation among my countrymen having a more burning interest in the beliefs handed down from my fathers
Gal  But when it was the good pleasure of God by whom I was marked out even from my mothers body through his grace
Gal  To give the revelation of his Son in me so that I might give the news of him to the Gentiles then I did not take the opinion of flesh and blood
Gal  And I went not up to Jerusalem to those who were Apostles before me but I went away into Arabia and again I came back to Damascus
Gal  Then after three years I went up to Jerusalem to see Cephas and was there with him fifteen days
Gal  But of the other Apostles I saw only James the Lords brother
Gal  Now God is witness that the things which I am writing to you are true
Gal  Then I came to the parts of Syria and Cilicia
Gal  And the churches of Judaea which were in Christ still had no knowledge of my face or person
Gal  Only it came to their ears that he who at one time was cruel to us is now preaching the faith which before had been attacked by him
Gal  And they gave glory to God in me
Gal  Then after the space of fourteen years I went up again to Jerusalem with Barnabas taking Titus with me
Gal  And I went up by revelation and I put before them the good news which I was preaching among the Gentiles but privately before those who were of good name so that the work which I was or had been doing might not be without effect
Gal  But not even Titus who was with me being a Greek was made to undergo circumcision
Gal  And that because of the false brothers let in secretly who came searching out our free condition which we have in Christ Jesus so that they might make servants of us
Gal  To whom we gave way not even for an hour so that the true words of the good news might still be with you
Gal  But from those who seemed to be important whatever they were has no weight with me God does not take mans person into account those who seemed to be important gave nothing new to me
Gal  But quite the opposite when they saw that I had been made responsible for preaching the good news to those without circumcision even as Peter had been for those of the circumcision
Gal  Because he who was working in Peter as the Apostle of the circumcision was working no less in me among the Gentiles
Gal  When they saw the grace which was given to me James and Cephas and John who had the name of being pillars gave to me and Barnabas their right hands as friends so that we might go to the Gentiles and they to the circumcision
Gal  Only it was their desire that we would give thought to the poor which very thing I had much in mind to do
Gal  But when Cephas came to Antioch I made a protest against him to his face because he was clearly in the wrong
Gal  For before certain men came from James he did take food with the Gentiles but when they came he went back and made himself separate fearing those who were of the circumcision
Gal  And the rest of the Jews went after him so that even Barnabas was overcome by their false ways
Gal  But when I saw that they were not living uprightly in agreement with the true words of the good news I said to Cephas before them all If you being a Jew are living like the Gentiles and not like the Jews how will you make the Gentiles do the same as the Jews
Gal  We being Jews by birth and not sinners of the Gentiles
Gal  Being conscious that a man does not get righteousness by the works of the law but through faith in Jesus Christ we had faith in Christ Jesus so that we might get righteousness by faith in Christ and not by the works of the law because by the works of the law will no flesh get righteousness
Gal  But if while we were desiring to get righteousness through Christ we ourselves were seen to be sinners is Christ a servant of sin In no way
Gal  For if I put up again those things which I gave to destruction I am seen to be a wrongdoer
Gal  For I through the law have become dead to the law so that I might be living to God
Gal  I have been put to death on the cross with Christ still I am living no longer I but Christ is living in me and that life which I now am living in the flesh I am living by faith the faith of the Son of God who in love for me gave himself up for me
Gal  I do not make the grace of God of no effect because if righteousness is through the law then Christ was put to death for nothing
Gal  O foolish Galatians by what strange powers have you been tricked to whom it was made clear that Jesus Christ was put to death on the cross
Gal  Give me an answer to this one question Did the Spirit come to you through the works of the law or by the hearing of faith
Gal  Are you so foolish having made a start in the Spirit will you now be made complete in the flesh
Gal  Did you undergo such a number of things to no purpose if it is in fact to no purpose
Gal  He who gives you the Spirit and does works of power among you is it by the works of law or by the hearing of faith
Gal  Even as Abraham had faith in God and it was put to his account as righteousness
Gal  Be certain then that those who are of faith the same are sons of Abraham
Gal  And the holy Writings seeing before the event that God would give the Gentiles righteousness by faith gave the good news before to Abraham saying In you will all the nations have a blessing
Gal  So then those who are of faith have a part in the blessing of Abraham who was full of faith
Gal  For all who are of the works of the law are under a curse because it is said in the Writings A curse is on everyone who does not keep on doing all the things which are ordered in the book of the law
Gal  Now that no man gets righteousness by the law in the eyes of God is clear because The upright will be living by faith
Gal  And the law is not of faith but He who does them will have life by them
Gal  Christ has made us free from the curse of the law having become a curse for us because it is said in the Writings A curse on everyone who is put to death by hanging on a tree
Gal  So that on the Gentiles might come the blessing of Abraham in Christ Jesus in order that we through faith might have the Spirit which God had undertaken to give
Gal  Brothers as men would say even a mans agreement when it has been made certain may not be put on one side or have additions made to it
Gal  Now to Abraham were the undertakings given and to his seed He says not And to seeds as of a great number but as of one he says And to your seed which is Christ
Gal  Now this I say The law which came four hundred and thirty years after does not put an end to the agreement made before by God so as to make the undertaking without effect
Gal  Because if the heritage is by the law it is no longer dependent on the word of God but God gave it to Abraham by his word
Gal  What then is the law It was an addition made because of sin till the coming of the seed to whom the undertaking had been given and it was ordered through angels by the hand of a gobetween
Gal  Now a gobetween is not a gobetween of one but God is one
Gal  Is the law then against the words of God in no way because if there had been a law which was able to give life truly righteousness would have been by the law
Gal  However the holy Writings have put all things under sin so that that for which God gave the undertaking based on faith in Jesus Christ might be given to those who have such faith
Gal  But before faith came we were kept in prison under the law waiting for the revelation of the faith which was to come
Gal  So the law has been a servant to take us to Christ so that we might have righteousness by faith
Gal  But now that faith is come we are no longer under a servant
Gal  Because you are all sons of God through faith in Christ Jesus
Gal  For all those of you who were given baptism into Christ did put on Christ
Gal  There is no Jew or Greek servant or free male or female because you are all one in Jesus Christ
Gal  And if you are Christs then you are Abrahams seed and yours is the heritage by the right of Gods undertaking given to Abraham
Gal  But I say that as long as the son is a child he is in no way different from a servant though he is lord of all
Gal  But is under keepers and managers till the time fixed by the father
Gal  So we when we were young were kept under the first rules of the world
Gal  But when the time had come God sent out his Son made of a woman made under the law
Gal  That he might make them free who were under the law and that we might be given the place of sons
Gal  And because you are sons God has sent out the Spirit of his Son into our hearts saying Abba Father
Gal  So that you are no longer a servant but a son and if a son then the heritage of God is yours
Gal  But at that time having no knowledge of God you were servants to those who by right are no gods
Gal  But now that you have come to have knowledge of God or more truly God has knowledge of you how is it that you go back again to the poor and feeble first things desiring to be servants to them again
Gal  You keep days and months and fixed times and years
Gal  I am in fear of you that I may have been working for you to no purpose
Gal  My desire for you brothers is that you may be as I am because I am as you are You have done me no wrong
Gal  But you have knowledge that with a feeble body I was preaching the good news to you the first time
Gal  And you did not have a poor opinion of me because of the trouble in my flesh or put shame on it but you took me to your hearts as an angel of God even as Christ Jesus
Gal  Where then is that happy condition of yours because I give you witness that if possible you would have taken out your eyes and given them to me
Gal  So then am I no longer your friend because I give you true words
Gal  Their interest in you is not good but their desire is that you may be shut out so that you may go after them
Gal  But it is good to have an interest in a good cause at all times and not only when I am present with you
Gal  My children of whom I am again in birthpains till Christ is formed in you
Gal  Truly my desire is to be present with you now using a changed voice for I am troubled about you
Gal  Say you whose desire it is to be under the law do you not give ear to the law
Gal  Because it is in the Writings that Abraham had two sons one by the servantwoman and one by the free woman
Gal  Now the son by the servantwoman has his birth after the flesh but the son by the free woman has his birth through the undertaking of God
Gal  Which things have a secret sense because these women are the two agreements one from the mountain of Sinai giving birth to servants which is Hagar
Gal  Now this Hagar is the mountain Sinai in Arabia and is the image of the Jerusalem which now is which is a servant with her children
Gal  But the Jerusalem on high is free which is our mother
Gal  For it is in the Writings You who have never given birth be glad give cries of joy you who have had no birthpains for the children of her who has been given up by her husband are more than those of the woman who has a husband
Gal  Now we brothers as Isaac was are the children of the undertaking of God
Gal  But as in those days he who had birth after the flesh was cruel to him who had birth after the Spirit even so it is now
Gal  What then do the Writings say Send away the servantwoman and her son for the son of the servantwoman will not have a part in the heritage with the son of the free woman
Gal  So brothers we are not children of the servantwoman but of the free woman
Gal  Christ has truly made us free then keep your free condition and let no man put a yoke on you again
Gal  See I Paul say to you that if you undergo circumcision Christ will be of no use to you
Gal  Yes I give witness again to every man who undergoes circumcision that he will have to keep all the law
Gal  You are cut off from Christ you who would have righteousness by the law you are turned away from grace
Gal  For we through the Spirit by faith are waiting for the hope of righteousness
Gal  Because in Christ Jesus having circumcision or not having circumcision are equally of no profit but only faith working through love
Gal  You were going on well who was the cause of your not giving ear to what is true
Gal  This ready belief did not come from him who had made you his
Gal  A little leaven makes a change in all the mass
Gal  I am certain about you in the Lord that you will be of no other mind but he who is troubling you will have his punishment whoever he is
Gal  But I brothers if I am still preaching circumcision why am I still attacked then has the shame of the cross been taken away
Gal  My desire is that they who give you trouble might even be cut off themselves
Gal  Because you brothers were marked out to be free only do not make use of your free condition to give the flesh its chance but through love be servants one to another
Gal  For all the law is made complete in one word even in this Have love for your neighbour as for yourself
Gal  But if you are given to fighting with one another take care that you are not the cause of destruction one to another
Gal  But I say Go on in the Spirit and you will not come under the rule of the evil desires of the flesh
Gal  For the flesh has desires against the Spirit and the Spirit against the flesh because these are opposite the one to the other so that you may not do the things which you have a mind to do
Gal  But if you are guided by the Spirit you are not under the law
Gal  Now the works of the flesh are clear which are these evil desire unclean things wrong use of the senses
Gal  Worship of images use of strange powers hates fighting desire for what another has angry feelings attempts to get the better of others divisions false teachings
Gal  Envy uncontrolled drinking and feasting and such things of which I give you word clearly even as I did in the past that they who do such things will have no part in the kingdom of God
Gal  But the fruit of the Spirit is love joy peace a quiet mind kind acts welldoing faith
Gal  Gentle behaviour control over desires against such there is no law
Gal  And those who are Christs have put to death on the cross the flesh with its passions and its evil desires
Gal  If we are living by the Spirit by the Spirit let us be guided
Gal  Let us not be full of selfglory making one another angry having envy of one another
Gal  Brothers if a man is taken in any wrongdoing you who are of the Spirit will put such a one right in a spirit of love keeping watch on yourself for fear that you yourself may be tested
Gal  Take on yourselves one anothers troubles and so keep the law of Christ
