Gal  For if a man has an idea that he is something when he is nothing he is tricked by himself
Gal  But let every man make test of his work and then will his cause for glory be in himself only and not in his neighbour
Gal  Because every man is responsible for his part of the work
Gal  But let him who gets teaching in the word give a part in all good things to his teacher
Gal  Be not tricked God is not made sport of for whatever seed a man puts in that will he get back as grain
Gal  Because he who puts in the seed of the flesh will of the flesh get the reward of death but he who puts in the seed of the Spirit will of the Spirit get the reward of eternal life
Gal  And let us not get tired of welldoing for at the right time we will get in the grain if we do not give way to weariness
Gal  So then as we have the chance let us do good to all men and specially to those who are of the family of the faith
Gal  See the size of the handwriting which I myself have made use of in writing to you
Gal  Those who have the desire to seem important in the flesh put force on you to undergo circumcision only that they may not be attacked because of the cross of Christ
Gal  Because even those who undergo circumcision do not themselves keep the law but they would have you undergo circumcision so that they may have glory in your flesh
Gal  But far be it from me to have glory in anything but only in the cross of our Lord Jesus Christ through which this world has come to an end on the cross for me and I for it
Gal  For having circumcision is nothing and not having circumcision is nothing but only a new order of existence
Gal  And on all who are guided by this rule be peace and mercy and on the Israel of God
Gal  From this time on let no man be a trouble to me because my body is marked with the marks of Jesus
Gal  The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit brothers So be it
Eph  Paul an Apostle of Christ Jesus by the purpose of God to the saints who are at Ephesus and those who have faith in Christ Jesus
Eph  Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Eph  Praise be to the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ who has given us every blessing of the Spirit in the heavens in Christ
Eph  Even as he made selection of us in him from the first so that we might be holy and free from all evil before him in love
Eph  As we were designed before by him for the position of sons to himself through Jesus Christ in the good pleasure of his purpose
Eph  To the praise of the glory of his grace which he freely gave to us in the Loved One
Eph  In whom we have salvation through his blood the forgiveness of our sins through the wealth of his grace
Eph  Which he gave us in full measure in all wisdom and care
Eph  Having made clear to us the secret of his purpose in agreement with the design which he had in mind to put into his hands
Eph  The ordering of the times when they are complete so that all things might come to a head in Christ the things in heaven and the things on the earth in him I say
Eph  In whom we have a heritage being marked out from the first in his purpose who does all things in agreement with his designs
Eph  So that his glory might have praise through us who first had hope in Christ
Eph  In whom you having been given the true word the good news of your salvation and through your faith in him were given the sign of the Holy Spirit of hope
Eph  Which is the firstfruit of our heritage till God gets back that which is his to the praise of his glory
Eph  For this cause I having had news of the faith in the Lord Jesus which is among you and which you make clear to all the saints
Eph  Give praise without end for you keeping you in mind in my prayers
Eph  That the God of our Lord Jesus Christ the Father of glory may give to you a spirit of wisdom and revelation in the knowledge of him
Eph  And that having the eyes of your heart full of light you may have knowledge of what is the hope of his purpose what is the wealth of the glory of his heritage in the saints
Eph  And how unlimited is his power to us who have faith as is seen in the working of the strength of his power
Eph  By which he made Christ come back from the dead and gave him a place at his right hand in heaven
Eph  Far over all rule and authority and power and every name which is named not only in the present order but in that which is to come
Eph  And he has put all things under his feet and has made him to be head over all things to the church
Eph  Which is his body the full measure of him in whom all things are made complete
Eph  And to you did he give life when you were dead through your wrongdoing and sins
Eph  In which you were living in the past after the ways of this present world doing the pleasure of the lord of the power of the air the spirit who is now working in those who go against the purpose of God
Eph  Among whom we all at one time were living in the pleasures of our flesh giving way to the desires of the flesh and of the mind and the punishment of God was waiting for us even as for the rest
Eph  But God being full of mercy through the great love which he had for us
Eph  Even when we were dead through our sins gave us life together with Christ by grace you have salvation
Eph  So that we came back from death with him and are seated with him in the heavens in Christ Jesus
Eph  That in the time to come he might make clear the full wealth of his grace in his mercy to us in Christ Jesus
Eph  Because by grace you have salvation through faith and that not of yourselves it is given by God
Eph  Not by works so that no man may take glory to himself
Eph  For by his act we were given existence in Christ Jesus to do those good works which God before made ready for us so that we might do them
Eph  For this reason keep it in mind that in the past you the Gentiles in the flesh who are looked on as being outside the circumcision by those who have circumcision in the flesh made by hands
Eph  That you were at that time without Christ being cut off from any part in Israels rights as a nation having no part in Gods agreement having no hope and without God in the world
Eph  But now in Christ Jesus you who at one time were far off are made near in the blood of Christ
Eph  For he is our peace who has made the two into one and by whom the middle wall of division has been broken down
Eph  Having in his flesh put an end to that which made the division between us even the law with its rules and orders so that he might make in himself of the two one new man so making peace
Eph  And that the two might come into agreement with God in one body through the cross so putting an end to that division
Eph  And he came preaching peace to you who were far off and to those who were near
Eph  Because through him the two of us are able to come near in one Spirit to the Father
Eph  So then you are no longer as those who have no part or place in the kingdom of God but you are numbered among the saints and of the family of God
Eph  Resting on the base of the Apostles and prophets Christ Jesus himself being the chief keystone
Eph  In whom all the building rightly joined together comes to be a holy house of God in the Lord
Eph  In whom you with the rest are united together as a livingplace of God in the Spirit
Eph  For this cause I Paul the prisoner of Christ Jesus for you Gentiles
Eph  If that ordering of the grace of God has come to your knowledge which was given to me for you
Eph  How by revelation the secret was made clear to me as I said before in a short letter
Eph  By the reading of which you will be clear about my knowledge of the secret of Christ
Eph  Which in other generations was not given to the sons of men but the revelation of it has now been made to his holy Apostles and prophets in the Spirit
Eph  Which is that the Gentiles have a part in the heritage and in the same body and in the same hope in Christ through the good news
Eph  Of which I was made a preacher through that grace of God which was given to me in the measure of the working of his power
Eph  To me who am less than the least of all the saints was this grace given so that I might make clear to the Gentiles the good news of the unending wealth of Christ
Eph  And make all men see what is the ordering of the secret which from the first has been kept in God who made all things
Eph  So that now to the rulers and the authorities in the heavens might be made clear through the church the wideshining wisdom of God
Eph  Which is seen in his eternal purpose in Christ Jesus our Lord
Eph  By whom we come near to God without fear through faith in him
Eph  For this reason it is my prayer that you may not become feeble because of my troubles for you which are your glory
Eph  For this cause I go down on my knees before the Father
Eph  From whom every family in heaven and on earth is named
Eph  That in the wealth of his glory he would make you strong with power through his Spirit in your hearts
Eph  So that Christ may have his place in your hearts through faith and that you being rooted and based in love
Eph  May have strength to see with all the saints how wide and long and high and deep it is
Eph  And to have knowledge of the love of Christ which is outside all knowledge so that you may be made complete as God himself is complete
Eph  Now to him who is able to do in full measure more than all our desires or thoughts through the power which is working in us
Eph  To him be the glory in the church and in Christ Jesus to all generations for ever and ever So be it
Eph  I then the prisoner in the Lord make this request from my heart that you will see that your behaviour is a credit to the position which Gods purpose has given you
Eph  With all gentle and quiet behaviour taking whatever comes putting up with one another in love
Eph  Taking care to keep the harmony of the Spirit in the yoke of peace
Eph  There is one body and one Spirit even as you have been marked out by God in the one hope of his purpose for you
Eph  One Lord one faith one baptism
Eph  One God and Father of all who is over all and through all and in all
Eph  But to every one of us has grace been given in the measure of the giving of Christ
Eph  For this reason he says He went up on high taking his prisoners with him and gave freely to men
Eph  Now this He went up what is it but that he first went down into the lower parts of the earth
Eph  He who went down is the same who went up far over all the heavens so that he might make all things complete
Eph  And he gave some as Apostles and some prophets and some preachers of the good news and some to give care and teaching
Eph  For the training of the saints as servants in the church for the building up of the body of Christ
Eph  Till we all come to the harmony of the faith and of the knowledge of the Son of God to full growth to the full measure of Christ
Eph  So that we may be no longer children sent this way and that turned about by every wind of teaching by the twisting and tricks of men by the deceits of error
Eph  But saying true words in love may come to full growth in him who is the head even Christ
Eph  Through whom all the body being rightly formed and united together by the full working of every part is increased to the building up of itself in love
Eph  This I say then and give witness in the Lord that you are to go no longer in the way of the Gentiles whose minds are turned to that which has no profit
Eph  Whose thoughts are dark to whom the life of God is strange because they are without knowledge and their hearts have been made hard
Eph  Who having no more power of feeling have given themselves up to evil passions to do all unclean things with overmuch desire
Eph  For this was not the teaching of Christ which was given to you
Eph  If in fact you gave ear to him and were given teaching in him even as what is true is made clear in Jesus
Eph  That you are to put away in relation to your earlier way of life the old man which has become evil by love of deceit
Eph  And be made new in the spirit of your mind
Eph  And put on the new man to which God has given life in righteousness and a true and holy way of living
Eph  And so putting away false words let everyone say what is true to his neighbour for we are parts one of another
Eph  Be angry without doing wrong let not the sun go down on your wrath
Eph  And do not give way to the Evil One
Eph  Let him who was a thief be so no longer but let him do good work with his hands so that he may have something to give to him who is in need
Eph  Let no evil talk come out of your mouth but only what is good for giving necessary teaching and for grace to those who give ear
Eph  And do not give grief to the Holy Spirit of God by whom you were marked for the day of salvation
Eph  Let all bitter sharp and angry feeling and noise and evil words be put away from you with all unkind acts
Eph  And be kind to one another full of pity having forgiveness for one another even as God in Christ had forgiveness for you
Eph  Let it then be your desire to be like God as wellloved children
Eph  And be living in love even as Christ had love for you and gave himself up for us an offering to God for a perfume of a sweet smell
Eph  But evil acts of the flesh and all unclean things or desire for others property let it not even be named among you as is right for saints
Eph  And let there be no low behaviour or foolish talk or words said in sport which are not right but in place of them the giving of praise
Eph  Being certain of this that no man who gives way to the passions of the flesh no unclean person or one who has desire for the property of others or who gives worship to images has any heritage in the kingdom of Christ and God
Eph  Do not be turned from the right way by foolish words for because of these things the punishment of God comes on those who do not put themselves under him
Eph  Have no part with such men
Eph  For you at one time were dark but now are light in the Lord let your behaviour be that of children of light
Eph  Because the fruit of the light is in all righteousness and in everything which is good and true
Eph  Testing by experience what is wellpleasing to the Lord
Eph  And have no company with the works of the dark which give no fruit but make their true quality clear
Eph  For the things which are done by them in secret it is shame even to put into words
Eph  But all things when their true quality is seen are made clear by the light because everything which is made clear is light
Eph  For this reason he says Be awake you who are sleeping and come up from among the dead and Christ will be your light
Eph  Take care then how you are living not as unwise but as wise
Eph  Making good use of the time because the days are evil
Eph  For this reason then do not be foolish but be conscious of the Lords pleasure
Eph  And do not take overmuch wine by which one may be overcome but be full of the Spirit
Eph  Joining with one another in holy songs of praise and of the Spirit using your voice in songs and making melody in your heart to the Lord
Eph  Giving praise at all times for all things in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ to God even the Father
Eph  Letting yourselves be ruled by one another in the fear of Christ
Eph  Wives be under the authority of your husbands as of the Lord
Eph  For the husband is the head of the wife as Christ is the head of the church being himself the saviour of the body
Eph  And as the church is under Christs authority so let wives be under the rule of their husbands in all things
Eph  Husbands have love for your wives even as Christ had love for the church and gave himself for it
Eph  So that he might make it holy having made it clean with the washing of water by the word
Eph  And might take it for himself a church full of glory not having one mark or fold or any such thing but that it might be holy and complete
Eph  Even so it is right for husbands to have love for their wives as for their bodies He who has love for his wife has love for himself
Eph  For no man ever had hate for his flesh but he gives it food and takes care of it even as Christ does for the church
Eph  Because we are parts of his body
Eph  For this cause will a man go away from his father and mother and be joined to his wife and the two will become one flesh
Eph  This is a great secret but my words are about Christ and the church
Eph  But do you everyone have love for his wife even as for himself and let the wife see that she has respect for her husband
Eph  Children do what is ordered by your fathers and mothers in the Lord for this is right
Eph  Give honour to your father and mother which is the first rule having a reward
Eph  So that all may be well for you and your life may be long on the earth
Eph  And you fathers do not make your children angry but give them training in the teaching and fear of the Lord
Eph  Servants do what is ordered by those who are your natural masters having respect and fear for them with all your heart as to Christ
Eph  Not only under your masters eye as pleasers of men but as servants of Christ doing the pleasure of God from the heart
Eph  Doing your work readily as to the Lord and not to men
Eph  In the knowledge that for every good thing anyone does he will have his reward from the Lord If he is a servant or if he is free
Eph  And you masters do the same things to them not making use of violent words in the knowledge that their Master and yours is in heaven and he has no respect for a mans position
Eph  Lastly be strong in the Lord and in the strength of his power
Eph  Take up Gods instruments of war so that you may be able to keep your position against all the deceits of the Evil One
Eph  For our fight is not against flesh and blood but against authorities and powers against the worldrulers of this dark night against the spirits of evil in the heavens
Eph  For this reason take up all the arms of God so that you may be able to be strong in the evil day and having done all to keep your place
Eph  Take your place then having your body clothed with the true word and having put on the breastplate of righteousness
Eph  Be ready with the good news of peace as shoes on your feet
Eph  And most of all using faith as a cover to keep off all the flaming arrows of the Evil One
Eph  And take salvation for your headdress and the sword of the Spirit which is the word of God
Eph  With prayers and deep desires making requests at all times in the Spirit and keeping watch with strong purpose in prayer for all the saints
Eph  And for me that words may be given to me in the opening of my mouth to make clear without fear the secret of the good news
Eph  For which I am a representative in chains and that I may say without fear the things which it is right for me to say
Eph  But so that you may have knowledge of my business and how I am Tychicus the wellloved brother and tested servant in the Lord will give you news of all things
Eph  Whom I have sent to you for this very purpose so that you may have knowledge of our position and that he may give comfort to your hearts
Eph  Peace be to the brothers and love with faith from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Eph  Grace be with all those who have true love for our Lord Jesus Christ
Phl  Paul and Timothy servants of Jesus Christ to all the saints in Christ Jesus at Philippi with the Bishops and Deacons of the church
Phl  Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Phl  I give praise to my God at every memory of you
Phl  And in all my prayers for you all making my request with joy
Phl  Because of your help in giving the good news from the first day till now
Phl  For I am certain of this very thing that he by whom the good work was started in you will make it complete till the day of Jesus Christ
Phl  So it is right for me to take thought for you all in this way because I have you in my heart for in my chains and in my arguments before the judges in support of the good news making clear that it is true you all have your part with me in grace
Phl  For God is my witness how my love goes out to you all in the loving mercies of Christ Jesus
Phl  And my prayer is that you may be increased more and more in knowledge and experience
Phl  So that you may give your approval to the best things that you may be true and without wrongdoing till the day of Christ
Phl  Being full of the fruits of righteousness which are through Jesus Christ to the glory and praise of God
Phl  Now it is my purpose to make clear to you brothers that the cause of the good news has been helped by my experiences
Phl  So that it became clear through all the Praetorium and to all the rest that I was a prisoner on account of Christ
Phl  And most of the brothers in the Lord taking heart because of my chains are all the stronger to give the word of God without fear
Phl  Though some are preaching Christ out of envy and competition others do it out of a good heart
Phl  These do it from love conscious that I am responsible for the cause of the good news
Phl  But those are preaching Christ in a spirit of competition not from their hearts but with the purpose of giving me pain in my prison
Phl  What then only that in every way falsely or truly the preaching of Christ goes on and in this I am glad and will be glad
Phl  For I am conscious that this will be for my salvation through your prayer and the giving out of the stored wealth of the Spirit of Jesus Christ
Phl  In the measure of my strong hope and belief that in nothing will I be put to shame but that without fear as at all times so now will Christ have glory in my body by life or by death
Phl  For to me life is Christ and death is profit
Phl  But if I go on living in the fleshif this is the fruit of my workthen I do not see what decision to make
Phl  I am in a hard position between the two having a desire to go away and be with Christ which is very much better
Phl  Still to go on in the flesh is more necessary because of you
Phl  And being certain of this I am conscious that I will go on yes and go on with you all for your growth and joy in the faith
Phl  So that your pride in me may be increased in Christ Jesus through my being present with you again
Phl  Only let your behaviour do credit to the good news of Christ so that if I come and see you or if I am away from you I may have news of you that you are strong in one spirit working together with one soul for the faith of the good news
Phl  Having no fear of those who are against you which is a clear sign of their destruction but of your salvation and that from God
Phl  Because to you it has been given in the cause of Christ not only to have faith in him but to undergo pain on his account
Phl  Fighting the same fight which you saw in me and now have word of in me
Phl  If then there is any comfort in Christ any help given by love any uniting of hearts in the Spirit any loving mercies and pity
Phl  Make my joy complete by being of the same mind having the same love being in harmony and of one mind
Phl  Doing nothing through envy or through pride but with low thoughts of self let everyone take others to be better than himself
Phl  Not looking everyone to his private good but keeping in mind the things of others
Phl  Let this mind be in you which was in Christ Jesus
Phl  To whom though himself in the form of God it did not seem that to take for oneself was to be like God
Phl  But he made himself as nothing taking the form of a servant being made like men
Phl  And being seen in form as a man he took the lowest place and let himself be put to death even the death of the cross
Phl  For this reason God has put him in the highest place and has given to him the name which is greater than every name
Phl  So that at the name of Jesus every knee may be bent of those in heaven and those on earth and those in the underworld
Phl  And that every tongue may give witness that Jesus Christ is Lord to the glory of God the Father
Phl  So then my loved ones as you have at all times done what I say not only when I am present but now much more when I am not with you give yourselves to working out your salvation with fear in your hearts
Phl  For it is God who is the cause of your desires and of your acts for his good pleasure
Phl  Do all things without protests and arguments
Phl  So that you may be holy and gentle children of God without sin in a twisted and foolish generation among whom you are seen as lights in the world
Phl  Offering the word of life so that I may have glory in you in the day of Christ because my running was not for nothing and my work was not without effect
Phl  And even if I am offered like a drink offering giving myself for the cause and work of your faith I am glad and have joy with you all
Phl  And in the same way do you be glad and have a part in my joy
Phl  But I am hoping in the Lord Jesus to send Timothy to you before long so that I may be comforted when I have news of you
Phl  For I have no man of like mind who will truly have care for you
Phl  For they all go after what is theirs not after the things of Christ
Phl  But his quality is clear to you how as a child is to its father so he was a help to me in the work of the good news
Phl  Him then I am hoping to send as quickly as possible when I am able to see how things will go for me
Phl  But I have faith in the Lord that I myself will come before long
Phl  But it seemed to me necessary to send to you Epaphroditus my brother who has taken part with me in the work and in the fight and your servant sent by you for help in my need
Phl  Because his heart was with you all and he was greatly troubled because you had news that he was ill
Phl  For in fact he was ill almost to death but God had mercy on him and not only on him but on me so that I might not have grief on grief
Phl  I have sent him then the more gladly so that when you see him again you may be happy and I may have the less sorrow
Phl  So take him to your hearts in the Lord with all joy and give honour to such as he is
Phl  Because for the work of Christ he was near to death putting his life in danger to make your care for me complete
Phl  For the rest my brothers be glad in the Lord Writing the same things to you is no trouble to me and for you it is safe
Phl  Be on the watch against dogs against the workers of evil against those of the circumcision
Phl  For we are the circumcision who give worship to God and have glory in Jesus Christ and have no faith in the flesh
Phl  Even though I myself might have faith in the flesh if any other man has reason to have faith in the flesh I have more
Phl  Being given circumcision on the eighth day of the nation of Israel of the tribe of Benjamin a Hebrew of Hebrews in relation to the law a Pharisee
Phl  In bitter hate I was cruel to the church I kept all the righteousness of the law to the last detail
Phl  But those things which were profit to me I gave up for Christ
Phl  Yes truly and I am ready to give up all things for the knowledge of Christ Jesus my Lord which is more than all for whom I have undergone the loss of all things and to me they are less than nothing so that I may have Christ as my reward
Phl  And be seen in him not having my righteousness which is of the law but that which is through faith in Christ the righteousness which is of God by faith
Phl  That I may have knowledge of him and of the power of his coming back from the dead and a part with him in his pains becoming like him in his death
Phl  If in any way I may have the reward of life from the dead
Phl  Not as if I had even now got the reward or been made complete but I go on in the hope that I may come to the knowledge of that for which I was made the servant of Christ Jesus
Phl  Brothers it is clear to me that I have not come to that knowledge but one thing I do letting go those things which are past and stretching out to the things which are before
Phl  I go forward to the mark even the reward of the high purpose of God in Christ Jesus
Phl  Then let us all who have come to full growth be of this mind and if in anything you are of a different mind even this will God make clear to you
Phl  Only as far as we have got let us be guided by the same rule
Phl  Brothers take me as your example and take note of those who are walking after the example we have given
Phl  For there are those of whom I have given you word before and do so now with sorrow who are haters of the cross of Christ
Phl  Whose end is destruction whose god is the stomach and whose glory is in their shame whose minds are fixed on the things of the earth
Phl  For our country is in heaven from where the Saviour for whom we are waiting will come even the Lord Jesus Christ
Phl  By whom this poor body of ours will be changed into the image of the body of his glory in the measure of the working by which he is able to put all things under himself
Phl  So my brothers well loved and very dear to me my joy and crown be strong in the Lord my loved ones
Phl  I make request to Euodias and Syntyche to be of the same mind in the Lord
Phl  And I make request to you true helper in my work to see to the needs of those women who took part with me in the good news with Clement and the rest of my brotherworkers whose names are in the book of life
Phl  Be glad in the Lord at all times again I say Be glad
Phl  Let your gentle behaviour be clear to all men The Lord is near
Phl  Have no cares but in everything with prayer and praise put your requests before God
Phl  And the peace of God which is deeper than all knowledge will keep your hearts and minds in Christ Jesus
Phl  For the rest my brothers whatever things are true whatever things have honour whatever things are upright whatever things are holy whatever things are beautiful whatever things are of value if there is any virtue and if there is any praise give thought to these things
Phl  The things which came to you by my teaching and preaching and which you saw in me these things do and the God of peace will be with you
Phl  But I am very glad in the Lord that your care for me has come to life again though you did in fact take thought for me but you were not able to give effect to it
Phl  But I will not say anything about my needs for I am able wherever I am to be dependent on myself
Phl  It is the same to me if I am looked down on or honoured everywhere and in all things I have the secret of how to be full and how to go without food how to have wealth and how to be in need
Phl  I am able to do all things through him who gives me strength
Phl  But you did well to have care for me in my need
Phl  And you have knowledge Philippians that when the good news first came to you when I went away from Macedonia no church took part with me in the business of giving to the saints but you only
Phl  Because even in Thessalonica you sent once and again to me in my need
Phl  Not that I am looking for an offering but for fruit which may be put to your credit
Phl  I have all things and more than enough I am made full having had from Epaphroditus the things which came from you a perfume of a sweet smell an offering well pleasing to God
Phl  And my God will give you all you have need of from the wealth of his glory in Christ Jesus
Phl  Now to God our Father be glory for ever and ever So be it
Phl  Give words of love to every saint in Christ Jesus The brothers who are with me send you their love
Phl  All the saints send their love to you specially those who are of Caesars house
Phl  The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit
Col  Paul an Apostle of Jesus Christ by the purpose of God and Timothy our brother
Col  To the saints and true brothers in Christ at Colossae Grace to you and peace from God our Father
Col  We give praise to God the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ making prayer for you at all times
Col  After hearing of your faith in Christ Jesus and of the love which you have for all the saints
Col  Through the hope which is in store for you in heaven knowledge of which was given to you before in the true word of the good news
Col  Which has come to you and which in all the world is giving fruit and increase as it has done in you from the day when it came to your ears and you had true knowledge of the grace of God
Col  As it was given to you by Epaphras our wellloved helper who is a true servant of Christ for us
Col  And who himself made clear to us your love in the Spirit
Col  For this reason we from the day when we had word of it keep on in prayer for you that you may be full of the knowledge of his purpose with all wisdom and experience of the Spirit
Col  Living uprightly in the approval of the Lord giving fruit in every good work and increasing in the knowledge of God
Col  Full of strength in the measure of the great power of his glory so that you may undergo all troubles with joy
Col  Giving praise to the Father who has given us a part in the heritage of the saints in light
Col  Who has made us free from the power of evil and given us a place in the kingdom of the Son of his love
Col  In whom we have our salvation the forgiveness of sins
Col  Who is the image of the unseen God coming into existence before all living things
Col  For by him all things were made in heaven and on earth things seen and things unseen authorities lords rulers and powers all things were made by him and for him
Col  He is before all things and in him all things have being
Col  And he is the head of the body the church the starting point of all things the first to come again from the dead so that in all things he might have the chief place
Col  For God in full measure was pleased to be in him
Col  Through him uniting all things with himself having made peace through the blood of his cross through him I say uniting all things which are on earth or in heaven
Col  And you who in the past were cut off and at war with God in your minds through evil works he has now made one
Col  In the body of his flesh through death so that you might be holy and without sin and free from all evil before him
Col  If you keep yourselves safely based in the faith not moved from the hope of the good news which came to you and which was given to every living being under heaven of which I Paul was made a servant
Col  Now I have joy in my pain because of you and in my flesh I undergo whatever is still needed to make the sorrows of Christ complete for the salvation of his body the church
Col  Of which I became a servant by the purpose of God which was given to me for you to give effect to the word of God
Col  The secret which has been kept from all times and generations but has now been made clear to his saints
Col  To whom God was pleased to give knowledge of the wealth of the glory of this secret among the Gentiles which is Christ in you the hope of glory
Col  Whom we are preaching guiding and teaching every man in all wisdom so that every man may be complete in Christ
Col  And for this purpose I am working using all my strength by the help of his power which is working in me strongly
Col  For it is my desire to give you news of the great fight I am making for you and for those at Laodicea and for all who have not seen my face in the flesh
Col  So that their hearts may be comforted and that being joined together in love they may come to the full wealth of the certain knowledge of the secret of God even Christ
Col  In whom are all the secret stores of wisdom and knowledge
Col  I say this so that you may not be turned away by any deceit of words
Col  For though I am not present in the flesh still I am with you in the spirit seeing with joy your order and your unchanging faith in Christ
Col  As then you took Christ Jesus the Lord so go on in him
Col  Rooted and based together in him strong in the faith which the teaching gave you giving praise to God at all times
Col  Take care that no one takes you away by force through mans wisdom and deceit going after the beliefs of men and the theories of the world and not after Christ
Col  For in him all the wealth of Gods being has a living form
Col  And you are complete in him who is the head of all rule and authority
Col  In whom you had a circumcision not made with hands in the putting off of the body of the flesh in the circumcision of Christ
Col  Having been put to death with him in baptism by which you came to life again with him through faith in the working of God who made him come back from the dead
Col  And you being dead through your sins and the evil condition of your flesh to you I say he gave life together with him and forgiveness of all our sins
Col  Having put an end to the handwriting of the law which was against us taking it out of the way by nailing it to his cross
Col  Having made himself free from the rule of authorities and powers he put them openly to shame glorying over them in it
Col  For this reason let no man be your judge in any question of food or drink or feast days or new moons or Sabbaths
Col  For these are an image of the things which are to come but the body is Christs
Col  Let no man take your reward from you by consciously making little of himself and giving worship to angels having his thoughts fixed on the things which he has seen being foolishly lifted up in his natural mind
Col  And not joined to the Head from whom all the body being given strength and kept together through its joins and bands has its growth with the increase of God
Col  If you were made free by your death with Christ from the rules of the world why do you put yourselves under the authority of orders
Col  Which say there may be no touching tasting or taking in your hands
Col  Rules which are all to come to an end with their use after the orders and teaching of men
Col  These things seem to have a sort of wisdom in selfordered worship and making little of oneself and being cruel to the body not honouring it by giving it its natural use
Col  If then you have a new life with Christ give your attention to the things of heaven where Christ is seated at the right hand of God
Col  Keep your mind on the higher things not on the things of earth
Col  For your life on earth is done and you have a secret life with Christ in God
Col  At the coming of Christ who is our life you will be seen with him in glory
Col  Then put to death your bodies which are of the earth wrong use of the flesh unclean things passion evil desires and envy which is the worship of strange gods
Col  Because of which the wrath of God comes on those who go against his orders
Col  Among whom you were living in the past when you did such things
Col  But now it is right for you to put away all these things wrath passion bad feeling curses unclean talk
Col  Do not make false statements to one another because you have put away the old man with all his doings
Col  And have put on the new man which has become new in knowledge after the image of his maker
Col  Where there is no Greek or Jew no one with circumcision or without circumcision no division between nations no servant or free man but Christ is all and in all
Col  As saints of God then holy and dearly loved let your behaviour be marked by pity and mercy kind feeling a low opinion of yourselves gentle ways and a power of undergoing all things
Col  Being gentle to one another and having forgiveness for one another if anyone has done wrong to his brother even as the Lord had forgiveness for you
Col  And more than all have love the only way in which you may be completely joined together
Col  And let the peace of Christ be ruling in your hearts as it was the purpose of God for you to be one body and give praise to God at all times
Col  Let the word of Christ be in you in all wealth of wisdom teaching and helping one another with songs of praise and holy words making melody to God with grace in your hearts
Col  And whatever you do in word or in act do all in the name of the Lord Jesus giving praise to God the Father through him
Col  Wives be under the authority of your husbands as is right in the Lord
Col  Husbands have love for your wives and be not bitter against them
Col  Children do the orders of your fathers and mothers in all things for this is pleasing to the Lord
Col  Fathers do not be hard on your children so that their spirit may not be broken
Col  Servants in all things do the orders of your natural masters not only when their eyes are on you as pleasers of men but with all your heart fearing the Lord
Col  Whatever you do do it readily as to the Lord and not to men
Col  Being certain that the Lord will give you the reward of the heritage for you are the servants of the Lord Christ
Col  For the wrongdoer will have punishment for the wrong he has done without respect for any mans position
Col  Masters give your servants what is right and equal conscious that you have a Master in heaven
Col  Give yourselves to prayer at all times keeping watch with praise
Col  And making prayer for us that God may give us an open door for the preaching of the word the secret of Christ for which I am now in chains
Col  So that I may make it clear as it is right for me to do
Col  Be wise in your behaviour to those who are outside making good use of the time
Col  Let your talk be with grace mixed with salt so that you may be able to give an answer to everyone
Col  Tychicus will give you news of all my business he is a dear brother and true servant and helper in the word
Col  And I have sent him to you for this very purpose so that you may have news of how we are and so that he may give your hearts comfort
Col  And with him I have sent Onesimus the true and wellloved brother who is one of you They will give you word of everything which is taking place here
Col  Aristarchus my brotherprisoner sends his love to you and Mark a relation of Barnabas about whom you have been given orders if he comes to you be kind to him
Col  And Jesus whose other name is Justus these are of the circumcision they are my only brotherworkers for the kingdom of God who have been a comfort to me
Col  Epaphras who is one of you a servant of Christ Jesus sends you his love ever taking thought for you in his prayers that you may be complete and fully certain of all the purpose of God
Col  For I give witness of him that he has undergone much trouble for you and for those in Laodicea and in Hierapolis
Col  Luke our wellloved medical friend and Demas send you their love
Col  Give my love to the brothers in Laodicea and to Nymphas and the church in their house
Col  And when this letter has been made public among you let the same be done in the church of Laodicea and see that you have the letter from Laodicea
Col  Say to Archippus See that you do the work which the Lord has given you to do
Col  I Paul give you this word of love in my handwriting Keep in memory that I am a prisoner Grace be with you
Ts  Paul and Silvanus and Timothy to the church of the Thessalonians in God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ Grace to you and peace
Ts  We give praise to God at all times for you keeping you in memory in our prayers
Ts  Having ever in mind your work of faith and acts of love and the strength of your hope in our Lord Jesus Christ before our God and Father
Ts  Being conscious my brothers dear to God that you have been marked out by Gods purpose
Ts  Because our good news came to you not in word only but in power and in the Holy Spirit so that you were completely certain of it even as you saw what our behaviour to you was like from our love to you
Ts  And you took us and the Lord as your example after the word had come to you in much trouble with joy in the Holy Spirit
Ts  So that you became an example to all those who have faith in Christ in Macedonia and Achaia
Ts  For not only was the word of the Lord sounding out from you in Macedonia and Achaia but in every place your faith in God is made clear so that we have no need to say anything
Ts  For they themselves give the news of how we came among you and how you were turned from images to God to the worship of a true and living God
Ts  Waiting for his Son from heaven who came back from the dead even Jesus our Saviour from the wrath to come
Ts  For you yourselves brothers are conscious that our coming among you was not without effect
Ts  But after we had first undergone much pain and been cruelly attacked as you saw at Philippi by the help of God we gave you the good news without fear though everything was against us
Ts  For our witness does not come from error or from an unclean heart or from deceit
Ts  But even as the good news was given to us by the approval of God so we give it out not as pleasing men but God by whom our hearts are tested
Ts  For it is common knowledge among you that we never made use of smoothsounding false words and God is witness that at no time were we secretly desiring profit for ourselves
Ts  Or looking for glory from men from you or from others when we might have made ourselves a care to you as Apostles of Christ
Ts  But we were gentle among you like a woman caring for her little ones
Ts  Even so being full of loving desire for you we took delight in giving you not only Gods good news but even our lives because you were dear to us
Ts  For you have the memory my brothers of our trouble and care how working night and day so that we might not be a trouble to any of you we gave you the good news of God
Ts  You are witnesses with God how holy and upright and free from all evil was our way of life among you who have faith
Ts  Even as you saw how like a father with his children we were teaching and comforting you all and giving witness
Ts  So that your lives might be pleasing to God who has given you a part in his kingdom and his glory
Ts  And for this cause we still give praise to God that when the word came to your ears through us you took it not as the word of man but as it truly is the word of God which has living power in you who have faith
Ts  For you my brothers took as your examples the churches of God which are in Judaea in Christ Jesus because you underwent the same things from your countrymen as they did from the Jews
Ts  Who put to death the Lord Jesus and the prophets violently driving us out who are unpleasing to God and against all men
Ts  Who to make the measure of their sins complete kept us from giving the word of salvation to the Gentiles but the wrath of God is about to come on them in the fullest degree
Ts  But we my brothers being away from you for a short time in body but not in heart had all the more desire to see your face
Ts  For which reason we made attempts to come to you even I Paul once and again but Satan kept us from coming
Ts  For what is our hope or joy or crown of glory Are not even you before our Lord Jesus at his coming
Ts  For you are our glory and our joy
Ts  At last our desire to have news of you was so strong that while we ourselves were waiting at Athens
Ts  We sent Timothy our brother and Gods servant in the good news of Christ to give you strength and comfort in your faith
Ts  So that no man might be moved by these troubles because you see that these things are part of Gods purpose for us
Ts  And when we were with you we said to you that trouble was before us and so it came about as you see
Ts  For this reason when I was no longer able to keep quiet I sent to get news of your faith fearing that you might be tested by the Evil One and that our work might come to nothing
Ts  But now that Timothy has come to us from you and has given us good news of your faith and love and that you have happy memories of us desiring greatly to see us even as we do to see you
Ts  For this cause brothers in all our trouble and grief we were comforted about you because of your faith
Ts  For it is life to us if you keep your faith in the Lord unchanged
Ts  For how great is the praise which we give to God for you and how great the joy with which we are glad because of you before our God
Ts  Night and day requesting God again and again that we may see your face and make your faith complete
Ts  Now may our God and Father himself and our Lord Jesus make a way for us to come to you
Ts  And the Lord give you increase of love in fullest measure to one another and to all men even as our love to you
Ts  So that your hearts may be strong and free from all sin before our God and Father at the coming of our Lord Jesus with all his saints
Ts  And last of all the prayer which we make to you from our heart and in the name of the Lord Jesus is this that as we made clear to you what sort of behaviour is pleasing to God as in fact you are doing now so you will go on in these ways but more and more
Ts  Because you have in mind the orders we gave you through the Lord Jesus
Ts  For the purpose of God for you is this that you may be holy and may keep yourselves from the desires of the flesh
Ts  So that every one of you may keep his body holy and in honour
Ts  Not in the passion of evil desires like the Gentiles who have no knowledge of God
Ts  And that no man may make attempts to get the better of his brother in business for the Lord is the judge in all these things as we said to you before and gave witness
Ts  Because it is Gods purpose that our way of life may be not unclean but holy
Ts  Whoever then goes against this word goes against not man but God who gives his Holy Spirit to you
Ts  But about loving the brothers there is no need for me to say anything to you in this letter for you have the teaching of God that love for one another is right and necessary
Ts  And truly you are lovers of all the brothers in Macedonia but it is our desire that your love may be increased still more
Ts  And that you may take pride in being quiet and doing your business working with your hands as we gave you orders
Ts  That you may be respected by those who are outside and may have need of nothing
Ts  But it is our desire brothers that you may be certain about those who are sleeping so that you may have no need for sorrow as others have who are without hope
Ts  For if we have faith that Jesus underwent death and came back again even so those who are sleeping will come again with him by Gods power
Ts  For this we say to you by the word of the Lord that we who are still living at the coming of the Lord will not go before those who are sleeping
Ts  Because the Lord himself will come down from heaven with a word of authority with the voice of the chief angel with the sound of a horn and the dead in Christ will come to life first
Ts  Then we who are still living will be taken up together with them into the clouds to see the Lord in the air and so will we be for ever with the Lord
Ts  So then give comfort to one another with these words
Ts  But about the times and their order my brothers there is no need for me to say anything to you
Ts  For you yourselves have the knowledge that the day of the Lord will come like a thief in the night
Ts  When they say There is peace and no danger then sudden destruction will come on them as birthpains on a woman with child and they will not be able to get away from it
Ts  But you my brothers are not in the dark for that day to overtake you like a thief
Ts  For you are all sons of light and of the day we are not of the night or of the dark
Ts  So then let us not take our rest as the others do but let us be selfcontrolled and awake
Ts  For those who are sleeping do so in the night and those who are the worse for drink are so in the night
Ts  But let us who are of the day be serious putting on the breastplate of faith and love and on our heads the hope of salvation
Ts  For Gods purpose for us is not wrath but salvation through our Lord Jesus Christ
Ts  Who was put to death for us so that awake or sleeping we may have a part in his life
Ts  So then go on comforting and building up one another as you have been doing
Ts  But we make this request to you my brothers give attention to those who are working among you who are over you in the Lord to keep order among you
Ts  And have a high opinion of them in love because of their work Be at peace among yourselves
Ts  And our desire is that you will keep control over those whose lives are not well ordered giving comfort to the feeblehearted supporting those with little strength and putting up with much from all
Ts  Let no one give evil for evil but ever go after what is good for one another and for all
Ts  Have joy at all times
Ts  Keep on with your prayers
Ts  In everything give praise for this is the purpose of God in Christ Jesus for you
Ts  Do not put out the light of the Spirit
Ts  Do not make little of the words of the prophets
Ts  Let all things be tested keep to what is good
Ts  Keep from every form of evil
Ts  And may the God of peace himself make you holy in every way and may your spirit and soul and body be free from all sin at the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ
Ts  God by whom you have been marked out in his purpose is unchanging and will make it complete
Ts  Brothers keep us in mind in your prayers
Ts  Give all the brothers a holy kiss
Ts  I give orders in the name of the Lord that all the brothers are to be present at the reading of this letter
Ts  The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you
Ts  Paul and Silvanus and Timothy to the church of the Thessalonians in God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Ts  Grace to you and peace from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Ts  It is right for us to give praise to God at all times for you brothers because of the great increase of your faith and the wealth of your love for one another
Ts  So that we ourselves take pride in you in the churches of God for your untroubled mind and your faith in all the troubles and sorrows which you are going through
Ts  Which is a clear sign of the decision which God in his righteousness has made to give you a part in his kingdom for which you have undergone this pain
Ts  For it is an act of righteousness on Gods part to give trouble as their reward to those who are troubling you
Ts  And to you who are troubled rest with us when the Lord Jesus comes from heaven with the angels of his power in flames of fire
Ts  To give punishment to those who have no knowledge of God and to those who do not give ear to the good news of our Lord Jesus
Ts  Whose reward will be eternal destruction from the face of the Lord and from the glory of his strength
Ts  At his coming when he will have glory in his saints and will be a cause of wonder in all those who had faith because our witness among you had effect in that day
Ts  For this reason you are ever in our prayers that you may seem to our God such as may have a part in his purpose and that by his power he will make all his good purpose and the work of faith complete
Ts  So that glory may be given to the name of our Lord Jesus through you and you may have glory in him by the grace of our God and the Lord Jesus Christ
Ts  Now as to the coming of the Lord Jesus Christ and our meeting with him it is our desire my brothers
Ts  That you may not be moved in mind or troubled by a spirit or by a word or by a letter as from us with the suggestion that the day of the Lord is even now come
Ts  Give no belief to false words because there will first be a falling away from the faith and the revelation of the man of sin the son of destruction
Ts  Who puts himself against all authority lifting himself up over all which is named God or is given worship so that he takes his seat in the Temple of God putting himself forward as God
Ts  Have you no memory of what I said when I was with you giving you word of these things
Ts  And now it is clear to you what is keeping back his revelation till the time comes for him to be seen
Ts  For the secret of evil is even now at work but there is one who is keeping back the evil till he is taken out of the way
Ts  And then will come the revelation of that evil one whom the Lord Jesus will put to death with the breath of his mouth and give to destruction by the revelation of his coming
Ts  Even the one whose coming is marked by the working of Satan with all power and signs and false wonders
Ts  And with every deceit of wrongdoing among those whose fate is destruction because they were quite without that love of the true faith by which they might have salvation
Ts  And for this cause God will give them up to the power of deceit and they will put their faith in what is false
Ts  So that they all may be judged who had no faith in what is true but took pleasure in evil
Ts  But it is right for us to give praise to God at all times for you brothers loved by the Lord because it was the purpose of God from the first that you might have salvation being made holy by the Spirit and by faith in what is true
Ts  And in this purpose he gave you a part through the good news of which we were the preachers even that you might have part in the glory of our Lord Jesus Christ
Ts  So then brothers be strong in purpose and keep the teaching which has been given to you by word or by letter from us
Ts  Now our Lord Jesus Christ himself and God our Father who had love for us and has given us eternal comfort and good hope through grace
Ts  Give you comfort and strength in every good work and word
Ts  For the rest my brothers let there be prayer for us that the word of the Lord may go forward with increasing glory even as it does with you
Ts  And that we may be made free from foolish and evil men for not all have faith
Ts  But the Lord is true who will give you strength and keep you safe from evil
Ts  And we have faith in the Lord about you that you are doing and will do the things about which we give you orders
Ts  And may your hearts be guided by the Lord into the love of God and quiet waiting for Christ
Ts  Now we give you orders brothers in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ to keep away from all those whose behaviour is not well ordered and in harmony with the teaching which they had from us
Ts  For you yourselves are used to taking us as your example because our life among you was ruled by order
Ts  And we did not take food from any man for nothing but were working hard night and day not to be a trouble to any of you
Ts  Not because we have not the right but to make ourselves an example to you so that you might do the same
Ts  For even when we were with you we gave you orders saying If any man does no work let him not have food
Ts  For it has come to our ears that there are some among you whose behaviour is uncontrolled who do no work at all but are overinterested in the business of others
Ts  Now to such we give orders and make request in the Lord Jesus that working quietly they get their living
Ts  And you my brothers do not get tired of welldoing
Ts  And if any man does not give attention to what we have said in this letter take note of that man and keep away from him so that he may be shamed
Ts  Have no feeling of hate for him but take him in hand seriously as a brother
Ts  Now the Lord of peace himself give you peace at all times and in every way May the Lord be with you all
Ts  These words of love to you at the end are in my writing Pauls writing and this is the mark of every letter from me
Ts  May the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all
Ti  Paul an Apostle of Jesus Christ by the order of God our Saviour and Christ Jesus our hope
Ti  To Timothy my true child in the faith Grace mercy peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord
Ti  It was my desire when I went on into Macedonia that you might make a stop at Ephesus to give orders to certain men not to put forward a different teaching
Ti  Or to give attention to stories and long lists of generations from which come questionings and doubts in place of Gods ordered way of life which is in faith
Ti  But the effect of the order is love coming from a clean heart and a knowledge of what is right and true faith
Ti  From which some have been turned away giving themselves to foolish talking
Ti  Desiring to be teachers of the law though they have no knowledge of what they say or of the statements which they make so certainly
Ti  We are conscious that the law is good if a man makes a right use of it
Ti  With the knowledge that the law is made not for the upright man but for those who have no respect for law and order for evil men and sinners for the unholy and those who have no religion for those who put their fathers or mothers to death for takers of life
Ti  For those who go after loose women for those with unnatural desires for those who take men prisoners who make false statements and false oaths and those who do any other things against the right teaching
Ti  Which may be seen in the good news of the glory of the great God which was given into my care
Ti  I give praise to him who gave me power Christ Jesus our Lord because he took me to be true making me his servant
Ti  Though I had said violent words against God and done cruel acts causing great trouble but I was given mercy because I did it without knowledge not having faith
Ti  And the grace of our Lord was very great with faith and love which is in Christ Jesus
Ti  It is a true saying in which all may put their faith that Christ Jesus came into the world to give salvation to sinners of whom I am the chief
Ti  But for this reason I was given mercy so that in me the chief of sinners Jesus Christ might make clear all his mercy as an example to those who in the future would have faith in him to eternal life
Ti  Now to the King eternal everliving unseen the only God be honour and glory for ever and ever So be it
Ti  This order I give to you Timothy my son in harmony with the words of the prophets about you so that by them you may be strong fighting the good fight
Ti  Keeping faith and being conscious of welldoing for some by not doing these things have gone wrong in relation to the faith
Ti  Such are Hymenaeus and Alexander whom I have given up to Satan so that they may say no more evil words against God
Ti  My desire is first of all that you will make requests and prayers and give praise for all men
Ti  For kings and all those in authority so that we may have a calm and quiet life in all fear of God and serious behaviour
Ti  This is good and pleasing in the eyes of God our Saviour
Ti  Whose desire is that all men may have salvation and come to the knowledge of what is true
Ti  For there is one God and one peacemaker between God and men the man Christ Jesus
Ti  Who gave himself as an offering for all witness of which was to be given at the right time
Ti  And of this I became a preacher and an Apostle what I say is true not false and a teacher of the Gentiles in the true faith
Ti  It is my desire then that in every place men may give themselves to prayer lifting up holy hands without wrath or argument
Ti  And that women may be dressed in simple clothing with a quiet and serious air not with twisted hair and gold or jewels or robes of great price
Ti  But clothed with good works as is right for women who are living in the fear of God
Ti  Let a woman quietly take the place of a learner and be under authority
Ti  In my opinion it is right for a woman not to be a teacher or to have rule over a man but to be quiet
Ti  For Adam was first formed then Eve
Ti  And Adam was not taken by deceit but the woman being tricked became a wrongdoer
Ti  But if they go on in faith and love and holy selfcontrol she will be kept safe at the time of childbirth
Ti  This is a true saying A man desiring the position of a Bishop has a desire for a good work
Ti  The Bishop then is to be a man of good name the husband of one wife selfcontrolled seriousminded having respect for order opening his house freely to guests a ready teacher
Ti  Not quickly moved to wrath or blows but gentle no fighter no lover of money
Ti  Ruling his house well having his children under control with all serious behaviour
Ti  For if a man has not the art of ruling his house how will he take care of the church of God
Ti  Not one newly taken into the church for fear that through his high opinion of himself he may come into the same sin as the Evil One
Ti  And he is to have a good name among those outside the church so that nothing may be said against him and he may not be taken by the designs of the Evil One
Ti  Deacons in the same way are to be serious in their behaviour not false in word not given to taking much wine or greatly desiring the wealth of this world
Ti  Keeping the secret of the faith in a heart free from sin
Ti  And let these first be put to the test then let them become Deacons if there is nothing against them
Ti  Women are to be serious in behaviour saying no evil of others controlling themselves true in all things
Ti  Let Deacons be husbands of one wife ruling their children and their houses well
Ti  For those who have done good work as Deacons get for themselves a good position and become free from fear in the faith which is in Christ Jesus
Ti  I am writing these things to you though I am hoping to come to you before long
Ti  But if I am long in coming this will make clear to you what behaviour is right for men in the house of God which is the church of the living God the pillar and base of what is true
Ti  And without argument great is the secret of religion He who was seen in the flesh who was given Gods approval in the spirit was seen by the angels of whom the good news was given among the nations in whom the world had faith who was taken up in glory
Ti  But the Spirit says clearly that in later times some will be turned away from the faith giving their minds to spirits of deceit and the teachings of evil spirits
Ti  Through the false ways of men whose words are untrue whose hearts are burned as with a heated iron
Ti  Who keep men from being married and from taking food which God made to be taken with praise by those who have faith and true knowledge
Ti  Because everything which God has made is good and nothing is evil if it is taken with praise
Ti  For it is made holy by the word of God and by prayer
Ti  If you keep these things before the minds of the brothers you will be a good servant of Christ Jesus trained in the words of the faith and of the right teaching which has been your guide
Ti  But have nothing to do with unclean and foolish stories Give yourself training in religion
Ti  For the training of the body is of profit for a little but religion is of profit in every way giving hope for the life which now is and for that which is to come
Ti  This is a true saying in which all may put their faith
Ti  And this is the purpose of all our work and our fighting because our hope is in the living God who is the Saviour of all men and specially of those who have faith
Ti  Let these be your orders and your teaching
Ti  Let no one make little of you because you are young but be an example to the church in word in behaviour in love in faith in holy living
Ti  Till I come give attention to the reading of the holy Writings to comforting the saints and to teaching
Ti  Make use of that grace in you which was given to you by the word of the prophets when the rulers of the church put their hands on you
Ti  Have a care for these things give yourself to them with all your heart so that all may see how you go forward
Ti  Give attention to yourself and your teaching Go on in these things for in doing so you will get salvation for yourself and for those who give hearing to you
Ti  Do not say sharp words to one who has authority in the church but let your talk be as to a father and to the younger men as to brothers
Ti  To the older women as to mothers to the younger as to sisters with a clean heart
Ti  Give honour to widows who are truly widows
Ti  But if any widow has children or childrens children let these see that it is right to take care of their family and their fathers and mothers for this is pleasing in the eyes of God
Ti  Now she who is truly a widow and without family puts her hope in God giving herself to prayer day and night
Ti  But she who gives herself to pleasure is dead while she is living
Ti  Give orders to this effect so that no evil may be said of anyone
Ti  If anyone has no care for his family and those in his house he is false to the faith and is worse than one who has no faith
Ti  Let no woman be numbered among the widows who is under sixty years old and only if she has been the wife of one man
Ti  And if witness is given of her good works if she has had the care of children if she has been kind to travellers washing the feet of the saints helping those who are in trouble giving herself to good works
Ti  But to the younger widows say No for when their love is turned away from Christ they have a desire to be married
Ti  And they are judged because they have been false to their first faith
Ti  And they get into the way of doing no work going about from house to house and not only doing no work but talking foolishly being overinterested in the business of others saying things which they have no right to say
Ti  So it is my desire that the younger widows may be married and have children controlling their families and giving the Evil One no chance to say anything against them
Ti  For even now some are turned away to Satan
Ti  If any woman of the faith has relations who are widows let her give them help so that the care of them does not come on the church and so it may give help to those who are truly widowed
Ti  Let rulers whose rule is good be honoured twice over specially those whose work is preaching and teaching
Ti  For the Writings say It is not right to keep the ox from taking the grain when he is crushing it And The worker has a right to his reward
Ti  Do not take as true any statement made against one in authority but only if two or three give witness to it
Ti  Say sharp words to sinners when all are present so that the rest may be in fear
Ti  I give you orders before God and Christ Jesus and the angels of Gods selection to keep these orders without giving thought to one side more than another
Ti  Do not put hands on any man without thought and have no part in other mens sins keep yourself clean
Ti  Do not take only water as your drink but take a little wine for the good of your stomach and because you are frequently ill
Ti  The sins of some men are clearly seen going before them to be judged but with others their sins go after them
Ti  In the same way there are good works which are clearly seen and those which are not so may not be kept secret
Ti  Let all who are servants under the yoke give all honour to their masters so that no evil may be said against the name of God and his teaching
Ti  And let those whose masters are of the faith have respect for them because they are brothers working for them the more readily because those who take part in the good work are of the faith and are dear Give orders and teaching about these things
Ti  If any man gives different teaching not in agreement with the true words of our Lord Jesus Christ and with the teaching which is in agreement with true religion
Ti  He has an overhigh opinion of himself being without knowledge having only an unhealthy love of questionings and wars of words from which come envy fighting cruel words evil thoughts
Ti  Bitter talk of men who being evil in mind and dead to what is true take the faith to be a way of making profit
Ti  But true faith with peace of mind is of great profit
Ti  For we came into the world with nothing and we are not able to take anything out
Ti  But if we have food and a roof over us let that be enough
Ti  But those who have a desire for wealth are falling into danger and are taken as in a net by a number of foolish and damaging desires through which men are overtaken by death and destruction
Ti  For the love of money is a root of all evil and some whose hearts were fixed on it have been turned away from the faith and been wounded with unnumbered sorrows
Ti  But you O man of God keep yourself from these things and go after righteousness religion faith love a quiet mind gentle behaviour
Ti  Be fighting the good fight of the faith take for yourself the life eternal for which you were marked out and of which you gave witness in the eyes of all
Ti  I give you orders before God the giver of life and Christ Jesus who before Pontius Pilate gave witness to the faith
Ti  To keep the word untouched by evil clear from all shame till the revelation of our Lord Jesus Christ
Ti  Which at the right time he will make clear who is the eternal and only Ruler King of kings and Lord of lords
Ti  Who only has life for ever living in light to which no man may come near whom no man has seen or is able to see to whom be honour and power for ever So be it
Ti  Give orders to those who have money and goods in this life not to be lifted up in their minds or to put their hope in the uncertain chances of wealth but in God who gives us in full measure all things for our use
Ti  And to do good having wealth in good works being quick to give taking part with one another
Ti  Making ready for themselves a safe place for the time to come so that the true life may be theirs
Ti  O Timothy take good care of that which is given to you turning away from the wrong and foolish talk and arguments of that knowledge which is falsely so named
Ti  Through which some who gave their minds to it have been turned away from the faith Grace be with you
Ti  Paul an Apostle of Jesus Christ by the purpose of God in the hope of the life which is in Christ Jesus
Ti  To Timothy my wellloved child Grace mercy peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord
Ti  I give praise to God whose servant I have been with a heart free from sin from the time of my fathers because in my prayers at all times the thought of you is with me night and day
Ti  Desiring to see you keeping in my memory your weeping so that I may be full of joy
Ti  Having in mind your true faith which first was in your mothers mother Lois and in your mother Eunice and I am certain is now in you
Ti  For this reason I say to you Let that grace of God which is in you given to you by my hands have living power
Ti  For God did not give us a spirit of fear but of power and of love and of selfcontrol
Ti  Have no feeling of shame then for the witness of our Lord or for me his prisoner but undergo all things for the good news in the measure of the power of God
Ti  Who gave us salvation marking us out for his purpose not on account of our works but in the measure of his purpose and his grace which was given to us in Christ Jesus before times eternal
Ti  But has now been made clear by the revelation of our Saviour Christ Jesus who put an end to death and made life unending come to light through the good news
Ti  Of which I was made a preacher and an Apostle and a teacher
Ti  And for which I undergo these things but I have no feeling of shame For I have knowledge of him in whom I have faith and I am certain that he is able to keep that which I have given into his care till that day
Ti  Keep the form of those true words which you had from me in faith and love which is in Christ Jesus
Ti  That good thing which was given to you keep safe through the Holy Spirit which is in us
Ti  You have had news that all those in Asia went away from me among whom are Phygelus and Hermogenes
Ti  May the Lord give mercy to the house of Onesiphorus because he frequently gave me help and had no feeling of shame because I was in chains
Ti  But when he was in Rome he went in search of me everywhere and came to me
Ti  May he have the Lords mercy in that day and of all he did for me at Ephesus you have full knowledge
Ti  So then my child be strong in the grace which is in Christ Jesus
Ti  And the things which I have said to you before a number of witnesses give to those of the faith so that they may be teachers of others
Ti  Be ready to do without the comforts of life as one of the army of Christ Jesus
Ti  A fighting man when he is with the army keeps himself free from the business of this life so that he may be pleasing to him who has taken him into his army
Ti  And if a man takes part in a competition he does not get the crown if he has not kept the rules
Ti  It is right for the worker in the fields to be the first to take of the fruit
Ti  Give thought to what I say for the Lord will give you wisdom in all things
Ti  Keep in mind Jesus Christ of the seed of David who came back from the dead as my good news gives witness
Ti  In which I put up with the hardest conditions even prison chains like one who has done a crime but the word of God is not in chains
Ti  But I undergo all things for the saints so that they may have salvation in Christ Jesus with eternal glory
Ti  This is a true saying If we undergo death with him then will we be living with him
Ti  If we go on to the end then we will be ruling with him if we say we have no knowledge of him then he will say he has no knowledge of us
Ti  If we are without faith still he keeps faith for he will never be untrue to himself
Ti  Put these things before them giving them orders in the name of the Lord to keep themselves from fighting about words which is of no profit only causing error in their hearers
Ti  Let it be your care to get the approval of God as a workman who has no cause for shame giving the true word in the right way
Ti  But take no part in wrong and foolish talk for those who do so will go farther into evil
Ti  And their words will be like poisoned wounds in the flesh such are Hymenaeus and Philetus
Ti  Men whose ideas are all false who say that the coming back from the dead has even now taken place overturning the faith of some
Ti  But Gods strong base is unchanging having this sign The Lord has knowledge of those who are his and Let everyone by whom the name of the Lord is named be turned away from evil
Ti  Now in a great house there are not only vessels of gold and silver but others of wood and earth and some which are honoured and some without honour
Ti  If a man makes himself clean from these he will be a vessel for honour made holy ready for the masters use ready for every good work
Ti  But keep yourself from those desires of the flesh which are strong when the body is young and go after righteousness faith love peace with those whose prayers go up to the Lord from a clean heart
Ti  And put away foolish and uncontrolled questionings seeing that they are a cause of trouble
Ti  For it is not right for the Lords servant to make trouble but he is to be gentle to all ready in teaching putting up with wrong
Ti  Gently guiding those who go against the teaching if by chance God may give them a change of heart and true knowledge
Ti  And so they may get themselves free from the net of the Evil One being made the prisoners of the Lords servant for the purpose of God
Ti  But be certain of this that in the last days times of trouble will come
Ti  For men will be lovers of self lovers of money uplifted in pride given to bitter words going against the authority of their fathers never giving praise having no religion
Ti  Without natural love bitter haters saying evil of others violent and uncontrolled hating all good
Ti  False to their friends acting without thought lifted up in mind loving pleasure more than God
Ti  Having a form of religion but turning their backs on the power of it go not with these
Ti  For these are they who go secretly into houses making prisoners of foolish women weighted down with sin turned from the way by their evil desires
Ti  Ever learning and never coming to the knowledge of what is true
Ti  And as James and Jambres went against Moses so do these go against what is true men of evil minds who tested by faith are seen to be false
Ti  But they will go no farther for their foolish behaviour will be clear to all men as theirs was in the end
Ti  But you took as your example my teaching behaviour purpose and faith my long waiting my love my quiet undergoing of trouble
Ti  My punishments and pain the things which came to me at Antioch at Iconium at Lystra the cruel attacks made on me and the Lord made me free from them all
Ti  Yes and all whose purpose is to be living in the knowledge of God in Christ Jesus will be cruelly attacked
