Ti  Evil and false men will become worse and worse using deceit and themselves overcome by deceit
Ti  But see that you keep to the teaching you have been given and the things of which you are certain conscious of who has been your teacher
Ti  And that from the time when you were a child you have had knowledge of the holy Writings which are able to make you wise to salvation through faith in Christ Jesus
Ti  Every holy Writing which comes from God is of profit for teaching for training for guiding for education in righteousness
Ti  So that the man of God may be complete trained and made ready for every good work
Ti  I give you orders before God and Christ Jesus who will be the judge of the living and the dead and by his revelation and his kingdom
Ti  Be preaching the word at all times in every place make protests say sharp words give comfort with long waiting and teaching
Ti  For the time will come when they will not take the true teaching but moved by their desires they will get for themselves a great number of teachers for the pleasure of hearing them
Ti  And shutting their ears to what is true will be turned away to belief in foolish stories
Ti  But be selfcontrolled in all things do without comfort go on preaching the good news completing the work which has been given you to do
Ti  For I am even now being offered and my end is near
Ti  I have made a good fight I have come to the end of my journey I have kept the faith
Ti  From now on the crown of righteousness is made ready for me which the Lord the upright judge Will give to me at that day and not only to me but to all those who have had love for his revelation
Ti  Do your best to come to me before long
Ti  For Demas has gone away from me for love of this present life and has gone to Thessalonica Crescens has gone to Galatia Titus to Dalmatia
Ti  Only Luke is with me Get Mark and take him with you for he is of use to me in the work
Ti  Tychicus I sent to Ephesus
Ti  The coat which I did not take from Troas and which is with Carpus get when you come and the books specially the papers
Ti  Alexander the copperworker did me much wrong the Lord will give him the reward of his works
Ti  But be on the watch for him for he was violent in his attacks on our teaching
Ti  At my first meeting with my judges no one took my part but all went away from me May it not be put to their account
Ti  But the Lord was by my side and gave me strength so that through me the news might be given out in full measure and all the Gentiles might give ear and I was taken out of the mouth of the lion
Ti  The Lord will keep me safe from every evil work and will give me salvation in his kingdom in heaven to whom be glory for ever and ever So be it
Ti  Give my love to Prisca and Aquila and those of the house of Onesiphorus
Ti  Erastus was stopping at Corinth but Trophimus when I last saw him was at Miletus ill
Ti  Do your best to come before the winter Eubulus sends you his love and Pudens and Linus and Claudia and all the brothers
Ti  The Lord be with your spirit Grace be with you
Tit  Paul a servant of God and an Apostle of Jesus Christ in agreement with the faith of the saints of God and the full knowledge of what is true in harmony with religion
Tit  In the hope of eternal life which was made certain before eternal time by the word of God who is ever true
Tit  Who in his time made clear his word in the good news of which by the order of God our Saviour I became a preacher
Tit  To Titus my true child in our common faith Grace and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Saviour
Tit  I did not take you with me when I went away from Crete so that you might do what was necessary to put things in order there placing men in authority over the churches in every town as I said to you
Tit  Men having a good record husbands of one wife whose children are of the faith children of whom it may not be said that they are given to loose living or are uncontrolled
Tit  For it is necessary for a Bishop to be a man of virtue as Gods servant not pushing himself forward not quickly moved to wrath or blows not desiring profit for himself
Tit  But opening his house freely to guests a lover of what is good seriousminded upright holy selfcontrolled
Tit  Keeping to the true word of the teaching so that he may be able to give comfort by right teaching and overcome the arguments of the doubters
Tit  For there are men who are not ruled by law foolish talkers false teachers specially those of the circumcision
Tit  By whom some families have been completely overturned who take money for teaching things which are not right these will have to be stopped
Tit  One of their prophets has said The men of Crete are ever false evil beasts lovers of food hating work
Tit  This witness is true So say sharp words to them so that they may come to the right faith
Tit  Giving no attention to the fictions of the Jews and the rules of men who have no true knowledge
Tit  To the clean in heart all things are clean but to those who are unclean and without faith nothing is clean they become unclean in mind and in thought
Tit  They say that they have knowledge of God while by their acts they are turning their backs on him they are hated by all hardhearted and judged to be without value for any good work
Tit  But let your words be in agreement with true and right teaching
Tit  That old men are to be simple in their tastes serious wise true in faith in love and of a quiet mind
Tit  That old women are to be selfrespecting in behaviour not saying evil of others not given to taking much wine teachers of that which is good
Tit  Training the younger women to have love for their husbands and children
Tit  To be wise in mind clean in heart kind working in their houses living under the authority of their husbands so that no evil may be said of the word of God
Tit  To the young men give orders to be wise and seriousminded
Tit  In all things see that you are an example of good works holy in your teaching serious in behaviour
Tit  Saying true and right words against which no protest may be made so that he who is not on our side may be put to shame unable to say any evil of us
Tit  Servants are to be under the authority of their masters pleasing them in all things without argument
Tit  Not taking what is not theirs but giving clear signs of their good faith in all things doing credit to the teaching of God our Saviour
Tit  For the grace of God has come giving salvation to all men
Tit  Training us so that turning away from evil and the desires of this world we may be living wisely and uprightly in the knowledge of God in this present life
Tit  Looking for the glad hope the revelation of the glory of our great God and Saviour Jesus Christ
Tit  Who gave himself for us so that he might make us free from all wrongdoing and make for himself a people clean in heart and on fire with good works
Tit  On all these points give teaching and help and make clear what is right with all authority Let all men give you honour
Tit  Make clear to them that they are to put themselves under rulers and authorities to do what they are ordered to be ready for every good work
Tit  To say no evil of any man not to be fighters to give way to others to be gentle in behaviour to all men
Tit  For in the past we were foolish hard in heart turned from the true way servants of evil desires and pleasures living in bad feeling and envy hated and hating one another
Tit  But when the mercy of God our Saviour and his love to man was seen
Tit  Not by works of righteousness which we did ourselves but in the measure of his mercy he gave us salvation through the washing of the new birth and the giving of new life in the Holy Spirit
Tit  Which he gave us freely through Jesus Christ our Saviour
Tit  So that having been given righteousness through grace we might have a part in the heritage the hope of eternal life
Tit  This is a true saying and it is my desire that you may give certain witness about these things so that those who have had faith in God may give attention to good works These things are good and of profit to men
Tit  But have nothing to do with foolish questionings and lists of generations and fights and arguments about the law for they are of no profit and foolish
Tit  A man whose opinions are not those of the church after a first and second protest is to be kept out of your society
Tit  Clearly he is in error and a sinner being selfjudged
Tit  When I send Artemas or Tychicus to you do your best to come to me at Nicopolis for it is my purpose to be there for the winter
Tit  Send Zenas the man of law and Apollos on their journey with all care so that they may be in need of nothing
Tit  And let our people go on with good works for necessary purposes so that they may not be without fruit
Tit  All who are with me send you their love Give our love to our friends in the faith Grace be with you all
Phm  Paul a prisoner of Jesus Christ and Timothy our brother to Philemon our dear helper in the faith
Phm  And to Apphia our sister and to Archippus our brother in Gods army and to the church in your house
Phm  Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ
Phm  I give praise to God at all times and make prayer for you
Phm  Hearing of the love and the faith which you have to the Lord Jesus and to all the saints
Phm  That the faith which you have in common with them may be working with power in the knowledge of every good thing in you for Christ
Phm  For I had great joy and comfort in your love because the hearts of the saints have been made strong again through you brother
Phm  And so though I might in the name of Christ give you orders to do what is right
Phm  Still because of love in place of an order I make a request to you I Paul an old man and now a prisoner of Christ Jesus
Phm  My request is for my child Onesimus the child of my chains
Phm  Who in the past was of no profit to you but now is of profit to you and to me
Phm  Whom I have sent back to you him who is my very heart
Phm  Though my desire was to keep him with me to be my servant in the chains of the good news in your place
Phm  But without your approval I would do nothing so that your good works might not be forced but done freely from your heart
Phm  For it is possible that for this reason he was parted from you for a time so that you might have him for ever
Phm  No longer as a servant but more than a servant a brother very dear to me specially but much more to you in the flesh as well as in the Lord
Phm  If then you take me to be your friend and brother take him in as myself
Phm  If he has done you any wrong or is in debt to you for anything put it to my account
Phm  I Paul writing this myself say I will make payment to you and I do not say to you that you are in debt to me even for your life
Phm  So brother let me have joy of you in the Lord give new life to my heart in Christ
Phm  Being certain that you will do my desire I am writing to you in the knowledge that you will do even more than I say
Phm  And make a room ready for me for I am hoping that through your prayers I will be given to you
Phm  Epaphras my brotherprisoner in Christ Jesus sends you his love
Phm  And so do Mark Aristarchus Demas and Luke my brotherworkers
Phm  The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit So be it
Heb  In times past the word of God came to our fathers through the prophets in different parts and in different ways
Heb  But now at the end of these days it has come to us through his Son to whom he has given all things for a heritage and through whom he made the order of the generations
Heb  Who being the outshining of his glory the true image of his substance supporting all things by the word of his power having given himself as an offering making clean from sins took his seat at the right hand of God in heaven
Heb  Having become by so much better than the angels as the name which is his heritage is more noble than theirs
Heb  To which of the angels did God say at any time You are my Son this day I have given you being or I will be his Father and he will be my Son
Heb  And again when he is sending his only Son into the world he says Let all the angels of God give him worship
Heb  And of the angels he says Who makes his angels winds and his servants flames of fire
Heb  But of the Son he says Your seat of power O God is for ever and ever and the rod of your kingdom is a rod of righteousness
Heb  You have been a lover of righteousness and a hater of evil and so God your God has put the oil of joy on your head more than on the heads of those who are with you
Heb  You Lord at the first did put the earth on its base and the heavens are the works of your hands
Heb  They will come to their end but you are for ever they will become old as a robe
Heb  They will be rolled up like a cloth even like a robe and they will be changed but you are the same and your years will have no end
Heb  But of which of the angels has he said at any time Take your seat at my right hand till I put all those who are against you under your feet
Heb  Are they not all helping spirits who are sent out as servants to those whose heritage will be salvation
Heb  For this reason there is the more need for us to give attention to the things which have come to our ears for fear that by chance we might be slipping away
Heb  Because if the word which came through the angels was fixed and in the past every evil act against Gods orders was given its full punishment
Heb  What will come on us if we do not give our minds to such a great salvation a salvation of which our fathers first had knowledge through the words of the Lord and which was made certain to us by those to whom his words came
Heb  And God was a witness with them by signs and wonders and by more than natural powers and by his distribution of the Holy Spirit at his pleasure
Heb  For he did not make the angels rulers over the world to come of which I am writing
Heb  But a certain writer has given his witness saying What is man that you keep him in mind what is the son of man that you take him into account
Heb  You made him a little lower than the angels you gave him a crown of glory and honour and made him ruler over all the works of your hands
Heb  You put all things under his feet For in making man the ruler over all things God did not put anything outside his authority though we do not see everything under him now
Heb  But we see him who was made a little lower than the angels even Jesus crowned with glory and honour because he let himself be put to death so that by the grace of God he might undergo death for all men
Heb  Because it was right for him for whom and through whom all things have being in guiding his sons to glory to make the captain of their salvation complete through pain
Heb  For he who makes holy and those who are made holy are all of one family and for this reason it is no shame for him to give them the name of brothers
Heb  Saying I will give the knowledge of your name to my brothers I will make a song of praise to you before the church
Heb  And again he says I will put my faith in him And again See I am here and the children which God has given to me
Heb  And because the children are flesh and blood he took a body himself and became like them so that by his death he might put an end to him who had the power of death that is to say the Evil One
Heb  And let those who all their lives were in chains because of their fear of death go free
Heb  For truly he does not take on the life of angels but that of the seed of Abraham
Heb  Because of this it was necessary for him to be made like his brothers in every way so that he might be a high priest full of mercy and keeping faith in everything to do with God making offerings for the sins of the people
Heb  For having been put to the test himself he is able to give help to others when they are tested
Heb  For this reason holy brothers marked out to have a part in heaven give thought to Jesus the representative and high priest of our faith
Heb  Who kept faith with God who gave him his place even as Moses did in all his house
Heb  And it was right for this man to have more honour than Moses even as the builder of a house has more honour than the house
Heb  For every house has a builder but the builder of all things is God
Heb  And Moses certainly kept faith as a servant in all his house and as a witness of those things which were to be said later
Heb  But Christ as a son over his house whose house are we if we keep our hearts fixed in the glad and certain hope till the end
Heb  And so as the Holy Spirit says Today if you let his voice come to your ears
Heb  Be not hard of heart as when you made me angry on the day of testing in the waste land
Heb  When your fathers put me to the test and saw my works for forty years
Heb  So that I was angry with this generation and I said Their hearts are in error at all times and they have no knowledge of my ways
Heb  And being angry I made an oath saying They may not come into my rest
Heb  My brothers take care that there is not by chance in any one of you an evil heart without belief turning away from the living God
Heb  But give comfort to one another every day as long as it is still Today so that no one among you may be made hard by the deceit of sin
Heb  For if we keep the substance of the faith which we had at the start even till the end we have a part with Christ
Heb  As it is said Today if you will let his voice come to your ears be not hard of heart as when you made him angry
Heb  Who made him angry when his voice came to them was it not all those who came out of Egypt with Moses
Heb  And with whom was he angry for forty years was it not with those who did evil who came to their deaths in the waste land
Heb  And to whom did he make an oath that they might not come into his rest was it not to those who went against his orders
Heb  So we see that they were not able to go in because they had no belief
Heb  Let us then though we still have Gods word that we may come into his rest go in fear that some of you may be unable to do so
Heb  And truly the good news came to us even as it did to them but the hearing of the word did them no good because they were not united in faith with the true hearers
Heb  For those of us who have belief come into his rest even as he has said As I said in my oath when I was angry They may not come into my rest though the works were done from the time of the making of the world
Heb  For in one place he has said of the seventh day And God had rest from all his works on the seventh day
Heb  And in the same place he says again They will not come into my rest
Heb  So that as it is clear that some have to go in and that the first hearers of the good news were not able to go in because they went against Gods orders
Heb  After a long time again naming a certain day he says in David Today as he had said before Today if you will let his voice come to your ears be not hard of heart
Heb  For if Joshua had given them rest he would not have said anything about another day
Heb  So that there is still a Sabbathkeeping for the people of God
Heb  For the man who comes into his rest has had rest from his works as God did from his
Heb  Because of this let us have a strong desire to come into that rest and let no one go after the example of those who went against Gods orders
Heb  For the word of God is living and full of power and is sharper than any twoedged sword cutting through and making a division even of the soul and the spirit the bones and the muscles and quick to see the thoughts and purposes of the heart
Heb  And there is nothing made which is not completely clear to him there is nothing covered but all things are open to the eyes of him with whom we have to do
Heb  Having then a great high priest who has made his way through the heavens even Jesus the Son of God let us be strong in our faith
Heb  For we have not a high priest who is not able to be touched by the feelings of our feeble flesh but we have one who has been tested in all points as we ourselves are tested but without sin
Heb  Then let us come near to the seat of grace without fear so that mercy may be given to us and we may get grace for our help in time of need
Heb  Every high priest who is taken from among men is given his position to take care of the interests of men in those things which have to do with God so that he may make offerings for sins
Heb  He is able to have feeling for those who have no knowledge and for those who are wandering from the true way because he himself is feeble
Heb  And being feeble he has to make sinofferings for himself as well as for the people
Heb  And no man who is not given authority by God as Aaron was takes this honour for himself
Heb  In the same way Christ did not take for himself the glory of being made a high priest but was given it by him who said You are my Son this day I have given you being
Heb  As he says in another place You are a priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek
Heb  Who in the days of his flesh having sent up prayers and requests with strong crying and weeping to him who was able to give him salvation from death had his prayer answered because of his fear of God
Heb  And though he was a Son through the pain which he underwent the knowledge came to him of what it was to be under Gods orders
Heb  And when he had been made complete he became the giver of eternal salvation to all those who are under his orders
Heb  Being named by God a high priest of the order of Melchizedek
Heb  Of whom we have much to say which it is hard to make clear because you are slow of hearing
Heb  And though by this time it would be right for you to be teachers you still have need of someone to give you teaching about the first simple rules of Gods revelation you have become like babies who have need of milk and not of solid food
Heb  For everyone who takes milk is without experience of the word of righteousness he is a child
Heb  But solid food is for men of full growth even for those whose senses are trained by use to see what is good and what is evil
Heb  For this reason let us go on from the first things about Christ to full growth not building again that on which it is based that is the turning of the heart from dead works and faith in God
Heb  The teaching of baptisms and of the putting on of hands and of the future life of the dead and of the judging on the last day
Heb  Now we will do this if God lets us
Heb  As for those who at one time saw the light tasting the good things from heaven and having their part in the Holy Spirit
Heb  With knowledge of the good word of God and of the powers of the coming time
Heb  And then let themselves be turned away it is not possible for their hearts to be made new a second time because they themselves put the Son of God on the cross again openly shaming him
Heb  For a land drinking in the frequent rain and producing good plants for those for whom it is worked has a blessing from God
Heb  But if it sends up thorns and evil plants it is of no use and is ready to be cursed its only end is to be burned
Heb  But my loved ones though we say this we are certain that you have better things in you things which go with salvation
Heb  For God is true and will not put away from him the memory of your work and of your love for his name in the help which you gave and still give to the saints
Heb  And it is our desire that you may all keep the same high purpose in certain hope to the end
Heb  So that you may not be slow in heart but may take as your example those to whom God has given their heritage because of their faith and their long waiting
Heb  For when God made his oath to Abraham because there was no greater oath he made it by himself
Heb  Saying Be certain that I will give you my blessing and make your numbers very great
Heb  And so when he had been waiting calmly for a long time Gods word to him was put into effect
Heb  For men at all times make their oaths by what is greater and any argument is ended by the decision of the oath
Heb  So that when it was Gods desire to make it specially clear to those who by his word were to have the heritage that his purpose was fixed he made it more certain with an oath
Heb  So that we who have gone in flight from danger to the hope which has been put before us may have a strong comfort in two unchanging things in which it is not possible for God to be false
Heb  And this hope is like a strong band for our souls fixed and certain and going in to that which is inside the veil
Heb  Where Jesus has gone before us as a high priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek
Heb  For this Melchizedek the king of Salem a priest of the Most High God who gave Abraham his blessing meeting him when he came back after putting the kings to death
Heb  And to whom Abraham gave a tenth part of everything which he had being first named King of righteousness and then in addition King of Salem that is to say King of peace
Heb  Being without father or mother or family having no birth or end to his life being made like the Son of God is a priest for ever
Heb  Now see how great this man was to whom our father Abraham gave a tenth part of what he had got in the fight
Heb  And it is true that by the law those of the sons of Levi who have the position of priests may take a tenth part of the peoples goods that is to say they take it from their brothers though these are the sons of Abraham
Heb  But this man who was not of their family took the tenth from Abraham and gave a blessing to him to whom God had given his undertaking
Heb  But there is no doubt that the less gets his blessing from the greater
Heb  Now at the present time men over whom death has power take the tenth but then it was taken by one of whom it is witnessed that he is living
Heb  And we may say that in Abraham even Levi who has a right to take the tenth part gave it
Heb  Because he was still in his fathers body when Melchizedek came to him
Heb  Now if it was possible for things to be made complete through the priests of the house of Levi for the law was given to the people in connection with them what need was there for another priest who was of the order of Melchizedek and not of the order of Aaron
Heb  Because if the priests are changed it is necessary to make a change in the law
Heb  For he of whom these things are said comes of another tribe of which no man has ever made offerings at the altar
Heb  Because it is clear that our Lord comes out of Judah and Moses said nothing about priests from that tribe
Heb  And this is even more clear if a second priest has come up who is like Melchizedek
Heb  That is to say not made by a law based on the flesh but by the power of a life without end
Heb  For it has been witnessed of him You are a priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek
Heb  So the law which went before is put on one side because it was feeble and without profit
Heb  Because the law made nothing complete and in its place there is a better hope through which we come near to God
Heb  And as this is not without the taking of an oath
Heb  For those were made priests without an oath but this one was made a priest with an oath by him who says of him The Lord gave his oath which he will not take back that you are a priest for ever
Heb  By so much is it a better agreement which we have through Jesus
Heb  And it is true that there have been a great number of those priests because death does not let them go on for ever
Heb  But this priest because his life goes on for ever is unchanging
Heb  So that he is fully able to be the saviour of all who come to God through him because he is ever living to make prayer to God for them
Heb  It was right for us to have such a high priest one who is holy and without evil doing no wrong having no part with sinners and made higher than the heavens
Heb  Who has no need to make offerings for sins every day like those high priests first for himself and then for the people because he did this once and for ever when he made an offering of himself
Heb  The law makes high priests of men who are feeble but the word of the oath which was made after the law gives that position to a Son in whom all good is for ever complete
Heb  Now of the things we are saying this is the chief point We have such a high priest who has taken his place at the right hand of Gods high seat of glory in heaven
Heb  As a servant of the holy things and of the true Tent which was put up by God not by man
Heb  Now every high priest is given authority to take to God the things which are given and to make offerings so that it is necessary for this man like them to have something for an offering
Heb  If he had been on earth he would not have been a priest at all because there are other priests who make the offerings ordered by the law
Heb  Being servants of that which is a copy and an image of the things in heaven as Moses when he was about to make the Tent had special orders from God for See he said that you make everything like the design which you saw in the mountain
Heb  But now his position as priest is higher because through him God has made a better agreement with man based on the giving of better things
Heb  For if that first agreement had been as good as possible there would have been no place for a second
Heb  For protesting against them he says See the days are coming when I will make a new agreement with the house of Israel and with the house of Judah
Heb  Not like the agreement which I made with their fathers when I took them by the hand to be their guide out of the land of Egypt for they did not keep the agreement with me and I gave them up says the Lord
Heb  For this is the agreement which I will make with the people of Israel after those days I will put my laws into their minds writing them in their hearts and I will be their God and they will be my people
Heb  And there will be no need for every man to be teaching his brother or his neighbour saying This is the knowledge of the Lord for they will all have knowledge of me great and small
Heb  And I will have mercy on their evildoing and I will not keep their sins in mind
Heb  When he says A new agreement he has made the first agreement old But anything which is getting old and past use will not be seen much longer
Heb  Now the first agreement had its rules of worship and a holy order
Heb  For the first Tent was made ready having in it the vessels for the lights and the table and the ordering of the bread and this is named the holy place
Heb  And inside the second veil was the place which is named the Holy of holies
Heb  Having a vessel of gold in it for burning perfumes and the ark of the agreement which was covered with gold and which had in it a pot made of gold for the manna and Aarons rod which put out buds and the stones with the writing of the agreement
Heb  And over it were the winged ones of glory with their wings covering the mercyseat about which it is not possible now to say anything in detail
Heb  Now while these things were in existence the priests went into the first Tent at all times for prayer and the making of offerings
Heb  But only the high priest went into the second once a year not without making an offering of blood for himself and for the errors of the people
Heb  The Holy Spirit witnessing by this that the way into the holy place had not at that time been made open while the first Tent was still in being
Heb  And this is an image of the present time when the offerings which are given are not able to make the heart of the worshipper completely clean
Heb  Because they are only rules of the flesh of meats and drinks and washings which have their place till the time comes when things will be put right
Heb  But now Christ has come as the high priest of the good things of the future through this greater and better Tent not made with hands that is to say not of this world
Heb  And has gone once and for ever into the holy place having got eternal salvation not through the blood of goats and young oxen but through his blood
Heb  For if the blood of goats and oxen and the dust from the burning of a young cow being put on the unclean make the flesh clean
Heb  How much more will the blood of Christ who being without sin made an offering of himself to God through the Holy Spirit make your hearts clean from dead works to be servants of the living God
Heb  And for this cause it is through him that a new agreement has come into being so that after the errors under the first agreement had been taken away by his death the word of God might have effect for those who were marked out for an eternal heritage
Heb  Because where there is a testament there has to be the death of the man who made it
Heb  For a testament has effect after death for what power has it while the man who made it is living
Heb  So that even the first agreement was not made without blood
Heb  For when Moses had given all the rules of the law to the people he took the blood of goats and young oxen with water and red wool and hyssop and put it on the book itself and on all the people
Heb  Saying This blood is the sign of the agreement which God has made with you
Heb  And the blood was put on the Tent and all the holy vessels in the same way
Heb  And by the law almost all things are made clean with blood and without blood there is no forgiveness
Heb  For this cause it was necessary to make the copies of the things in heaven clean with these offerings but the things themselves are made clean with better offerings than these
Heb  For Christ did not go into a holy place which had been made by mens hands as the copy of the true one but he went into heaven itself and now takes his place before the face of God for us
Heb  And he did not have to make an offering of himself again and again as the high priest goes into the holy place every year with blood which is not his
Heb  For then he would have undergone a number of deaths from the time of the making of the world but now he has come to us at the end of the old order to put away sin by the offering of himself
Heb  And because by Gods law death comes to men once and after that they are judged
Heb  So Christ having at his first coming taken on himself the sins of men will be seen a second time without sin by those who are waiting for him for their salvation
Heb  For the law being only a poor copy of the future good things and not the true image of those things is never able to make the people who come to the altar every year with the same offerings completely clean
Heb  For if this had been possible would there not have been an end of those offerings because the worshippers would have been made completely clean and would have been no longer conscious of sins
Heb  But year by year there is a memory of sins in those offerings
Heb  Because it is not possible for the blood of oxen and goats to take away sins
Heb  So that when he comes into the world he says You had no desire for offerings but you made a body ready for me
Heb  You had no joy in burned offerings or in offerings for sin
Heb  Then I said See I have come to do your pleasure O God as it is said of me in the roll of the book
Heb  After saying You had no desire for offerings for burned offerings or offerings for sin which are made by the law and you had no pleasure in them
Heb  Then he said See I have come to do your pleasure He took away the old order so that he might put the new order in its place
Heb  By that pleasure we have been made holy by the offering of the body of Jesus Christ once and for ever
Heb  And every priest takes his place at the altar day by day doing what is necessary and making again and again the same offerings which are never able to take away sins
Heb  But when Jesus had made one offering for sins for ever he took his place at the right hand of God
Heb  And has been waiting there from that time till all who are against him are made a footrest for his feet
Heb  Because by one offering he has made complete for ever those who are made holy
Heb  And the Holy Spirit is a witness for us for after he had said
Heb  This is the agreement which I will make with them after those days says the Lord I will put my laws in their hearts writing them in their minds he said
Heb  And I will keep no more memory of their sins and of their evildoings
Heb  Now where there is forgiveness of these there is no more offering for sin
Heb  So then my brothers being able to go into the holy place without fear because of the blood of Jesus
Heb  By the new and living way which he made open for us through the veil that is to say his flesh
Heb  And having a great priest over the house of God
Heb  Let us go in with true hearts in certain faith having our hearts made free from the sense of sin and our bodies washed with clean water
Heb  Let us keep the witness of our hope strong and unshaking for he is true who has given his word
Heb  And let us be moving one another at all times to love and good works
Heb  Not giving up our meetings as is the way of some but keeping one another strong in faith and all the more because you see the day coming near
Heb  For if we do evil on purpose after we have had the knowledge of what is true there is no more offering for sins
Heb  But only a great fear of being judged and of the fire of wrath which will be the destruction of the haters of God
Heb  A man who has gone against the law of Moses is put to death without pity on the word of two or three witnesses
Heb  But will not the man by whom the Son of God has been crushed under foot and the blood of the agreement with which he was washed clean has been taken as an unholy thing and who has had no respect for the Spirit of grace be judged bad enough for a very much worse punishment
Heb  For we have had experience of him who says Punishment is mine I will give reward And again The Lord will be judge of his people
Heb  We may well go in fear of falling into the hands of the living God
Heb  But give thought to the days after you had seen the light when you went through a great war of troubles
Heb  In part in being attacked by angry words and cruel acts before the eyes of everyone and in part in being united with those who were attacked in this way
Heb  For you had pity on those who were in prison and had joy in the loss of your property in the knowledge that you still had a better property and one which you would keep for ever
Heb  So do not give up your hope which will be greatly rewarded
Heb  For having done what was right in Gods eyes you have need of waiting before his word has effect for you
Heb  In a very little time he who is coming will come he will not be slow
Heb  But the upright man will be living by his faith and if he goes back my soul will have no pleasure in him
Heb  But we are not of those who go back to destruction but of those who have faith even to the salvation of the soul
Heb  Now faith is the substance of things hoped for and the sign that the things not seen are true
Heb  For by it our fathers had Gods approval
Heb  By faith it is clear to us that the order of events was fixed by the word of God so that what is seen has not been made from things which only seem to be
Heb  By faith Abel made a better offering to God than Cain and he had witness through it of his righteousness God giving his approval of his offering and his voice still comes to us through it though he is dead
Heb  By faith Enoch was taken up to heaven so that he did not see death he was seen no longer for God took him away for before he was taken witness had been given that he was wellpleasing to God
Heb  And without faith it is not possible to be wellpleasing to him for it is necessary for anyone who comes to God to have the belief that God is and that he is a rewarder of all those who make a serious search for him
Heb  By faith Noah being moved by the fear of God made ready an ark for the salvation of his family because God had given him news of things which were not seen at the time and through it the world was judged by him and he got for his heritage the righteousness which is by faith
Heb  By faith Abraham did as God said when he was ordered to go out into a place which was to be given to him as a heritage and went out without knowledge of where he was going
Heb  By faith he was a wanderer in the land of the agreement as in a strange land living in tents with Isaac and Jacob who had a part with him in the same heritage
Heb  For he was looking for the strong town whose builder and maker is God
Heb  And by faith Sarah herself had power to give birth when she was very old because she had faith in him who gave his word
Heb  So that from one man who was near to death came children in number as the stars in heaven or as the sand by the seaside which may not be numbered
Heb  All these came to their end in faith not having had the heritage but having seen it with delight far away they gave witness that they were wanderers and not of the earth
Heb  For those who say such things make it clear that they are searching for a country for themselves
Heb  And truly if they had kept in mind the country from which they went out they would have had chances of turning back
Heb  But now their desire is for a better country that is to say for one in heaven and so it is no shame to God to be named their God for he has made ready a town for them
Heb  By faith Abraham made an offering of Isaac when he was tested and he with whom the agreement had been made gave up as an offering the only son of his body
Heb  Of whom it had been said From Isaac will your seed take their name
Heb  Judging that God was able to give life even to the dead and because of this he did get him back as if from death
Heb  By faith Isaac blessing Jacob and Esau gave news of things to come
Heb  By faith Jacob gave a blessing to the two sons of Joseph when he was near to death and gave God worship supported by his stick
Heb  By faith Joseph when his end was near said that the children of Israel would go out of Egypt and gave orders about his bones
Heb  By faith Moses was kept secretly by his father and mother for three months after his birth because they saw that he was a fair child and they had no fear of the kings orders
Heb  By faith Moses when he became a man had no desire to be named the son of Pharaohs daughter
Heb  Feeling that it was better to undergo pain with the people of God than for a short time to have a taste of the pleasures of sin
Heb  Judging a part in the shame of Christ to be better than all the wealth of Egypt for he was looking forward to his reward
Heb  By faith he went out of Egypt not being turned from his purpose by fear of the wrath of the king for he kept on his way as seeing him who is unseen
Heb  By faith he kept the Passover and put the sign of the blood on the houses so that the angel of destruction might not put their oldest sons to death
Heb  By faith they went through the Red Sea as if it had been dry land though the Egyptians were overcome by the water when they made an attempt to do the same
Heb  By faith the walls of Jericho came down after they had been circled for seven days
Heb  By faith Rahab the loose woman was not put to death with those who had gone against Gods orders because she had taken into her house in peace those sent to see the land
Heb  What more am I to say For there would not be time to give the stories of Gideon Barak Samson and Jephthah of David and Samuel and the prophets
Heb  Who through faith overcame kingdoms did righteousness got their reward kept the mouths of lions shut
Heb  Put out the power of fire got safely away from the edge of the sword were made strong when they had been feeble became full of power in war and put to flight the armies of the nations
Heb  Women had their dead given back to them living others let themselves be cruelly attacked having no desire to go free so that they might have a better life to come
Heb  And others were tested by being laughed at or by blows and even with chains and prisons
Heb  They were stoned they were cut up with knives they were tested they were put to death with the sword they went about in sheepskins and in goatskins being poor and in pain and cruelly attacked
Heb  Wandering in waste places and in mountains and in holes in the rocks for whom the world was not good enough
Heb  And not one of these got the good things of the agreement though they all had a good record through faith
Heb  Because God had kept some better thing for us so that it was not possible for them to become complete without us
Heb  For this reason as we are circled by so great a cloud of witnesses putting off every weight and the sin into which we come so readily let us keep on running in the way which is marked out for us
Heb  Having our eyes fixed on Jesus the guide and end of our faith who went through the pains of the cross not caring for the shame because of the joy which was before him and who has now taken his place at the right hand of Gods seat of power
Heb  Give thought to him who has undergone so much of the hate of sinners against himself so that you may not be tired and feeble of purpose
Heb  Till now you have not given your blood in your fight against sin
Heb  And you have not kept in mind the word which says to you as to sons My son do not make little of the Lords punishment and do not give up hope when you are judged by him
Heb  For the Lord sends punishment on his loved ones everyone whom he takes as his son has experience of his rod
Heb  It is for your training that you undergo these things God is acting to you as a father does to his sons for what son does not have punishment from his father
Heb  But if you have not that punishment of which we all have our part then you are not true sons but children of shame
Heb  And again if the fathers of our flesh gave us punishment and had our respect how much more will we be under the authority of the Father of spirits and have life
Heb  For they truly gave us punishment for a short time as it seemed good to them but he does it for our profit so that we may become holy as he is
Heb  At the time all punishment seems to be pain and not joy but after those who have been trained by it get from it the peacegiving fruit of righteousness
Heb  For this cause let the hands which are hanging down be lifted up and let the feeble knees be made strong
Heb  And make straight roads for your feet so that the feeble may not be turned out of the way but may be made strong
Heb  Let your desire be for peace with all men and to be made holy without which no man may see the Lord
Heb  Looking with care to see that no man among you in his behaviour comes short of the grace of God for fear that some bitter root may come up to be a trouble to you and that some of you may be made unclean by it
Heb  And that there may not be any evil liver or any man without respect for God like Esau who let his birthright go for a plate of food
Heb  For you have knowledge that even long after when he was desiring the blessing for his heritage he was turned away though he made his request frequently and with weeping because the past might not be changed
Heb  You have not come to a mountain which may be touched and is burning with fire and to a black cloud and a dark smoke and a violent wind
Heb  And to the sound of a horn and the voice of words the hearers of which made request that not a word more might be said to them
Heb  For the order which said If the mountain is touched even by a beast the beast is to be stoned seemed hard to them
Heb  And the vision was so overpowering that even Moses said I am shaking and full of fear
Heb  But you have come to the mountain of Zion to the place of the living God to the Jerusalem which is in heaven and to an army of angels which may not be numbered
Heb  To the great meeting and church of the first of those who are named in heaven and to God the judge of all and to the spirits of good men made complete
Heb  And to Jesus by whom the new agreement has been made between God and man and to the sign of the blood which says better things than Abels blood
Heb  See that you give ear to his voice which comes to you For if those whose ears were shut to the voice which came to them on earth did not go free from punishment what chance have we of going free if we give no attention to him whose voice comes from heaven
Heb  Whose voice was the cause of the shaking of the earth but now he has made an oath saying There will be still one more shaking not only of the earth but of heaven
Heb  And the words Still one more make it clear that there will be a taking away of those things which are shaking as of things which are made so that there may be only those things of which no shaking is possible
Heb  If then we have a kingdom which will never be moved let us have grace so that we may give God such worship as is pleasing to him with fear and respect
Heb  For our God is an allburning fire
Heb  Go on loving your brothers in the faith
Heb  Take care to keep open house because in this way some have had angels as their guests without being conscious of it
Heb  Keep in mind those who are in chains as if you were chained with them and those who are in trouble as being yourselves in the body
Heb  Let married life be honoured among all of you and not made unclean for men untrue in married life will be judged by God
Heb  Be free from the love of money and pleased with the things which you have for he himself has said I will be with you at all times
Heb  So that we say with a good heart The Lord is my helper I will have no fear what is man able to do to me
Heb  Keep in mind those who were over you and who gave you the word of God seeing the outcome of their way of life let your faith be like theirs
Heb  Jesus Christ is the same yesterday and today and for ever
Heb  Do not be turned away by different strange teachings because it is good for your hearts to be made strong by grace and not by meats which were of no profit to those who took so much trouble over them
Heb  We have an altar from which those priests who are servants in the Tent may not take food
Heb  For the bodies of the beasts whose blood is taken into the holy place by the high priest as an offering for sin are burned outside the circle of the tents
Heb  For this reason Jesus was put to death outside the walls so that he might make the people holy by his blood
Heb  Let us then go out to him outside the circle of the tents taking his shame on ourselves
Heb  For here we have no fixed restingplace but our search is for the one which is to come
Heb  Let us then make offerings of praise to God at all times through him that is to say the fruit of lips giving witness to his name
Heb  But go on doing good and giving to others because God is wellpleased with such offerings
Heb  Give ear to those who are rulers over you and do as they say for they keep watch over your souls ready to give an account of them let them be able to do this with joy and not with grief because that would be of no profit to you
Heb  Make prayers for us for we are certain that our hearts are free from the sense of sin desiring the right way of life in all things
Heb  I make this request more strongly in the hope of coming back to you more quickly
Heb  Now may the God of peace who made that great keeper of his flock even our Lord Jesus come back from the dead through the blood of the eternal agreement
Heb  Make you full of every good work and ready to do all his desires working in us whatever is pleasing in his eyes through Jesus Christ and may the glory be given to him for ever and ever So be it
Heb  But brothers take kindly the words which I have said for your profit for I have not sent you a long letter
Heb  Our brother Timothy has been let out of prison and if he comes here in a short time he and I will come to you together
Heb  Give words of love from me to those who are rulers over you and to all the saints Those who are in Italy send you their love
Heb  May grace be with you all
Jas  James a servant of God and of the Lord Jesus Christ sends words of love to the twelve tribes of the Jews living in all parts of the earth
Jas  Let it be all joy to you my brothers when you undergo tests of every sort
Jas  Because you have the knowledge that the testing of your faith gives you the power of going on in hope
Jas  But let this power have its full effect so that you may be made complete needing nothing
Jas  But if any man among you is without wisdom let him make his request to God who gives freely to all without an unkind word and it will be given to him
Jas  Let him make his request in faith doubting nothing for he who has doubt in his heart is like the waves of the sea which are troubled by the driving of the wind
Jas  Let it not seem to such a man that he will get anything from the Lord
Jas  For there is a division in his mind and he is uncertain in all his ways
Jas  But let the brother of low position be glad that he is lifted up
Jas  But the man of wealth that he is made low because like the flower of the grass he will come to his end
Jas  For when the sun comes up with its burning heat the grass gets dry and the grace of its form is gone with the falling flower so the man of wealth comes to nothing in his ways
Jas  There is a blessing on the man who undergoes testing because if he has Gods approval he will be given the crown of life which the Lord has said he will give to those who have love for him
Jas  Let no man say when he is tested I am tested by God for it is not possible for God to be tested by evil and he himself puts no man to such a test
Jas  But every man is tested when he is turned out of the right way by the attraction of his desire
Jas  Then when its time comes desire gives birth to sin and sin when it is of full growth gives birth to death
Jas  Do not be turned from the right way dear brothers
Jas  Every good and true thing is given to us from heaven coming from the Father of lights with whom there is no change or any shade made by turning
Jas  Of his purpose he gave us being by his true word so that we might be in a sense the firstfruits of all the things which he had made
Jas  You have knowledge of this dear brothers But let every man be quick in hearing slow in words slow to get angry
Jas  For the righteousness of God does not come about by the wrath of man
Jas  For this reason putting away all dirty behaviour and the overweight of evil take into your souls without pride the word which being planted there is able to give you salvation
Jas  But be doers of the word and not only hearers of it blinding yourselves with false ideas
Jas  Because if any man is a hearer of the word and not a doer he is like a man looking at his natural face in a glass
Jas  For after looking at himself he goes away and in a short time he has no memory of what he was like
Jas  But he who goes on looking into the true law which makes him free being not a hearer without memory but a doer putting it into effect this man will have a blessing on his acts
Jas  If a man seems to have religion and has no control over his tongue but lets himself be tricked by what is false this mans religion is of no value
Jas  The religion which is holy and free from evil in the eyes of our God and Father is this to take care of children who have no fathers and of widows who are in trouble and to keep oneself untouched by the world
Jas  My brothers if you have the faith of our Lord Jesus Christ of glory do not take a mans position into account
Jas  For if a man comes into your Synagogue in fair clothing and with a gold ring and a poor man comes in with dirty clothing
Jas  And you do honour to the man in fair clothing and say Come here and take this good place and you say to the poor man Take up your position there or be seated at my feet
Jas  Is there not a division in your minds have you not become judges with evil thoughts
Jas  Give ear my dear brothers are not those who are poor in the things of this world marked out by God to have faith as their wealth and for their heritage the kingdom which he has said he will give to those who have love for him
Jas  But you have put the poor man to shame Are not the men of wealth rulers over you do they not take you by force before their judges
Jas  Do they not say evil of the holy name which was given to you
Jas  But if you keep the greatest law of all as it is given in the holy Writings Have love for your neighbour as for yourself you do well
Jas  But if you take a mans position into account you do evil and are judged as evildoers by the law
Jas  For anyone who keeps all the law but makes a slip in one point is judged to have gone against it all
Jas  For he who said Do not be untrue in married life is the same who said Put no man to death Now if you are not untrue in married life but you put a man to death the law is broken
Jas  Let your words and your acts be those of men who are to be judged by the law which makes free
Jas  For the man who has had no mercy will be judged without mercy but mercy takes pride in overcoming judging
Jas  What use is it my brothers for a man to say that he has faith if he does nothing will such a faith give him salvation
Jas  If a brother or a sister is without clothing and in need of the days food
Jas  And one of you says to them Go in peace be warm and full of food but you do not give them the things of which their bodies have need what profit is there in this
Jas  Even so faith without works is dead
Jas  But a man may say You have faith and I have works let me see your faith without your works and I will make my faith clear to you by my works
Jas  You have the belief that God is one and you do well the evil spirits have the same belief shaking with fear
Jas  Do you not see O foolish man that faith without works is of no use
Jas  Was not the righteousness of Abraham our father judged by his works when he made an offering of Isaac his son on the altar
Jas  You see that his faith was helping his works and was made complete by them
Jas  And the holy Writings were put into effect which said And Abraham had faith in God and it was put to his account as righteousness and he was named the friend of God
Jas  You see that a mans righteousness is judged by his works and not by his faith only
Jas  And in the same way was not the righteousness of Rahab the loose woman judged by her works when she took into her house those who were sent and let them go out by another way
Jas  For as the body without the spirit is dead even so faith without works is dead
Jas  Do not all be teachers my brothers because we teachers will be judged more hardly than others
Jas  For we all go wrong in a number of things If a man never makes a slip in his talk then he is a complete man and able to keep all his body in control
Jas  Now if we put bits of iron into horses mouths so that they may be guided by us we have complete control of their bodies
Jas  And again ships though they are so great and are moved by violent winds are turned by a very small guidingblade at the impulse of the man who is using it
Jas  Even so the tongue is a small part of the body but it takes credit for great things How much wood may be lighted by a very little fire
Jas  And the tongue is a fire it is the power of evil placed in our bodies making all the body unclean putting the wheel of life on fire and getting its fire from hell
Jas  For every sort of beast and bird and every living thing on earth and in the sea has been controlled by man and is under his authority
Jas  But the tongue may not be controlled by man it is an unresting evil it is full of the poison of death
Jas  With it we give praise to our Lord and Father and with it we put a curse on men who are made in Gods image
Jas  Out of the same mouth comes blessing and cursing My brothers it is not right for these things to be so
Jas  Does the fountain send from the same outlet sweet and bitter water
Jas  Is a figtree able to give us olives my brothers or do we get figs from a vine or sweet water from the salt sea
Jas  Who has wisdom and good sense among you let him make his works clear by a life of gentle wisdom
Jas  But if you have bitter envy in your heart and the desire to get the better of others have no pride in this talking falsely against what is true
Jas  This wisdom is not from heaven but is of the earth and the flesh and the Evil One
Jas  For where envy is and the desire to get the better of others there is no order but every sort of evildoing
Jas  But the wisdom which is from heaven is first holy then gentle readily giving way in argument full of peace and mercy and good works not doubting not seeming other than it is
Jas  And the fruit of righteousness is planted in peace for those who make peace
Jas  What is the cause of wars and fighting among you is it not in your desires which are at war in your bodies
Jas  You are burning with desire and have not your desire so you put men to death you are full of envy and you are not able to get your desire so you are fighting and making war you have not your desire because you do not make request for it
Jas  You make your request but you do not get it because your request has been wrongly made desiring the thing only so that you may make use of it for your pleasure
Jas  O you who are false to God do you not see that the friends of this world are not Gods friends Every man desiring to be a friend of this world makes himself a hater of God
Jas  Or does it seem to you that it is for nothing that the holy Writings say The spirit which God put into our hearts has a strong desire for us
Jas  But he gives more grace So that the Writings say God is against the men of pride but he gives grace to those who make themselves low before him
Jas  For this cause be ruled by God but make war on the Evil One and he will be put to flight before you
Jas  Come near to God and he will come near to you Make your hands clean you evildoers put away deceit from your hearts you false in mind
Jas  Be troubled with sorrow and weeping let your laughing be turned to sorrow and your joy to grief
Jas  Make yourselves low in the eyes of the Lord and you will be lifted up by him
Jas  Do not say evil against one another my brothers He who says evil against his brother or makes himself his brothers judge says evil against the law and is judging the law and in judging the law you become not a doer of the law but a judge
Jas  There is only one judge and lawgiver even he who has the power of salvation and of destruction but who are you to be your neighbours judge
Jas  How foolish it is to say Today or tomorrow we will go into this town and be there for a year and do business there and get wealth
Jas  When you are not certain what will take place tomorrow What is your life It is a mist which is seen for a little time and then is gone
Jas  But the right thing to say would be If it is the Lords pleasure and if we are still living we will do this and that
Jas  But now you go on glorying in your pride and all such glorying is evil
Jas  The man who has knowledge of how to do good and does not do it to him it is sin
Jas  Come now you men of wealth give yourselves to weeping and crying because of the bitter troubles which are coming to you
Jas  Your wealth is unclean and insects have made holes in your clothing
Jas  Your gold and your silver are wasted and their waste will be a witness against you burning into your flesh You have put by your store in the last days
Jas  See the money which you falsely kept back from the workers cutting the grass in your field is crying out against you and the cries of those who took in your grain have come to the ears of the Lord of armies
Jas  You have been living delicately on earth and have taken your pleasure you have made your hearts fat for a day of destruction
Jas  You have given your decision against the upright man and have put him to death He puts up no fight against you
Jas  Go on waiting calmly my brothers till the coming of the Lord like the farmer waiting for the good fruit of the earth till the early and late rains have come
Jas  Be as calm in your waiting let your hearts be strong because the coming of the Lord is near
Jas  Say no hard things against one another brothers so that you will not be judged see the judge is waiting at the doors
Jas  Take as an example of pain nobly undergone and of strength in trouble the prophets who gave to men the words of the Lord
Jas  We say that those men who have gone through pain are happy you have the story of Job and the troubles through which he went and have seen that the Lord was full of pity and mercy in the end
Jas  But most of all my brothers do not take oaths not by the heaven or by the earth or by any other thing but let your Yes be Yes and your No be No so that you may not be judged
Jas  Is anyone among you in trouble let him say prayers Is anyone glad let him make a song of praise
Jas  Is anyone among you ill let him send for the rulers of the church and let them say prayers over him putting oil on him in the name of the Lord
Jas  And by the prayer of faith the man who is ill will be made well and he will be lifted up by the Lord and for any sin which he has done he will have forgiveness
Jas  So then make a statement of your sins to one another and say prayers for one another so that you may be made well The prayer of a good man is full of power in its working
Jas  Elijah was a man of flesh and blood as we are and he made a strong prayer that there might be no rain and there was no rain on the earth for three years and six months
Jas  And he made another prayer and the heaven sent down rain and the earth gave her fruit
Jas  My brothers if one of you has gone out of the way of the true faith and another has made him see his error
Jas  Be certain that he through whom a sinner has been turned from the error of his way keeps a soul from death and is the cause of forgiveness for sins without number
Pe  Peter an Apostle of Jesus Christ to the saints who are living in Pontus Galatia Cappadocia Asia and Bithynia
Pe  Who through the purpose of God have been made holy by the Spirit disciples of Jesus made clean by his blood May you have grace and peace in full measure
Pe  Praise be to the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ who through his great mercy has given us a new birth and a living hope by the coming again of Jesus Christ from the dead
Pe  And a heritage fair holy and for ever new waiting in heaven for you
Pe  Who by the power of God are kept through faith for that salvation which will be seen at the last day
Pe  You have cause for great joy in this though it may have been necessary for you to be troubled for a little time being tested in all sorts of ways
Pe  So that the true metal of your faith being of much greater value than gold which though it comes to an end is tested by fire may come to light in praise and glory and honour at the revelation of Jesus Christ
Pe  To whom your love is given though you have not seen him and the faith which you have in him though you do not see him now gives you joy greater than words and full of glory
Pe  For so you have the true end of your faith even the salvation of your souls
Pe  For the prophets who gave the news of the grace which would come to you made search with all care for knowledge of this salvation
Pe  Attempting to see what sort of time the Spirit of Christ which was in them was pointing to when it gave witness to the pains which Christ would undergo and the glories which would come after them
Pe  And it was made clear to those prophets that they were Gods servants not for themselves but for you to give you word of the things which have now come to your ears from the preachers of the good news through the Holy Spirit sent down from heaven things which even angels have a desire to see
Pe  So make your minds ready and keep on the watch hoping with all your power for the grace which is to come to you at the revelation of Jesus Christ
Pe  Like children ruled by God do not go back to the old desires of the time when you were without knowledge
Pe  But be holy in every detail of your lives as he whose servants you are is holy
Pe  Because it has been said in the Writings You are to be holy for I am holy
Pe  And if you give the name of Father to him who judging every man by his acts has no respect for a mans position then go in fear while you are on this earth
Pe  Being conscious that you have been made free from that foolish way of life which was your heritage from your fathers not through a payment of things like silver or gold which come to destruction
Pe  But through holy blood like that of a clean and unmarked lamb even the blood of Christ
Pe  Who was marked out by God before the making of the world but was caused to be seen in these last times for you
Pe  Who through him have faith in God who took him up again from the dead into glory so that your faith and hope might be in God
Pe  And as you have made your souls clean being ruled by what is true and loving one another without deceit see that your love is warm and from the heart
Pe  Because you have had a new birth not from the seed of man but from eternal seed through the word of a living and unchanging God
Pe  For it is said All flesh is like grass and all its glory like the flower of the grass The grass becomes dry and the flower dead
Pe  But the word of the Lord is eternal And this is the word of the good news which was given to you
Pe  So putting away all wrongdoing and all tricks and deceits and envies and evil talk
Pe  Be full of desire for the true milk of the word as babies at their mothers breasts so that you may go on to salvation
Pe  If you have had a taste of the grace of the Lord
Pe  To whom you come as to a living stone not honoured by men but of great and special value to God
Pe  You as living stones are being made into a house of the spirit a holy order of priests making those offerings of the spirit which are pleasing to God through Jesus Christ
Pe  Because it is said in the Writings See I am placing a keystone in Zion of great and special value and the man who has faith in him will not be put to shame
Pe  And the value is for you who have faith but it is said for those without faith The very stone which the builders put on one side was made the chief stone of the building
Pe  And A stone of falling a rock of trouble the word is the cause of their fall because they go against it and this was the purpose of God
Pe  But you are a special people a holy nation priests and kings a people given up completely to God so that you may make clear the virtues of him who took you out of the dark into the light of heaven
Pe  In the past you were not a people but now you are the people of God then there was no mercy for you but now mercy has been given to you
Pe  My loved ones I make this request with all my heart that as those for whom this world is a strange country you will keep yourselves from the desires of the flesh which make war against the soul
Pe  Being of good behaviour among the Gentiles so that though they say now that you are evildoers they may see your good works and give glory to God when he comes to be their judge
Pe  Keep all the laws of men because of the Lord those of the king who is over all
Pe  And those of the rulers who are sent by him for the punishment of evildoers and for the praise of those who do well
Pe  Because it is Gods pleasure that foolish and narrowminded men may be put to shame by your good behaviour
Pe  As those who are free not using your free position as a cover for wrongdoing but living as the servants of God
Pe  Have respect for all loving the brothers fearing God honouring the king
Pe  Servants take orders from your masters with all respect not only if they are good and gentle but even if they are badhumoured
Pe  For it is a sign of grace if a man desiring to do right in the eyes of God undergoes pain as punishment for something which he has not done
Pe  What credit is it if when you have done evil you take your punishment quietly but if you are given punishment for doing right and take it quietly this is pleasing to God
Pe  This is Gods purpose for you because Jesus himself underwent punishment for you giving you an example so that you might go in his footsteps
Pe  Who did no evil and there was no deceit in his mouth
Pe  To sharp words he gave no sharp answer when he was undergoing pain no angry word came from his lips but he put himself into the hands of the judge of righteousness
Pe  He took our sins on himself giving his body to be nailed on the tree so that we being dead to sin might have a new life in righteousness and by his wounds we have been made well
Pe  Because like sheep you had gone out of the way but now you have come back to him who keeps watch over your souls
Pe  Wives be ruled by your husbands so that even if some of them give no attention to the word their hearts may be changed by the behaviour of their wives
Pe  When they see your holy behaviour in the fear of God
Pe  Do not let your ornaments be those of the body such as dressing of the hair or putting on of jewels of gold or fair clothing
Pe  But let them be those of the unseen man of the heart the evershining ornament of a gentle and quiet spirit which is of great price in the eyes of God
Pe  And these were the ornaments of the holy women of the past whose hope was in God being ruled by their husbands
Pe  As Sarah was ruled by Abraham naming him lord whose children you are if you do well and are not put in fear by any danger
Pe  And you husbands give thought to your way of life with your wives giving honour to the woman who is the feebler vessel but who has an equal part in the heritage of the grace of life so that you may not be kept from prayer
Pe  Last of all see that you are all in agreement feeling for one another loving one another like brothers full of pity without pride
Pe  Not giving back evil for evil or curse for curse but in place of cursing blessing because this is the purpose of God for you that you may have a heritage of blessing
Pe  For it is said Let the man who has a love of life desiring to see good days keep his tongue from evil and his lips from words of deceit
Pe  And let him be turned from evil and do good searching for peace and going after it with all his heart
Pe  For the eyes of the Lord are on the upright and his ears are open to their prayers but the face of the Lord is against those who do evil
Pe  Who will do you any damage if you keep your minds fixed on what is good
Pe  But you are happy if you undergo pain because of righteousness have no part in their fear and do not be troubled
Pe  But give honour to Christ in your hearts as your Lord and be ready at any time when you are questioned about the hope which is in you to give an answer in the fear of the Lord and without pride
Pe  Being conscious that you have done no wrong so that those who say evil things about your good way of life as Christians may be put to shame
Pe  Because if it is Gods purpose for you to undergo pain it is better to do so for welldoing than for evildoing
Pe  Because Christ once went through pain for sins the upright one taking the place of sinners so that through him we might come back to God being put to death in the flesh but given life in the Spirit
Pe  By whom he went to the spirits in prison preaching to those
Pe  Who in the days of Noah went against Gods orders but God in his mercy kept back the punishment while Noah got ready the ark in which a small number that is to say eight persons got salvation through water
Pe  And baptism of which this is an image now gives you salvation not by washing clean the flesh but by making you free from the sense of sin before God through the coming again of Jesus Christ from the dead
Pe  Who has gone into heaven and is at the right hand of God angels and authorities and powers having been put under his rule
Pe  So that as Jesus was put to death in the flesh do you yourselves be of the same mind for the death of the flesh puts an end to sin
Pe  So that you may give the rest of your lives in the flesh not to the desires of men but to the purpose of God
Pe  Because for long enough in times past we have been living after the way of the Gentiles given up to the desires of the flesh to drinking and feasting and loose behaviour and unclean worship of images
Pe  And they are wondering that you no longer go with them in this violent wasting of life and are saying evil things of you
Pe  But they will have to give an account of themselves to him who is ready to be the judge of the living and the dead
Pe  For this was the reason why the good news of Jesus was given even to the dead so that they might be judged as men in the flesh but might be living before God in the spirit
Pe  But the end of all things is near so be serious in your behaviour and keep on the watch with prayer
Pe  And most of all be warm in your love for one another because in love there is forgiveness for sins without number
Pe  Keep open house for all with a glad heart
Pe  Making distribution among one another of whatever has been given to you like true servants of the unmeasured grace of God
Pe  If anyone has anything to say let it be as the words of God if anyone has the desire to be the servant of others let him do it in the strength which is given by God so that in all things God may have the glory through Jesus Christ whose are the glory and the power for ever
Pe  Dear brothers do not be surprised as if it was something strange if your faith is tested as by fire
Pe  But be glad that you are given a part in the pains of Christ so that at the revelation of his glory you may have great joy
Pe  If men say evil things of you because of the name of Christ happy are you for the Spirit of glory and of God is resting on you
Pe  Let no one among you undergo punishment as a taker of life or as a thief or as an evildoer or as one who is overinterested in other mens business
Pe  But if he undergoes punishment as a Christian that is no shame to him let him give glory to God in this name
Pe  For the time has come for the judging starting with the church of God but if it makes a start with us what will be the end of those who are not under the rule of God
Pe  And if it is hard for even the good man to get salvation what chance has the man without religion or the sinner
Pe  For this reason let those who by the purpose of God undergo punishment keep on in welldoing and put their souls into the safe hands of their Maker
Pe  I who am myself one of the rulers of the church and a witness of the death of Christ having my part in the coming glory send this serious request to the chief men among you
Pe  Keep watch over the flock of God which is in your care using your authority not as forced to do so but gladly and not for unclean profit but with a ready mind
Pe  Not as lords over Gods heritage but making yourselves examples to the flock
Pe  And at the coming of the chief Keeper of the sheep you will be given the eternal crown of glory
Pe  And in the same way let the younger men be ruled by the older ones Let all of you put away pride and make yourselves ready to be servants for God is a hater of pride but he gives grace to those who make themselves low
Pe  For this cause make yourselves low under the strong hand of God so that when the time comes you may be lifted up
Pe  Putting all your troubles on him for he takes care of you
Pe  Be serious and keep watch the Evil One who is against you goes about like a lion with open mouth in search of food
Pe  Do not give way to him but be strong in your faith in the knowledge that your brothers who are in the world undergo the same troubles
Pe  And after you have undergone pain for a little time the God of all grace who has given you a part in his eternal glory through Christ Jesus will himself give you strength and support and make you complete in every good thing
Pe  His is the power for ever So be it
